mat|1|1|	biblos geneseōs iēsou christou, uiou dauid uiou abraam.
mat|1|2|	abraam egennēse ton isaak, isaak de egennēse ton iakōb, iakōb de egennēse ton ioudan kai tous adelphous autou,
mat|1|3|	ioudas de egennēse ton phares kai ton zara ek tēs thamar, phares de egennēse ton esrōm, esrōm de egennēse ton aram,
mat|1|4|	aram de egennēse ton aminadab, aminadab de egennēse ton naassōn, naassōn de egennēse ton salmōn,
mat|1|5|	salmōn de egennēse ton booz ek tēs rachab, booz de egennēse ton ōbēd ek tēs routh, ōbēd de egennēse ton iessai,
mat|1|6|	iessai de egennēse ton dauid ton basilea. dauid de o basileus egennēse ton solomōna ek tēs tou ouriou,
mat|1|7|	solomōn de egennēse ton roboam, roboam de egennēse ton abia, abia de egennēse ton asa,
mat|1|8|	asa de egennēse ton iōsaphat, iōsaphat de egennēse ton iōram, iōram de egennēse ton ozian,
mat|1|9|	ozias de egennēse ton iōatham, iōatham de egennēse ton achaz, achaz de egennēse ton ezekian,
mat|1|10|	ezekias de egennēse ton manassē, manassēs de egennēse ton amōn, amōn de egennēse ton iōsian,
mat|1|11|	iōsias de egennēse ton iechonian kai tous adelphous autou epi tēs metoikesias babulōnos.
mat|1|12|	meta de tēn metoikesian babulōnos iechonias egennēse ton salathiēl, salathiēl de egennēse ton zorobabel,
mat|1|13|	zorobabel de egennēse ton abioud, abioud de egennēse ton eliakeim, eliakeim de egennēse ton azōr,
mat|1|14|	azōr de egennēse ton sadōk, sadōk de egennēse ton acheim, acheim de egennēse ton elioud,
mat|1|15|	elioud de egennēse ton eleazar, eleazar de egennēse ton matthan, matthan de egennēse ton iakōb,
mat|1|16|	iakōb de egennēse ton iōsēph ton andra marias, ex ēs egennēthē iēsous o legomenos christos.
mat|1|17|	pasai oun ai geneai apo abraam eōs dauid geneai dekatessares, kai apo dauid eōs tēs metoikesias babulōnos geneai dekatessares, kai apo tēs metoikesias babulōnos eōs tou christou geneai dekatessares.
mat|1|18|	tou de iēsou christou ē gennēsis outōs ēn. mnēsteutheisēs gar tēs mētros autou marias tō iōsēph, prin ē sunelthein autous eurethē en gastri echousa ek pneumatos agiou.
mat|1|19|	iōsēph de o anēr autēs, dikaios ōn kai mē thelōn autēn paradeigmatisai, eboulēthē lathra apolusai autēn.
mat|1|20|	tauta de autou enthumēthentos idou aggelos kuriou kat onar ephanē autō legōn iōsēph uios dauid, mē phobēthēs paralabein mariam tēn gunaika sou to gar en autē gennēthen ek pneumatos estin agiou.
mat|1|21|	texetai de uion kai kaleseis to onoma autou iēsoun autos gar sōsei ton laon autou apo tōn amartiōn autōn.
mat|1|22|	touto de olon gegonen ina plērōthē to rēthen upo tou kuriou dia tou prophētou legontos
mat|1|23|	idou ē parthenos en gastri exei kai texetai uion, kai kalesousi to onoma autou emmanouēl, o esti methermēneuomenon meth ēmōn o theos.
mat|1|24|	diegertheis de o iōsēph apo tou upnou epoiēsen ōs prosetaxen autō o aggelos kuriou kai parelabe tēn gunaika autou,
mat|1|25|	kai ouk eginōsken autēn eōs ou eteke ton uion autēs ton prōtotokon, kai ekalese to onoma autou iēsoun.
mat|2|1|	tou de iēsou gennēthentos en bēthleem tēs ioudaias en ēmerais ērōdou tou basileōs, idou magoi apo anatolōn paregenonto eis ierosoluma
mat|2|2|	legontes pou estin o techtheis basileus tōn ioudaiōn? eidomen gar autou ton astera en tē anatolē kai ēlthomen proskunēsai autō.
mat|2|3|	akousas de ērōdēs o basileus etarachthē kai pasa ierosoluma met autou,
mat|2|4|	kai sunagagōn pantas tous archiereis kai grammateis tou laou epunthaneto par autōn pou o christos gennatai.
mat|2|5|	oi de eipon autō en bēthleem tēs ioudaias outō gar gegraptai dia tou prophētou
mat|2|6|	kai su bēthleem, gē iouda, oudamōs elachistē ei en tois ēgemosin iouda ek sou gar exeleusetai ēgoumenos, ostis poimanei ton laon mou ton israēl.
mat|2|7|	tote ērōdēs lathra kalesas tous magous ēkribōse par autōn ton chronon tou phainomenou asteros,
mat|2|8|	kai pempsas autous eis bēthleem eipe poreuthentes akribōs exetasate peri tou paidiou, epan de eurēte, apaggeilate moi, opōs kagō elthōn proskunēsō autō.
mat|2|9|	oi de akousantes tou basileōs eporeuthēsan kai idou o astēr on eidon en tē anatolē proēgen autous, eōs elthōn estē epanō ou ēn to paidion
mat|2|10|	idontes de ton astera echarēsan charan megalēn sphodra,
mat|2|11|	kai elthontes eis tēn oikian eidon to paidion meta marias tēs mētros autou, kai pesontes prosekunēsan autō, kai anoixantes tous thēsaurous autōn prosēnegkan autō dōra, chruson kai libanon kai smurnan
mat|2|12|	kai chrēmatisthentes kat onar mē anakampsai pros ērōdēn, di allēs odou anechōrēsan eis tēn chōran autōn.
mat|2|13|	anachōrēsantōn de autōn idou aggelos kuriou phainetai kat onar tō iōsēph legōn egertheis paralabe to paidion kai tēn mētera autou kai pheuge eis aigupton, kai isthi ekei eōs an eipō soi mellei gar ērōdēs zētein to paidion tou apolesai auto.
mat|2|14|	o de egertheis parelabe to paidion kai tēn mētera autou nuktos kai anechōrēsen eis aigupton,
mat|2|15|	kai ēn ekei eōs tēs teleutēs ērōdou, ina plērōthē to rēthen upo tou kuriou dia tou prophētou legontos ex aiguptou ekalesa ton uion mou.
mat|2|16|	tote ērōdēs idōn oti enepaichthē upo tōn magōn, ethumōthē lian, kai aposteilas aneile pantas tous paidas tous en bēthleem kai en pasi tois oriois autēs apo dietous kai katōterō, kata ton chronon on ēkribōse para tōn magōn.
mat|2|17|	tote eplērōthē to rēthen upo ieremiou tou prophētou legontos
mat|2|18|	phōnē en rama ēkousthē, thrēnos kai klauthmos kai odurmos polus rachēl klaiousa ta tekna autēs, kai ouk ēthele paraklēthēnai, oti ouk eisin.
mat|2|19|	teleutēsantos de tou ērōdou idou aggelos kuriou kat onar phainetai tō iōsēph en aiguptō
mat|2|20|	legōn egertheis paralabe to paidion kai tēn mētera autou kai poreuou eis gēn israēl tethnēkasi gar oi zētountes tēn psuchēn tou paidiou.
mat|2|21|	o de egertheis parelabe to paidion kai tēn mētera autou kai ēlthen eis gēn israēl.
mat|2|22|	akousas de oti archelaos basileuei epi tēs ioudaias anti ērōdou tou patros autou, ephobēthē ekei apelthein chrēmatistheis de kat onar anechōrēsen eis ta merē tēs galilaias,
mat|2|23|	kai elthōn katōkēsen eis polin legomenēn nazaret, opōs plērōthē to rēthen dia tōn prophētōn oti nazōraios klēthēsetai.
mat|3|1|	en de tais ēmerais ekeinais paraginetai iōannēs o baptistēs kērussōn en tē erēmō tēs ioudaias
mat|3|2|	kai legōn metanoeite ēggike gar ē basileia tōn ouranōn.
mat|3|3|	outos gar estin o rētheis upo ēsaiou tou prophētou legontos phōnē boōntos en tē erēmō, etoimasate tēn odon kuriou, eutheias poieite tas tribous autou.
mat|3|4|	autos de o iōannēs eiche to enduma autou apo trichōn kamēlou kai zōnēn dermatinēn peri tēn osphun autou, ē de trophē autou ēn akrides kai meli agrion.
mat|3|5|	tote exeporeueto pros auton ierosoluma kai pasa ē ioudaia kai pasa ē perichōros tou iordanou,
mat|3|6|	kai ebaptizonto en tō iordanē up autou exomologoumenoi tas amartias autōn.
mat|3|7|	idōn de pollous tōn pharisaiōn kai saddoukaiōn erchomenous epi to baptisma autou eipen autois gennēmata echidnōn, tis upedeixen umin phugein apo tēs mellousēs orgēs?
mat|3|8|	poiēsate oun karpon axion tēs metanoias,
mat|3|9|	kai mē doxēte legein en eautois, patera echomen ton abraam legō gar umin oti dunatai o theos ek tōn lithōn toutōn egeirai tekna tō abraam.
mat|3|10|	ēdē de kai ē axinē pros tēn rizan tōn dendrōn keitai pan oun dendron mē poioun karpon kalon ekkoptetai kai eis pur balletai.
mat|3|11|	egō men baptizō umas en udati eis metanoian o de opisō mou erchomenos ischuroteros mou estin, ou ouk eimi ikanos ta upodēmata bastasai autos umas baptisei en pneumati agiō kai puri.
mat|3|12|	ou to ptuon en tē cheiri autou kai diakathariei tēn alōna autou, kai sunaxei ton siton autou eis tēn apothēkēn, to de achuron katakausei puri asbestō.
mat|3|13|	tote paraginetai o iēsous apo tēs galilaias epi ton iordanēn pros ton iōannēn tou baptisthēnai up autou.
mat|3|14|	o de iōannēs diekōluen auton legōn egō chreian echō upo sou baptisthēnai, kai su erchē pros me?
mat|3|15|	apokritheis de o iēsous eipe pros auton aphes arti outō gar prepon estin ēmin plērōsai pasan dikaiosunēn. tote aphiēsin auton
mat|3|16|	kai baptistheis o iēsous anebē euthus apo tou udatos kai idou aneōchthēsan autō oi ouranoi, kai eide to pneuma tou theou katabainon ōsei peristeran kai erchomenon ep auton
mat|3|17|	kai idou phōnē ek tōn ouranōn legousa outos estin o uios mou o agapētos, en ō eudokēsa.
mat|4|1|	tote o iēsous anēchthē eis tēn erēmon upo tou pneumatos peirasthēnai upo tou diabolou,
mat|4|2|	kai nēsteusas ēmeras tessarakonta kai nuktas tessarakonta usteron epeinase.
mat|4|3|	kai proselthōn autō o peirazōn eipen ei uios ei tou theou, eipe ina oi lithoi outoi artoi genōntai.
mat|4|4|	o de apokritheis eipe gegraptai, ouk ep artō monō zēsetai anthrōpos, all epi panti rēmati ekporeuomenō dia stomatos theou.
mat|4|5|	tote paralambanei auton o diabolos eis tēn agian polin, kai istēsin auton epi to pterugion tou ierou
mat|4|6|	kai legei autō ei uios ei tou theou, bale seauton katō gegraptai gar oti tois aggelois autou enteleitai peri sou, kai epi cheirōn arousi se, mēpote proskopsēs pros lithon ton poda sou.
mat|4|7|	ephē autō o iēsous palin gegraptai, ouk ekpeiraseis kurion ton theon sou.
mat|4|8|	palin paralambanei auton o diabolos eis oros upsēlon lian, kai deiknusin autō pasas tas basileias tou kosmou kai tēn doxan autōn
mat|4|9|	kai legei autō tauta panta soi dōsō, ean pesōn proskunēsēs moi.
mat|4|10|	tote legei autō o iēsous upage opisō mou, satana gegraptai gar, kurion ton theon sou proskunēseis kai autō monō latreuseis.
mat|4|11|	tote aphiēsin auton o diabolos, kai idou aggeloi prosēlthon kai diēkonoun autō.
mat|4|12|	akousas de o iēsous oti iōannēs paredothē, anechōrēsen eis tēn galilaian,
mat|4|13|	kai katalipōn tēn nazaret elthōn katōkēsen eis kapernaoum tēn parathalassian en oriois zaboulōn kai nephthaleim,
mat|4|14|	ina plērōthē to rēthen dia ēsaiou tou prophētou legontos
mat|4|15|	gē zaboulōn kai gē nephthaleim, odon thalassēs, peran tou iordanou, galilaia tōn ethnōn,
mat|4|16|	o laos o kathēmenos en skotei eide phōs mega, kai tois kathēmenois en chōra kai skia thanatou phōs aneteilen autois.
mat|4|17|	apo tote ērxato o iēsous kērussein kai legein metanoeite ēggike gar ē basileia tōn ouranōn.
mat|4|18|	peripatōn de para tēn thalassan tēs galilaias eide duo adelphous, simōna ton legomenon petron kai andrean ton adelphon autou, ballontas amphiblēstron eis tēn thalassan ēsan gar alieis
mat|4|19|	kai legei autois deute opisō mou kai poiēsō umas alieis anthrōpōn.
mat|4|20|	oi de eutheōs aphentes ta diktua ēkolouthēsan autō.
mat|4|21|	kai probas ekeithen eiden allous duo adelphous, iakōbon ton tou zebedaiou kai iōannēn ton adelphon autou, en tō ploiō meta zebedaiou tou patros autōn katartizontas ta diktua autōn, kai ekalesen autous.
mat|4|22|	oi de eutheōs aphentes to ploion kai ton patera autōn ēkolouthēsan autō.
mat|4|23|	kai periēgen olēn tēn galilaian o iēsous didaskōn en tais sunagōgais autōn kai kērussōn to euaggelion tēs basileias kai therapeuōn pasan noson kai pasan malakian en tō laō.
mat|4|24|	kai apēlthen ē akoē autou eis olēn tēn surian, kai prosēnegkan autō pantas tous kakōs echontas poikilais nosois kai basanois sunechomenous, kai daimonizomenous kai selēniazomenous kai paralutikous, kai etherapeusen autous
mat|4|25|	kai ēkolouthēsan autō ochloi polloi apo tēs galilaias kai dekapoleōs kai ierosolumōn kai ioudaias kai peran tou iordanou.
mat|5|1|	idōn de tous ochlous anebē eis to oros, kai kathisantos autou prosēlthon autō oi mathētai autou,
mat|5|2|	kai anoixas to stoma autou edidasken autous legōn
mat|5|3|	makarioi oi ptōchoi tō pneumati, oti autōn estin ē basileia tōn ouranōn.
mat|5|4|	makarioi oi penthountes, oti autoi paraklēthēsontai.
mat|5|5|	makarioi oi praeis, oti autoi klēronomēsousi tēn gēn.
mat|5|6|	makarioi oi peinōntes kai dipsōntes tēn dikaiosunēn, oti autoi chortasthēsontai.
mat|5|7|	makarioi oi eleēmones, oti autoi eleēthēsontai.
mat|5|8|	makarioi oi katharoi tē kardia, oti autoi ton theon opsontai.

mat|5|11|	makarioi este otan oneidisōsin umas kai diōxōsi kai eipōsi pan ponēron rēma kath umōn pseudomenoi eneken emou.
mat|5|12|	chairete kai agalliasthe, oti o misthos umōn polus en tois ouranois outō gar ediōxan tous prophētas tous pro umōn.
mat|5|13|	umeis este to alas tēs gēs ean de to alas mōranthē, en tini alisthēsetai? eis ouden ischuei eti ei mē blēthēnai exō kai katapateisthai upo tōn anthrōpōn.
mat|5|14|	umeis este to phōs tou kosmou. ou dunatai polis krubēnai epanō orous keimenē
mat|5|15|	oude kaiousi luchnon kai titheasi auton upo ton modion, all epi tēn luchnian, kai lampei pasi tois en tē oikia.
mat|5|16|	outō lampsatō to phōs umōn emprosthen tōn anthrōpōn, opōs idōsin umōn ta kala erga kai doxasōsi ton patera umōn ton en tois ouranois.
mat|5|17|	mē nomisēte oti ēlthon katalusai ton nomon ē tous prophētas ouk ēlthon katalusai, alla plērōsai.
mat|5|18|	amēn gar legō umin, eōs an parelthē o ouranos kai ē gē, iōta en ē mia keraia ou mē parelthē apo tou nomou eōs an panta genētai.
mat|5|19|	os ean oun lusē mian tōn entolōn toutōn tōn elachistōn kai didaxē outō tous anthrōpous, elachistos klēthēsetai en tē basileia tōn ouranōn os d an poiēsē kai didaxē, outos megas klēthēsetai en tē basileia tōn ouranōn.
mat|5|20|	legō gar umin oti ean mē perisseusē ē dikaiosunē umōn pleion tōn grammateōn kai pharisaiōn, ou mē eiselthēte eis tēn basileian tōn ouranōn.
mat|5|21|	ēkousate oti errethē tois archaiois, ou phoneuseis os d an phoneusē, enochos estai tē krisei.
mat|5|22|	egō de legō umin oti pas o orgizomenos tō adelphō autou eikē enochos estai tē krisei os d an eipē tō adelphō autou raka, enochos estai tō sunedriō os d an eipē mōre, enochos estai eis tēn geennan tou puros.
mat|5|23|	ean oun prospherēs to dōron sou epi to thusiastērion kakei mnēsthēs oti o adelphos sou echei ti kata sou,
mat|5|24|	aphes ekei to dōron sou emprosthen tou thusiastēriou, kai upage prōton diallagēthi tō adelphō sou, kai tote elthōn prosphere to dōron sou.
mat|5|25|	isthi eunoōn tō antidikō sou tachu eōs otou ei en tē odō met autou, mēpote se paradō o antidikos tō kritē kai o kritēs se paradō tō upēretē, kai eis phulakēn blēthēsē
mat|5|26|	amēn legō soi, ou mē exelthēs ekeithen eōs ou apodōs ton eschaton kodrantēn.
mat|5|27|	ēkousate oti errethē tois archaiois, ou moicheuseis.
mat|5|28|	egō de legō umin oti pas o blepōn gunaika pros to epithumēsai autēn ēdē emoicheusen autēn en tē kardia autou.
mat|5|29|	ei de o ophthalmos sou o dexios skandalizei se, exele auton kai bale apo sou sumpherei gar soi ina apolētai en tōn melōn sou kai mē olon to sōma sou blēthē eis geennan.
mat|5|30|	kai ei ē dexia sou cheir skandalizei se, ekkopson autēn kai bale apo sou sumpherei gar soi ina apolētai en tōn melōn sou kai mē olon to sōma sou blēthē eis geennan.
mat|5|31|	errethē de os an apolusē tēn gunaika autou, dotō autē apostasion.
mat|5|32|	egō de legō umin oti os an apolusē tēn gunaika autou parektos logou porneias, poiei autēn moichasthai, kai os ean apolelumenēn gamēsē, moichatai.
mat|5|33|	palin ēkousate oti errethē tois archaiois, ouk epiorkēseis, apodōseis de tō kuriō tous orkous sou.
mat|5|34|	egō de legō umin mē omosai olōs mēte en tō ouranō, oti thronos esti tou theou
mat|5|35|	mēte en tē gē, oti upopodion esti tōn podōn autou mēte eis ierosoluma, oti polis esti tou megalou basileōs
mat|5|36|	mēte en tē kephalē sou omosēs, oti ou dunasai mian tricha leukēn ē melainan poiēsai.
mat|5|37|	estō de o logos umōn nai nai, ou ou to de perisson toutōn ek tou ponērou estin.
mat|5|38|	ēkousate oti errethē, ophthalmon anti ophthalmou kai odonta anti odontos
mat|5|39|	egō de legō umin mē antistēnai tō ponērō all ostis se rapisei epi tēn dexian siagona, strepson autō kai tēn allēn
mat|5|40|	kai tō thelonti soi krithēnai kai ton chitōna sou labein, aphes autō kai to imation
mat|5|41|	kai ostis se aggareusei milion en, upage met autou duo
mat|5|42|	tō aitounti se didou kai ton thelonta apo sou daneisasthai mē apostraphēs.
mat|5|43|	ēkousate oti errethē, agapēseis ton plēsion sou kai misēseis ton echthron sou.
mat|5|44|	egō de legō umin, agapate tous echthrous umōn, eulogeite tous katarōmenous umas, kalōs poieite tois misousin umas kai proseuchesthe uper tōn epēreazontōn umas kai diōkontōn umas,
mat|5|45|	opōs genēsthe uioi tou patros umōn tou en ouranois, oti ton ēlion autou anatellei epi ponērous kai agathous kai brechei epi dikaious kai adikous.
mat|5|46|	ean gar agapēsēte tous agapōntas umas, tina misthon echete? ouchi kai oi telōnai to auto poiousi?
mat|5|47|	kai ean aspasēsthe tous philous umōn monon, ti perisson poieite? ouchi kai oi telōnai outō poiousin?
mat|5|48|	esesthe oun umeis teleioi, ōsper o patēr umōn o en tois ouranois teleios estin.
mat|6|1|	prosechete tēn eleēmosunēn umōn mē poiein emprosthen tōn anthrōpōn pros to theathēnai autois ei de mēge, misthon ouk echete para tō patri umōn tō en tois ouranois.
mat|6|2|	otan oun poiēs eleēmosunēn, mē salpisēs emprosthen sou, ōsper oi upokritai poiousin en tais sunagōgais kai en tais rumais, opōs doxasthōsin upo tōn anthrōpōn amēn legō umin, apechousi ton misthon autōn.
mat|6|3|	sou de poiountos eleēmosunēn mē gnōtō ē aristera sou ti poiei ē dexia sou,
mat|6|4|	opōs ē sou ē eleēmosunē en tō kruptō, kai o patēr sou o blepōn en tō kruptō apodōsei soi en tō phanerō.
mat|6|5|	kai otan proseuchē, ouk esē ōsper oi upokritai, oti philousin en tais sunagōgais kai en tais gōniais tōn plateiōn estōtes proseuchesthai, opōs an phanōsi tois anthrōpois amēn legō umin oti apechousi ton misthon autōn.
mat|6|6|	su de otan proseuchē, eiselthe eis to tamieion sou, kai kleisas tēn thuran sou proseuxai tō patri sou tō en tō kruptō, kai o patēr sou o blepōn en tō kruptō apodōsei soi en tō phanerō.
mat|6|7|	proseuchomenoi de mē battologēsēte ōsper oi ethnikoi dokousi gar oti en tē polulogia autōn eisakousthēsontai.
mat|6|8|	mē oun omoiōthēte autois oide gar o patēr umōn ōn chreian echete pro tou umas aitēsai auton.
mat|6|9|	outōs oun proseuchesthe umeis pater ēmōn o en tois ouranois agiasthētō to onoma sou
mat|6|10|	elthetō ē basileia sou genēthētō to thelēma sou, ōs en ouranō, kai epi tēs gēs
mat|6|11|	ton arton ēmōn ton epiousion dos ēmin sēmeron
mat|6|12|	kai aphes ēmin ta opheilēmata ēmōn, ōs kai ēmeis aphiemen tois opheiletais ēmōn
mat|6|13|	kai mē eisenegkēs ēmas eis peirasmon, alla rusai ēmas apo tou ponērou. oti sou estin ē basileia kai ē dunamis kai ē doxa eis tous aiōnas amēn.
mat|6|14|	ean gar aphēte tois anthrōpois ta paraptōmata autōn, aphēsei kai umin o patēr umōn o ouranios
mat|6|15|	ean de mē aphēte tois anthrōpois ta paraptōmata autōn, oude o patēr umōn aphēsei ta paraptōmata umōn.
mat|6|16|	otan de nēsteuēte, mē ginesthe ōsper oi upokritai skuthrōpoi aphanizousi gar ta prosōpa autōn opōs phanōsi tois anthrōpois nēsteuontes amēn legō umin oti apechousi ton misthon autōn.
mat|6|17|	su de nēsteuōn aleipsai sou tēn kephalēn kai to prosōpon sou nipsai,
mat|6|18|	opōs mē phanēs tois anthrōpois nēsteuōn, alla tō patri sou tō en tō kruptō, kai o patēr sou o blepōn en tō kruptō apodōsei soi en tō phanerō.
mat|6|19|	mē thēsaurizete umin thēsaurous epi tēs gēs, opou sēs kai brōsis aphanizei, kai opou kleptai diorussousi kai kleptousi
mat|6|20|	thēsaurizete de umin thēsaurous en ouranō, opou oute sēs oute brōsis aphanizei, kai opou kleptai ou diorussousin oude kleptousin
mat|6|21|	opou gar estin o thēsauros umōn, ekei estai kai ē kardia umōn.
mat|6|22|	o luchnos tou sōmatos estin o ophthalmos ean oun o ophthalmos sou aplous ē, olon to sōma sou phōteinon estai
mat|6|23|	ean de o ophthalmos sou ponēros ē, olon to sōma sou skoteinon estai. ei oun to phōs to en soi skotos esti, to skotos poson?
mat|6|24|	oudeis dunatai dusi kuriois douleuein ē gar ton ena misēsei kai ton eteron agapēsei, ē enos anthexetai kai tou eterou kataphronēsei. ou dunasthe theō douleuein kai mamōna.
mat|6|25|	dia touto legō umin, mē merimnate tē psuchē umōn ti phagēte kai ti piēte, mēde tō sōmati umōn ti endusēsthe ouchi ē psuchē pleion esti tēs trophēs kai to sōma tou endumatos?
mat|6|26|	emblepsate eis ta peteina tou ouranou, oti ou speirousin oude therizousin oude sunagousin eis apothēkas, kai o patēr umōn o ouranios trephei auta ouch umeis mallon diapherete autōn?
mat|6|27|	tis de ex umōn merimnōn dunatai prostheinai epi tēn ēlikian autou pēchun ena?
mat|6|28|	kai peri endumatos ti merimnate? katamathete ta krina tou agrou pōs auxanei ou kopia oude nēthei
mat|6|29|	legō de umin oti oude solomōn en pasē tē doxē autou periebaleto ōs en toutōn.
mat|6|30|	ei de ton chorton tou agrou, sēmeron onta kai aurion eis klibanon ballomenon, o theos outōs amphiennusin, ou pollō mallon umas, oligopistoi?
mat|6|31|	mē oun merimnēsēte legontes, ti phagōmen ē ti piōmen ē ti peribalōmetha?
mat|6|32|	panta gar tauta ta ethnē epizētei oide gar o patēr umōn o ouranios oti chrēzete toutōn apantōn.
mat|6|33|	zēteite de prōton tēn basileian tou theou kai tēn dikaiosunēn autou, kai tauta panta prostethēsetai umin.
mat|6|34|	mē oun merimnēsēte eis tēn aurion ē gar aurion merimnēsei ta eautēs arketon tē ēmera ē kakia autēs.
mat|7|1|	mē krinete, ina mē krithēte
mat|7|2|	en ō gar krimati krinete krithēsesthe, kai en ō metrō metreite metrēthēsetai umin.
mat|7|3|	ti de blepeis to karphos to en tō ophthalmō tou adelphou sou, tēn de en tō sō ophthalmō dokon ou katanoeis?
mat|7|4|	ē pōs ereis tō adelphō sou, aphes ekbalō to karphos apo tou ophthalmou sou, kai idou ē dokos en tō ophthalmō sou?
mat|7|5|	upokrita, ekbale prōton tēn dokon ek tou ophthalmou sou, kai tote diablepseis ekbalein to karphos ek tou ophthalmou tou adelphou sou.
mat|7|6|	mē dōte to agion tois kusi mēde balēte tous margaritas umōn emprosthen tōn choirōn, mēpote katapatēsōsin autous en tois posin autōn kai straphentes rēxōsin umas.
mat|7|7|	aiteite, kai dothēsetai umin, zēteite, kai eurēsete, krouete, kai anoigēsetai umin
mat|7|8|	pas gar o aitōn lambanei kai o zētōn euriskei kai tō krouonti anoigēsetai.
mat|7|9|	ē tis estin ex umōn anthrōpos, on ean aitēsē o uios autou arton, mē lithon epidōsei autō?
mat|7|10|	kai ean ichthun aitēsē, mē ophin epidōsei autō?
mat|7|11|	ei oun umeis, ponēroi ontes, oidate domata agatha didonai tois teknois umōn, posō mallon o patēr umōn o en tois ouranois dōsei agatha tois aitousin auton?
mat|7|12|	panta oun osa an thelēte ina poiōsin umin oi anthrōpoi, outō kai umeis poieite autois outos gar estin o nomos kai oi prophētai.
mat|7|13|	eiselthete dia tēs stenēs pulēs oti plateia ē pulē kai euruchōros ē odos ē apagousa eis tēn apōleian, kai polloi eisin oi eiserchomenoi di autēs.
mat|7|14|	ti stenē ē pulē kai tethlimmenē ē odos ē apagousa eis tēn zōēn, kai oligoi eisin oi euriskontes autēn!
mat|7|15|	prosechete de apo tōn pseudoprophētōn, oitines erchontai pros umas en endumasi probatōn, esōthen de eisi lukoi arpages.
mat|7|16|	apo tōn karpōn autōn epignōsesthe autous. mēti sullegousin apo akanthōn staphulēn ē apo tribolōn suka?
mat|7|17|	outō pan dendron agathon karpous kalous poiei, to de sapron dendron karpous ponērous poiei.
mat|7|18|	ou dunatai dendron agathon karpous ponērous poiein, oude dendron sapron karpous kalous poiein.
mat|7|19|	pan dendron mē poioun karpon kalon ekkoptetai kai eis pur balletai.
mat|7|20|	arage apo tōn karpōn autōn epignōsesthe autous.
mat|7|21|	ou pas o legōn moi kurie kurie, eiseleusetai eis tēn basileian tōn ouranōn, all o poiōn to thelēma tou patros mou tou en ouranois.
mat|7|22|	polloi erousi moi en ekeinē tē ēmera kurie kurie, ou tō sō onomati proephēteusamen, kai tō sō onomati daimonia exebalomen, kai tō sō onomati dunameis pollas epoiēsamen?
mat|7|23|	kai tote omologēsō autois oti oudepote egnōn umas apochōreite ap emou oi ergazomenoi tēn anomian.

mat|8|1|	katabanti de autō apo tou orous ēkolouthēsan autō ochloi polloi.

mat|8|3|	kai ekteinas tēn cheira ēpsato autou o iēsous legōn thelō, katharisthēti. kai eutheōs ekatharisthē autou ē lepra.
mat|8|4|	kai legei autō o iēsous ora mēdeni eipēs, alla upage seauton deixon tō ierei kai prosenegke to dōron o prosetaxe mōsēs eis marturion autois.

mat|8|11|	legō de umin oti polloi apo anatolōn kai dusmōn ēxousi kai anaklithēsontai meta abraam kai isaak kai iakōb en tē basileia tōn ouranōn,

mat|10|1|	kai proskalesamenos tous dōdeka mathētas autou edōken autois exousian pneumatōn akathartōn ōste ekballein auta kai therapeuein pasan noson kai pasan malakian.
mat|10|2|	tōn de dōdeka apostolōn ta onomata eisi tauta prōtos simōn o legomenos petros kai andreas o adelphos autou, iakōbos o tou zebedaiou kai iōannēs o adelphos autou,

mat|10|13|	kai ean men ē ē oikia axia, elthetō ē eirēnē umōn ep autēn ean de mē ē axia, ē eirēnē umōn pros umas epistraphētō.
mat|10|14|	kai os ean mē dexētai umas mēde akousē tous logous umōn, exerchomenoi exō tēs oikias ē tēs poleōs ekeinēs ektinaxate ton koniorton tōn podōn umōn.
mat|10|15|	amēn legō umin, anektoteron estai gē sodomōn kai gomorras en ēmera kriseōs ē tē polei ekeinē.

mat|10|19|	otan de paradōsousin umas, mē merimnēsēte pōs ē ti lalēsete dothēsetai gar umin en ekeinē tē ōra ti lalēsete.
mat|10|20|	ou gar umeis este oi lalountes, alla to pneuma tou patros umōn to laloun en umin.

mat|10|23|	otan de diōkōsin umas en tē polei tautē, pheugete eis tēn allēn amēn gar legō umin, ou mē telesēte tas poleis tou israēl eōs an elthē o uios tou anthrōpou.
mat|10|24|	ouk esti mathētēs uper ton didaskalon oude doulos uper ton kurion autou.
mat|10|25|	arketon tō mathētē ina genētai ōs o didaskalos autou, kai tō doulō ōs o kurios autou. ei ton oikodespotēn beelzeboul ekalesan, posō mallon tous oikiakous autou?
mat|10|26|	mē oun phobēthēte autous ouden gar esti kekalummenon o ouk apokaluphthēsetai, kai krupton o ou gnōsthēsetai.
mat|10|27|	o legō umin en tē skotia, eipate en tō phōti, kai o eis to ous akouete, kēruxate epi tōn dōmatōn.
mat|10|28|	kai mē phobēthēte apo tōn apoktennontōn to sōma, tēn de psuchēn mē dunamenōn apokteinai phobēthēte de mallon ton dunamenon kai psuchēn kai sōma apolesai en geennē.
mat|10|29|	ouchi duo strouthia assariou pōleitai? kai en ex autōn ou peseitai epi tēn gēn aneu tou patros umōn.

mat|10|41|	o dechomenos prophētēn eis onoma prophētou misthon prophētou lēpsetai, kai o dechomenos dikaion eis onoma dikaiou misthon dikaiou lēpsetai.
mat|10|42|	kai os ean potisē ena tōn mikrōn toutōn potērion psuchrou monon eis onoma mathētou, amēn legō umin, ou mē apolesē ton misthon autou.
mat|11|1|	kai egeneto ote etelesen o iēsous diatassōn tois dōdeka mathētais autou metebē ekeithen tou didaskein kai kērussein en tais polesin autōn.
mat|11|2|	o de iōannēs akousas en tō desmōtēriō ta erga tou christou, pempsas duo tōn mathētōn autou
mat|11|3|	eipen autō su ei o erchomenos ē eteron prosdokōmen?

mat|11|5|	tuphloi anablepousi kai chōloi peripatousi, leproi katharizontai kai kōphoi akouousi, nekroi egeirontai kai ptōchoi euaggelizontai
mat|11|6|	kai makarios estin os ean mē skandalisthē en emoi.
mat|11|7|	toutōn de poreuomenōn ērxato o iēsous legein tois ochlois peri iōannou ti exēlthete eis tēn erēmon theasasthai? kalamon upo anemou saleuomenon?
mat|11|8|	alla ti exēlthete idein? anthrōpon en malakois imatiois ēmphiesmenon? idou oi ta malaka phorountes en tois oikois tōn basileōn eisin.

mat|11|11|	amēn legō umin, ouk egēgertai en gennētois gunaikōn meizōn iōannou tou baptistou o de mikroteros en tē basileia tōn ouranōn meizōn autou estin.
mat|11|12|	apo de tōn ēmerōn iōannou tou baptistou eōs arti ē basileia tōn ouranōn biazetai, kai biastai arpazousin autēn.

mat|11|21|	ouai soi, chorazin, ouai soi, bēthsaida oti ei en turō kai sidōni egenēthēsan ai dunameis ai genomenai en umin, palai an en sakkō kai spodō kathēmenai metenoēsan.
mat|11|22|	plēn legō umin, turō kai sidōni anektoteron estai en ēmera kriseōs ē umin.

mat|11|24|	plēn legō umin oti gē sodomōn anektoteron estai en ēmera kriseōs ē soi.

mat|12|1|	en ekeinō tō kairō eporeuthē o iēsous tois sabbasi dia tōn sporimōn oi de mathētai autou epeinasan, kai ērxanto tillein stachuas kai esthiein.
mat|12|2|	oi de pharisaioi idontes eipon autō idou oi mathētai sou poiousin o ouk exesti poiein en sabbatō.

mat|12|33|	ē poiēsate to dendron kalon, kai ton karpon autou kalon, ē poiēsate to dendron sapron, kai ton karpon autou sapron ek gar tou karpou to dendron ginōsketai.

mat|12|41|	andres nineuitai anastēsontai en tē krisei meta tēs geneas tautēs kai katakrinousin autēn, oti metenoēsan eis to kērugma iōna, kai idou pleion iōna ōde.

mat|12|46|	eti de autou lalountos tois ochlois idou ē mētēr kai oi adelphoi autou eistēkeisan exō, zētountes lalēsai autō.

mat|13|1|	en de tē ēmera ekeinē exelthōn o iēsous tēs oikias ekathēto para tēn thalassan
mat|13|2|	kai sunēchthēsan pros auton ochloi polloi, ōste auton eis ploion embanta kathēsthai, kai pas o ochlos epi ton aigialon eistēkei.
mat|13|3|	kai elalēsen autois polla en parabolais legōn idou exēlthen o speirōn tou speirai.
mat|13|4|	kai en tō speirein auton a men epese para tēn odon, kai elthonta ta peteina katephagen auta
mat|13|5|	alla de epesen epi ta petrōdē, opou ouk eiche gēn pollēn, kai eutheōs exaneteile dia to mē echein bathos gēs,
mat|13|6|	ēliou de anateilantos ekaumatisthē, kai dia to mē echein rizan exēranthē
mat|13|7|	alla de epesen epi tas akanthas, kai anebēsan ai akanthai kai apepnixan auta
mat|13|8|	alla de epesen epi tēn gēn tēn kalēn kai edidou karpon o men ekaton, o de exēkonta, o de triakonta.
mat|13|9|	o echōn ōta akouein akouetō.

mat|13|11|	o de apokritheis eipen autois oti umin dedotai gnōnai ta mustēria tēs basileias tōn ouranōn, ekeinois de ou dedotai.
mat|13|12|	ostis gar echei, dothēsetai autō kai perisseuthēsetai ostis de ouk echei, kai o echei arthēsetai ap autou.
mat|13|13|	dia touto en parabolais autois lalō, ina blepontes mē blepōsi kai akouontes mē akouōsi mēde sunōsi,
mat|13|14|	mēpote epistrepsōsi kai tote plērōthēsetai autois ē prophēteia ēsaiou ē legousa akoē akousete kai ou mē sunēte, kai blepontes blepsete kai ou mē idēte
mat|13|15|	epachunthē gar ē kardia tou laou toutou, kai tois ōsi bareōs ēkousan, kai tous ophthalmous autōn ekammusan, mēpote idōsi tois ophthalmois kai tois ōsin akousōsi kai tē kardia sunōsi kai epistrepsōsi, kai iasomai autous.
mat|13|16|	umōn de makarioi oi ophthalmoi, oti blepousi, kai ta ōta umōn, oti akouousin.
mat|13|17|	amēn gar legō umin oti polloi prophētai kai dikaioi epethumēsan idein a blepete, kai ouk eidon, kai akousai a akouete, kai ouk ēkousan.
mat|13|18|	umeis oun akousate tēn parabolēn tou speirantos.
mat|13|19|	pantos akouontos ton logon tēs basileias kai mē sunientos, erchetai o ponēros kai airei to esparmenon en tē kardia autou outos estin o para tēn odon spareis.
mat|13|20|	o de epi ta petrōdē spareis, outos estin o ton logon akouōn kai eutheōs meta charas dechomenos kai lambanōn auton
mat|13|21|	ouk echei de rizan en eautō, alla proskairos esti, genomenēs de thlipseōs ē diōgmou dia ton logon euthus skandalizetai.
mat|13|22|	o de eis tas akanthas spareis, outos estin o ton logon akouōn, kai ē merimna tou aiōnos toutou kai ē apatē tou ploutou sumpnigei ton logon, kai akarpos ginetai.
mat|13|23|	o de epi tēn gēn tēn kalēn spareis, outos estin o ton logon akouōn kai suniōn os dē karpophorei kai poiei o men ekaton, o de exēkonta, o de triakonta.
mat|13|24|	allēn parabolēn parethēken autois legōn ōmoiōthē ē basileia tōn ouranōn anthrōpō speiranti kalon sperma en tō agrō autou

mat|13|26|	ote de eblastēsen o chortos kai karpon epoiēse, tote ephanē kai ta zizania.
mat|13|27|	proselthontes de oi douloi tou oikodespotou eipon autō kurie, ouchi kalon sperma espeiras en tō sō agrō? pothen oun echei zizania?

mat|13|30|	aphete sunauxanesthai amphotera mechri tou therismou, kai en kairō tou therismou erō tois theristais sullexate prōton ta zizania kai dēsate auta eis desmas pros to katakausai auta, ton de siton sunagagete eis tēn apothēkēn mou.
mat|13|31|	allēn parabolēn parethēken autois legōn omoia estin ē basileia tōn ouranōn kokkō sinapeōs, on labōn anthrōpos espeiren en tō agrō autou
mat|13|32|	o mikroteron men esti pantōn tōn spermatōn, otan de auxēthē, meizon pantōn tōn lachanōn esti kai ginetai dendron, ōste elthein ta peteina tou ouranou kai kataskēnoun en tois kladois autou.
mat|13|33|	allēn parabolēn elalēsen autois omoia estin ē basileia tōn ouranōn zumē, ēn labousa gunē enekrupsen eis aleurou sata tria, eōs ou ezumōthē olon.
mat|13|34|	tauta panta elalēsen o iēsous en parabolais tois ochlois, kai chōris parabolēs ouden elalei autois,
mat|13|35|	opōs plērōthē to rēthen dia tou prophētou legontos anoixō en parabolais to stoma mou, ereuxomai kekrummena apo katabolēs kosmou.
mat|13|36|	tote apheis tous ochlous ēlthen eis tēn oikian autou. kai prosēlthon autō oi mathētai autou legontes phrason ēmin tēn parabolēn tōn zizaniōn tou agrou.
mat|13|37|	o de apokritheis eipen autois o speirōn to kalon sperma estin o uios tou anthrōpou
mat|13|38|	o de agros estin o kosmos to de kalon sperma, outoi eisin oi uioi tēs basileias ta de zizania eisin oi uioi tou ponērou
mat|13|39|	o de echthros o speiras auta estin o diabolos o de therismos sunteleia tou aiōnos estin oi de theristai aggeloi eisin.
mat|13|40|	ōsper oun sullegetai ta zizania kai puri kaietai, outōs estai en tē sunteleia tou aiōnos toutou.
mat|13|41|	apostelei o uios tou anthrōpou tous aggelous autou, kai sullexousin ek tēs basileias autou panta ta skandala kai tous poiountas tēn anomian,
mat|13|42|	kai balousin autous eis tēn kaminon tou puros ekei estai o klauthmos kai o brugmos tōn odontōn.
mat|13|43|	tote oi dikaioi eklampsousin ōs o ēlios en tē basileia tou patros autōn. o echōn ōta akouein akouetō.
mat|13|44|	palin omoia estin ē basileia tōn ouranōn thēsaurō kekrummenō en tō agrō, on eurōn anthrōpos ekrupse, kai apo tēs charas autou upagei kai panta osa echei pōlei kai agorazei ton agron ekeinon.
mat|13|45|	palin omoia estin ē basileia tōn ouranōn anthrōpō emporō zētounti kalous margaritas
mat|13|46|	os eurōn ena polutimon margaritēn apelthōn peprake panta osa eiche kai ēgorasen auton.

mat|13|48|	ēn, ote eplērōthē, anabibasantes autēn epi ton aigialon kai kathisantes sunelexan ta kala eis aggeia, ta de sapra exō ebalon.

mat|13|50|	kai balousin autous eis tēn kaminon tou puros ekei estai o klauthmos kai o brugmos tōn odontōn.

mat|13|55|	ouch outos estin o tou tektonos uios? ouchi ē mētēr autou legetai mariam kai oi adelphoi autou iakōbos kai iōsēs kai simōn kai ioudas?

mat|14|2|	kai eipe tois paisin autou outos estin iōannēs o baptistēs autos ēgerthē apo tōn nekrōn, kai dia touto ai dunameis energousin en autō.
mat|14|3|	o gar ērōdēs kratēsas ton iōannēn edēsen auton kai etheto en phulakē dia ērōdiada tēn gunaika philippou tou adelphou autou.

mat|17|1|	kai meth ēmeras ex paralambanei o iēsous ton petron kai iakōbon kai iōannēn ton adelphon autou kai anapherei autous eis oros upsēlon kat idian

mat|17|3|	kai idou ōphthēsan autois mōsēs kai ēlias met autou sullalountes.
mat|17|4|	apokritheis de o petros eipe tō iēsou kurie, kalon estin ēmas ōde einai ei theleis, poiēsōmen ōde treis skēnas, soi mian kai mōsei mian kai mian ēlia.
mat|17|5|	eti autou lalountos idou nephelē phōteinē epeskiasen autous, kai idou phōnē ek tēs nephelēs legousa outos estin o uios mou o agapētos, en ō eudokēsa autou akouete
mat|17|6|	kai akousantes oi mathētai epeson epi prosōpon autōn kai ephobēthēsan sphodra.
mat|17|7|	kai proselthōn o iēsous ēpsato autōn kai eipen egerthēte kai mē phobeisthe.
mat|17|8|	eparantes de tous ophthalmous autōn oudena eidon ei mē ton iēsoun monon.
mat|17|9|	kai katabainontōn autōn apo tou orous eneteilato autois o iēsous legōn mēdeni eipēte to orama eōs ou o uios tou anthrōpou ek nekrōn anastē.
mat|17|10|	kai epērōtēsan auton oi mathētai autou legontes ti oun oi grammateis legousin oti ēlian dei elthein prōton?
mat|17|11|	o de iēsous apokritheis eipen autois ēlias men erchetai prōton kai apokatastēsei panta
mat|17|12|	legō de umin oti ēlias ēdē ēlthe, kai ouk epegnōsan auton, all epoiēsan en autō osa ēthelēsan outō kai o uios tou anthrōpou mellei paschein up autōn.
mat|17|13|	tote sunēkan oi mathētai oti peri iōannou tou baptistou eipen autois.
mat|17|14|	kai elthontōn autōn pros ton ochlon prosēlthen autō anthrōpos gonupetōn auton kai legōn
mat|17|15|	kurie, eleēson mou ton uion, oti selēniazetai kai kakōs paschei pollakis gar piptei eis to pur kai pollakis eis to udōr.
mat|17|16|	kai prosēnegka auton tois mathētais sou, kai ouk ēdunēthēsan auton therapeusai.
mat|17|17|	apokritheis de o iēsous eipen ō genea apistos kai diestrammenē! eōs pote esomai meth umōn? eōs pote anexomai umōn? pherete moi auton ōde.
mat|17|18|	kai epetimēsen autō o iēsous, kai exēlthen ap autou to daimonion kai etherapeuthē o pais apo tēs ōras ekeinēs.
mat|17|19|	tote proselthontes oi mathētai tō iēsou kat idian eipon diati ēmeis ouk ēdunēthēmen ekbalein auto?
mat|17|20|	o de iēsous eipen autois dia tēn apistian umōn. amēn gar legō umin, ean echēte pistin ōs kokkon sinapeōs, ereite tō orei toutō, metabēthi enteuthen ekei, kai metabēsetai, kai ouden adunatēsei umin.
mat|17|21|	touto de to genos ouk ekporeuetai ei mē en proseuchē kai nēsteia.
mat|17|22|	anastrephomenōn de autōn eis tēn galilaian eipen autois o iēsous mellei o uios tou anthrōpou paradidosthai eis cheiras anthrōpōn
mat|17|23|	kai apoktenousin auton, kai tē tritē ēmera egerthēsetai. kai elupēthēsan sphodra.
mat|17|24|	elthontōn de autōn eis kapernaoum prosēlthon oi ta didrachma lambanontes tō petrō kai eipon o didaskalos umōn ou telei ta didrachma?
mat|17|25|	legei, nai. kai ote eisēlthen eis tēn oikian, proephthasen auton o iēsous legōn ti soi dokei, simōn? oi basileis tēs gēs apo tinōn lambanousi telē ē kēnson? apo tōn uiōn autōn ē apo tōn allotriōn?
mat|17|26|	legei autō o petros apo tōn allotriōn. ephē autō o iēsous arage eleutheroi eisin oi uioi.
mat|17|27|	ina de mē skandalisōmen autous, poreutheis eis tēn thalassan bale agkistron kai ton anabanta prōton ichthun aron, kai anoixas to stoma autou eurēseis statēra ekeinon labōn dos autois anti emou kai sou.
mat|18|1|	en ekeinē tē ōra prosēlthon oi mathētai tō iēsou legontes tis ara meizōn estin en tē basileia tōn ouranōn?
mat|18|2|	kai proskalesamenos o iēsous paidion estēsen auto en mesō autōn kai eipen
mat|18|3|	amēn legō umin, ean mē straphēte kai genēsthe ōs ta paidia, ou mē eiselthēte eis tēn basileian tōn ouranōn.
mat|18|4|	ostis oun tapeinōsei eauton ōs to paidion touto, outos estin o meizōn en tē basileia tōn ouranōn.
mat|18|5|	kai os ean dexētai paidion toiouton en epi tō onomati mou, eme dechetai
mat|18|6|	os d an skandalisē ena tōn mikrōn toutōn tōn pisteuontōn eis eme, sumpherei autō ina kremasthē mulos onikos eis ton trachēlon autou kai katapontisthē en tō pelagei tēs thalassēs.
mat|18|7|	ouai tō kosmō apo tōn skandalōn anagkē gar estin elthein ta skandala plēn ouai tō anthrōpō ekeinō di ou to skandalon erchetai.
mat|18|8|	ei de ē cheir sou ē o pous sou skandalizei se, ekkopson auta kai bale apo sou kalon soi estin eiselthein eis tēn zōēn chōlon ē kullon, ē duo cheiras ē duo podas echonta blēthēnai eis to pur to aiōnion.
mat|18|9|	kai ei o ophthalmos sou skandalizei se, exele auton kai bale apo sou kalon soi esti monophthalmon eis tēn zōēn eiselthein, ē duo ophthalmous echonta blēthēnai eis tēn geennan tou puros.
mat|18|10|	orate mē kataphronēsēte enos tōn mikrōn toutōn legō gar umin oti oi aggeloi autōn en ouranois dia pantos blepousi to prosōpon tou patros mou tou en ouranois.
mat|18|11|	ēlthe gar o uios tou anthrōpou sōsai to apolōlos.
mat|18|12|	ti umin dokei? ean genētai tini anthrōpō ekaton probata kai planēthē en ex autōn, ouchi apheis ta enenēkonta ennea epi ta orē, poreutheis zētei to planōmenon?
mat|18|13|	kai ean genētai eurein auto, amēn legō umin oti chairei ep autō mallon ē epi tois enenēkonta ennea tois mē peplanēmenois.
mat|18|14|	outōs ouk esti thelēma emprosthen tou patros umōn tou en ouranois ina apolētai eis tōn mikrōn toutōn.
mat|18|15|	ean de amartēsē eis se o adelphos sou, upage kai elegxon auton metaxu sou kai autou monou ean sou akousē, ekerdēsas ton adelphon sou
mat|18|16|	ean de mē akousē, paralabe meta sou eti ena ē duo, ina epi stomatos duo marturōn ē triōn stathē pan rēma.
mat|18|17|	ean de parakousē autōn, eipe tē ekklēsia ean de kai tēs ekklēsias parakousē, estō soi ōsper o ethnikos kai o telōnēs.
mat|18|18|	amēn legō umin, osa ean dēsēte epi tēs gēs, estai dedemena en tō ouranō, kai osa ean lusēte epi tēs gēs, estai lelumena en tō ouranō.
mat|18|19|	palin amēn legō umin oti ean duo umōn sumphōnēsōsin epi tēs gēs peri pantos pragmatos ou ean aitēsōntai, genēsetai autois para tou patros mou tou en ouranois.
mat|18|20|	ou gar eisi duo ē treis sunēgmenoi eis to emon onoma, ekei eimi en mesō autōn.
mat|18|21|	tote proselthōn autō o petros eipe kurie, posakis amartēsei eis eme o adelphos mou kai aphēsō autō? eōs eptakis?
mat|18|22|	legei autō o iēsous ou legō soi eōs eptakis, all eōs ebdomēkontakis epta.
mat|18|23|	dia touto ōmoiōthē ē basileia tōn ouranōn anthrōpō basilei, os ēthelēse sunarai logon meta tōn doulōn autou.
mat|18|24|	arxamenou de autou sunairein prosēnechthē autō eis opheiletēs muriōn talantōn.
mat|18|25|	mē echontos de autou apodounai ekeleusen auton o kurios autou prathēnai kai tēn gunaika autou kai ta tekna kai panta osa eiche, kai apodothēnai.
mat|18|26|	pesōn oun o doulos prosekunei autō legōn kurie, makrothumēson ep emoi kai panta soi apodōsō.
mat|18|27|	splagchnistheis de o kurios tou doulou ekeinou apelusen auton kai to daneion aphēken autō.
mat|18|28|	exelthōn de o doulos ekeinos euren ena tōn sundoulōn autou, os ōpheilen autō ekaton dēnaria, kai kratēsas auton epnige legōn apodos moi ei ti opheileis.
mat|18|29|	pesōn oun o sundoulos autou eis tous podas autou parekalei auton legōn makrothumēson ep emoi kai apodōsō soi.
mat|18|30|	o de ouk ēthelen, alla apelthōn ebalen auton eis phulakēn eōs ou apodō to opheilomenon.
mat|18|31|	idontes de oi sundouloi autou ta genomena elupēthēsan sphodra, kai elthontes diesaphēsan tō kuriō eautōn panta ta genomena.
mat|18|32|	tote proskalesamenos auton o kurios autou legei autō doule ponēre, pasan tēn opheilēn ekeinēn aphēka soi, epei parekalesas me.
mat|18|33|	ouk edei kai se eleēsai ton sundoulon sou, ōs kai egō se ēleēsa?
mat|18|34|	kai orgistheis o kurios autou paredōken auton tois basanistais eōs ou apodō pan to opheilomenon autō.
mat|18|35|	outō kai o patēr mou o epouranios poiēsei umin, ean mē aphēte ekastos tō adelphō autou apo tōn kardiōn umōn ta paraptōmata autōn.
mat|19|1|	kai egeneto ote etelesen o iēsous tous logous toutous metēren apo tēs galilaias kai ēlthen eis ta oria tēs ioudaias peran tou iordanou.
mat|19|2|	kai ēkolouthēsan autō ochloi polloi, kai etherapeusen autous ekei.
mat|19|3|	kai prosēlthon autō oi pharisaioi peirazontes auton kai legontes autō ei exestin anthrōpō apolusai tēn gunaika autou kata pasan aitian?
mat|19|4|	o de apokritheis eipen autois ouk anegnōte oti o poiēsas ap archēs arsen kai thēlu epoiēsen autous kai eipen,
mat|19|5|	eneken toutou kataleipsei anthrōpos ton patera autou kai tēn mētera kai kollēthēsetai tē gunaiki autou, kai esontai oi duo eis sarka mian?
mat|19|6|	ōste ouketi eisi duo, alla sarx mia. o oun o theos sunezeuxen, anthrōpos mē chōrizetō.
mat|19|7|	legousin autō ti oun mōsēs eneteilato dounai biblion apostasiou kai apolusai autēn?

mat|19|9|	legō de umin oti os an apolusē tēn gunaika autou mē epi porneia kai gamēsē allēn, moichatai kai o apolelumenēn gamēsas moichatai.

mat|19|18|	legei autō poias? o de iēsous eipe to ou phoneuseis, ou moicheuseis, ou klepseis, ou pseudomarturēseis,

mat|19|21|	ephē autō o iēsous ei theleis teleios einai, upage pōlēson sou ta uparchonta kai dos ptōchois, kai exeis thēsauron en ouranō, kai deuro akolouthei moi.
mat|19|22|	akousas de o neaniskos ton logon apēlthe lupoumenos ēn gar echōn ktēmata polla.
mat|19|23|	o de iēsous eipe tois mathētais autou amēn legō umin oti duskolōs plousios eiseleusetai eis tēn basileian tōn ouranōn.

mat|20|1|	omoia gar estin ē basileia tōn ouranōn anthrōpō oikodespotē, ostis exēlthen ama prōi misthōsasthai ergatas eis ton ampelōna autou.

mat|20|3|	kai exelthōn peri tritēn ōran eiden allous estōtas en tē agora argous,
mat|20|4|	kai ekeinois eipen upagete kai umeis eis ton ampelōna, kai o ean ē dikaion dōsō umin.

mat|20|7|	legousin autō oti oudeis ēmas emisthōsato. legei autois upagete kai umeis eis ton ampelōna, kai o ean ē dikaion lēpsesthe.

mat|20|22|	apokritheis de o iēsous eipen ouk oidate ti aiteisthe. dunasthe piein to potērion o egō mellō pinein, ē to baptisma o egō baptizomai baptisthēnai? legousin autō dunametha.

mat|21|1|	kai ote ēggisan eis ierosoluma kai ēlthon eis bēthsphagē pros to oros tōn elaiōn, tote o iēsous apesteile duo mathētas
mat|21|2|	legōn autois poreuthēte eis tēn kōmēn tēn apenanti umōn, kai eutheōs eurēsete onon dedemenēn kai pōlon met autēs lusantes agagete moi.
mat|21|3|	kai ean tis umin eipē ti, ereite oti o kurios autōn chreian echei eutheōs de apostellei autous.
mat|21|4|	touto de olon gegonen ina plērōthē to rēthen dia tou prophētou legontos
mat|21|5|	eipate tē thugatri siōn, idou o basileus sou erchetai soi praus kai epibebēkōs epi onon kai pōlon uion upozugiou.
mat|21|6|	poreuthentes de oi mathētai kai poiēsantes kathōs prosetaxen autois o iēsous,
mat|21|7|	ēgagon tēn onon kai ton pōlon, kai epethēkan epanō autōn ta imatia autōn, kai epekathisen epanō autōn.
mat|21|8|	o de pleistos ochlos estrōsan eautōn ta imatia en tē odō, alloi de ekopton kladous apo tōn dendrōn kai estrōnnuon en tē odō.
mat|21|9|	oi de ochloi oi proagontes kai oi akolouthountes ekrazon legontes ōsanna tō uiō dauid eulogēmenos o erchomenos en onomati kuriou ōsanna en tois upsistois.
mat|21|10|	kai eiselthontos autou eis ierosoluma eseisthē pasa ē polis legousa tis estin outos?
mat|21|11|	oi de ochloi elegon outos estin iēsous o prophētēs o apo nazaret tēs galilaias.
mat|21|12|	kai eisēlthen o iēsous eis to ieron tou theou, kai exebale pantas tous pōlountas kai agorazontas en tō ierō, kai tas trapezas tōn kollubistōn katestrepse kai tas kathedras tōn pōlountōn tas peristeras,

mat|21|28|	ti de umin dokei? anthrōpos tis eiche tekna duo, kai proselthōn tō prōtō eipe teknon, upage sēmeron ergazou en tō ampelōni mou.
mat|21|29|	o de apokritheis eipen ou thelō usteron de metamelētheis apēlthe.

mat|21|33|	allēn parabolēn akousate. anthrōpos tis ēn oikodespotēs, ostis ephuteusen ampelōna kai phragmon autō periethēke kai ōruxen en autō lēnon kai ōkodomēse purgon, kai exedoto auton geōrgois kai apedēmēsen.

mat|24|29|	eutheōs de meta tēn thlipsin tōn ēmerōn ekeinōn o ēlios skotisthēsetai kai ē selēnē ou dōsei to pheggos autēs, kai oi asteres pesountai apo tou ouranou, kai ai dunameis tōn ouranōn saleuthēsontai.
mat|24|30|	kai tote phanēsetai to sēmeion tou uiou tou anthrōpou en tō ouranō, kai tote kopsontai pasai ai phulai tēs gēs kai opsontai ton uion tou anthrōpou erchomenon epi tōn nephelōn tou ouranou meta dunameōs kai doxēs pollēs.
mat|24|31|	kai apostelei tous aggelous autou meta salpiggos phōnēs megalēs, kai episunaxousi tous eklektous autou ek tōn tessarōn anemōn ap akrōn ouranōn eōs akrōn autōn.
mat|24|32|	apo de tēs sukēs mathete tēn parabolēn. otan ēdē o klados autēs genētai apalos kai ta phulla ekphuē, ginōskete oti eggus to theros
mat|24|33|	outō kai umeis otan idēte tauta panta, ginōskete oti eggus estin epi thurais.
mat|24|34|	amēn legō umin, ou mē parelthē ē genea autē eōs an panta tauta genētai.
mat|24|35|	o ouranos kai ē gē pareleusontai, oi de logoi mou ou mē parelthōsi.
mat|24|36|	peri de tēs ēmeras ekeinēs kai ōras oudeis oiden, oude oi aggeloi tōn ouranōn, ei mē o patēr mou monos.
mat|24|37|	ōsper de ai ēmerai tou nōe, outōs estai kai ē parousia tou uiou tou anthrōpou.
mat|24|38|	ōsper gar ēsan en tais ēmerais tais pro tou kataklusmou trōgontes kai pinontes, gamountes kai ekgamizontes, achri ēs ēmeras eisēlthe nōe eis tēn kibōton,
mat|24|39|	kai ouk egnōsan eōs ēlthen o kataklusmos kai ēren apantas, outōs estai kai ē parousia tou uiou tou anthrōpou.
mat|24|40|	tote duo esontai en tō agrō, o eis paralambanetai kai o eis aphietai
mat|24|41|	duo alēthousai en tō mulōni, mia paralambanetai kai mia aphietai.
mat|24|42|	grēgoreite oun, oti ouk oidate poia ōra o kurios umōn erchetai.
mat|24|43|	ekeino de ginōskete oti ei ēdei o oikodespotēs poia phulakē o kleptēs erchetai, egrēgorēsen an kai ouk an eiase diorugēnai tēn oikian autou.
mat|24|44|	dia touto kai umeis ginesthe etoimoi, oti ē ōra ou dokeite o uios tou anthrōpou erchetai.
mat|24|45|	tis ara estin o pistos doulos kai phronimos, on katestēsen o kurios autou epi tēs therapeias autou tou didonai autois tēn trophēn en kairō?
mat|24|46|	makarios o doulos ekeinos on elthōn o kurios autou eurēsei poiounta outōs.
mat|24|47|	amēn legō umin oti epi pasi tois uparchousin autou katastēsei auton.
mat|24|48|	ean de eipē o kakos doulos ekeinos en tē kardia autou, chronizei o kurios mou elthein,
mat|24|49|	kai arxētai tuptein tous sundoulous autou, esthiē de kai pinē meta tōn methuontōn,

mat|24|51|	kai dichotomēsei auton, kai to meros autou meta tōn upokritōn thēsei ekei estai o klauthmos kai o brugmos tōn odontōn.
mat|25|1|	tote omoiōthēsetai ē basileia tōn ouranōn deka parthenois, aitines labousai tas lampadas autōn exēlthon eis apantēsin tou numphiou.
mat|25|2|	pente de ēsan ex autōn phronimoi kai ai pente mōrai.
mat|25|3|	aitines mōrai labousai tas lampadas eautōn ouk elabon meth eautōn elaion
mat|25|4|	ai de phronimoi elabon elaion en tois aggeiois autōn meta tōn lampadōn autōn.
mat|25|5|	chronizontos de tou numphiou enustaxan pasai kai ekatheudon.
mat|25|6|	mesēs de nuktos kraugē gegonen idou o numphios erchetai, exerchesthe eis apantēsin autou.
mat|25|7|	tote ēgerthēsan pasai ai parthenoi ekeinai kai ekosmēsan tas lampadas autōn.

mat|25|16|	poreutheis de o ta pente talanta labōn eirgasato en autois kai epoiēsen alla pente talanta.
mat|25|17|	ōsautōs kai o ta duo ekerdēse kai autos alla duo.
mat|25|18|	o de to en labōn apelthōn ōruxen en tē gē kai apekrupse to argurion tou kuriou autou.
mat|25|19|	meta de chronon polun erchetai o kurios tōn doulōn ekeinōn kai sunairei met autōn logon.
mat|25|20|	kai proselthōn o ta pente talanta labōn prosēnegken alla pente talanta legōn kurie, pente talanta moi paredōkas ide alla pente talanta ekerdēsa ep autois.
mat|25|21|	ephē autō o kurios autou eu, doule agathe kai piste! epi oliga ēs pistos, epi pollōn se katastēsō eiselthe eis tēn charan tou kuriou sou.
mat|25|22|	proselthōn de kai o ta duo talanta labōn eipe kurie, duo talanta moi paredōkas ide alla duo talanta ekerdēsa ep autois.
mat|25|23|	ephē autō o kurios autou eu, doule agathe kai piste! epi oliga ēs pistos, epi pollōn se katastēsō eiselthe eis tēn charan tou kuriou sou.
mat|25|24|	proselthōn de kai o to en talanton eilēphōs eipe kurie egnōn se oti sklēros ei anthrōpos, therizōn opou ouk espeiras kai sunagōn othen ou dieskorpisas
mat|25|25|	kai phobētheis apelthōn ekrupsa to talanton sou en tē gē ide echeis to son.
mat|25|26|	apokritheis de o kurios autou eipen autō ponēre doule kai oknēre! ēdeis oti therizō opou ouk espeira kai sunagō othen ou dieskorpisa!
mat|25|27|	edei oun se balein to argurion mou tois trapezitais, kai elthōn egō ekomisamēn an to emon sun tokō.
mat|25|28|	arate oun ap autou to talanton kai dote tō echonti ta deka talanta.
mat|25|29|	tō gar echonti panti dothēsetai kai perisseuthēsetai, apo de tou mē echontos kai o echei arthēsetai ap autou.
mat|25|30|	kai ton achreion doulon ekbalete eis to skotos to exōteron ekei estai o klauthmos kai o brugmos tōn odontōn.
mat|25|31|	otan de elthē o uios tou anthrōpou en tē doxē autou kai pantes oi agioi aggeloi met autou, tote kathisei epi thronou doxēs autou,
mat|25|32|	kai sunachthēsetai emprosthen autou panta ta ethnē, kai aphoriei autous ap allēlōn ōsper o poimēn aphorizei ta probata apo tōn eriphōn,
mat|25|33|	kai stēsei ta men probata ek dexiōn autou, ta de eriphia ex euōnumōn.
mat|25|34|	tote erei o basileus tois ek dexiōn autou deute oi eulogēmenoi tou patros mou, klēronomēsate tēn ētoimasmenēn umin basileian apo katabolēs kosmou.
mat|25|35|	epeinasa gar, kai edōkate moi phagein, edipsēsa, kai epotisate me, xenos ēmēn, kai sunēgagete me,

mat|26|1|	kai egeneto ote etelesen o iēsous pantas tous logous toutous eipe tois mathētais autou
mat|26|2|	oidate oti meta duo ēmeras to pascha ginetai, kai o uios tou anthrōpou paradidotai eis to staurōthēnai.
mat|26|3|	tote sunēchthēsan oi archiereis kai oi grammateis kai oi presbuteroi tou laou eis tēn aulēn tou archiereōs tou legomenou kaiapha,
mat|26|4|	kai sunebouleusanto ina ton iēsoun dolō kratēsōsi kai apokteinōsin.
mat|26|5|	elegon de mē en tē eortē, ina mē thorubos genētai en tō laō.

mat|26|31|	pantes umeis skandalisthēsesthe en emoi en tē nukti tautē gegraptai gar, pataxō ton poimena, kai diaskorpisthēsontai ta probata tēs poimnēs

mat|26|64|	legei autō o iēsous su eipas plēn legō umin, ap arti opsesthe ton uion tou anthrōpou kathēmenon ek dexiōn tēs dunameōs kai erchomenon epi tōn nephelōn tou ouranou.
mat|26|65|	tote o archiereus dierrēxe ta imatia autou legōn oti eblasphēmēse ti eti chreian echomen marturōn? ide nun ēkousate tēn blasphēmian autou
mat|26|66|	ti umin dokei? oi de apokrithentes eipon enochos thanatou esti.
mat|26|67|	tote eneptusan eis to prosōpon autou kai ekolaphisan auton, oi de errapisan

mat|26|69|	o de petros exō ekathēto en tē aulē kai prosēlthen autō mia paidiskē legousa kai su ēstha meta iēsou tou galilaiou.
mat|26|70|	o de ērnēsato emprosthen autōn pantōn legōn ouk oida ti legeis.
mat|26|71|	exelthonta de auton eis ton pulōna eiden auton allē kai legei autois ekei kai outos ēn meta iēsou tou nazōraiou.
mat|26|72|	kai palin ērnēsato meth orkou oti ouk oida ton anthrōpon.
mat|26|73|	meta mikron de proselthontes oi estōtes eipon tō petrō alēthōs kai su ex autōn ei kai gar ē lalia sou dēlon se poiei.
mat|26|74|	tote ērxato katathematizein kai omnuein oti ouk oida ton anthrōpon. kai eutheōs alektōr ephōnēse.
mat|26|75|	kai emnēsthē o petros tou rēmatos iēsou eirēkotos autō oti prin alektora phōnēsai tris aparnēsē me kai exelthōn exō eklause pikrōs.
mat|27|1|	prōias de genomenēs sumboulion elabon pantes oi archiereis kai oi presbuteroi tou laou kata tou iēsou ōste thanatōsai auton
mat|27|2|	kai dēsantes auton apēgagon kai paredōkan auton pontiō pilatō tō ēgemoni.
mat|27|3|	tote idōn ioudas o paradidous auton oti katekrithē, metamelētheis apestrepse ta triakonta arguria tois archiereusi kai tois presbuterois
mat|27|4|	legōn ēmarton paradous aima athōon. oi de eipon ti pros ēmas? su opsei.
mat|27|5|	kai ripsas ta arguria en tō naō anechōrēse, kai apelthōn apēgxato.
mat|27|6|	oi de archiereis labontes ta arguria eipon ouk exesti balein auta eis ton korbanan, epei timē aimatos esti.
mat|27|7|	sumboulion de labontes ēgorasan ex autōn ton agron tou kerameōs eis taphēn tois xenois
mat|27|8|	dio eklēthē o agros ekeinos agros aimatos eōs tēs sēmeron.
mat|27|9|	tote eplērōthē to rēthen dia ieremiou tou prophētou legontos kai elabon ta triakonta arguria, tēn timēn tou tetimēmenou on etimēsanto apo uiōn israēl,
mat|27|10|	kai edōkan auta eis ton agron tou kerameōs, katha sunetaxe moi kurios.
mat|27|11|	o de iēsous estē emprosthen tou ēgemonos kai epērōtēsen auton o ēgemōn legōn su ei o basileus tōn ioudaiōn? o de iēsous ephē autō su legeis.
mat|27|12|	kai en tō katēgoreisthai auton upo tōn archiereōn kai tōn presbuterōn ouden apekrinato.
mat|27|13|	tote legei autō o pilatos ouk akoueis posa sou katamarturousi?
mat|27|14|	kai ouk apekrithē autō pros oude en rēma, ōste thaumazein ton ēgemona lian.
mat|27|15|	kata de eortēn eiōthei o ēgemōn apoluein ena tō ochlō desmion, on ēthelon.
mat|27|16|	eichon de tote desmion episēmon legomenon barabban.
mat|27|17|	sunēgmenōn oun autōn eipen autois o pilatos tina thelete apolusō umin? barabban ē iēsoun ton legomenon christon?
mat|27|18|	ēdei gar oti dia phthonon paredōkan auton.
mat|27|19|	kathēmenou de autou epi tou bēmatos apesteile pros auton ē gunē autou legousa mēden soi kai tō dikaiō ekeinō polla gar epathon sēmeron kat onar di auton.
mat|27|20|	oi de archiereis kai oi presbuteroi epeisan tous ochlous ina aitēsōntai ton barabban, ton de iēsoun apolesōsin.
mat|27|21|	apokritheis de o ēgemōn eipen autois tina thelete apo tōn duo apolusō umin? oi de eipon barabban.
mat|27|22|	legei autois o pilatos ti oun poiēsō iēsoun ton legomenon christon? legousin autō pantes staurōthētō.
mat|27|23|	o de ēgemōn ephē ti gar kakon epoiēsen? oi de perissōs ekrazon legontes staurōthētō.
mat|27|24|	idōn de o pilatos oti ouden ōphelei, alla mallon thorubos ginetai, labōn udōr apenipsato tas cheiras apenanti tou ochlou legōn athōos eimi apo tou aimatos tou dikaiou toutou umeis opsesthe.
mat|27|25|	kai apokritheis pas o laos eipe to aima autou eph ēmas kai epi ta tekna ēmōn.
mat|27|26|	tote apelusen autois ton barabban, ton de iēsoun phragellōsas paredōken ina staurōthē.
mat|27|27|	tote oi stratiōtai tou ēgemonos paralabontes ton iēsoun eis to praitōrion sunēgagon ep auton olēn tēn speiran
mat|27|28|	kai ekdusantes auton periethēkan autō chlamuda kokkinēn,
mat|27|29|	kai plexantes stephanon ex akanthōn epethēkan epi tēn kephalēn autou kai kalamon epi tēn dexian autou, kai gonupetēsantes emprosthen autou enepaizon autō legontes chaire o basileus tōn ioudaiōn
mat|27|30|	kai emptusantes eis auton elabon ton kalamon kai etupton eis tēn kephalēn autou.
mat|27|31|	kai ote enepaixan autō, exedusan auton tēn chlamuda kai enedusan auton ta imatia autou, kai apēgagon auton eis to staurōsai.
mat|27|32|	exerchomenoi de euron anthrōpon kurēnaion onomati simōna touton ēggareusan ina arē ton stauron autou.
mat|27|33|	kai elthontes eis topon legomenon golgotha, o esti legomenos kraniou topos,
mat|27|34|	edōkan autō piein oxos meta cholēs memigmenon kai geusamenos ouk ēthele piein.
mat|27|35|	staurōsantes de auton diemerisanto ta imatia autou balontes klēron,
mat|27|36|	kai kathēmenoi etēroun auton ekei.
mat|27|37|	kai epethēkan epanō tēs kephalēs autou tēn aitian autou gegrammenēn outos estin iēsous o basileus tōn ioudaiōn.
mat|27|38|	tote staurountai sun autō duo lēstai, eis ek dexiōn kai eis ex euōnumōn.
mat|27|39|	oi de paraporeuomenoi eblasphēmoun auton kinountes tas kephalas autōn
mat|27|40|	kai legontes o kataluōn ton naon kai en trisin ēmerais oikodomōn! sōson seauton ei uios ei tou theou, katabēthi apo tou staurou.
mat|27|41|	omoiōs de kai oi archiereis empaizontes meta tōn grammateōn kai presbuterōn kai pharisaiōn elegon
mat|27|42|	allous esōsen, eauton ou dunatai sōsai ei basileus israēl esti, katabatō nun apo tou staurou kai pisteusomen ep autō
mat|27|43|	pepoithen epi ton theon, rusasthō nun auton, ei thelei auton eipe gar oti theou eimi uios.
mat|27|44|	to d auto kai oi lēstai oi sustaurōthentes autō ōneidizon auton.
mat|27|45|	apo de ektēs ōras skotos egeneto epi pasan tēn gēn eōs ōras enatēs.
mat|27|46|	peri de tēn enatēn ōran aneboēsen o iēsous phōnē megalē legōn ēli ēli, lima sabachthani? tout esti, thee mou thee mou, inati me egkatelipes?
mat|27|47|	tines de tōn ekei estōtōn akousantes elegon oti ēlian phōnei outos.
mat|27|48|	kai eutheōs dramōn eis ex autōn kai labōn spoggon plēsas te oxous kai peritheis kalamō epotizen auton.
mat|27|49|	oi de loipoi elegon aphes idōmen ei erchetai ēlias sōsōn auton.
mat|27|50|	o de iēsous palin kraxas phōnē megalē aphēke to pneuma.
mat|27|51|	kai idou to katapetasma tou naou eschisthē eis duo apo anōthen eōs katō, kai ē gē eseisthē kai ai petrai eschisthēsan,
mat|27|52|	kai ta mnēmeia aneōchthēsan kai polla sōmata tōn kekoimēmenōn agiōn ēgerthē,
mat|27|53|	kai exelthontes ek tōn mnēmeiōn, meta tēn egersin autou eisēlthon eis tēn agian polin kai enephanisthēsan pollois.
mat|27|54|	o de ekatontarchos kai oi met autou tērountes ton iēsoun, idontes ton seismon kai ta genomena ephobēthēsan sphodra legontes alēthōs theou uios ēn outos.
mat|27|55|	ēsan de ekei kai gunaikes pollai apo makrothen theōrousai, aitines ēkolouthēsan tō iēsou apo tēs galilaias diakonousai autō
mat|27|56|	en ais ēn maria ē magdalēnē, kai maria ē tou iakōbou kai iōsē mētēr, kai ē mētēr tōn uiōn zebedaiou.
mat|27|57|	opsias de genomenēs ēlthen anthrōpos plousios apo arimathaias, tounoma iōsēph, os kai autos emathēteuse tō iēsou
mat|27|58|	outos proselthōn tō pilatō ētēsato to sōma tou iēsou. tote o pilatos ekeleusen apodothēnai to sōma.
mat|27|59|	kai labōn to sōma o iōsēph enetulixen auto sindoni kathara,
mat|27|60|	kai ethēken auto en tō kainō autou mnēmeiō o elatomēsen en tē petra, kai proskulisas lithon megan tē thura tou mnēmeiou apēlthen.
mat|27|61|	ēn de ekei maria ē magdalēnē kai ē allē maria, kathēmenai apenanti tou taphou.
mat|27|62|	tē de epaurion, ētis esti meta tēn paraskeuēn, sunēchthēsan oi archiereis kai oi pharisaioi pros pilaton
mat|27|63|	legontes kurie, emnēsthēmen oti ekeinos o planos eipen eti zōn, meta treis ēmeras egeiromai.
mat|27|64|	keleuson oun asphalisthēnai ton taphon eōs tēs tritēs ēmeras, mēpote elthontes oi mathētai autou nuktos klepsōsin auton kai eipōsi tō laō, ēgerthē apo tōn nekrōn kai estai ē eschatē planē cheirōn tēs prōtēs.
mat|27|65|	ephē autois o pilatos echete koustōdian upagete asphalisasthe ōs oidate.
mat|27|66|	oi de poreuthentes ēsphalisanto ton taphon sphragisantes ton lithon meta tēs koustōdias.
mat|28|1|	opse de sabbatōn, tē epiphōskousē eis mian sabbatōn, ēlthe maria ē magdalēnē kai ē allē maria theōrēsai ton taphon.
mat|28|2|	kai idou seismos egeneto megas aggelos gar kuriou katabas ex ouranou proselthōn apekulise ton lithon apo tēs thuras kai ekathēto epanō autou.
mat|28|3|	ēn de ē idea autou ōs astrapē kai to enduma autou leukon ōsei chiōn.
mat|28|4|	apo de tou phobou autou eseisthēsan oi tērountes kai egenonto ōsei nekroi.
mat|28|5|	apokritheis de o aggelos eipe tais gunaixi mē phobeisthe umeis oida gar oti iēsoun ton estaurōmenon zēteite
mat|28|6|	ouk estin ōde ēgerthē gar kathōs eipe. deute idete ton topon opou ekeito o kurios.
mat|28|7|	kai tachu poreutheisai eipate tois mathētais autou oti ēgerthē apo tōn nekrōn, kai idou proagei umas eis tēn galilaian ekei auton opsesthe idou eipon umin.
mat|28|8|	kai exelthousai tachu apo tou mnēmeiou meta phobou kai charas megalēs edramon apaggeilai tois mathētais autou.
mat|28|9|	ōs de eporeuonto apaggeilai tois mathētais autou, kai idou iēsous apēntēsen autais legōn chairete. ai de proselthousai ekratēsan autou tous podas kai prosekunēsan autō.
mat|28|10|	tote legei autais o iēsous mē phobeisthe upagete apaggeilate tois adelphois mou ina apelthōsin eis tēn galilaian, kakei me opsontai.
mat|28|11|	poreuomenōn de autōn idou tines tēs koustōdias elthontes eis tēn polin apēggeilan tois archiereusin apanta ta genomena.
mat|28|12|	kai sunachthentes meta tōn presbuterōn sumboulion te labontes arguria ikana edōkan tois stratiōtais legontes
mat|28|13|	eipate oti oi mathētai autou nuktos elthontes eklepsan auton ēmōn koimōmenōn.
mat|28|14|	kai ean akousthē touto epi tou ēgemonos, ēmeis peisomen auton kai umas amerimnous poiēsomen.
mat|28|15|	oi de labontes ta arguria epoiēsan ōs edidachthēsan. kai diephēmisthē o logos outos para ioudaiois mechri tēs sēmeron.
mat|28|16|	oi de endeka mathētai eporeuthēsan eis tēn galilaian, eis to oros ou etaxato autois o iēsous.
mat|28|17|	kai idontes auton prosekunēsan autō, oi de edistasan.
mat|28|18|	kai proselthōn o iēsous elalēsen autois legōn edothē moi pasa exousia en ouranō kai epi gēs.
mat|28|19|	poreuthentes mathēteusate panta ta ethnē, baptizontes autous eis to onoma tou patros kai tou uiou kai tou agiou pneumatos,
mat|28|20|	didaskontes autous tērein panta osa eneteilamēn umin kai idou egō meth umōn eimi pasas tas ēmeras eōs tēs sunteleias tou aiōnos. amēn.
mar|1|1|	archē tou euaggeliou iēsou christou, uiou tou theou.
mar|1|2|	ōs gegraptai en tois prophētais, idou egō apostellō ton aggelon mou pro prosōpou sou, os kataskeuasei tēn odon sou emprosthen sou
mar|1|3|	phōnē boōntos en tē erēmō, etoimasate tēn odon kuriou, eutheias poieite tas tribous autou,
mar|1|4|	egeneto iōannēs baptizōn en tē erēmō kai kērussōn baptisma metanoias eis aphesin amartiōn.
mar|1|5|	kai exeporeueto pros auton pasa ē ioudaia chōra kai oi ierosolumitai, kai ebaptizonto pantes en tō iordanē potamō up autou exomologoumenoi tas amartias autōn.
mar|1|6|	ēn de o iōannēs endedumenos trichas kamēlou kai zōnēn dermatinēn peri tēn osphun autou, kai esthiōn akridas kai meli agrion.
mar|1|7|	kai ekērusse legōn erchetai o ischuroteros mou opisō mou, ou ouk eimi ikanos kupsas lusai ton imanta tōn upodēmatōn autou.
mar|1|8|	egō men ebaptisa umas en udati, autos de baptisei umas en pneumati agiō.
mar|1|9|	kai egeneto en ekeinais tais ēmerais ēlthen o iēsous apo nazaret tēs galilaias kai ebaptisthē upo iōannou eis ton iordanēn.
mar|1|10|	kai eutheōs anabainōn apo tou udatos eide schizomenous tous ouranous kai to pneuma ōs peristeran katabainon ep auton
mar|1|11|	kai phōnē egeneto ek tōn ouranōn su ei o uios mou o agapētos, en soi ēudokēsa.
mar|1|12|	kai eutheōs to pneuma auton ekballei eis tēn erēmon
mar|1|13|	kai ēn ekei en tē erēmō ēmeras tessarakonta peirazomenos upo tou satana, kai ēn meta tōn thēriōn, kai oi aggeloi diēkonoun autō.
mar|1|14|	meta de to paradothēnai iōannēn ēlthen o iēsous eis tēn galilaian kērussōn to euaggelion tēs basileias tou theou
mar|1|15|	kai legōn oti peplērōtai o kairos kai ēggiken ē basileia tou theou metanoeite kai pisteuete en tō euaggeliō.
mar|1|16|	peripatōn de para tēn thalassan tēs galilaias eide simōna kai andrean ton adelphon autou tou simōnos, ballontas amphiblēstron en tē thalassē ēsan gar alieis
mar|1|17|	kai eipen autois o iēsous deute opisō mou, kai poiēsō umas genesthai alieis anthrōpōn.
mar|1|18|	kai eutheōs aphentes ta diktua autōn ēkolouthēsan autō.
mar|1|19|	kai probas ekeithen oligon eiden iakōbon ton tou zebedaiou kai iōannēn ton adelphon autou, kai autous en tō ploiō katartizontas ta diktua,
mar|1|20|	kai eutheōs ekalesen autous. kai aphentes ton patera autōn zebedaion en tō ploiō meta tōn misthōtōn apēlthon opisō autou.
mar|1|21|	kai eisporeuontai eis kapernaoum kai eutheōs tois sabbasin eiselthōn eis tēn sunagōgēn edidaske.
mar|1|22|	kai exeplēssonto epi tē didachē autou ēn gar didaskōn autous ōs exousian echōn, kai ouch ōs oi grammateis.
mar|1|23|	kai ēn en tē sunagōgē autōn anthrōpos en pneumati akathartō, kai anekraxe
mar|1|24|	legōn ea, ti ēmin kai soi, iēsou nazarēne? ēlthes apolesai ēmas? oida se tis ei, o agios tou theou.
mar|1|25|	kai epetimēsen autō o iēsous legōn phimōthēti kai exelthe ex autou.
mar|1|26|	kai sparaxan auton to pneuma to akatharton kai kraxan phōnē megalē exēlthen ex autou.
mar|1|27|	kai ethambēthēsan pantes, ōste suzētein pros eautous legontas ti esti touto? tis ē didachē ē kainē autē, oti kat exousian kai tois pneumasi tois akathartois epitassei, kai upakouousin autō?
mar|1|28|	kai exēlthen ē akoē autou euthus eis olēn tēn perichōron tēs galilaias.
mar|1|29|	kai eutheōs ek tēs sunagōgēs exelthontes ēlthon eis tēn oikian simōnos kai andreou meta iakōbou kai iōannou.
mar|1|30|	ē de penthera simōnos katekeito puressousa. kai eutheōs legousin autō peri autēs.
mar|1|31|	kai proselthōn ēgeiren autēn kratēsas tēs cheiros autēs, kai aphēken autēn o puretos eutheōs, kai diēkonei autois.
mar|1|32|	opsias de genomenēs, ote edu o ēlios, epheron pros auton pantas tous kakōs echontas kai tous daimonizomenous.
mar|1|33|	kai ēn ē polis olē episunēgmenē pros tēn thuran
mar|1|34|	kai etherapeuse pollous kakōs echontas poikilais nosois, kai daimonia polla exebale, kai ouk ēphie lalein ta daimonia, oti ēdeisan auton christon einai.
mar|1|35|	kai prōi ennucha lian anastas exēlthe kai apēlthen eis erēmon topon, kakei prosēucheto.
mar|1|36|	kai katediōxan auton o simōn kai oi met autou,
mar|1|37|	kai eurontes auton legousin autō oti pantes se zētousi.
mar|1|38|	kai legei autois agōmen eis tas echomenas kōmopoleis, ina kai ekei kēruxō eis touto gar exelēlutha.
mar|1|39|	kai ēn kērussōn en tais sunagōgais autōn eis olēn tēn galilaian kai ta daimonia ekballōn.
mar|1|40|	kai erchetai pros auton lepros parakalōn auton kai gonupetōn auton kai legōn autō oti ean thelēs, dunasai me katharisai.
mar|1|41|	o de iēsous splagchnistheis, ekteinas tēn cheira ēpsato autou kai legei autō thelō, katharisthēti.
mar|1|42|	kai eipontos autou eutheōs apēlthen ap autou ē lepra, kai ekatharisthē.
mar|1|43|	kai embrimēsamenos autō eutheōs exebalen auton kai legei autō
mar|1|44|	ora mēdeni mēden eipēs, all upage seauton deixon tō ierei kai prosenegke peri tou katharismou sou a prosetaxe mōusēs eis marturion autois.
mar|1|45|	o de exelthōn ērxato kērussein polla kai diaphēmizein ton logon, ōste mēketi auton dunasthai phanerōs eis polin eiselthein, all exō en erēmois topois ēn kai ērchonto pros auton pantachothen.
mar|2|1|	kai eisēlthe palin eis kapernaoum di ēmerōn kai ēkousthē oti eis oikon esti.
mar|2|2|	kai eutheōs sunēchthēsan polloi, ōste mēketi chōrein mēde ta pros tēn thuran kai elalei autois ton logon.
mar|2|3|	kai erchontai pros auton paralutikon pherontes, airomenon upo tessarōn
mar|2|4|	kai mē dunamenoi proseggisai autō dia ton ochlon, apestegasan tēn stegēn opou ēn, kai exoruxantes chalōsi ton krabatton, eph ō o paralutikos katekeito.
mar|2|5|	idōn de o iēsous tēn pistin autōn legei tō paralutikō teknon, apheōntai soi ai amartiai sou.
mar|2|6|	ēsan de tines tōn grammateōn ekei kathēmenoi kai dialogizomenoi en tais kardiais autōn
mar|2|7|	ti outos outō lalei blasphēmias? tis dunatai aphienai amartias ei mē eis o theos?
mar|2|8|	kai eutheōs epignous o iēsous tō pneumati autou oti outōs autoi dialogizontai en eautois, eipen autois ti tauta dialogizesthe en tais kardiais umōn?
mar|2|9|	ti estin eukopōteron, eipein tō paralutikō, apheōntai sou ai amartiai, ē eipein, egeire kai aron ton krabatton sou kai peripatei?
mar|2|10|	ina de eidēte oti exousian echei o uios tou anthrōpou aphienai epi tēs gēs amartias—legei tō paralutikō
mar|2|11|	soi legō, egeire kai aron ton krabatton sou kai upage eis ton oikon sou.
mar|2|12|	kai ēgerthē eutheōs, kai aras ton krabatton exēlthen enantion pantōn, ōste existasthai pantas kai doxazein ton theon legontas oti oudepote outōs eidomen.
mar|2|13|	kai exēlthe palin para tēn thalassan kai pas o ochlos ērcheto pros auton, kai edidasken autous.
mar|2|14|	kai paragōn eide leuin ton tou alphaiou, kathēmenon epi to telōnion, kai legei autō akolouthei moi. kai anastas ēkolouthēsen autō.
mar|2|15|	kai egeneto en tō katakeisthai auton en tē oikia autou, kai polloi telōnai kai amartōloi sunanekeinto tō iēsou kai tois mathētais autou ēsan gar polloi, kai ēkolouthēsan autō.
mar|2|16|	kai oi grammateis kai oi pharisaioi idontes auton esthionta meta tōn telōnōn kai amartōlōn elegon tois mathētais autou ti oti meta tōn telōnōn kai amartōlōn esthiei kai pinei?
mar|2|17|	kai akousas o iēsous legei autois ou chreian echousin oi ischuontes iatrou, all oi kakōs echontes ouk ēlthon kalesai dikaious, alla amartōlous eis metanoian.
mar|2|18|	kai ēsan oi mathētai iōannou kai oi tōn pharisaiōn nēsteuontes. kai erchontai kai legousin autō diati oi mathētai iōannou kai oi tōn pharisaiōn nēsteuousin, oi de soi mathētai ou nēsteuousi?
mar|2|19|	kai eipen autois o iēsous mē dunantai oi uioi tou numphōnos, en ō o numphios met autōn esti, nēsteuein? oson chronon meth eautōn echousi ton numphion, ou dunantai nēsteuein.
mar|2|20|	eleusontai de ēmerai otan aparthē ap autōn o numphios, kai tote nēsteusousin en ekeinais tais ēmerais.
mar|2|21|	oudeis epiblēma rakous agnaphou epirraptei epi imatiō palaiō ei de mēge, airei to plērōma autou, to kainon tou palaiou, kai cheiron schisma ginetai.
mar|2|22|	kai oudeis ballei oinon neon eis askous palaious ei de mē, rēssei o oinos o neos tous askous, kai o oinos ekcheitai kai oi askoi apolountai alla oinon neon eis askous kainous blēteon.
mar|2|23|	kai egeneto paraporeuesthai auton en tois sabbasi dia tōn sporimōn, kai ērxanto oi mathētai autou odon poiein tillontes tous stachuas.
mar|2|24|	kai oi pharisaioi elegon autō ide ti poiousin en tois sabbasin o ouk exesti.
mar|2|25|	kai autos elegen autois oudepote anegnōte ti epoiēse dauid ote chreian esche kai epeinasen autos kai oi met autou?
mar|2|26|	pōs eisēlthen eis ton oikon tou theou epi abiathar archiereōs kai tous artous tēs protheseōs ephagen, ous ouk exesti phagein ei mē tois iereusi, kai edōke kai tois sun autō ousi?
mar|2|27|	kai elegen autois to sabbaton dia ton anthrōpon egeneto, ouch o anthrōpos dia to sabbaton
mar|2|28|	ōste kurios estin o uios tou anthrōpou kai tou sabbatou.
mar|3|1|	kai eisēlthe palin eis tēn sunagōgēn kai ēn ekei anthrōpos exērammenēn echōn tēn cheira.
mar|3|2|	kai paretēroun auton ei tois sabbasi therapeusei auton, ina katēgorēsōsin autou.
mar|3|3|	kai legei tō anthrōpō tō exērammenēn echonti tēn cheira egeire eis to meson.
mar|3|4|	kai legei autois exesti tois sabbasin agathopoiēsai ē kakopoiēsai? psuchēn sōsai ē apokteinai? oi de esiōpōn.
mar|3|5|	kai periblepsamenos autous met orgēs, sullupoumenos epi tē pōrōsei tēs kardias autōn, legei tō anthrōpō ekteinon tēn cheira sou. kai exeteine, kai apokatestathē ē cheir autou ugiēs ōs ē allē.
mar|3|6|	kai exelthontes oi pharisaioi eutheōs meta tōn ērōdianōn sumboulion epoioun kat autou, opōs auton apolesōsi.
mar|3|7|	kai o iēsous anechōrēse meta tōn mathētōn autou pros tēn thalassan kai polu plēthos apo tēs galilaias ēkolouthēsan autō,
mar|3|8|	kai apo tēs ioudaias kai apo ierosolumōn kai apo tēs idoumaias kai peran tou iordanou kai oi peri turon kai sidōna, plēthos polu, akousantes osa epoiei, ēlthon pros auton.
mar|3|9|	kai eipe tois mathētais autou ina ploiarion proskarterē autō dia ton ochlon, ina mē thlibōsin auton
mar|3|10|	pollous gar etherapeusen, ōste epipiptein autō ina autou apsōntai osoi eichon mastigas
mar|3|11|	kai ta pneumata ta akatharta, otan auton etheōroun, prosepipton autō kai ekrazon legonta oti su ei o uios tou theou.
mar|3|12|	kai polla epetima autois ina mē phaneron auton poiēsōsi.
mar|3|13|	kai anabainei eis to oros, kai proskaleitai ous ēthelen autos, kai apēlthon pros auton.
mar|3|14|	kai epoiēse dōdeka, ina ōsi met autou kai ina apostellē autous kērussein
mar|3|15|	kai echein exousian therapeuein tas nosous kai ekballein ta daimonia
mar|3|16|	kai epethēken onoma tō simōni petron,
mar|3|17|	kai iakōbon ton tou zebedaiou kai iōannēn ton adelphon tou iakōbou kai epethēken autois onomata boanerges, o estin uioi brontēs
mar|3|18|	kai andrean kai philippon kai bartholomaion kai matthaion kai thōman kai iakōbon ton tou alphaiou kai thaddaion kai simōna ton kananitēn
mar|3|19|	kai ioudan iskariōtēn, os kai paredōken auton.
mar|3|20|	kai erchontai eis oikon kai sunerchetai palin ochlos, ōste mē dunasthai autous mēde arton phagein.
mar|3|21|	kai akousantes oi par autou exēlthon kratēsai auton elegon gar oti exestē.
mar|3|22|	kai oi grammateis oi apo ierosolumōn katabantes elegon oti beelzeboul echei, kai oti en tō archonti tōn daimoniōn ekballei ta daimonia.
mar|3|23|	kai proskalesamenos autous en parabolais elegen autois pōs dunatai satanas satanan ekballein?
mar|3|24|	kai ean basileia eph eautēn meristhē, ou dunatai stathēnai ē basileia ekeinē
mar|3|25|	kai ean oikia eph eautēn meristhē, ou dunatai stathēnai ē oikia ekeinē.
mar|3|26|	kai ei o satanas anestē eph eauton kai memeristai, ou dunatai stathēnai, alla telos echei.
mar|3|27|	oudeis dunatai ta skeuē tou ischurou eiselthōn eis tēn oikian autou diarpasai, ean mē prōton ton ischuron dēsē, kai tote tēn oikian autou diarpasei.
mar|3|28|	amēn legō umin oti panta aphethēsetai tois uiois tōn anthrōpōn ta amartēmata kai ai blasphēmiai osas ean blasphēmēsōsin
mar|3|29|	os d an blasphēmēsē eis to pneuma to agion, ouk echei aphesin eis ton aiōna, all enochos estin aiōniou kriseōs
mar|3|30|	oti elegon, pneuma akatharton echei.
mar|3|31|	erchontai oun ē mētēr autou kai oi adelphoi autou, kai exō estōtes apesteilan pros auton phōnountes auton.
mar|3|32|	kai ekathēto peri auton ochlos eipon de autō idou ē mētēr sou kai oi adelphoi sou exō zētousi se.
mar|3|33|	kai apekrithē autois legōn tis estin ē mētēr mou ē oi adelphoi mou?
mar|3|34|	kai periblepsamenos kuklō tous peri auton kathēmenous legei ide ē mētēr mou kai oi adelphoi mou
mar|3|35|	os gar an poiēsē to thelēma tou theou, outos adelphos mou kai adelphē mou kai mētēr esti.
mar|4|1|	kai palin ērxato didaskein para tēn thalassan kai sunēchthē pros auton ochlos polus, ōste auton embanta eis to ploion kathēsthai en tē thalassē kai pas o ochlos pros tēn thalassan epi tēs gēs ēsan.
mar|4|2|	kai edidasken autous en parabolais polla, kai elegen autois en tē didachē autou
mar|4|3|	akouete. idou exēlthen o speirōn tou speirai.
mar|4|4|	kai egeneto en tō speirein o men epesen epi tēn odon, kai ēlthon ta peteina kai katephagen auto
mar|4|5|	kai allo epesen epi to petrōdes, opou ouk eiche gēn pollēn, kai eutheōs exaneteile dia to mē echein bathos gēs,
mar|4|6|	ēliou de anateilantos ekaumatisthē, kai dia to mē echein rizan exēranthē
mar|4|7|	kai allo epesen eis tas akanthas, kai anebēsan ai akanthai kai sunepnixan auto, kai karpon ouk edōke
mar|4|8|	kai allo epesen eis tēn gēn tēn kalēn kai edidou karpon anabainonta kai auxanonta, kai epheren en triakonta kai en exēkonta kai en ekaton.
mar|4|9|	kai elegen autois o echōn ōta akouein akouetō.
mar|4|10|	ote de egeneto kata monas, ērōtēsan auton oi peri auton sun tois dōdeka tēn parabolēn.
mar|4|11|	kai elegen autois umin dedotai gnōnai ta mustēria tēs basileias tou theou ekeinois de tois exō en parabolais ta panta ginetai,
mar|4|12|	ina blepontes blepōsi kai mē idōsi, kai akouontes akouōsi kai mē suniōsi, mēpote epistrepsōsi kai aphethē autois ta amartēmata.
mar|4|13|	kai legei autois ouk oidate tēn parabolēn tautēn, kai pōs pasas tas parabolas gnōsesthe?
mar|4|14|	o speirōn ton logon speirei.
mar|4|15|	outoi de eisin oi para tēn odon opou speiretai o logos, kai otan akousōsin, euthus erchetai o satanas kai airei ton logon ton esparmenon en tais kardiais autōn.
mar|4|16|	kai outoi omoiōs eisin oi epi ta petrōdē speiromenoi, oi otan akousōsi ton logon, euthus meta charas lambanousin auton,
mar|4|17|	kai ouk echousi rizan en eautois, alla proskairoi eisin eita genomenēs thlipseōs ē diōgmou dia ton logon, euthus skandalizontai.
mar|4|18|	kai outoi eisin oi eis tas akanthas speiromenoi, oi ton logon akouontes,
mar|4|19|	kai ai merimnai tou aiōnos toutou kai ē apatē tou ploutou kai ai peri ta loipa epithumiai eisporeuomenai sumpnigousi ton logon, kai akarpos ginetai.
mar|4|20|	kai outoi eisin oi epi tēn gēn tēn kalēn sparentes, oitines akouousi ton logon kai paradechontai, kai karpophorousin en triakonta kai en exēkonta kai en ekaton.
mar|4|21|	kai elegen autois mēti erchetai o luchnos ina upo ton modion tethē ē upo tēn klinēn? ouch ina epi tēn luchnian epitethē?
mar|4|22|	ou gar esti krupton o ean mē phanerōthē, oude egeneto apokruphon all ina elthē eis phaneron.
mar|4|23|	ei tis echei ōta akouein, akouetō.
mar|4|24|	kai elegen autois blepete ti akouete. en ō metrō metreite, metrēthēsetai umin, kai prostethēsetai umin tois akouousin.
mar|4|25|	os gar an echē, dothēsetai autō kai os ouk echei, kai o echei arthēsetai ap autou.
mar|4|26|	kai elegen outōs estin ē basileia tou theou, ōs an anthrōpos balē ton sporon epi tēs gēs,
mar|4|27|	kai katheudē kai egeirētai nukta kai ēmeran, kai o sporos blastanē kai mēkunētai ōs ouk oiden autos.
mar|4|28|	automatē gar ē gē karpophorei, prōton chorton, eita stachun, eita plērē siton en tō stachui.
mar|4|29|	otan de paradō o karpos, eutheōs apostellei to drepanon, oti parestēken o therismos.
mar|4|30|	kai elege pōs omoiōsōmen tēn basileian tou theou? ē en tini parabolē parabalōmen autēn?
mar|4|31|	ōs kokkon sinapeōs, os otan sparē epi tēs gēs, mikroteros pantōn tōn spermatōn esti tōn epi tēs gēs
mar|4|32|	kai otan sparē, anabainei kai ginetai meizōn pantōn tōn lachanōn, kai poiei kladous megalous, ōste dunasthai upo tēn skian autou ta peteina tou ouranou kataskēnoun.
mar|4|33|	kai toiautais parabolais pollais elalei autois ton logon, kathōs ēdunanto akouein,
mar|4|34|	chōris de parabolēs ouk elalei autois ton logon kat idian de tois mathētais autou epelue panta.
mar|4|35|	kai legei autois en ekeinē tē ēmera opsias genomenēs dielthōmen eis to peran.
