mar|4|38|	kai ēn autos epi tē prumnē epi to proskephalaion katheudōn kai diegeirousin auton kai legousin autō didaskale, ou melei soi oti apollumetha?
mar|4|39|	kai diegertheis epetimēse tō anemō kai eipe tē thalassē siōpa, pephimōso. kai ekopasen o anemos, kai egeneto galēnē megalē.

mar|5|1|	kai ēlthon eis to peran tēs thalassēs eis tēn chōran tōn gergesēnōn.
mar|5|2|	kai exelthontos autou ek tou ploiou eutheōs apēntēsen autō ek tōn mnēmeiōn anthrōpos en pneumati akathartō,
mar|5|3|	os tēn katoikēsin eichen en tois mnēmasi, kai oute alusesin oudeis ēdunato auton dēsai,
mar|5|4|	dia to auton pollakis pedais kai alusesi dedesthai, kai diespasthai up autou tas aluseis kai tas pedas suntetriphthai, kai oudeis ischuen auton damasai
mar|5|5|	kai dia pantos nuktos kai ēmeras en tois mnēmasi kai en tois oresin ēn krazōn kai katakoptōn eauton lithois.

mar|5|11|	ēn de ekei agelē choirōn megalē boskomenē pros tō orei
mar|5|12|	kai parekalesan auton pantes oi daimones legontes pempson ēmas eis tous choirous, ina eis autous eiselthōmen.
mar|5|13|	kai epetrepsen autois eutheōs o iēsous. kai exelthonta ta pneumata ta akatharta eisēlthon eis tous choirous kai ōrmēsen ē agelē kata tou krēmnou eis tēn thalassan ēsan de ōs dischilioi kai epnigonto en tē thalassē.
mar|5|14|	kai oi boskontes tous choirous ephugon kai apēggeilan eis tēn polin kai eis tous agrous kai exēlthon idein ti esti to gegonos.
mar|5|15|	kai erchontai pros ton iēsoun, kai theōrousi ton daimonizomenon kathēmenon kai imatismenon kai sōphronounta, ton eschēkota ton legeōna, kai ephobēthēsan.
mar|5|16|	kai diēgēsanto autois oi idontes pōs egeneto tō daimonizomenō kai peri tōn choirōn.

mar|5|20|	kai apēlthe kai ērxato kērussein en tē dekapolei osa epoiēsen autō o iēsous, kai pantes ethaumazon.
mar|5|21|	kai diaperasantos tou iēsou en tō ploiō palin eis to peran sunēchthē ochlos polus ep auton, kai ēn para tēn thalassan.
mar|5|22|	kai erchetai eis tōn archisunagōgōn, onomati iaeiros, kai idōn auton piptei pros tous podas autou
mar|5|23|	kai parekalei auton polla, legōn oti to thugatrion mou eschatōs echei, ina elthōn epithēs autē tas cheiras, opōs sōthē kai zēsetai.
mar|5|24|	kai apēlthe met autou kai ēkolouthei autō ochlos polus, kai sunethlibon auton.
mar|5|25|	kai gunē tis ousa en rusei aimatos etē dōdeka,
mar|5|26|	kai polla pathousa upo pollōn iatrōn kai dapanēsasa ta par eautēs panta, kai mēden ōphelētheisa, alla mallon eis to cheiron elthousa,
mar|5|27|	akousasa peri tou iēsou, elthousa en tō ochlō opisthen ēpsato tou imatiou autou
mar|5|28|	elege gar en eautē oti ean apsōmai kan tōn imatiōn autou, sōthēsomai.

mar|5|31|	kai elegon autō oi mathētai autou blepeis ton ochlon sunthlibonta se, kai legeis tis mou ēpsato?
mar|5|32|	kai perieblepeto idein tēn touto poiēsasan.

mar|6|1|	kai exēlthen ekeithen kai ēlthen eis tēn patrida eautou kai akolouthousin autō oi mathētai autou.
mar|6|2|	kai genomenou sabbatou ērxato en tē sunagōgē didaskein kai polloi akouontes exeplēssonto legontes pothen toutō tauta? kai tis ē sophia ē dotheisa autō, kai dunameis toiautai dia tōn cheirōn autou ginontai?
mar|6|3|	ouch outos estin o tektōn, o uios tēs marias, adelphos de iakōbou kai iōsē kai iouda kai simōnos? kai ouk eisin ai adelphai autou ōde pros ēmas? kai eskandalizonto en autō.
mar|6|4|	elege de autois o iēsous oti ouk esti prophētēs atimos ei mē en tē patridi autou kai en tois suggenesi kai en tē oikia autou.
mar|6|5|	kai ouk ēdunato ekei oudemian dunamin poiēsai, ei mē oligois arrōstois epitheis tas cheiras etherapeuse.
mar|6|6|	kai ethaumaze dia tēn apistian autōn. kai periēge tas kōmas kuklō didaskōn.
mar|6|7|	kai proskaleitai tous dōdeka, kai ērxato autous apostellein duo duo, kai edidou autois exousian tōn pneumatōn tōn akathartōn,
mar|6|8|	kai parēggeilen autois ina mēden airōsin eis odon ei mē rabdon monon, mē pēran, mē arton, mē eis tēn zōnēn chalkon,
mar|6|9|	all upodedemenous sandalia, kai mē endedusthai duo chitōnas.
mar|6|10|	kai elegen autois opou ean eiselthēte eis oikian, ekei menete eōs an exelthēte ekeithen
mar|6|11|	kai osoi ean mē dexōntai umas mēde akousōsin umōn, ekporeuomenoi ekeithen ektinaxate ton choun ton upokatō tōn podōn umōn eis marturion autois amēn legō umin, anektoteron estai sodomois ē gomorrois en ēmera kriseōs ē tē polei ekeinē.
mar|6|12|	kai exelthontes ekērusson ina metanoēsōsi,
mar|6|13|	kai daimonia polla exeballon, kai ēleiphon elaiō pollous arrōstous kai etherapeuon.
mar|6|14|	kai ēkousen o basileus ērōdēs phaneron gar egeneto to onoma autou kai elegen oti iōannēs o baptizōn ek nekrōn ēgerthē, kai dia touto energousin ai dunameis en autō.
mar|6|15|	alloi elegon oti ēlias estin alloi de elegon oti prophētēs estin ōs eis tōn prophētōn.
mar|6|16|	akousas de o ērōdēs eipen oti on egō apekephalisa iōannēn, outos estin autos ēgerthē ek nekrōn.
mar|6|17|	autos gar o ērōdēs aposteilas ekratēse ton iōannēn kai edēsen auton en phulakē dia ērōdiada tēn gunaika philippou tou adelphou autou, oti autēn egamēsen.
mar|6|18|	elege gar o iōannēs tō ērōdē oti ouk exesti soi echein tēn gunaika tou adelphou sou.
mar|6|19|	ē de ērōdias eneichen autō kai ēthelen auton apokteinai, kai ouk ēdunato
mar|6|20|	o gar ērōdēs ephobeito ton iōannēn, eidōs auton andra dikaion kai agion, kai sunetērei auton, kai akousas autou polla epoiei kai ēdeōs autou ēkoue.
mar|6|21|	kai genomenēs ēmeras eukairou, ote ērōdēs tois genesiois autou deipnon epoiei tois megistasin autou kai tois chiliarchois kai tois prōtois tēs galilaias,
mar|6|22|	kai eiselthousēs tēs thugatros autēs tēs ērōdiados kai orchēsamenēs kai aresasēs tō ērōdē kai tois sunanakeimenois, eipen o basileus tō korasiō aitēson me o ean thelēs, kai dōsō soi.
mar|6|23|	kai ōmosen autē oti o ean me aitēsēs dōsō soi, eōs ēmisous tēs basileias mou.
mar|6|24|	ē de exelthousa eipe tē mētri autēs ti aitēsomai? ē de eipe tēn kephalēn iōannou tou baptistou.
mar|6|25|	kai eiselthousa eutheōs meta spoudēs pros ton basilea ētēsato legousa thelō ina moi dōs exautēs epi pinaki tēn kephalēn iōannou tou baptistou.
mar|6|26|	kai perilupos genomenos o basileus, dia tous orkous kai tous sunanakeimenous ouk ēthelēsen autēn athetēsai.
mar|6|27|	kai eutheōs aposteilas o basileus spekoulatōra epetaxen enechthēnai tēn kephalēn autou.
mar|6|28|	o de apelthōn apekephalisen auton en tē phulakē, kai ēnegke tēn kephalēn autou epi pinaki kai edōken autēn tō korasiō, kai to korasion edōken autēn tē mētri autēs.
mar|6|29|	kai akousantes oi mathētai autou ēlthon kai ēran to ptōma autou, kai ethēkan auto en mnēmeiō.
mar|6|30|	kai sunagontai oi apostoloi pros ton iēsoun, kai apēggeilan autō panta, kai osa epoiēsan kai osa edidaxan.
mar|6|31|	kai eipen autois deute umeis autoi kat idian eis erēmon topon, kai anapauesthe oligon ēsan gar oi erchomenoi kai oi upagontes polloi, kai oude phagein eukairoun.
mar|6|32|	kai apēlthon eis erēmon topon en ploiō kat idian.
mar|6|33|	kai eidon autous upagontas, kai epegnōsan autous polloi, kai pezē apo pasōn tōn poleōn sunedramon ekei kai proēlthon autous kai sunēlthon pros auton.
mar|6|34|	kai exelthōn o iēsous eide polun ochlon kai esplagchnisthē ep autois, oti ēsan ōs probata mē echonta poimena, kai ērxato didaskein autous polla.
mar|6|35|	kai ēdē ōras pollēs genomenēs proselthontes autō oi mathētai autou legousin oti erēmos estin o topos kai ēdē ōra pollē
mar|6|36|	apoluson autous, ina apelthontes eis tous kuklō agrous kai kōmas agorasōsin eautois artous ti gar phagōsin ouk echousin.
mar|6|37|	o de apokritheis eipen autois dote autois umeis phagein. kai legousin autō apelthontes agorasōmen dēnariōn diakosiōn artous kai dōmen autois phagein?
mar|6|38|	o de legei autois posous artous echete? upagete kai idete. kai gnontes legousi pente, kai duo ichthuas.
mar|6|39|	kai epetaxen autois anaklinai pantas sumposia sumposia epi tō chlōrō chortō.
mar|6|40|	kai anepeson prasiai prasiai ana ekaton kai ana pentēkonta.
mar|6|41|	kai labōn tous pente artous kai tous duo ichthuas anablepsas eis ton ouranon eulogēse, kai kateklase tous artous kai edidou tois mathētais ina parathōsin autois, kai tous duo ichthuas emerise pasi.
mar|6|42|	kai ephagon pantes kai echortasthēsan,
mar|6|43|	kai ēran klasmatōn dōdeka kophinous plēreis, kai apo tōn ichthuōn.
mar|6|44|	kai ēsan oi phagontes tous artous pentakischilioi andres.
mar|6|45|	kai eutheōs ēnagkase tous mathētas autou embēnai eis to ploion kai proagein eis to peran pros bēthsaidan, eōs autos apolusē ton ochlon
mar|6|46|	kai apotaxamenos autois apēlthen eis to oros proseuxasthai.
mar|6|47|	kai opsias genomenēs ēn to ploion en mesō tēs thalassēs, kai autos monos epi tēs gēs.
mar|6|48|	kai idōn autous basanizomenous en tō elaunein ēn gar o anemos enantios autois kai peri tetartēn phulakēn tēs nuktos erchetai pros autous peripatōn epi tēs thalassēs, kai ēthele parelthein autous.
mar|6|49|	oi de idontes auton peripatounta epi tēs thalassēs edoxan phantasma einai, kai anekraxan
mar|6|50|	pantes gar auton eidon kai etarachthēsan. kai eutheōs elalēse met autōn kai legei autois tharseite, egō eimi, mē phobeisthe.
mar|6|51|	kai anebē eis to ploion pros autous, kai ekopasen o anemos kai lian ek perissou en eautois existanto kai ethaumazon.
mar|6|52|	ou gar sunēkan epi tois artois, all ēn autōn ē kardia pepōrōmenē.
mar|6|53|	kai diaperasantes apēlthon epi tēn gēn gennēsaret kai prosōrmisthēsan.
mar|6|54|	kai exelthontōn autōn ek tou ploiou eutheōs epignontes auton
mar|6|55|	periedramon olēn tēn perichōron ekeinēn kai ērxanto epi tois krabattois tous kakōs echontas peripherein opou ēkouon oti ekei esti
mar|6|56|	kai opou an eiseporeueto eis kōmas ē poleis ē agrous, en tais agorais etithesan tous asthenountas kai parekaloun auton ina kan tou kraspedou tou imatiou autou apsōntai kai osoi an ēptonto autou, esōzonto.
mar|7|1|	kai sunagontai pros auton oi pharisaioi kai tines tōn grammateōn elthontes apo ierosolumōn
mar|7|2|	kai idontes tinas tōn mathētōn autou koinais chersi, tout estin aniptois, esthiontas artous, emempsanto
mar|7|3|	oi gar pharisaioi kai pantes oi ioudaioi, ean mē pugmē nipsōntai tas cheiras, ouk esthiousi, kratountes tēn paradosin tōn presbuterōn
mar|7|4|	kai apo agoras, ean mē baptisōntai, ouk esthiousi kai alla polla estin a parelabon kratein, baptismous potēriōn kai xestōn kai chalkiōn kai klinōn
mar|7|5|	epeita eperōtōsin auton oi pharisaioi kai oi grammateis diati ou peripatousin oi mathētai sou kata tēn paradosin tōn presbuterōn, all aniptois chersin esthiousi ton arton?
mar|7|6|	o de apokritheis eipen autois oti kalōs proephēteusen ēsaias peri umōn tōn upokritōn, ōs gegraptai outos o laos tois cheilesi me tima, ē de kardia autōn porrō apechei ap emou
mar|7|7|	matēn de sebontai me, didaskontes didaskalias entalmata anthrōpōn.
mar|7|8|	aphentes gar tēn entolēn tou theou krateite tēn paradosin tōn anthrōpōn, baptismous xestōn kai potēriōn, kai alla paromoia toiauta polla poieite.
mar|7|9|	kai elegen autois kalōs atheteite tēn entolēn tou theou ina tēn paradosin umōn tērēsēte.
mar|7|10|	mōusēs gar eipe tima ton patera sou kai tēn mētera sou kai o kakologōn patera ē mētera thanatō teleutatō
mar|7|11|	umeis de legete ean eipē anthrōpos tō patri ē tē mētri, korban, o esti dōron, o ean ex emou ōphelēthēs,
mar|7|12|	kai ouketi aphiete auton ouden poiēsai tō patri autou ē tē mētri autou,
mar|7|13|	akurountes ton logon tou theou tē paradosei umōn ē paredōkate kai paromoia toiauta polla poieite.
mar|7|14|	kai proskalesamenos panta ton ochlon elegen autois akouete mou pantes kai suniete.
mar|7|15|	ouden estin exōthen tou anthrōpou eisporeuomenon eis auton o dunatai auton koinōsai, alla ta ekporeuomena esti ta koinounta ton anthrōpon.
mar|7|16|	ei tis echei ōta akouein, akouetō] .
mar|7|17|	kai ote eisēlthen eis oikon apo tou ochlou, epērōtōn auton oi mathētai autou peri tēs parabolēs.
mar|7|18|	kai legei autois outō kai umeis asunetoi este? oupō noeite oti pan to exōthen eisporeuomenon eis ton anthrōpon ou dunatai auton koinōsai?
mar|7|19|	oti ouk eisporeuetai autou eis tēn kardian, all eis tēn koilian, kai eis ton aphedrōna ekporeuetai, katharizon panta ta brōmata.
mar|7|20|	elege de oti to ek tou anthrōpou ekporeuomenon, ekeino koinoi ton anthrōpon.
mar|7|21|	esōthen gar ek tēs kardias tōn anthrōpōn oi dialogismoi oi kakoi ekporeuontai, moicheiai, porneiai, phonoi,
mar|7|22|	klopai, pleonexiai, ponēriai, dolos, aselgeia, ophthalmos ponēros, blasphēmia, uperēphania, aphrosunē
mar|7|23|	panta tauta ta ponēra esōthen ekporeuetai kai koinoi ton anthrōpon.
mar|7|24|	kai ekeithen anastas apēlthen eis ta methoria turou kai sidōnos. kai eiselthōn eis oikian oudena ēthele gnōnai, kai ouk ēdunēthē lathein.
mar|7|25|	akousasa gar gunē peri autou, ēs eiche to thugatrion autēs pneuma akatharton, elthousa prosepese pros tous podas autou
mar|7|26|	de gunē ēn ellēnis, surophoinikissa tō genei kai ērōta auton ina to daimonion ekbalē ek tēs thugatros autēs.
mar|7|27|	o de iēsous eipen autē aphes prōton chortasthēnai ta tekna ou gar esti kalon labein ton arton tōn teknōn kai tois kunariois balein.
mar|7|28|	ē de apekrithē kai legei autō nai, kurie kai ta kunaria upokatō tēs trapezēs esthiousin apo tōn psichiōn tōn paidiōn.
mar|7|29|	kai eipen autē dia touton ton logon upage exelēluthe to daimonion ek tēs thugatros sou.
mar|7|30|	kai apelthousa eis ton oikon autēs eure to paidion beblēmenon epi tēn klinēn kai to daimonion exelēluthos.
mar|7|31|	kai palin exelthōn ek tōn oriōn turou kai sidōnos ēlthe pros tēn thalassan tēs galilaias ana meson tōn oriōn dekapoleōs.
mar|7|32|	kai pherousin autō kōphon mogilalon kai parakalousin auton ina epithē autō tēn cheira.
mar|7|33|	kai apolabomenos auton apo tou ochlou kat idian ebale tous daktulous autou eis ta ōta autou, kai ptusas ēpsato tēs glōssēs autou,
mar|7|34|	kai anablepsas eis ton ouranon estenaxe kai legei autō ephphatha, o esti dianoichthēti.
mar|7|35|	kai eutheōs diēnoichthēsan autou ai akoai kai eluthē o desmos tēs glōssēs autou, kai elalei orthōs.
mar|7|36|	kai diesteilato autois ina mēdeni eipōsin oson de autos autois diestelleto, mallon perissoteron ekērusson.
mar|7|37|	kai uperperissōs exeplēssonto legontes kalōs panta pepoiēke kai tous kōphous poiei akouein kai tous alalous lalein.
mar|8|1|	en ekeinais tais ēmerais palin pollou ochlou ontos kai mē echontōn ti phagōsi, proskalesamenos o iēsous tous mathētas autou legei autois
mar|8|2|	splagchnizomai epi ton ochlon, oti ēdē ēmerai treis prosmenousi moi kai ouk echousi ti phagōsi
mar|8|3|	kai ean apolusō autous nēsteis eis oikon autōn, ekluthēsontai en tē odō tines gar autōn apo makrothen ēkasi.
mar|8|4|	kai apekrithēsan autō oi mathētai autou pothen toutous dunēsetai tis ōde chortasai artōn ep erēmias?
mar|8|5|	kai epērōta autous posous echete artous? oi de eipon epta.
mar|8|6|	kai parēggeile tō ochlō anapesein epi tēs gēs kai labōn tous epta artous eucharistēsas eklase kai edidou tois mathētais autou ina paratithōsi kai parethēkan tō ochlō.
mar|8|7|	kai eichon ichthudia oliga kai auta eulogēsas eipe paratithenai kai auta.
mar|8|8|	ephagon de kai echortasthēsan, kai ēran perisseumata klasmatōn epta spuridas.
mar|8|9|	ēsan de ōs tetrakischilioi kai apelusen autous.
mar|8|10|	kai embas euthus eis to ploion meta tōn mathētōn autou ēlthen eis ta merē dalmanoutha.
mar|8|11|	kai exēlthon oi pharisaioi kai ērxanto suzētein autō, zētountes par autou sēmeion apo tou ouranou, peirazontes auton.
mar|8|12|	kai anastenaxas tō pneumati autou legei ti ē genea autē sēmeion epizētei? amēn legō umin, ei dothēsetai tē genea tautē sēmeion.
mar|8|13|	kai apheis autous eis to ploion apēlthe palin.

mar|8|16|	kai dielogizonto pros allēlous legontes oti artous ouk echomen.
mar|8|17|	kai gnous o iēsous legei autois ti dialogizesthe oti artous ouk echete? oupō noeite oude suniete? eti pepōrōmenēn echete tēn kardian umōn?
mar|8|18|	ophthalmous echontes ou blepete, kai ōta echontes ouk akouete? kai ou mnēmoneuete?
mar|8|19|	ote tous pente artous eklasa eis tous pentakischilious, kai posous kophinous klasmatōn plēreis ērate? legousin autō dōdeka.
mar|8|20|	ote de tous epta eis tous tetrakischilious, posōn spuridōn plērōmata klasmatōn ērate? oi de eipon epta.
mar|8|21|	kai elegen autois oupō suniete?
mar|8|22|	kai erchetai eis bēthsaida. kai pherousin autō tuphlon kai parakalousin auton ina autou apsētai.
mar|8|23|	kai epilabomenos tēs cheiros tou tuphlou exēgagen auton exō tēs kōmēs, kai ptusas eis ta ommata autou, epitheis tas cheiras autō epērōta auton ei ti blepei.
mar|8|24|	kai anablepsas elege blepō tous anthrōpous ōs dendra peripatountas.
mar|8|25|	eita palin epethēke tas cheiras epi tous ophthalmous autou kai epoiēsen auton anablepsai, kai apokatestathē, kai eneblepse tēlaugōs apantas.
mar|8|26|	kai apesteilen auton eis ton oikon autou legōn mēde eis tēn kōmēn eiselthēs mēde eipēs tini en tē kōmē.
mar|8|27|	kai exēlthen o iēsous kai oi mathētai autou eis tas kōmas kaisareias tēs philippou kai en tē odō epērōta tous mathētas autou legōn autois tina me legousin oi anthrōpoi einai?
mar|8|28|	oi de apekrithēsan iōannēn ton baptistēn, kai alloi ēlian, alloi de ena tōn prophētōn.

mar|8|30|	kai epetimēsen autois ina mēdeni legōsi peri autou.
mar|8|31|	kai ērxato didaskein autous oti dei ton uion tou anthrōpou polla pathein, kai apodokimasthēnai apo tōn presbuterōn kai tōn archiereōn kai tōn grammateōn, kai apoktanthēnai, kai meta treis ēmeras anastēnai
mar|8|32|	kai parrēsia ton logon elalei. kai proslabomenos auton o petros ērxato epitiman autō.

mar|8|35|	os gar an thelē tēn psuchēn autou sōsai, apolesei autēn os d an apolesē tēn eautou psuchēn eneken emou kai tou euaggeliou, outos sōsei autēn.

mar|8|38|	os gar ean epaischunthē me kai tous emous logous en tē genea tautē tē moichalidi kai amartōlō, kai o uios tou anthrōpou epaischunthēsetai auton otan elthē en tē doxē tou patros autou meta tōn aggelōn tōn agiōn.
mar|9|1|	kai elegen autois amēn legō umin oti eisi tines tōn ōde estēkotōn, oitines ou mē geusōntai thanatou eōs an idōsi tēn basileian tou theou elēluthuian en dunamei.
mar|9|2|	kai meth ēmeras ex paralambanei o iēsous ton petron kai ton iakōbon kai ton iōannēn kai anapherei autous eis oros upsēlon kat idian monous kai metemorphōthē emprosthen autōn,
mar|9|3|	kai ta imatia autou egeneto stilbonta, leuka lian ōs chiōn, oia gnapheus epi tēs gēs ou dunatai outō leukanai.
mar|9|4|	kai ōphthē autois ēlias sun mōusei, kai ēsan sullalountes tō iēsou. kai apokritheis o petros legei tō iēsou
mar|9|5|	rabbi, kalon estin ēmas ōde einai kai poiēsōmen skēnas treis, soi mian kai mōusei mian kai ēlia mian.
mar|9|6|	ou gar ēdei ti lalēsē ēsan gar ekphoboi.
mar|9|7|	kai egeneto nephelē episkiazousa autois, kai ēlthe phōnē ek tēs nephelēs legousa outos estin o uios mou o agapētos autou akouete.
mar|9|8|	kai exapina periblepsamenoi ouketi oudena eidon, alla ton iēsoun monon meth eautōn.
mar|9|9|	katabainontōn de autōn apo tou orous diesteilato autois ina mēdeni diēgēsōntai a eidon, ei mē otan o uios tou anthrōpou ek nekrōn anastē.
mar|9|10|	kai ton logon ekratēsan, pros eautous suzētountes ti esti to ek nekrōn anastēnai.
mar|9|11|	kai epērōtōn auton legontes, oti legousin oi grammateis oti ēlian dei elthein prōton.
mar|9|12|	o de apokritheis eipen autois ēlias men elthōn prōton apokathista panta kai pōs gegraptai epi ton uion tou anthrōpou ina polla pathē kai exoudenōthē?
mar|9|13|	alla legō umin oti kai ēlias elēluthe, kai epoiēsan autō osa ēthelēsan, kathōs gegraptai ep auton.
mar|9|14|	kai elthōn pros tous mathētas eiden ochlon polun peri autous, kai grammateis suzētountas autois.
mar|9|15|	kai eutheōs pas o ochlos idontes auton exethambēthēsan, kai prostrechontes ēspazonto auton.
mar|9|16|	kai epērōtēse tous grammateis ti suzēteite pros eautous?
mar|9|17|	kai apokritheis eis ek tou ochlou eipe didaskale, ēnegka ton uion mou pros se, echonta pneuma alalon.
mar|9|18|	kai opou an auton katalabē, rēssei auton, kai aphrizei kai trizei tous odontas autou, kai xērainetai kai eipon tois mathētais sou ina auto ekbalōsi, kai ouk ischusan.
mar|9|19|	o de apokritheis autō legei ō genea apistos, eōs pote pros umas esomai? eōs pote anexomai umōn? pherete auton pros me. kai ēnegkan auton pros auton.
mar|9|20|	kai idōn auton eutheōs to pneuma esparaxen auton, kai pesōn epi tēs gēs ekulieto aphrizōn.
mar|9|21|	kai epērōtēse ton patera autou posos chronos estin ōs touto gegonen autō? o de eipe paidiothen.
mar|9|22|	kai pollakis auton kai eis pur ebale kai eis udata, ina apolesē auton all ei ti dunasai, boēthēson ēmin splagchnistheis eph ēmas.
mar|9|23|	o de iēsous eipen autō to ei dunasai pisteusai, panta dunata tō pisteuonti.
mar|9|24|	kai eutheōs kraxas o patēr tou paidiou meta dakruōn elege pisteuō, kurie boēthei mou tē apistia.
mar|9|25|	idōn de o iēsous oti episuntrechei ochlos, epetimēse tō pneumati tō akathartō legōn autō to pneuma to alalon kai kōphon, egō soi epitassō, exelthe ex autou kai mēketi eiselthēs eis auton.
mar|9|26|	kai kraxan kai polla sparaxan auton exēlthe, kai egeneto ōsei nekros, ōste pollous legein oti apethanen.
mar|9|27|	o de iēsous kratēsas auton tēs cheiros ēgeiren auton, kai anestē.
mar|9|28|	kai eiselthonta auton eis oikon oi mathētai autou epērōtōn auton kat idian, oti ēmeis ouk ēdunēthēmen ekbalein auto.
mar|9|29|	kai eipen autois touto to genos en oudeni dunatai exelthein ei mē en proseuchē kai nēsteia.
mar|9|30|	kai ekeithen exelthontes pareporeuonto dia tēs galilaias, kai ouk ēthelen ina tis gnō

mar|9|32|	oi de ēgnooun to rēma, kai ephobounto auton eperōtēsai.

mar|9|38|	apekrithē autō o iōannēs legōn didaskale, eidomen tina en tō onomati sou ekballonta daimonia, os ouk akolouthei ēmin, kai ekōlusamen auton, oti ouk akolouthei ēmin.
mar|9|39|	o de iēsous eipe mē kōluete auton oudeis gar estin os poiēsei dunamin epi tō onomati mou kai dunēsetai tachu kakologēsai me.
mar|9|40|	os gar ouk esti kath umōn, uper umōn estin.

mar|9|42|	kai os an skandalisē ena tōn mikrōn toutōn tōn pisteuontōn eis eme, kalon estin autō mallon ei perikeitai lithos mulikos peri ton trachēlon autou kai beblētai eis tēn thalassan.
mar|9|43|	kai ean skandalizē se ē cheir sou, apokopson autēn kalon soi esti kullon eis tēn zōēn eiselthein, ē tas duo cheiras echonta apelthein eis tēn geennan, eis to pur to asbeston,
mar|9|44|	opou o skōlēx autōn ou teleuta kai to pur ou sbennutai.

mar|9|46|	opou o skōlēx autōn ou teleuta kai to pur ou sbennutai.

mar|9|48|	opou o skōlēx autōn ou teleuta kai to pur ou sbennutai.

mar|10|2|	kai proselthontes oi pharisaioi epērōtōn auton ei exestin andri gunaika apolusai, peirazontes auton.
mar|10|3|	o de apokritheis eipen autois ti umin eneteilato mōusēs?

mar|10|5|	kai apokritheis o iēsous eipen autois pros tēn sklērokardian umōn egrapsen umin tēn entolēn tautēn

mar|10|7|	eneken toutou kataleipsei anthrōpos ton patera autou kai tēn mētera, kai proskollēthēsetai pros tēn gunaika autou, kai esontai oi duo eis sarka mian.

mar|10|22|	o de stugnasas epi tō logō apēlthe lupoumenos ēn gar echōn ktēmata polla.
mar|10|23|	kai periblepsamenos o iēsous legei tois mathētais autou pōs duskolōs oi ta chrēmata echontes eis tēn basileian tou theou eiseleusontai!

mar|10|31|	polloi de esontai prōtoi eschatoi kai eschatoi prōtoi.

mar|12|1|	kai ērxato autois en parabolais legein ampelōna ephuteusen anthrōpos kai periethēke phragmon kai ōruxen upolēnion kai ōkodomēse purgon, kai exedoto auton geōrgois kai apedēmēse.

mar|12|20|	epta oun adelphoi ēsan. kai o prōtos elabe gunaika, kai apothnēskōn ouk aphēke sperma.

mar|12|29|	o de iēsous apekrithē autō oti prōtē pantōn entolē akoue, israēl, kurios o theos ēmōn kurios eis esti
mar|12|30|	kai agapēseis kurion ton theon sou ex olēs tēs kardias sou kai ex olēs tēs psuchēs sou kai ex olēs tēs dianoias sou kai ex olēs tēs ischuos sou. autē prōtē entolē.

mar|12|32|	kai eipen autō o grammateus kalōs, didaskale, ep alētheias eipas oti eis esti kai ouk estin allos plēn autou
mar|12|33|	kai to agapan auton ex olēs tēs kardias kai ex olēs tēs suneseōs kai ex olēs tēs psuchēs kai ex olēs tēs ischuos, kai to agapan ton plēsion ōs eauton pleion esti pantōn tōn olokautōmatōn kai thusiōn.
mar|12|34|	kai o iēsous idōn oti nounechōs apekrithē, eipen autō ou makran ei apo tēs basileias tou theou kai oudeis ouketi etolma auton eperōtēsai.
mar|12|35|	kai apokritheis o iēsous elege didaskōn en tō ierō pōs legousin oi grammateis oti o christos uios dauid esti?
mar|12|36|	autos gar dauid eipen en pneumati agiō legei o kurios tō kuriō mou, kathou ek dexiōn mou eōs an thō tous echthrous sou upopodion tōn podōn sou.
mar|12|37|	autos oun dauid legei auton kurion kai pothen uios autou esti? kai o polus ochlos ēkouen autou ēdeōs.
mar|12|38|	kai elegen autois en tē didachē autou blepete apo tōn grammateōn tōn thelontōn en stolais peripatein kai aspasmous en tais agorais
mar|12|39|	kai prōtokathedrias en tais sunagōgais kai prōtoklisias en tois deipnois.
mar|12|40|	oi katesthiontes tas oikias tōn chērōn kai prophasei makra proseuchomenoi! outoi lēpsontai perissoteron krima.
mar|12|41|	kai kathisas o iēsous katenanti tou gazophulakiou etheōrei pōs o ochlos ballei chalkon eis to gazophulakion.
mar|12|42|	kai polloi plousioi eballon polla kai elthousa mia chēra ptōchē ebale lepta duo, o esti kodrantēs.
mar|12|43|	kai proskalesamenos tous mathētas autou eipen autois amēn legō umin oti ē chēra ē ptōchē autē pleion pantōn ebale tōn ballontōn eis to gazophulakion
mar|12|44|	pantes gar ek tou perisseuontos autois ebalon autē de ek tēs usterēseōs autēs panta osa eichen ebalen, olon ton bion autēs.
mar|13|1|	kai ekporeuomenou autou ek tou ierou legei autō eis tōn mathētōn autou didaskale, ide potapoi lithoi kai potapai oikodomai.
mar|13|2|	kai o iēsous apokritheis eipen autō blepeis tautas tas megalas oikodomas? ou mē aphethē ōde lithos epi lithon os ou mē kataluthē.
mar|13|3|	kai kathēmenou autou eis to oros tōn elaiōn katenanti tou ierou, epērōtōn auton kat idian petros kai iakōbos kai iōannēs kai andreas
mar|13|4|	eipe ēmin pote tauta estai, kai ti to sēmeion otan mellē panta tauta sunteleisthai?
mar|13|5|	o de iēsous apokritheis ērxato legein autois blepete mē tis umas planēsē.
mar|13|6|	polloi gar eleusontai epi tō onomati mou legontes oti egō eimi, kai pollous planēsousin.
mar|13|7|	otan de akousēte polemous kai akoas polemōn, mē throeisthe dei gar genesthai, all oupō to telos.
mar|13|8|	egerthēsetai gar ethnos epi ethnos kai basileia epi basileian, kai esontai seismoi kata topous, kai esontai limoi kai tarachai.
mar|13|9|	archai ōdinōn tauta. blepete de umeis eautous. paradōsousi gar umas eis sunedria kai en tais sunagōgais autōn darēsesthe, kai epi ēgemonōn kai basileōn stathēsesthe eneken emou eis marturion autois.
mar|13|10|	kai eis panta ta ethnē dei prōton kēruchthēnai to euaggelion.
mar|13|11|	otan de agagōsin umas paradidontes, mē promerimnate ti lalēsēte, mēde meletate, all o ean dothē umin en ekeinē tē ōra, touto laleite ou gar umeis este oi lalountes, alla to pneuma to agion.
mar|13|12|	paradōsei de adelphos adelphon eis thanaton kai patēr teknon, kai epanastēsontai tekna epi goneis kai thanatōsousin autous.
mar|13|13|	kai esesthe misoumenoi upo pantōn dia to onoma mou o de upomeinas eis telos, outos sōthēsetai.
mar|13|14|	otan de idēte to bdelugma tēs erēmōseōs to rēthen upo daniēl tou prophētou estōs opou ou dei—o anaginōskōn noeitō—tote oi en tē ioudaia pheugetōsan eis ta orē,
mar|13|15|	o de epi tou dōmatos mē katabatō eis tēn oikian mēde eiselthetō arai ti ek tēs oikias autou,
mar|13|16|	kai o eis ton agron ōn mē epistrepsatō eis ta opisō arai to imation autou.
mar|13|17|	ouai de tais en gastri echousais kai tais thēlazousais en ekeinais tais ēmerais.
mar|13|18|	proseuchesthe de ina mē genētai ē phugē umōn cheimōnos.
mar|13|19|	esontai gar ai ēmerai ekeinai thlipsis, oia ou gegone toiautē ap archēs ktiseōs ēs ektisen o theos eōs tou nun kai ou mē genētai.
mar|13|20|	kai ei mē ekolobōse kurios tas ēmeras, ouk an esōthē pasa sarx alla dia tous eklektous ous exelexato ekolobōse tas ēmeras.
mar|13|21|	kai tote ean tis umin eipē, idou ōde o christos, idou ekei, mē pisteuete.
mar|13|22|	egerthēsontai gar pseudochristoi kai pseudoprophētai kai dōsousi sēmeia kai terata pros to apoplanan, ei dunaton, kai tous eklektous.
mar|13|23|	umeis de blepete idou proeirēka umin apanta.
mar|13|24|	all en ekeinais tais ēmerais, meta tēn thlipsin ekeinēn o ēlios skotisthēsetai, kai ē selēnē ou dōsei to pheggos autēs,
mar|13|25|	kai oi asteres esontai ek tou ouranou piptontes, kai ai dunameis ai en tois ouranois saleuthēsontai.
mar|13|26|	kai tote opsontai ton uion tou anthrōpou erchomenon en nephelais meta dunameōs pollēs kai doxēs.
mar|13|27|	kai tote apostelei tous aggelous autou kai episunaxei tous eklektous autou ek tōn tessarōn anemōn, ap akrou tēs gēs eōs akrou tou ouranou.
mar|13|28|	apo de tēs sukēs mathete tēn parabolēn. otan autēs o klados ēdē genētai apalos kai ekphuē ta phulla, ginōskete oti eggus to theros estin
mar|13|29|	outō kai umeis, otan idēte tauta ginomena, ginōskete oti eggus estin epi thurais.
mar|13|30|	amēn legō umin oti ou mē parelthē ē genea autē mechris ou panta tauta genētai.
mar|13|31|	o ouranos kai ē gē pareleusontai, oi de emoi logoi ou mē pareleusontai.
mar|13|32|	peri de tēs ēmeras ekeinēs ē tēs ōras oudeis oiden, oude oi aggeloi en ouranō, oude o uios, ei mē o patēr.
mar|13|33|	blepete, agrupneite kai proseuchesthe ouk oidate gar pote o kairos estin.
mar|13|34|	ōs anthrōpos apodēmos, apheis tēn oikian autou, kai dous tois doulois autou tēn exousian, kai ekastō to ergon autou, kai tō thurōrō eneteilato ina grēgorē.
mar|13|35|	grēgoreite oun ouk oidate gar pote o kurios tēs oikias erchetai, opse ē mesonuktiou ē alektorophōnias ē prōi
mar|13|36|	mē elthōn exaiphnēs eurē umas katheudontas.
mar|13|37|	a de umin legō, pasi legō grēgoreite.
mar|14|1|	ēn de to pascha kai ta azuma meta duo ēmeras. kai ezētoun oi archiereis kai oi grammateis pōs auton en dolō kratēsantes apokteinōsin.
mar|14|2|	elegon de mē en tē eortē, mēpote thorubos estai tou laou.
mar|14|3|	kai ontos autou en bēthania en tē oikia simōnos tou leprou, katakeimenou autou ēlthe gunē echousa alabastron murou nardou pistikēs polutelous, kai suntripsasa to alabastron katecheen autou kata tēs kephalēs.
mar|14|4|	ēsan de tines aganaktountes pros eautous legontes eis ti ē apōleia autē tou murou gegonen?
mar|14|5|	ēdunato gar touto to muron prathēnai epanō triakosiōn dēnariōn kai dothēnai tois ptōchois kai enebrimōnto autē.
mar|14|6|	o de iēsous eipen aphete autēn ti autē kopous parechete? kalon ergon eirgasato en emoi.
mar|14|7|	pantote gar tous ptōchous echete meth eautōn, kai otan thelēte dunasthe autous eu poiēsai eme de ou pantote echete.
mar|14|8|	o eschen autē epoiēse proelabe murisai mou to sōma eis ton entaphiasmon.
mar|14|9|	amēn legō umin, opou ean kēruchthē to euaggelion touto eis olon ton kosmon, kai o epoiēsen autē lalēthēsetai eis mnēmosunon autēs.
mar|14|10|	kai ioudas o iskariōtēs, eis tōn dōdeka, apēlthe pros tous archiereis ina paradō auton autois.
mar|14|11|	oi de akousantes echarēsan, kai epēggeilanto autō arguria dounai kai ezētei pōs eukairōs auton paradō.
mar|14|12|	kai tē prōtē ēmera tōn azumōn, ote to pascha ethuon, legousin autō oi mathētai autou pou theleis apelthontes etoimasōmen ina phagēs to pascha?
mar|14|13|	kai apostellei duo tōn mathētōn autou kai legei autois upagete eis tēn polin, kai apantēsei umin anthrōpos keramion udatos bastazōn akolouthēsate autō,
mar|14|14|	kai opou ean eiselthē, eipate tō oikodespotē oti o didaskalos legei pou esti to kataluma mou opou to pascha meta tōn mathētōn mou phagō?
mar|14|15|	kai autos umin deixei anōgaion mega estrōmenon etoimon ekei etoimasate ēmin.
mar|14|16|	kai exēlthon oi mathētai autou kai ēlthon eis tēn polin, kai euron kathōs eipen autois, kai ētoimasan to pascha.
mar|14|17|	kai opsias genomenēs erchetai meta tōn dōdeka
mar|14|18|	kai anakeimenōn autōn kai esthiontōn eipen o iēsous amēn legō umin oti eis ex umōn paradōsei me, o esthiōn met emou.
mar|14|19|	oi de ērxanto lupeisthai kai legein autō eis kath eis mēti egō? kai allos mēti egō?
mar|14|20|	o de apokritheis eipen autois eis ek tōn dōdeka, o embaptomenos met emou eis to trublion.
mar|14|21|	o men uios tou anthrōpou upagei kathōs gegraptai peri autou ouai de tō anthrōpō ekeinō, di ou o uios tou anthrōpou paradidotai kalon ēn autō ei ouk egennēthē o anthrōpos ekeinos.
mar|14|22|	kai esthiontōn autōn labōn o iēsous arton eulogēsas eklase kai edōken autois kai eipe labete phagete touto esti to sōma mou.
mar|14|23|	kai labōn to potērion eucharistēsas edōken autois, kai epion ex autou pantes.
mar|14|24|	kai eipen autois touto esti to aima mou to tēs kainēs diathēkēs to peri pollōn ekchunomenon.
mar|14|25|	amēn legō umin oti ouketi ou mē piō ek tou gennēmatos tēs ampelou eōs tēs ēmeras ekeinēs otan auto pinō kainon en tē basileia tou theou.
mar|14|26|	kai umnēsantes exēlthon eis to oros tōn elaiōn.
mar|14|27|	kai legei autois o iēsous oti pantes skandalisthēsesthe en emoi en tē nukti tautē oti gegraptai, pataxō ton poimena kai diaskorpisthēsontai ta probata
mar|14|28|	alla meta to egerthēnai me proaxō umas eis tēn galilaian.
mar|14|29|	o de petros ephē autō kai ei pantes skandalisthēsontai, all ouk egō.
mar|14|30|	kai legei autō o iēsous amēn legō soi oti su sēmeron en tē nukti tautē prin ē dis alektora phōnēsai tris aparnēsē me.

mar|14|35|	kai proelthōn mikron epesen epi prosōpon epi tēs gēs, kai prosēucheto ina, ei dunaton esti, parelthē ap autou ē ōra,
mar|14|36|	kai elegen abba o patēr, panta dunata soi parenegke to potērion ap emou touto all ou ti egō thelō, all ei ti su.
mar|14|37|	kai erchetai kai euriskei autous katheudontas, kai legei tō petrō simōn, katheudeis? ouk ischusate mian ōran grēgorēsai?
mar|14|38|	grēgoreite kai proseuchesthe, ina mē eiselthēte eis peirasmon to men pneuma prothumon, ē de sarx asthenēs.
mar|14|39|	kai palin apelthōn prosēuxato ton auton logon eipōn.

mar|14|41|	kai erchetai to triton kai legei autois katheudete loipon kai anapauesthe! apechei ēlthen ē ōra idou paradidotai o uios tou anthrōpou eis tas cheiras tōn amartōlōn
mar|14|42|	egeiresthe, agōmen idou o paradidous me ēggike.
mar|14|43|	kai eutheōs, eti autou lalountos, paraginetai ioudas o iskariōtēs, eis tōn dōdeka, kai met autou ochlos polus meta machairōn kai xulōn, apestalmenoi para tōn archiereōn kai grammateōn kai tōn presbuterōn.
mar|14|44|	dedōkei de o paradidous auton sussēmon autois legōn on an philēsō, autos esti kratēsate auton kai apagagete asphalōs.
mar|14|45|	kai elthōn eutheōs proselthōn autō legei chaire, rabbi, kai katephilēsen auton.

mar|14|47|	eis de tis tōn parestēkotōn spasamenos tēn machairan epaise ton doulon tou archiereōs kai apheilen autou to ōtion.
mar|14|48|	kai apokritheis o iēsous eipen autois ōs epi lēstēn exēlthete meta machairōn kai xulōn sullabein me
mar|14|49|	kath ēmeran pros umas ēmēn en tō ierō didaskōn, kai ouk ekratēsate me. all ina plērōthōsin ai graphai.
mar|14|50|	kai aphentes auton ephugon pantes.
mar|14|51|	kai eis tis neaniskos ēkolouthēsen autō, peribeblēmenos sindona epi gumnou kai kratousin auton oi neaniskoi.
mar|14|52|	o de katalipōn tēn sindona gumnos ephugen ap autōn.
mar|14|53|	kai apēgagon ton iēsoun pros ton archierea kai sunerchontai autō pantes oi archiereis kai oi presbuteroi kai oi grammateis.
mar|14|54|	kai o petros apo makrothen ēkolouthēsen autō eōs esō eis tēn aulēn tou archiereōs, kai ēn sugkathēmenos meta tōn upēretōn kai thermainomenos pros to phōs.
mar|14|55|	oi de archiereis kai olon to sunedrion ezētoun kata tou iēsou marturian eis to thanatōsai auton, kai ouch euriskon
mar|14|56|	polloi gar epseudomarturoun kat autou, kai isai ai marturiai ouk ēsan.
mar|14|57|	kai tines anastantes epseudomarturoun kat autou legontes

mar|14|59|	kai oude outōs isē ēn ē marturia autōn.

mar|14|62|	o de iēsous eipen egō eimi kai opsesthe ton uion tou anthrōpou ek dexiōn kathēmenon tēs dunameōs kai erchomenon epi tōn nephelōn tou ouranou.
mar|14|63|	o de archiereus diarrēxas tous chitōnas autou legei ti eti chreian echomen marturōn?
mar|14|64|	ēkousate pantōs tēs blasphēmias ti umin phainetai? oi de pantes katekrinan auton einai enochon thanatou.
mar|14|65|	kai ērxanto tines emptuein autō kai perikaluptein to prosōpon autou kai kolaphizein auton kai legein autō prophēteuson ēmin tis estin o paisas se. kai oi upēretai rapismasin auton ebalon.
mar|14|66|	kai ontos tou petrou katō en tē aulē erchetai mia tōn paidiskōn tou archiereōs,

mar|14|70|	o de palin ērneito. kai meta mikron palin oi parestōtes elegon tō petrō alēthōs ex autōn ei kai gar galilaios ei kai ē lalia sou omoiazei.
mar|14|71|	o de ērxato anathematizein kai omnunai oti ouk oida ton anthrōpon touton on legete. kai ek deuterou alektōr ephōnēse.

mar|15|1|	kai eutheōs epi to prōi sumboulion poiēsantes oi archiereis meta tōn presbuterōn kai grammateōn kai olon to sunedrion, dēsantes ton iēsoun apēnegkan kai paredōkan tō pilatō.
mar|15|2|	kai epērōtēsen auton o pilatos su ei o basileus tōn ioudaiōn? o de apokritheis eipen autō su legeis.
mar|15|3|	kai katēgoroun autou oi archiereis polla, autos de ouden apekrinato.
mar|15|4|	o de pilatos palin epērōta auton legōn ouk apokrinē ouden? ide posa sou katamarturousin.
mar|15|5|	o de iēsous ouketi ouden apekrithē, ōste thaumazein ton pilaton.
mar|15|6|	kata de eortēn apeluen autois ena desmion, onper ētounto.
mar|15|7|	ēn de o legomenos barabbas meta tōn sustasiastōn dedemenos, oitines en tē stasei phonon pepoiēkeisan.
mar|15|8|	kai anaboēsas o ochlos ērxato aiteisthai kathōs aei epoiei autois.
mar|15|9|	o de pilatos apekrithē autois legōn thelete apolusō umin ton basilea tōn ioudaiōn?
mar|15|10|	eginōske gar oti dia phthonon paradedōkeisan auton oi archiereis.
mar|15|11|	oi de archiereis aneseisan ton ochlon ina mallon ton barabban apolusē autois.
mar|15|12|	o de pilatos apokritheis palin eipen autois ti oun thelete poiēsō on legete ton basilea tōn ioudaiōn?
mar|15|13|	oi de palin ekraxan staurōson auton.
mar|15|14|	o de pilatos elegen autois ti gar epoiēse kakon? oi de perissoterōs ekraxan staurōson auton.
mar|15|15|	o de pilatos boulomenos tō ochlō to ikanon poiēsai, apelusen autois ton barabban, kai paredōke ton iēsoun phragellōsas ina staurōthē.
mar|15|16|	oi de stratiōtai apēgagon auton esō tēs aulēs, o esti praitōrion, kai sugkalousin olēn tēn speiran
mar|15|17|	kai enduousin auton porphuran kai perititheasin autō plexantes akanthinon stephanon,
mar|15|18|	kai ērxanto aspazesthai auton. chaire o basileus tōn ioudaiōn
mar|15|19|	kai etupton autou tēn kephalēn kalamō kai eneptuon autō, kai tithentes ta gonata prosekunoun autō.
mar|15|20|	kai ote enepaixan autō, exedusan auton tēn porphuran kai enedusan auton ta imatia ta idia, kai exagousin auton ina staurōsōsin auton.
mar|15|21|	kai aggareuousi paragonta tina simōna kurēnaion, erchomenon ap agrou, ton patera alexandrou kai rouphou, ina arē ton stauron autou.
mar|15|22|	kai pherousin auton epi golgotha topon, o esti methermēneuomenon kraniou topos.
mar|15|23|	kai edidoun autō piein esmurnismenon oinon o de ouk elabe.
mar|15|24|	kai staurōsantes auton diamerizontai ta imatia autou ballontes klēron ep auta tis ti arē.
mar|15|25|	ēn de ōra tritē kai estaurōsan auton.
mar|15|26|	kai ēn ē epigraphē tēs aitias autou epigegrammenē o basileus tōn ioudaiōn.
mar|15|27|	kai sun autō staurousi duo lēstas, ena ek dexiōn kai ena ex euōnumōn autou.
mar|15|28|	kai eplērōthē ē graphē ē legousa kai meta anomōn elogisthē.
mar|15|29|	kai oi paraporeuomenoi eblasphēmoun auton kinountes tas kephalas autōn kai legontes oua, o kataluōn ton naon kai en trisin ēmerais oikodomōn!
mar|15|30|	sōson seauton kai kataba apo tou staurou.
mar|15|31|	omoiōs de kai oi archiereis empaizontes pros allēlous meta tōn grammateōn elegon allous esōsen, eauton ou dunatai sōsai.
mar|15|32|	o christos o basileus tou israēl katabatō nun apo tou staurou, ina idōmen kai pisteusōmen autō. kai oi sunestaurōmenoi autō ōneidizon auton.
mar|15|33|	genomenēs de ōras ektēs skotos egeneto eph olēn tēn gēn eōs ōras enatēs
mar|15|34|	kai tē ōra tē enatē eboēsen o iēsous phōnē megalē legōn elōi elōi, lima sabachthani? o esti methermēneuomenon, o theos mou o theos mou, eis ti me egkatelipes?
mar|15|35|	kai tines tōn parestēkotōn akousantes elegon ide ēlian phōnei.
mar|15|36|	dramōn de eis kai gemisas spoggon oxous peritheis te kalamō epotizen auton legōn aphete idōmen ei erchetai ēlias kathelein auton.
mar|15|37|	o de iēsous apheis phōnēn megalēn exepneuse.
mar|15|38|	kai to katapetasma tou naou eschisthē eis duo apo anōthen eōs katō.
mar|15|39|	idōn de o kenturiōn o parestēkōs ex enantias autou oti outō kraxas exepneusen, eipen alēthōs o anthrōpos outos uios ēn theou.
mar|15|40|	ēsan de kai gunaikes apo makrothen theōrousai, en ais ēn kai maria ē magdalēnē kai maria ē tou iakōbou tou mikrou kai iōsē mētēr, kai salōmē,
mar|15|41|	ai kai ote ēn en tē galilaia ēkolouthoun autō kai diēkonoun autō, kai allai pollai ai sunanabasai autō eis ierosoluma.
mar|15|42|	kai ēdē opsias genomenēs, epei ēn paraskeuē, o esti prosabbaton,
mar|15|43|	elthōn iōsēph o apo arimathaias, euschēmōn bouleutēs, os kai autos ēn prosdechomenos tēn basileian tou theou, tolmēsas eisēlthe pros pilaton kai ētēsato to sōma tou iēsou.
mar|15|44|	o de pilatos ethaumasen ei ēdē tethnēke, kai proskalesamenos ton kenturiōna epērōtēsen auton ei palai apethane
mar|15|45|	kai gnous apo tou kenturiōnos edōrēsato to sōma tō iōsēph.
mar|15|46|	kai agorasas sindona kai kathelōn auton eneilēse tē sindoni kai katethēken auton en mnēmeiō, o ēn lelatomēmenon ek petras, kai prosekulise lithon epi tēn thuran tou mnēmeiou.
mar|15|47|	ē de maria ē magdalēnē kai maria iōsē etheōroun pou tithetai.
mar|16|1|	kai diagenomenou tou sabbatou maria ē magdalēnē kai maria ē tou iakōbou kai salōmē ēgorasan arōmata ina elthousai aleipsōsin auton.
mar|16|2|	kai lian prōi tēs mias sabbatōn erchontai epi to mnēmeion, anateilantos tou ēliou.
mar|16|3|	kai elegon pros eautas tis apokulisei ēmin ton lithon ek tēs thuras tou mnēmeiou?
mar|16|4|	kai anablepsasai theōrousin oti apokekulistai o lithos ēn gar megas sphodra.
mar|16|5|	kai eiselthousai eis to mnēmeion eidon neaniskon kathēmenon en tois dexiois, peribeblēmenon stolēn leukēn, kai exethambēthēsan.
mar|16|6|	o de legei autais mē ekthambeisthe iēsoun zēteite ton nazarēnon ton estaurōmenon ēgerthē, ouk estin ōde ide o topos opou ethēkan auton.
mar|16|7|	all upagete eipate tois mathētais autou kai tō petrō oti proagei umas eis tēn galilaian ekei auton opsesthe, kathōs eipen umin.
mar|16|8|	kai exelthousai ephugon apo tou mnēmeiou eiche de autas tromos kai ekstasis, kai oudeni ouden eipon ephobounto gar.
mar|16|9|	anastas de prōi prōtē sabbatou ephanē prōton maria tē magdalēnē, aph ēs ekbeblēkei epta daimonia.
mar|16|10|	ekeinē poreutheisa apēggeile tois met autou genomenois, penthousi kai klaiousi.
mar|16|11|	kakeinoi akousantes oti zē kai etheathē up autēs, ēpistēsan.
mar|16|12|	meta de tauta dusin ex autōn peripatousin ephanerōthē en etera morphē, poreuomenois eis agron.
mar|16|13|	kakeinoi apelthontes apēggeilan tois loipois oude ekeinois episteusan.
mar|16|14|	usteron anakeimenois autois tois endeka ephanerōthē, kai ōneidise tēn apistian autōn kai sklērokardian, oti tois theasamenois auton egēgermenon ouk episteusan.
mar|16|15|	kai eipen autois poreuthentes eis ton kosmon apanta kēruxate to euaggelion pasē tē ktisei.
mar|16|16|	o pisteusas kai baptistheis sōthēsetai, o de apistēsas katakrithēsetai.
mar|16|17|	sēmeia de tois pisteusasi tauta parakolouthēsei en tō onomati mou daimonia ekbalousi glōssais lalēsousi kainais
mar|16|18|	opheis arousi kan thanasimon ti piōsin, ou mē autous blapsei epi arrōstous cheiras epithēsousi, kai kalōs exousin.
mar|16|19|	o men oun kurios meta to lalēsai autois anelēphthē eis ton ouranon kai ekathisen ek dexiōn tou theou.
mar|16|20|	ekeinoi de exelthontes ekēruxan pantachou, tou kuriou sunergountos kai ton logon bebaiountos dia tōn epakolouthountōn sēmeiōn. amēn.
luk|1|1|	epeidēper polloi epecheirēsan anataxasthai diēgēsin peri tōn peplērophorēmenōn en ēmin pragmatōn
luk|1|2|	kathōs paredosan ēmin oi ap archēs autoptai kai upēretai genomenoi tou logou,

luk|1|5|	egeneto en tais ēmerais ērōdou tou basileōs tēs ioudaias iereus tis onomati zacharias ex ephēmerias abia, kai ē gunē autou ek tōn thugaterōn aarōn, kai to onoma autēs elisabet.
luk|1|6|	ēsan de dikaioi amphoteroi enōpion tou theou, poreuomenoi en pasais tais entolais kai dikaiōmasi tou kuriou amemptoi.

luk|1|18|	kai eipe zacharias pros ton aggelon kata ti gnōsomai touto? egō gar eimi presbutēs kai ē gunē mou probebēkuia en tais ēmerais autēs.
luk|1|19|	kai apokritheis o aggelos eipen autō egō eimi gabriēl o parestēkōs enōpion tou theou, kai apestalēn lalēsai pros se kai euaggelisasthai soi tauta.
luk|1|20|	kai idou esē siōpōn kai mē dunamenos lalēsai achri ēs ēmeras genētai tauta, anth ōn ouk episteusas tois logois mou, oitines plērōthēsontai eis ton kairon autōn.
luk|1|21|	kai ēn o laos prosdokōn ton zacharian, kai ethaumazon en tō chronizein auton en tō naō.

luk|1|23|	kai egeneto ōs eplēsthēsan ai ēmerai tēs leitourgias autou, apēlthen eis ton oikon autou.

luk|1|36|	kai idou elisabet ē suggenēs sou kai autē suneilēphuia uion en gērei autēs, kai outos mēn ektos estin autē tē kaloumenē steira

luk|2|5|	apograpsasthai sun mariam tē memnēsteumenē autō gunaiki, ousē egkuō.

luk|2|14|	doxa en upsistois theō kai epi gēs eirēnē, en anthrōpois eudokia.
luk|2|15|	kai egeneto ōs apēlthon ap autōn eis ton ouranon oi aggeloi, kai oi anthrōpoi oi poimenes eipon pros allēlous dielthōmen dē eōs bēthleem kai idōmen to rēma touto to gegonos, o o kurios egnōrisen ēmin.

luk|2|18|	kai pantes oi akousantes ethaumasan peri tōn lalēthentōn upo tōn poimenōn pros autous.

luk|2|20|	kai upestrepsan oi poimenes doxazontes kai ainountes ton theon epi pasin ois ēkousan kai eidon kathōs elalēthē pros autous.
luk|2|21|	kai ote eplēsthēsan ēmerai oktō tou peritemein to paidion, kai eklēthē to onoma autou iēsous, to klēthen upo tou aggelou pro tou sullēphthēnai auton en tē koilia.
luk|2|22|	kai ote eplēsthēsan ai ēmerai tou katharismou autōn kata ton nomon mōuseōs, anēgagon auton eis ierosoluma parastēsai tō kuriō,
luk|2|23|	kathōs gegraptai en nomō kuriou oti pan arsen dianoigon mētran agion tō kuriō klēthēsetai,

luk|2|26|	kai ēn autō kechrēmatismenon upo tou pneumatos tou agiou mē idein thanaton prin ē idē ton christon kuriou.

luk|2|28|	kai autos edexato auton eis tas agkalas autou kai eulogēse ton theon kai eipe

luk|2|33|	kai ēn iōsēph kai ē mētēr autou thaumazontes epi tois laloumenois peri autou.
luk|2|34|	kai eulogēsen autous sumeōn kai eipe pros mariam tēn mētera autou idou outos keitai eis ptōsin kai anastasin pollōn en tō israēl kai eis sēmeion antilegomenon.
luk|2|35|	kai sou de autēs tēn psuchēn dieleusetai romphaia, opōs an apokaluphthōsin ek pollōn kardiōn dialogismoi.
luk|2|36|	kai ēn anna prophētis, thugatēr phanouēl, ek phulēs asēr autē probebēkuia en ēmerais pollais, zēsasa etē meta andros epta apo tēs parthenias autēs,
luk|2|37|	kai autē chēra ōs etōn ogdoēkonta tessarōn, ē ouk aphistato apo tou ierou nēsteiais kai deēsesi latreuousa nukta kai ēmeran
luk|2|38|	kai autē autē tē ōra epistasa anthōmologeito tō kuriō kai elalei peri autou pasi tois prosdechomenois lutrōsin en ierousalēm.
luk|2|39|	kai ōs etelesan apanta ta kata ton nomon kuriou, upestrepsan eis tēn galilaian eis tēn polin eautōn nazaret.
luk|2|40|	to de paidion ēuxane kai ekrataiouto pneumati plēroumenon sophias, kai charis theou ēn ep auto.
luk|2|41|	kai eporeuonto oi goneis autou kat etos eis ierousalēm tē eortē tou pascha.
luk|2|42|	kai ote egeneto etōn dōdeka, anabantōn autōn eis ierosoluma kata to ethos tēs eortēs
luk|2|43|	kai teleiōsantōn tas ēmeras, en tō upostrephein autous upemeinen iēsous o pais en ierousalēm, kai ouk egnō iōsēph kai ē mētēr autou.
luk|2|44|	nomisantes de auton en tē sunodia einai ēlthon ēmeras odon kai anezētoun auton en tois suggenesi kai en tois gnōstois
luk|2|45|	kai mē eurontes auton upestrepsan eis ierousalēm zētountes auton.
luk|2|46|	kai egeneto meth ēmeras treis euron auton en tō ierō kathezomenon en mesō tōn didaskalōn kai akouonta autōn kai eperōtōnta autous
luk|2|47|	existanto de pantes oi akouontes autou epi tē sunesei kai tais apokrisesin autou.
luk|2|48|	kai idontes auton exeplagēsan, kai pros auton ē mētēr autou eipe teknon, ti epoiēsas ēmin outōs? idou o patēr sou kagō odunōmenoi ezētoumen se.
luk|2|49|	kai eipe pros autous ti oti ezēteite me? ouk ēdeite oti en tois tou patros mou dei einai me?
luk|2|50|	kai autoi ou sunēkan to rēma o elalēsen autois.
luk|2|51|	kai katebē met autōn kai ēlthen eis nazaret, kai ēn upotassomenos autois. kai ē mētēr autou dietērei panta ta rēmata tauta en tē kardia autēs.
luk|2|52|	kai iēsous proekopte sophia kai ēlikia kai chariti para theō kai anthrōpois.
luk|3|1|	en etei de pentekaidekatō tēs ēgemonias tiberiou kaisaros, ēgemoneuontos pontiou pilatou tēs ioudaias, kai tetrarchountos tēs galilaias ērōdou, philippou de tou adelphou autou tetrarchountos tēs itouraias kai trachōnitidos chōras, kai lusaniou tēs abilēnēs tetrarchountos,
luk|3|2|	ep archiereōs anna kai kaiapha, egeneto rēma theou epi iōannēn ton zachariou uion en tē erēmō,
luk|3|3|	kai ēlthen eis pasan tēn perichōron tou iordanou kērussōn baptisma metanoias eis aphesin amartiōn,
luk|3|4|	ōs gegraptai en biblō logōn ēsaiou tou prophētou legontos phōnē boōntos en tē erēmō, etoimasate tēn odon kuriou, eutheias poieite tas tribous autou
luk|3|5|	pasa pharagx plērōthēsetai kai pan oros kai bounos tapeinōthēsetai, kai estai ta skolia eis eutheian kai ai tracheiai eis odous leias,
luk|3|6|	kai opsetai pasa sarx to sōtērion tou theou.
luk|3|7|	elegen oun tois ekporeuomenois ochlois baptisthēnai up autou gennēmata echidnōn, tis upedeixen umin phugein apo tēs mellousēs orgēs?
luk|3|8|	poiēsate oun karpous axious tēs metanoias, kai mē arxēsthe legein en eautois, patera echomen ton abraam legō gar umin oti dunatai o theos ek tōn lithōn toutōn egeirai tekna tō abraam.
luk|3|9|	ēdē de kai ē axinē pros tēn rizan tōn dendrōn keitai pan oun dendron mē poioun karpon kalon ekkoptetai kai eis pur balletai.
luk|3|10|	kai epērōtōn auton oi ochloi legontes ti oun poiēsomen?
luk|3|11|	apokritheis de legei autois o echōn duo chitōnas metadotō tō mē echonti, kai o echōn brōmata omoiōs poieitō.
luk|3|12|	ēlthon de kai telōnai baptisthēnai, kai eipon pros auton didaskale, ti poiēsomen?
luk|3|13|	o de eipe pros autous mēden pleon para to diatetagmenon umin prassete.
luk|3|14|	epērōtōn de auton kai strateuomenoi legontes kai ēmeis ti poiēsomen? kai eipe pros autous mēdena sukophantēsēte mēde diaseisēte, kai arkeisthe tois opsōniois umōn.
luk|3|15|	prosdokōntos de tou laou kai dialogizomenōn pantōn en tais kardiais autōn peri tou iōannou, mēpote autos eiē o christos,
luk|3|16|	apekrinato o iōannēs apasi legōn egō men udati baptizō umas erchetai de o ischuroteros mou, ou ouk eimi ikanos lusai ton imanta tōn upodēmatōn autou autos umas baptisei en pneumati agiō kai puri.
luk|3|17|	ou to ptuon en tē cheiri autou kai diakathariei tēn alōna autou, kai sunaxei ton siton eis tēn apothēkēn autou, to de achuron katakausei puri asbestō.
luk|3|18|	polla men oun kai etera parakalōn euēggelizeto ton laon.
luk|3|19|	o de ērōdēs o tetrarchēs, elegchomenos up autou peri ērōdiados tēs gunaikos tou adelphou autou kai peri pantōn ōn epoiēse ponērōn o ērōdēs,
luk|3|20|	prosethēke kai touto epi pasi kai katekleise ton iōannēn en tē phulakē.
luk|3|21|	egeneto de en tō baptisthēnai apanta ton laon kai iēsou baptisthentos kai proseuchomenou aneōchthēnai ton ouranon
luk|3|22|	kai katabēnai to pneuma to agion sōmatikō eidei ōsei peristeran ep auton, kai phōnēn ex ouranou genesthai legousan su ei o uios mou o agapētos, en soi eudokēsa.
luk|3|23|	kai autos ēn o iēsous ōsei etōn triakonta archomenos, ōn, ōs enomizeto, uios iōsēph, tou ēli,
luk|3|24|	tou matthan, tou leui, tou melchi, tou iōanna, tou iōsēph,
luk|3|25|	tou mattathiou, tou amōs, tou naoum, tou eslim, tou naggai,
luk|3|26|	tou maath, tou mattathiou, tou semeu, tou iōsēch, tou iōda,
luk|3|27|	tou iōannan, tou rēsa, tou zorobabel, tou salathiēl, tou nēri,
luk|3|28|	tou melchi, tou addi, tou kōsam, tou elmōdam, tou ēr,
luk|3|29|	tou iōsē, tou eliezer, tou iōreim, tou matthat, tou leui,
luk|3|30|	tou sumeōn, tou iouda, tou iōsēph, tou iōna, tou eliakeim,
luk|3|31|	tou melea, tou mainan, tou mattatha, tou nathan, tou dauid,
luk|3|32|	tou iessai, tou ōbēd, tou booz, tou salmōn, tou naassōn,
luk|3|33|	tou aminadab, tou aram, tou iōram, tou esrōm, tou phares, tou iouda,
luk|3|34|	tou iakōb, tou isaak, tou abraam, tou thara, tou nachōr,
luk|3|35|	tou serouch, tou ragau, tou phalek, tou eber, tou sala,
luk|3|36|	tou kainan, tou arphaxad, tou sēm, tou nōe, tou lamech,
