luk|4|1|	iēsous de plērēs pneumatos agiou upestrepsen apo tou iordanou, kai ēgeto en tō pneumati eis tēn erēmon
luk|4|2|	ēmeras tessarakonta peirazomenos upo tou diabolou, kai ouk ephagen ouden en tais ēmerais ekeinais kai suntelestheisōn autōn usteron epeinase.
luk|4|3|	kai eipen autō o diabolos ei uios ei tou theou, eipe tō lithō toutō ina genētai artos.
luk|4|4|	kai apekrithē o iēsous pros auton legōn gegraptai oti ouk ep artō monō zēsetai anthrōpos, all epi panti rēmati ekporeuomenō dia stomatos theou.
luk|4|5|	kai anagagōn auton o diabolos eis oros upsēlon edeixen autō pasas tas basileias tēs oikoumenēs en stigmē chronou,
luk|4|6|	kai eipen autō o diabolos soi dōsō tēn exousian tautēn apasan kai tēn doxan autōn, oti emoi paradedotai, kai ō ean thelō didōmi autēn.
luk|4|7|	su oun ean proskunēsēs enōpion mou, estai sou pasa.
luk|4|8|	kai apokritheis autō eipen o iēsous upage opisō mou, satana gegraptai gar, kurion ton theon sou proskunēseis kai autō monō latreuseis.
luk|4|9|	kai ēgagen auton eis ierosoluma, kai estēsen auton epi to pterugion tou ierou kai eipen autō ei uios ei tou theou, bale seauton enteuthen katō
luk|4|10|	gegraptai gar oti tois aggelois autou enteleitai peri sou tou diaphulaxai se,
luk|4|11|	kai oti epi cheirōn arousi se, mēpote proskopsēs pros lithon ton poda sou.
luk|4|12|	kai apokritheis eipen autō o iēsous oti eirētai, ouk ekpeiraseis kurion ton theon sou.
luk|4|13|	kai suntelesas panta peirasmon o diabolos apestē ap autou achri kairou.
luk|4|14|	kai upestrepsen o iēsous en tē dunamei tou pneumatos eis tēn galilaian kai phēmē exēlthe kath olēs tēs perichōrou peri autou.
luk|4|15|	kai autos edidasken en tais sunagōgais autōn doxazomenos upo pantōn.
luk|4|16|	kai ēlthen eis tēn nazaret, ou ēn tethrammenos, kai eisēlthe kata to eiōthos autō en tē ēmera tōn sabbatōn eis tēn sunagōgēn, kai anestē anagnōnai.
luk|4|17|	kai epedothē autō biblion ēsaiou tou prophētou, kai anaptuxas to biblion eure ton topon ou ēn gegrammenon
luk|4|18|	pneuma kuriou ep eme, ou eineken echrise me, euaggelisasthai ptōchois apestalke me, iasasthai tous suntetrimmenous tēn kardian,
luk|4|19|	kēruxai aichmalōtois aphesin kai tuphlois anablepsin, aposteilai tethrausmenous en aphesei, kēruxai eniauton kuriou dekton.
luk|4|20|	kai ptuxas to biblion apodous tō upēretē ekathise kai pantōn en tē sunagōgē oi ophthalmoi ēsan atenizontes autō.
luk|4|21|	ērxato de legein pros autous oti sēmeron peplērōtai ē graphē autē en tois ōsin umōn.
luk|4|22|	kai pantes emarturoun autō kai ethaumazon epi tois logois tēs charitos tois ekporeuomenois ek tou stomatos autou kai elegon ouch outos estin o uios iōsēph?
luk|4|23|	kai eipe pros autous pantōs ereite moi tēn parabolēn tautēn iatre, therapeuson seauton osa ēkousamen genomena en tē kapernaoum, poiēson kai ōde en tē patridi sou.
luk|4|24|	eipe de amēn legō umin oti oudeis prophētēs dektos estin en tē patridi autou.
luk|4|25|	ep alētheias de legō umin, pollai chērai ēsan en tais ēmerais ēliou en tō israēl, ote ekleisthē o ouranos epi etē tria kai mēnas ex, ōs egeneto limos megas epi pasan tēn gēn,
luk|4|26|	kai pros oudemian autōn epemphthē ēlias ei mē eis sarepta tēs sidōnias pros gunaika chēran.
luk|4|27|	kai polloi leproi ēsan epi elisaiou tou prophētou en tō israēl, kai oudeis autōn ekatharisthē ei mē neeman o suros.
luk|4|28|	kai eplēsthēsan pantes thumou en tē sunagōgē akouontes tauta,
luk|4|29|	kai anastantes exebalon auton exō tēs poleōs kai ēgagon auton eōs ophruos tou orous, eph ou ē polis autōn ōkodomēto, eis to katakrēmnisai auton.
luk|4|30|	autos de dielthōn dia mesou autōn eporeueto.
luk|4|31|	kai katēlthen eis kapernaoum polin tēs galilaias, kai ēn didaskōn autous en tois sabbasi
luk|4|32|	kai exeplēssonto epi tē didachē autou, oti en exousia ēn o logos autou.
luk|4|33|	kai en tē sunagōgē ēn anthrōpos echōn pneuma daimoniou akathartou, kai anekraxe phōnē megalē
luk|4|34|	legōn ea, ti ēmin kai soi, iēsou nazarēne? ēlthes apolesai ēmas? oida se tis ei, o agios tou theou.
luk|4|35|	kai epetimēsen autō o iēsous legōn phimōthēti kai exelthe ex autou. kai ripsan auton to daimonion eis to meson exēlthen ap autou, mēden blapsan auton.
luk|4|36|	kai egeneto thambos epi pantas, kai sunelaloun pros allēlous legontes tis o logos outos, oti en exousia kai dunamei epitassei tois akathartois pneumasi, kai exerchontai?
luk|4|37|	kai exeporeueto ēchos peri autou eis panta topon tēs perichōrou.
luk|4|38|	anastas de ek tēs sunagōgēs eisēlthen eis tēn oikian simōnos. penthera de tou simōnos ēn sunechomenē puretō megalō, kai ērōtēsan auton peri autēs.
luk|4|39|	kai epistas epanō autēs epetimēse tō puretō, kai aphēken autēn parachrēma de anastasa diēkonei autois.
luk|4|40|	dunontos de tou ēliou pantes osoi eichon asthenountas nosois poikilais ēgagon autous pros auton o de eni ekastō autōn tas cheiras epititheis etherapeusen autous.
luk|4|41|	exērcheto de kai daimonia apo pollōn kraugazonta kai legonta oti su ei o christos o uios tou theou. kai epitimōn ouk eia auta lalein, oti ēdeisan ton christon auton einai.
luk|4|42|	genomenēs de ēmeras exelthōn eporeuthē eis erēmon topon kai oi ochloi epezētoun auton, kai ēlthon eōs autou kai kateichon auton tou mē poreuesthai ap autōn.
luk|4|43|	o de eipe pros autous oti kai tais eterais polesin euaggelisasthai me dei tēn basileian tou theou oti eis touto apestalmai.
luk|4|44|	kai ēn kērussōn eis tas sunagōgas tēs galilaias.
luk|5|1|	egeneto de en tō ton ochlon epikeisthai autō tou akouein ton logon tou theou kai autos ēn estōs para tēn limnēn gennēsaret,
luk|5|2|	kai eide duo ploia estōta para tēn limnēn oi de alieis apobantes ap autōn apeplunan ta diktua.
luk|5|3|	embas de eis en tōn ploiōn, o ēn tou simōnos, ērōtēsen auton apo tēs gēs epanagagein oligon kai kathisas edidasken ek tou ploiou tous ochlous.
luk|5|4|	ōs de epausato lalōn, eipe pros ton simōna epanagage eis to bathos kai chalasate ta diktua umōn eis agran.
luk|5|5|	kai apokritheis o simōn eipen autō epistata, di olēs tēs nuktos kopiasantes ouden elabomen epi de tō rēmati sou chalasō to diktuon.
luk|5|6|	kai touto poiēsantes sunekleisan plēthos ichthuōn polu dierrēgnuto de to diktuon autōn.
luk|5|7|	kai kateneusan tois metochois tois en tō eterō ploiō tou elthontas sullabesthai autois kai ēlthon kai eplēsan amphotera ta ploia, ōste buthizesthai auta.
luk|5|8|	idōn de simōn petros prosepese tois gonasin iēsou legōn exelthe ap emou, oti anēr amartōlos eimi, kurie
luk|5|9|	thambos gar perieschen auton kai pantas tous sun autō epi tē agra tōn ichthuōn ē sunelabon,
luk|5|10|	omoiōs de kai iakōbon kai iōannēn, uious zebedaiou, oi ēsan koinōnoi tō simōni. kai eipe pros ton simōna o iēsous mē phobou apo tou nun anthrōpous esē zōgrōn.
luk|5|11|	kai katagagontes ta ploia epi tēn gēn, aphentes apanta ēkolouthēsan autō.
luk|5|12|	kai egeneto en tō einai auton en mia tōn poleōn kai idou anēr plērēs lepras kai idōn ton iēsoun, pesōn epi prosōpon edeēthē autou legōn kurie, ean thelēs, dunasai me katharisai.
luk|5|13|	kai ekteinas tēn cheira ēpsato autou eipōn thelō, katharisthēti. kai eutheōs ē lepra apēlthen ap autou.
luk|5|14|	kai autos parēggeilen autō mēdeni eipein, alla apelthōn deixon seauton tō ierei kai prosenegke peri tou katharismou sou kathōs prosetaxe mōusēs eis marturion autois.
luk|5|15|	diērcheto de mallon o logos peri autou, kai sunērchonto ochloi polloi akouein kai therapeuesthai up autou apo tōn astheneiōn autōn
luk|5|16|	autos de ēn upochōrōn en tais erēmois kai proseuchomenos.
luk|5|17|	kai egeneto en mia tōn ēmerōn kai autos ēn didaskōn, kai ēsan kathēmenoi pharisaioi kai nomodidaskaloi oi ēsan elēluthotes ek pasēs kōmēs tēs galilaias kai ioudaias kai ierousalēm kai dunamis kuriou ēn eis to iasthai autous.
luk|5|18|	kai idou andres pherontes epi klinēs anthrōpon os ēn paralelumenos, kai ezētoun auton eisenegkein kai theinai enōpion autou.
luk|5|19|	kai mē eurontes poias eisenegkōsin auton dia ton ochlon, anabantes epi to dōma dia tōn keramōn kathēkan auton sun tō klinidiō eis to meson emprosthen tou iēsou.
luk|5|20|	kai idōn tēn pistin autōn eipen autō anthrōpe, apheōntai soi ai amartiai sou.
luk|5|21|	kai ērxanto dialogizesthai oi grammateis kai oi pharisaioi legontes tis estin outos os lalei blasphēmias? tis dunatai aphienai amartias ei mē monos o theos?
luk|5|22|	epignous de o iēsous tous dialogismous autōn apokritheis eipe pros autous ti dialogizesthe en tais kardiais umōn?
luk|5|23|	ti estin eukopōteron, eipein, apheōntai soi ai amartiai sou, ē eipein, egeire kai peripatei?
luk|5|24|	ina de eidēte oti exousian echei o uios tou anthrōpou epi tēs gēs aphienai amartias—eipe tō paralelumenō soi legō, egeire kai aras to klinidion sou poreuou eis ton oikon sou.
luk|5|25|	kai parachrēma anastas enōpion autōn, aras eph o katekeito apēlthen eis ton oikon autou doxazōn ton theon.
luk|5|26|	kai ekstasis elaben apantas kai edoxazon ton theon, kai eplēsthēsan phobou legontes oti eidomen paradoxa sēmeron.
luk|5|27|	kai meta tauta exēlthe kai etheasato telōnēn onomati leuin, kathēmenon epi to telōnion, kai eipen autō akolouthei moi.
luk|5|28|	kai katalipōn apanta anastas ēkolouthēsen autō.
luk|5|29|	kai epoiēse dochēn megalēn leuis autō en tē oikia autou, kai ēn ochlos telōnōn polus kai allōn oi ēsan met autōn katakeimenoi.
luk|5|30|	kai egogguzon oi grammateis autōn kai oi pharisaioi pros tous mathētas autou legontes diati meta tōn telōnōn kai amartōlōn esthiete kai pinete?
luk|5|31|	kai apokritheis o iēsous eipe pros autous ou chreian echousin oi ugiainontes iatrou, all oi kakōs echontes
luk|5|32|	ouk elēlutha kalesai dikaious, alla amartōlous eis metanoian.
luk|5|33|	oi de eipon pros auton diati oi mathētai iōannou nēsteuousi pukna kai deēseis poiountai, omoiōs kai oi tōn pharisaiōn, oi de soi esthiousi kai pinousin?
luk|5|34|	o de eipe pros autous mē dunasthe tous uious tou numphōnos, en ō o numphios met autōn esti, poiēsai nēsteuein?
luk|5|35|	eleusontai de ēmerai, kai otan aparthē ap autōn o numphios, tote nēsteusousin en ekeinais tais ēmerais.
luk|5|36|	elege de kai parabolēn pros autous oti oudeis epiblēma imatiou kainou epiballei epi imation palaion ei de mēge, kai to kainon schisei kai tō palaiō ou sumphōnei to epiblēma to apo tou kainou.
luk|5|37|	kai oudeis ballei oinon neon eis askous palaious ei de mēge, rēxei o oinos o neos tous askous, kai autos ekchuthēsetai kai oi askoi apolountai
luk|5|38|	alla oinon neon eis askous kainous blēteon, kai amphoteroi suntērountai.
luk|5|39|	kai oudeis piōn palaion eutheōs thelei neon legei gar o palaios chrēstoteros estin.
luk|6|1|	egeneto de en sabbatō deuteroprōtō diaporeuesthai auton dia tōn sporimōn kai etillon oi mathētai autou tous stachuas kai ēsthion psōchontes tais chersi.
luk|6|2|	tines de tōn pharisaiōn eipon autois ti poieite o ouk exesti poiein en tois sabbasi?
luk|6|3|	kai apokritheis pros autous eipen o iēsous oude touto anegnōte o epoiēse dauid opote epeinasen autos kai oi met autou ontes?
luk|6|4|	ōs eisēlthen eis ton oikon tou theou kai tous artous tēs protheseōs elabe kai ephage, kai edōke kai tois met autou, ous ouk exesti phagein ei mē monous tous iereis?
luk|6|5|	kai elegen autois oti kurios estin o uios tou anthrōpou kai tou sabbatou.
luk|6|6|	egeneto de kai en eterō sabbatō eiselthein auton eis tēn sunagōgēn kai didaskein kai ēn ekei anthrōpos, kai ē cheir autou ē dexia ēn xēra.
luk|6|7|	paretēroun de oi grammateis kai oi pharisaioi ei en tō sabbatō therapeusei, ina eurōsi katēgorian autou.
luk|6|8|	autos de ēdei tous dialogismous autōn, kai eipe tō anthrōpō tō xēran echonti tēn cheira egeire kai stēthi eis to meson. o de anastas estē.
luk|6|9|	eipen oun o iēsous pros autous eperōtēsō umas ti exesti tois sabbasin, agathopoiēsai ē kakopoiēsai, psuchēn sōsai ē apokteinai?
luk|6|10|	kai periblepsamenos pantas autous eipen autō ekteinon tēn cheira sou. o de epoiēse, kai apokatestathē ē cheir autou ōs ē allē.
luk|6|11|	autoi de eplēsthēsan anoias, kai dielaloun pros allēlous ti an poiēseian tō iēsou.
luk|6|12|	egeneto de en tais ēmerais tautais exēlthen eis to oros proseuxasthai, kai ēn dianuktereuōn en tē proseuchē tou theou.
luk|6|13|	kai ote egeneto ēmera, prosephōnēse tous mathētas autou, kai eklexamenos ap autōn dōdeka, ous kai apostolous ōnomase,
luk|6|14|	simōna, on kai ōnomase petron, kai andrean ton adelphon autou, iakōbon kai iōannēn, philippon kai bartholomaion,
luk|6|15|	matthaion kai thōman, iakōbon ton tou alphaiou kai simōna ton kaloumenon zēlōtēn,
luk|6|16|	ioudan iakōbou kai ioudan iskariōtēn, os kai egeneto prodotēs,
luk|6|17|	kai katabas met autōn estē epi topou pedinou, kai ochlos mathētōn autou, kai plēthos polu tou laou apo pasēs tēs ioudaias kai ierousalēm kai tēs paraliou turou kai sidōnos, oi ēlthon akousai autou kai iathēnai apo tōn nosōn autōn,
luk|6|18|	kai oi ochloumenoi apo pneumatōn akathartōn, kai etherapeuonto
luk|6|19|	kai pas o ochlos ezētei aptesthai autou, oti dunamis par autou exērcheto kai iato pantas.
luk|6|20|	kai autos eparas tous ophthalmous autou eis tous mathētas autou elege makarioi oi ptōchoi, oti umetera estin ē basileia tou theou.
luk|6|21|	makarioi oi peinōntes nun, oti chortasthēsesthe. makarioi oi klaiontes nun, oti gelasete.
luk|6|22|	makarioi este otan misēsōsin umas oi anthrōpoi, kai otan aphorisōsin umas kai oneidisōsi kai ekbalōsi to onoma umōn ōs ponēron eneka tou uiou tou anthrōpou.
luk|6|23|	charēte en ekeinē tē ēmera kai skirtēsate idou gar o misthos umōn polus en tō ouranō kata ta auta gar epoioun tois prophētais oi pateres autōn.
luk|6|24|	plēn ouai umin tois plousiois, oti apechete tēn paraklēsin umōn.
luk|6|25|	ouai umin oi empeplēsmenoi, oti peinasete. ouai umin oi gelōntes nun, oti penthēsete kai klausete.
luk|6|26|	ouai otan kalōs umas eipōsi pantes oi anthrōpoi kata ta auta gar epoioun tois pseudoprophētais oi pateres autōn.
luk|6|27|	alla umin legō tois akouousin agapate tous echthrous umōn, kalōs poieite tois misousin umas,
luk|6|28|	eulogeite tous katarōmenous umin, proseuchesthe uper tōn epēreazontōn umas.
luk|6|29|	tō tuptonti se epi tēn siagona pareche kai tēn allēn, kai apo tou airontos sou to imation kai ton chitōna mē kōlusēs.
luk|6|30|	panti de tō aitounti se didou, kai apo tou airontos ta sa mē apaitei.
luk|6|31|	kai kathōs thelete ina poiōsin umin oi anthrōpoi, kai umeis poieite autois omoiōs.
luk|6|32|	kai ei agapate tous agapōntas umas, poia umin charis esti? kai gar oi amartōloi tous agapōntas autous agapōsi.
luk|6|33|	kai ean agathopoiēte tous agathopoiountas umas, poia umin charis esti? kai gar oi amartōloi to auto poiousi.
luk|6|34|	kai ean daneizēte par ōn elpizete apolabein, poia umin charis esti? kai gar amartōloi amartōlois daneizousin ina apolabōsi ta isa.
luk|6|35|	plēn agapate tous echthrous umōn kai agathopoieite kai daneizete mēden apelpizontes, kai estai o misthos umōn polus, kai esesthe uioi upsistou, oti autos chrēstos estin epi tous acharistous kai ponērous.
luk|6|36|	ginesthe oun oiktirmones, kathōs kai o patēr umōn oiktirmōn esti.
luk|6|37|	kai mē krinete, kai ou mē krithēte mē katadikazete, kai ou mē katadikasthēte apoluete, kai apoluthēsesthe
luk|6|38|	didote, kai dothēsetai umin metron kalon, pepiesmenon kai sesaleumenon kai uperekchunomenon dōsousin eis ton kolpon umōn tō gar autō metrō, ō metreite, antimetrēthēsetai umin.
luk|6|39|	eipe de parabolēn autois mēti dunatai tuphlos tuphlon odēgein? ouchi amphoteroi eis bothunon pesountai?
luk|6|40|	ouk esti mathētēs uper ton didaskalon autou katērtismenos de pas estai ōs o didaskalos autou.
luk|6|41|	ti de blepeis to karphos to en tō ophthalmō tou adelphou sou, tēn de dokon tēn en tō idiō ophthalmō ou katanoeis?
luk|6|42|	ē pōs dunasai legein tō adelphō sou, adelphe, aphes ekbalō to karphos to en tō ophthalmō sou, autos tēn en tō ophthalmō sou dokon ou blepōn? upokrita, ekbale prōton tēn dokon ek tou ophthalmou sou, kai tote diablepseis ekbalein to karphos to en tō ophthalmō tou adelphou sou.
luk|6|43|	ou gar esti dendron kalon poioun karpon sapron, oude dendron sapron poioun karpon kalon
luk|6|44|	ekaston gar dendron ek tou idiou karpou ginōsketai. ou gar ex akanthōn sullegousi suka, oude ek batou trugōsi staphulēn.
luk|6|45|	o agathos anthrōpos ek tou agathou thēsaurou tēs kardias autou propherei to agathon, kai o ponēros anthrōpos ek tou ponērou thēsaurou tēs kardias autou propherei to ponēron ek gar tou perisseumatos tēs kardias lalei to stoma autou.
luk|6|46|	ti de me kaleite kurie kurie, kai ou poieite a legō?
luk|6|47|	pas o erchomenos pros me kai akouōn mou tōn logōn kai poiōn autous, upodeixō umin tini estin omoios
luk|6|48|	omoios estin anthrōpō oikodomounti oikian, os kai eskapse kai ebathune kai ethēke themelion epi tēn petran plēmmuras de genomenēs proserrēxen o potamos tē oikia ekeinē, kai ouk ischuse saleusai autēn tethemeliōto gar epi tēn petran.
luk|6|49|	o de akousas kai mē poiēsas omoios estin anthrōpō oikodomēsanti oikian epi tēn gēn chōris themeliou ē proserrēxen o potamos, kai euthus epese, kai egeneto to rēgma tēs oikias ekeinēs mega.
luk|7|1|	epei de eplērōse panta ta rēmata autou eis tas akoas tou laou, eisēlthen eis kapernaoum.
luk|7|2|	ekatontarchou de tinos doulos kakōs echōn ēmelle teleutan, os ēn autō entimos.
luk|7|3|	akousas de peri tou iēsou apesteile pros auton presbuterous tōn ioudaiōn erōtōn auton opōs elthōn diasōsē ton doulon autou.
luk|7|4|	oi de paragenomenoi pros ton iēsoun parekaloun auton spoudaiōs, legontes oti axios estin ō parexei touto.
luk|7|5|	agapa gar to ethnos ēmōn, kai tēn sunagōgēn autos ōkodomēsen ēmin.
luk|7|6|	o de iēsous eporeueto sun autois. ēdē de autou ou makran apechontos apo tēs oikias epempse pros auton o ekatontarchos philous legōn autō kurie, mē skullou ou gar eimi ikanos ina upo tēn stegēn mou eiselthēs
luk|7|7|	dio oude emauton ēxiōsa pros se elthein all eipe logō, kai iathēsetai o pais mou.
luk|7|8|	kai gar egō anthrōpos eimi upo exousian tassomenos, echōn up emauton stratiōtas, kai legō toutō, poreuthēti, kai poreuetai, kai allō, erchou, kai erchetai, kai tō doulō mou, poiēson touto, kai poiei.
luk|7|9|	akousas de tauta o iēsous ethaumasen auton, kai strapheis tō akolouthounti autō ochlō eipe legō umin, oude en tō israēl tosautēn pistin euron.
luk|7|10|	kai upostrepsantes oi pemphthentes eis ton oikon euron ton asthenounta doulon ugiainonta.
luk|7|11|	kai egeneto en tō exēs eporeueto eis polin kaloumenēn nain kai suneporeuonto autō oi mathētai autou ikanoi kai ochlos polus.
luk|7|12|	ōs de ēggise tē pulē tēs poleōs, kai idou exekomizeto tethnēkōs uios monogenēs tē mētri autou, kai autē ēn chēra, kai ochlos tēs poleōs ikanos ēn sun autē.
luk|7|13|	kai idōn autēn o kurios esplagchnisthē ep autē kai eipen autē mē klaie
luk|7|14|	kai proselthōn ēpsato tēs sorou, oi de bastazontes estēsan, kai eipe neaniske, soi legō, egerthēti.
luk|7|15|	kai anekathisen o nekros kai ērxato lalein, kai edōken auton tē mētri autou.
luk|7|16|	elabe de phobos pantas kai edoxazon ton theon, legontes oti prophētēs megas egēgertai en ēmin, kai oti epeskepsato o theos ton laon autou.
luk|7|17|	kai exēlthen o logos outos en olē tē ioudaia peri autou kai en pasē tē perichōrō.
luk|7|18|	kai apēggeilan iōannē oi mathētai autou peri pantōn toutōn.
luk|7|19|	kai proskalesamenos duo tinas tōn mathētōn autou o iōannēs epempse pros ton iēsoun legōn su ei o erchomenos ē eteron prosdokōmen?
luk|7|20|	paragenomenoi de pros auton oi andres eipon iōannēs o baptistēs apestalken ēmas pros se legōn su ei o erchomenos ē eteron prosdokōmen?
luk|7|21|	en autē de tē ōra etherapeuse pollous apo nosōn kai mastigōn kai pneumatōn ponērōn, kai tuphlois pollois echarisato to blepein.
luk|7|22|	kai apokritheis o iēsous eipen autois poreuthentes apaggeilate iōannē a eidete kai ēkousate tuphloi anablepousi kai chōloi peripatousi, leproi katharizontai, kōphoi akouousi, nekroi egeirontai, ptōchoi euaggelizontai
luk|7|23|	kai makarios estin os ean mē skandalisthē en emoi.
luk|7|24|	apelthontōn de tōn mathētōn iōannou ērxato legein pros tous ochlous peri iōannou ti exelēluthate eis tēn erēmon theasasthai? kalamon upo anemou saleuomenon?
luk|7|25|	alla ti exelēluthate idein? anthrōpon en malakois imatiois ēmphiesmenon? idou oi en imatismō endoxō kai truphē uparchontes en tois basileiois eisin.
luk|7|26|	alla ti exelēluthate idein? prophētēn? nai legō umin, kai perissoteron prophētou.
luk|7|27|	outos esti peri ou gegraptai, idou egō apostellō ton aggelon mou pro prosōpou sou, os kataskeuasei tēn odon sou emprosthen sou
luk|7|28|	legō gar umin, meizōn en gennētois gunaikōn prophētēs iōannou tou baptistou oudeis estin o de mikroteros en tē basileia tou theou meizōn autou esti.
luk|7|29|	kai pas o laos akousas kai oi telōnai edikaiōsan ton theon, baptisthentes to baptisma iōannou
luk|7|30|	oi de pharisaioi kai oi nomikoi tēn boulēn tou theou ēthetēsan eis eautous, mē baptisthentes up autou.
luk|7|31|	tini oun omoiōsō tous anthrōpous tēs geneas tautēs, kai tini eisin omoioi?
luk|7|32|	omoioi eisi paidiois tois en agora kathēmenois kai prosphōnousin allēlois kai legousin ēulēsamen umin, kai ouk ōrchēsasthe, ethrēnēsamen umin, kai ouk eklausate.
luk|7|33|	elēluthe gar iōannēs o baptistēs mēte arton esthiōn mēte oinon pinōn, kai legete daimonion echei.
luk|7|34|	elēluthen o uios tou anthrōpou esthiōn kai pinōn, kai legete idou anthrōpos phagos kai oinopotēs, philos telōnōn kai amartōlōn.
luk|7|35|	kai edikaiōthē ē sophia apo tōn teknōn autēs pantōn!
luk|7|36|	ērōta de tis auton tōn pharisaiōn ina phagē met autou kai eiselthōn eis tēn oikian tou pharisaiou aneklithē.
luk|7|37|	kai idou gunē en tē polei ētis ēn amartōlos, kai epignousa oti anakeitai en tē oikia tou pharisaiou, komisasa alabastron murou
luk|7|38|	kai stasa opisō para tous podas autou klaiousa, ērxato brechein tous podas autou tois dakrusi kai tais thrixi tēs kephalēs autēs exemasse, kai katephilei tous podas autou kai ēleiphe tō murō.
luk|7|39|	idōn de o pharisaios o kalesas auton eipen en eautō legōn outos ei ēn prophētēs, eginōsken an tis kai potapē ē gunē ētis aptetai autou, oti amartōlos esti.
luk|7|40|	kai apokritheis o iēsous eipe pros auton simōn, echō soi ti eipein. o de phēsi didaskale, eipe.
luk|7|41|	duo chreōpheiletai ēsan daneistē tini o eis ōpheile dēnaria pentakosia, o de eteros pentēkonta.
luk|7|42|	mē echontōn de autōn apodounai, amphoterois echarisato. tis oun autōn, eipe, pleion auton agapēsei?
luk|7|43|	apokritheis de o simōn eipen upolambanō oti ō to pleion echarisato. o de eipen autō orthōs ekrinas.
luk|7|44|	kai strapheis pros tēn gunaika tō simōni ephē blepeis tautēn tēn gunaika? eisēlthon sou eis tēn oikian, udōr epi tous podas mou ouk edōkas autē de tois dakrusin ebrexe mou tous podas kai tais thrixi tēs kephalēs autēs exemaxe.
luk|7|45|	philēma moi ouk edōkas autē de aph ēs eisēlthen ou dielipe kataphilousa mou tous podas.
luk|7|46|	elaiō tēn kephalēn mou ouk ēleipsas autē de murō ēleipse mou tous podas.
luk|7|47|	ou charin legō soi, apheōntai ai amartiai autēs ai pollai, oti ēgapēse polu ō de oligon aphietai, oligon agapa.
luk|7|48|	eipe de autē apheōntai sou ai amartiai.
luk|7|49|	kai ērxanto oi sunanakeimenoi legein en eautois tis outos estin os kai amartias aphiēsin?
luk|7|50|	eipe de pros tēn gunaika ē pistis sou sesōke se poreuou eis eirēnēn.
luk|8|1|	kai egeneto en tō kathexēs kai autos diōdeue kata polin kai kōmēn kērussōn kai euaggelizomenos tēn basileian tou theou, kai oi dōdeka sun autō,
luk|8|2|	kai gunaikes tines ai ēsan tetherapeumenai apo nosōn kai mastigōn kai pneumatōn ponērōn kai astheneiōn, maria ē kaloumenē magdalēnē, aph ēs daimonia epta exelēluthei,
luk|8|3|	kai iōanna gunē chouza epitropou ērōdou, kai sousanna kai eterai pollai, aitines diēkonoun autō apo tōn uparchontōn autais.
luk|8|4|	suniontos de ochlou pollou kai tōn kata polin epiporeuomenōn pros auton eipe dia parabolēs
luk|8|5|	exēlthen o speirōn tou speirai ton sporon autou. kai en tō speirein auton o men epese para tēn odon, kai katepatēthē, kai ta peteina tou ouranou katephagen auto
luk|8|6|	kai eteron epesen epi tēn petran, kai phuen exēranthē dia to mē echein ikmada
luk|8|7|	kai eteron epesen en mesō tōn akanthōn, kai sumphueisai ai akanthai apepnixan auto.
luk|8|8|	kai eteron epesen eis tēn gēn tēn agathēn, kai phuen epoiēse karpon ekatontaplasiona. tauta legōn ephōnei o echōn ōta akouein akouetō.
luk|8|9|	epērōtōn de auton oi mathētai autou legontes tis eiē ē parabolē autē?
luk|8|10|	o de eipen umin dedotai gnōnai ta mustēria tēs basileias tou theou, tois de loipois en parabolais, ina blepontes mē blepōsi kai akouontes mē suniōsin.
luk|8|11|	esti de autē ē parabolē o sporos estin o logos tou theou
luk|8|12|	oi de para tēn odon eisin oi akousantes, eita erchetai o diabolos kai airei ton logon apo tēs kardias autōn, ina mē pisteusantes sōthōsin.
luk|8|13|	oi de epi tēs petras oi otan akousōsi, meta charas dechontai ton logon, kai outoi rizan ouk echousin, oi pros kairon pisteuousi kai en kairō peirasmou aphistantai.
luk|8|14|	to de eis tas akanthas peson, outoi eisin oi akousantes, kai upo merimnōn kai ploutou kai ēdonōn tou biou poreuomenoi sumpnigontai kai ou telesphorousi.
luk|8|15|	to de en tē kalē gē, outoi eisin oitines en kardia kalē kai agathē akousantes ton logon katechousi kai karpophorousin en upomonē.
luk|8|16|	oudeis de luchnon apsas kaluptei auton skeuei ē upokatō klinēs tithēsin, all epi luchnias epitithēsin, ina oi eisporeuomenoi blepōsi to phōs.
luk|8|17|	ou gar esti krupton o ou phaneron genēsetai, oude apokruphon o ou gnōsthēsetai kai eis phaneron elthē.
luk|8|18|	blepete oun pōs akouete os gar ean echē, dothēsetai autō, kai os ean mē echē, kai o dokei echein arthēsetai ap autou.
luk|8|19|	paregenonto de pros auton ē mētēr kai oi adelphoi autou, kai ouk ēdunanto suntuchein autō dia ton ochlon.
luk|8|20|	kai apēggelē autō legontōn ē mētēr sou kai oi adelphoi sou estēkasin exō idein se thelontes.
luk|8|21|	o de apokritheis eipe pros autous mētēr mou kai adelphoi mou outoi eisin oi ton logon tou theou akouontes kai poiountes auton.
luk|8|22|	kai egeneto en mia tōn ēmerōn kai autos enebē eis ploion kai oi mathētai autou, kai eipe pros autous dielthōmen eis to peran tēs limnēs kai anēchthēsan.
luk|8|23|	pleontōn de autōn aphupnōse. kai katebē lailaps anemou eis tēn limnēn, kai suneplērounto kai ekinduneuon.
luk|8|24|	proselthontes de diēgeiran auton legontes epistata epistata, apollumetha! o de egertheis epetimēse tō anemō kai tō kludōni tou udatos, kai epausanto, kai egeneto galēnē.
luk|8|25|	eipe de autois pou estin ē pistis umōn? phobēthentes de ethaumasan legontes pros allēlous tis ara outos estin, oti kai tois anemois epitassei kai tō udati, kai upakouousin autō?
luk|8|26|	kai katepleusen eis tēn chōran tōn gadarēnōn, ētis estin antipera tēs galilaias.
luk|8|27|	exelthonti de autō epi tēn gēn upēntēsen autō anēr tis ek tēs poleōs, os eiche daimonia ek chronōn ikanōn, kai imation ouk enedidusketo kai en oikia ouk emenen, all en tois mnēmasin.
luk|8|28|	idōn de ton iēsoun kai anakraxas prosepesen autō kai phōnē megalē eipe ti emoi kai soi, iēsou, uie tou theou tou upsistou? deomai sou, mē me basanisēs.
luk|8|29|	parēggeile gar tō pneumati tō akathartō exelthein apo tou anthrōpou. pollois gar chronois sunērpakei auton, kai edesmeito alusesi kai pedais phulassomenos, kai diarrēssōn ta desma ēlauneto upo tou daimonos eis tas erēmous.
luk|8|30|	epērōtēse de auton o iēsous legōn ti soi estin onoma? o de eipe legeōn oti daimonia polla eisēlthen eis auton
luk|8|31|	kai parekalei auton ina mē epitaxē autois eis tēn abusson apelthein.
luk|8|32|	ēn de ekei agelē choirōn ikanōn boskomenōn en tō orei kai parekaloun auton ina epitrepsē autois eis ekeinous eiselthein kai epetrepsen autois.
luk|8|33|	exelthonta de ta daimonia apo tou anthrōpou eisēlthon eis tous choirous, kai ōrmēsen ē agelē kata tou krēmnou eis tēn limnēn kai apepnigē.
luk|8|34|	idontes de oi boskontes to gegenēmenon ephugon, kai apēggeilan eis tēn polin kai eis tous agrous.
luk|8|35|	exēlthon de idein to gegonos, kai ēlthon pros ton iēsoun kai euron kathēmenon ton anthrōpon, aph ou ta daimonia exelēluthei, imatismenon kai sōphronounta para tous podas tou iēsou, kai ephobēthēsan.
luk|8|36|	apēggeilan de autois oi idontes pōs esōthē o daimonistheis.
luk|8|37|	kai ērōtēsan auton apan to plēthos tēs perichōrou tōn gadarēnōn apelthein ap autōn, oti phobō megalō suneichonto. autos de embas eis to ploion upestrepsen.
luk|8|38|	edeeto de autou o anēr, aph ou exelēluthei ta daimonia, einai sun autō apeluse de auton o iēsous legōn
luk|8|39|	upostrephe eis ton oikon sou kai diēgou osa epoiēse soi o theos. kai apēlthe kath olēn tēn polin kērussōn osa epoiēsen autō o iēsous.
luk|8|40|	egeneto de en tō upostrepsai ton iēsoun apedexato auton o ochlos ēsan gar pantes prosdokōntes auton.
luk|8|41|	kai idou ēlthen anēr ō onoma iaeiros, kai autos archōn tēs sunagōgēs upērche kai pesōn para tous podas tou iēsou parekalei auton eiselthein eis ton oikon autou,
luk|8|42|	oti thugatēr monogenēs ēn autō ōs etōn dōdeka, kai autē apethnēsken. en de tō upagein auton oi ochloi sunepnigon auton.
luk|8|43|	kai gunē ousa en rusei aimatos apo etōn dōdeka, ētis iatrois prosanalōsasa olon ton bion ouk ischusen up oudenos therapeuthēnai,
luk|8|44|	proselthousa opisthen ēpsato tou kraspedou tou imatiou autou, kai parachrēma estē ē rusis tou aimatos autēs.
luk|8|45|	kai eipen o iēsous tis o apsamenos mou? arnoumenōn de pantōn eipen o petros kai oi sun autō epistata, oi ochloi sunechousi se kai apothlibousi, kai legeis tis o apsamenos mou?
luk|8|46|	o de iēsous eipen ēpsato mou tis egō gar egnōn dunamin exelthousan ap emou.
luk|8|47|	idousa de ē gunē oti ouk elathe, tremousa ēlthe kai prospesousa autō di ēn aitian ēpsato autou apēggeilen autō enōpion pantos tou laou, kai ōs iathē parachrēma.
luk|8|48|	o de eipen autē tharsei, thugater, ē pistis sou sesōke se poreuou eis eirēnēn.
luk|8|49|	eti autou lalountos erchetai tis para tou archisunagōgou legōn autō oti tethnēken ē thugatēr sou mē skulle ton didaskalon.
luk|8|50|	o de iēsous akousas apekrithē autō legōn mē phobou monon pisteue, kai sōthēsetai.
luk|8|51|	elthōn de eis tēn oikian ouk aphēken eiselthein oudena ei mē petron kai iōannēn kai iakōbon kai ton patera tēs paidos kai tēn mētera.
luk|8|52|	eklaion de pantes kai ekoptonto autēn. o de eipe mē klaiete ouk apethanen, alla katheudei.
luk|8|53|	kai kategelōn autou, eidotes oti apethanen.
luk|8|54|	autos de ekbalōn exō pantas kai kratēsas tēs cheiros autēs ephōnēse legōn ē pais, egeirou.
luk|8|55|	kai epestrepse to pneuma autēs, kai anestē parachrēma, kai dietaxen autē dothēnai phagein.
luk|8|56|	kai exestēsan oi goneis autois. o de parēggeilen autois mēdeni eipein to gegonos.
luk|9|1|	sugkalesamenos de tous dōdeka mathētas autou edōken autois dunamin kai exousian epi panta ta daimonia kai nosous therapeuein
luk|9|2|	kai apesteilen autous kērussein tēn basileian tou theou kai iasthai tous asthenountas,
luk|9|3|	kai eipe pros autous mēden airete eis tēn odon, mēte rabdous mēte pēran mēte arton mēte argurion mēte ana duo chitōnas echein.
luk|9|4|	kai eis ēn an oikian eiselthēte, ekei menete kai ekeithen exerchesthe.
luk|9|5|	kai osoi ean mē dexōntai umas, exerchomenoi apo tēs poleōs ekeinēs kai ton koniorton apo tōn podōn umōn apotinaxate eis marturion ep autous.
luk|9|6|	exerchomenoi de diērchonto kata tas kōmas euaggelizomenoi kai therapeuontes pantachou.
luk|9|7|	ēkouse de ērōdēs o tetrarchēs ta ginomena up autou panta, kai diēporei dia to legesthai upo tinōn oti iōannēs egēgertai ek tōn nekrōn,
luk|9|8|	upo tinōn de oti ēlias ephanē, allōn de oti prophētēs tis tōn archaiōn anestē.
luk|9|9|	kai eipen o ērōdēs iōannēn egō apekephalisa tis de estin outos peri ou egō akouō toiauta? kai ezētei idein auton.
luk|9|10|	kai upostrepsantes oi apostoloi diēgēsanto autō osa epoiēsan. kai paralabōn autous upechōrēse kat idian eis topon erēmon poleōs kaloumenēs bēthsaida.
luk|9|11|	oi de ochloi gnontes ēkolouthēsan autō, kai dexamenos autous elalei autois peri tēs basileias tou theou, kai tous chreian echontas therapeias iasato.
luk|9|12|	ē de ēmera ērxato klinein proselthontes de oi dōdeka eipon autō apoluson ton ochlon, ina poreuthentes eis tas kuklō kōmas kai tous agrous katalusōsi kai eurōsin episitismon, oti ōde en erēmō topō esmen.
luk|9|13|	eipe de pros autous dote autois umeis phagein. oi de eipon ouk eisin ēmin pleion ē pente artoi kai ichthues duo, ei mēti poreuthentes ēmeis agorasōmen eis panta ton laon touton brōmata
luk|9|14|	ēsan gar ōsei andres pentakischilioi. eipe de pros tous mathētas autou kataklinate autous klisias ana pentēkonta.
luk|9|15|	kai epoiēsan outō kai aneklinan apantas.
luk|9|16|	labōn de tous pente artous kai tous duo ichthuas, anablepsas eis ton ouranon eulogēsen autous kai kateklase, kai edidou tois mathētais paratheinai tō ochlō.
luk|9|17|	kai ephagon kai echortasthēsan pantes, kai ērthē to perisseusan autois klasmatōn kophinoi dōdeka.
luk|9|18|	kai egeneto en tō einai auton proseuchomenon katamonas, sunēsan autō oi mathētai, kai epērōtēsen autous legōn tina me legousin oi ochloi einai?
luk|9|19|	oi de apokrithentes eipon iōannēn ton baptistēn, alloi de ēlian, alloi de oti prophētēs tis tōn archaiōn anestē.
luk|9|20|	eipe de autois umeis de tina me legete einai? apokritheis de o petros eipe ton christon tou theou.
luk|9|21|	o de epitimēsas autois parēggeile mēdeni legein touto,
luk|9|22|	eipōn oti dei ton uion tou anthrōpou polla pathein kai apodokimasthēnai apo tōn presbuterōn kai archiereōn kai grammateōn, kai apoktanthēnai, kai tē tritē ēmera egerthēnai.
luk|9|23|	elege de pros pantas ei tis thelei opisō mou erchesthai, aparnēsasthō eauton kai aratō ton stauron autou kath ēmeran kai akoloutheitō moi.
luk|9|24|	os gar an thelē tēn psuchēn autou sōsai, apolesei autēn os d an apolesē tēn psuchēn autou eneken emou, outos sōsei autēn.
luk|9|25|	ti gar ōpheleitai anthrōpos kerdēsas ton kosmon olon, eauton de apolesas ē zēmiōtheis?
luk|9|26|	os gar ean epaischunthē me kai tous emous logous, touton o uios tou anthrōpou epaischunthēsetai otan elthē en tē doxē autou kai tou patros kai tōn agiōn aggelōn.
luk|9|27|	legō de umin alēthōs, eisi tines tōn ōde estēkotōn, oi ou mē geusōntai thanatou eōs an idōsi tēn basileian tou theou.
luk|9|28|	egeneto de meta tous logous toutous ōsei ēmerai oktō kai paralabōn ton petron kai iōannēn kai iakōbon anebē eis to oros proseuxasthai.
luk|9|29|	kai egeneto en tō proseuchesthai auton to eidos tou prosōpou autou eteron kai o imatismos autou leukos exastraptōn.
luk|9|30|	kai idou andres duo sunelaloun autō, oitines ēsan mōusēs kai ēlias,
luk|9|31|	oi ophthentes en doxē elegon tēn exodon autou ēn emelle plēroun en ierousalēm.
luk|9|32|	o de petros kai oi sun autō ēsan bebarēmenoi upnō diagrēgorēsantes de eidon tēn doxan autou kai tous duo andras tous sunestōtas autō.
luk|9|33|	kai egeneto en tō diachōrizesthai autous ap autou eipen o petros pros ton iēsoun epistata, kalon estin ēmas ōde einai kai poiēsōmen skēnas treis, mian soi kai mian mōusei kai mian ēlia, mē eidōs o legei.
luk|9|34|	tauta de autou legontos egeneto nephelē kai epeskiasen autous ephobēthēsan de en tō eiselthein ekeinous eis tēn nephelēn
luk|9|35|	kai phōnē egeneto ek tēs nephelēs legousa outos estin o uios mou o agapētos autou akouete.
luk|9|36|	kai en tō genesthai tēn phōnēn eurethē o iēsous monos. kai autoi esigēsan kai oudeni apēggeilan en ekeinais tais ēmerais ouden ōn eōrakasin.
luk|9|37|	egeneto de en tē exēs ēmera katelthontōn autōn apo tou orous sunēntēsen autō ochlos polus.
luk|9|38|	kai idou anēr apo tou ochlou aneboēse legōn didaskale, deomai sou, epiblepson epi ton uion mou, oti monogenēs moi esti
luk|9|39|	kai idou pneuma lambanei auton, kai exaiphnēs krazei kai sparassei auton meta aphrou, kai mogis apochōrei ap autou suntribon auton
luk|9|40|	kai edeēthēn tōn mathētōn sou ina ekbalōsin auto, kai ouk ēdunēthēsan.
luk|9|41|	apokritheis de o iēsous eipen ō genea apistos kai diestrammenē, eōs pote esomai pros umas kai anexomai umōn? prosagage ton uion sou ōde.
luk|9|42|	eti de proserchomenou autou errēxen auton to daimonion kai sunesparaxen epetimēse de o iēsous tō pneumati tō akathartō, kai iasato ton paida kai apedōken auton tō patri autou.
luk|9|43|	exeplēssonto de pantes epi tē megaleiotēti tou theou. pantōn de thaumazontōn epi pasin ois epoiēsen o iēsous, eipe pros tous mathētas autou
luk|9|44|	thesthe umeis eis ta ōta umōn tous logous toutous o gar uios tou anthrōpou mellei paradidosthai eis cheiras anthrōpōn.
luk|9|45|	oi de ēgnooun to rēma touto, kai ēn parakekalummenon ap autōn ina mē aisthōntai auto, kai ephobounto erōtēsai auton peri tou rēmatos toutou.
luk|9|46|	eisēlthe de dialogismos en autois, to tis an eiē meizōn autōn.

luk|9|48|	kai eipen autois os ean dexētai touto to paidion epi tō onomati mou, eme dechetai, kai os ean eme dexētai, dechetai ton aposteilanta me. o gar mikroteros en pasin umin uparchōn, outos esti megas.
luk|9|49|	apokritheis de o iōannēs eipen epistata, eidomen tina epi tō onomati sou ekballonta daimonia, kai ekōlusamen auton, oti ouk akolouthei meth ēmōn.
luk|9|50|	kai eipe pros auton o iēsous mē kōluete ou gar esti kath umōn os gar ouk esti kath umōn, uper umōn estin.
luk|9|51|	egeneto de en tō sumplērousthai tas ēmeras tēs analēpseōs autou kai autos estērixe to prosōpon autou tou poreuesthai eis ierousalēm,
luk|9|52|	kai apesteilen aggelous pro prosōpou autou. kai poreuthentes eisēlthon eis kōmēn samareitōn, ōste etoimasai autō
luk|9|53|	kai ouk edexanto auton, oti to prosōpon autou ēn poreuomenon eis ierousalēm.
luk|9|54|	idontes de oi mathētai autou iakōbos kai iōannēs eipon kurie, theleis eipōmen pur katabēnai apo ouranou kai analōsai autous, ōs kai ēlias epoiēse?
luk|9|55|	strapheis de epetimēsen autois kai eipen ouk oidate poiou pneumatos este umeis
luk|9|56|	o uios tou anthrōpou ouk ēlthe psuchas anthrōpōn apolesai, alla sōsai. kai eporeuthēsan eis eteran kōmēn.
luk|9|57|	egeneto de poreuomenōn autōn en tē odō eipe tis pros auton akolouthēsō soi opou ean aperchē, kurie.
luk|9|58|	kai eipen autō o iēsous ai alōpekes phōleous echousi kai ta peteina tou ouranou kataskēnōseis, o de uios tou anthrōpou ouk echei pou tēn kephalēn klinē.
luk|9|59|	eipe de pros eteron akolouthei moi o de eipe kurie, epitrepson moi apelthonti prōton thapsai ton patera mou.

luk|10|1|	meta de tauta anedeixen o kurios kai eterous ebdomēkonta, kai apesteilen autous ana duo pro prosōpou autou eis pasan polin kai topon ou ēmellen autos erchesthai.
luk|10|2|	elegen oun pros autous o men therismos polus, oi de ergatai oligoi deēthēte oun tou kuriou tou therismou opōs ekbalē ergatas eis ton therismon autou.
luk|10|3|	upagete idou egō apostellō umas ōs arnas en mesō lukōn.
luk|10|4|	mē bastazete ballantion, mē pēran, mēde upodēmata, kai mēdena kata tēn odon aspasēsthe.
luk|10|5|	eis ēn d an oikian eiserchēsthe, prōton legete eirēnē tō oikō toutō.
luk|10|6|	kai ean ē ekei uios eirēnēs, epanapausetai ep auton ē eirēnē umōn ei de mēge, eph umas epanakampsei.
luk|10|7|	en autē de tē oikia menete esthiontes kai pinontes ta par autōn axios gar o ergatēs tou misthou autou esti mē metabainete ex oikias eis oikian.

luk|10|12|	legō de umin oti sodomois en tē ēmera ekeinē anektoteron estai ē tē polei ekeinē.
luk|10|13|	ouai soi, chorazin, ouai soi, bēthsaida oti ei en turō kai sidōni egenonto ai dunameis ai genomenai en umin, palai an en sakkō kai spodō kathēmenoi metenoēsan.
luk|10|14|	plēn turō kai sidōni anektoteron estai en tē krisei ē umin.
luk|10|15|	kai su, kapernaoum, ē eōs tou ouranou upsōtheisa, eōs adou katabibasthēsē.
luk|10|16|	o akouōn umōn emou akouei, kai o athetōn umas eme athetei o de eme athetōn athetei ton aposteilanta me.
luk|10|17|	upestrepsan de oi ebdomēkonta meta charas legontes kurie, kai ta daimonia upotassetai ēmin en tō onomati sou.
luk|10|18|	eipe de autois etheōroun ton satanan ōs astrapēn ek tou ouranou pesonta.
luk|10|19|	idou didōmi umin tēn exousian tou patein epanō opheōn kai skorpiōn kai epi pasan tēn dunamin tou echthrou, kai ouden umas ou mē adikēsē.
luk|10|20|	plēn en toutō mē chairete, oti ta pneumata umin upotassetai chairete de oti ta onomata umōn egraphē en tois ouranois.
luk|10|21|	en autē tē ōra ēgalliasato tō pneumati o iēsous kai eipen exomologoumai soi, pater, kurie tou ouranou kai tēs gēs, oti apekrupsas tauta apo sophōn kai sunetōn, kai apekalupsas auta nēpiois nai, o patēr, oti outōs egeneto eudokia emprosthen sou.
luk|10|22|	kai strapheis pros tous mathētas eipe panta moi paredothē upo tou patros mou kai oudeis epiginōskei tis estin o uios, ei mē o patēr, kai tis estin o patēr, ei mē o uios kai ō ean boulētai o uios apokalupsai.
luk|10|23|	kai strapheis pros tous mathētas kat idian eipe makarioi oi ophthalmoi oi blepontes a blepete.
luk|10|24|	legō gar umin oti polloi prophētai kai basileis ēthelēsan idein a umeis blepete, kai ouk eidon, kai akousai a akouete, kai ouk ēkousan.
luk|10|25|	kai idou nomikos tis anestē ekpeirazōn auton kai legōn didaskale, ti poiēsas zōēn aiōnion klēronomēsō?
luk|10|26|	o de eipe pros auton en tō nomō ti gegraptai? pōs anaginōskeis?
luk|10|27|	o de apokritheis eipen agapēseis kurion ton theon sou ex olēs tēs kardias sou kai ex olēs tēs psuchēs sou kai ex olēs tēs ischuos sou kai ex olēs tēs dianoias sou, kai ton plēsion sou ōs seauton
luk|10|28|	eipe de autō orthōs apekrithēs touto poiei kai zēsē.
luk|10|29|	o de thelōn dikaioun eauton eipe pros ton iēsoun kai tis esti mou plēsion?
luk|10|30|	upolabōn de o iēsous eipen anthrōpos tis katebainen apo ierousalēm eis ierichō, kai lēstais periepesen oi kai ekdusantes auton kai plēgas epithentes apēlthon aphentes ēmithanē tugchanonta.
luk|10|31|	kata sugkurian de iereus tis katebainen en tē odō ekeinē, kai idōn auton antiparēlthen.
luk|10|32|	omoiōs de kai leuitēs genomenos kata ton topon, elthōn kai idōn antiparēlthe.
luk|10|33|	samareitēs de tis odeuōn ēlthe kat auton, kai idōn auton esplagchnisthē,
luk|10|34|	kai proselthōn katedēse ta traumata autou epicheōn elaion kai oinon, epibibasas de auton epi to idion ktēnos ēgagen auton eis pandocheion kai epemelēthē autou
luk|10|35|	kai epi tēn aurion exelthōn, ekbalōn duo dēnaria edōke tō pandochei kai eipen autō epimelēthēti autou, kai o ti an prosdapanēsēs, egō en tō epanerchesthai me apodōsō soi.
luk|10|36|	tis oun toutōn tōn triōn plēsion dokei soi gegonenai tou empesontos eis tous lēstas?
luk|10|37|	o de eipen o poiēsas to eleos met autou. eipen oun autō o iēsous poreuou kai su poiei omoiōs.
luk|10|38|	egeneto de en tō poreuesthai autous kai autos eisēlthen eis kōmēn tina. gunē de tis onomati martha upedexato auton eis ton oikon autēs.
luk|10|39|	kai tēde ēn adelphē kaloumenē maria, ē kai parakathisasa para tous podas tou iēsou ēkoue ton logon autou.
luk|10|40|	ē de martha periespato peri pollēn diakonian epistasa de eipe kurie, ou melei soi oti ē adelphē mou monēn me katelipe diakonein? eipe oun autē ina moi sunantilabētai.
luk|10|41|	apokritheis de eipen autē o iēsous martha martha, merimnas kai turbazē peri polla
luk|10|42|	enos de esti chreia maria de tēn agathēn merida exelexato, ētis ouk aphairethēsetai ap autēs.
luk|11|1|	kai egeneto en tō einai auton en topō tini proseuchomenon, ōs epausato, eipe tis tōn mathētōn autou pros auton kurie, didaxon ēmas proseuchesthai, kathōs kai iōannēs edidaxe tous mathētas autou.
luk|11|2|	eipe de autois otan proseuchēsthe, legete pater ēmōn o en tois ouranois agiasthētō to onoma sou elthetō ē basileia sou genēthētō to thelēma sou, ōs en ouranō, kai epi tēs gēs
luk|11|3|	ton arton ēmōn ton epiousion didou ēmin to kath ēmeran
luk|11|4|	kai aphes ēmin tas amartias ēmōn kai gar autoi aphiemen panti tō opheilonti ēmin kai mē eisenegkēs ēmas eis peirasmon, alla rusai ēmas apo tou ponērou.
luk|11|5|	kai eipe pros autous tis ex umōn exei philon, kai poreusetai pros auton mesonuktiou kai erei autō phile, chrēson moi treis artous,
luk|11|6|	epeidē philos mou paregeneto ex odou pros me kai ouk echō o parathēsō autō
luk|11|7|	kakeinos esōthen apokritheis eipē mē moi kopous pareche ēdē ē thura kekleistai kai ta paidia mou met emou eis tēn koitēn eisin ou dunamai anastas dounai soi?
luk|11|8|	legō umin, ei kai ou dōsei autō anastas dia to einai autou philon, dia ge tēn anaideian autou egertheis dōsei autō osōn chrēzei.
luk|11|9|	kagō umin legō, aiteite, kai dothēsetai umin, zēteite, kai eurēsete, krouete, kai anoigēsetai umin
luk|11|10|	pas gar o aitōn lambanei kai o zētōn euriskei kai tō krouonti anoichthēsetai.
luk|11|11|	tina de ex umōn ton patera aitēsei o uios arton, mē lithon epidōsei autō? ē kai ichthun, mē anti ichthuos ophin epidōsei autō?
luk|11|12|	ē kai ean aitēsē ōon, mē epidōsei autō skorpion?
luk|11|13|	ei oun umeis, uparchontes ponēroi, oidate domata agatha didonai tois teknois umōn, posō mallon o patēr o ex ouranou dōsei pneuma agathon tois aitousin auton?
luk|11|14|	kai ēn ekballōn daimonion, kai auto ēn kōphon egeneto de tou daimoniou exelthontos elalēsen o kōphos, kai ethaumazon oi ochloi
luk|11|15|	tines de ex autōn eipon en beelzeboul tō archonti tōn daimoniōn ekballei ta daimonia.
luk|11|16|	eteroi de peirazontes sēmeion par autou ezētoun ex ouranou.
luk|11|17|	autos de eidōs autōn ta dianoēmata eipen autois pasa basileia eph eautēn diameristheisa, erēmoutai, kai oikos epi oikon, piptei.
luk|11|18|	ei de kai o satanas eph eauton diemeristhē, pōs stathēsetai ē basileia autou, oti legete en beelzeboul me ekballein ta daimonia?
luk|11|19|	ei de egō en beelzeboul ekballō ta daimonia, oi uioi umōn en tini ekbalousi? dia touto autoi kritai umōn esontai.
luk|11|20|	ei de en daktulō theou ekballō ta daimonia, ara ephthasen eph umas ē basileia tou theou.
luk|11|21|	otan o ischuros kathōplismenos phulassē tēn eautou aulēn, en eirēnē esti ta uparchonta autou
luk|11|22|	epan de o ischuroteros autou epelthōn nikēsē auton, tēn panoplian autou airei, eph ē epepoithei, kai ta skula autou diadidōsin.
luk|11|23|	o mē ōn met emou kat emou esti, kai o mē sunagōn met emou skorpizei.
luk|11|24|	otan to akatharton pneuma exelthē apo tou anthrōpou, dierchetai di anudrōn topōn zētoun anapausin, kai mē euriskon legei upostrepsō eis ton oikon mou othen exēlthon
luk|11|25|	kai elthon euriskei sesarōmenon kai kekosmēmenon.

luk|11|27|	egeneto de en tō legein auton tauta eparasa tis gunē phōnēn ek tou ochlou eipen autō makaria ē koilia ē bastasasa se kai mastoi ous ethēlasas.

luk|11|29|	tōn de ochlōn epathroizomenōn ērxato legein ē genea autē genea ponēra esti sēmeion zētei, kai sēmeion ou dothēsetai autē ei mē to sēmeion iōna tou prophētou.
luk|11|30|	kathōs gar egeneto iōnas sēmeion tois nineuitais, outōs estai kai o uios tou anthrōpou tē genea tautē sēmeion.
luk|11|31|	basilissa notou egerthēsetai en tē krisei meta tōn andrōn tēs geneas tautēs kai katakrinei autous, oti ēlthen ek tōn peratōn tēs gēs akousai tēn sophian solomōntos, kai idou pleion solomōntos ōde.
luk|11|32|	andres nineui anastēsontai en tē krisei meta tēs geneas tautēs kai katakrinousin autēn, oti metenoēsan eis to kērugma iōna, kai idou pleion iōna ōde.
luk|11|33|	oudeis de luchnon apsas eis kruptēn tithēsin oude upo ton modion, all epi tēn luchnian, ina oi eisporeuomenoi to pheggos blepōsin.
luk|11|34|	o luchnos tou sōmatos estin o ophthalmos otan oun o ophthalmos sou aplous ē, kai olon to sōma sou phōteinon estin epan de ponēros ē, kai to sōma sou skoteinon.
luk|11|35|	skopei oun mē to phōs to en soi skotos estin.

luk|11|37|	en de tō lalēsai auton tauta ērōta auton pharisaios tis opōs aristēsē par autō eiselthōn de anepesen.
luk|11|38|	o de pharisaios idōn ethaumasen oti ou prōton ebaptisthē pro tou aristou.
luk|11|39|	eipe de o kurios pros auton nun umeis oi pharisaioi to exōthen tou potēriou kai tou pinakos katharizete, to de esōthen umōn gemei arpagēs kai ponērias.
luk|11|40|	aphrones! ouch o poiēsas to exōthen kai to esōthen epoiēse?
luk|11|41|	plēn ta enonta dote eleēmosunēn, kai idou apanta kathara umin estai.
luk|11|42|	all ouai umin tois pharisaiois, oti apodekatoute to ēduosmon kai to pēganon kai pan lachanon, kai parerchesthe tēn krisin kai tēn agapēn tou theou tauta de edei poiēsai, kakeina mē aphienai.

luk|12|1|	en ois episunachtheisōn tōn muriadōn tou ochlou ōs katapatein allēlous, ērxato legein pros tous mathētas autou prōton prosechete eautois apo tēs zumēs tōn pharisaiōn, ētis estin upokrisis.
luk|12|2|	ouden de sugkekalummenon estin o ouk apokaluphthēsetai, kai krupton o ou gnōsthēsetai
luk|12|3|	anth ōn osa en tē skotia eipate, en tō phōti akousthēsetai, kai o pros to ous elalēsate en tois tameiois, kēruchthēsetai epi tōn dōmatōn.
luk|12|4|	legō de umin tois philois mou mē phobēthēte apo tōn apoktennontōn to sōma, kai meta tauta mē echontōn perissoteron ti poiēsai.

luk|12|9|	o de arnēsamenos me enōpion tōn anthrōpōn aparnēthēsetai enōpion tōn aggelōn tou theou.

luk|12|23|	ouchi ē psuchē pleion esti tēs trophēs kai to sōma tou endumatos?

luk|12|25|	tis de ex umōn merimnōn dunatai prostheinai epi tēn ēlikian autou pēchun ena?

luk|12|37|	makarioi oi douloi ekeinoi, ous elthōn o kurios eurēsei grēgorountas. amēn legō umin oti perizōsetai kai anaklinei autous, kai parelthōn diakonēsei autois.
luk|12|38|	kai ean elthē en tē deutera phulakē kai en tē tritē phulakē elthē kai eurē outō, makarioi eisin oi douloi ekeinoi.

luk|12|42|	eipe de o kurios tis ara estin o pistos oikonomos kai phronimos, on katastēsei o kurios epi tēs therapeias autou tou didonai en kairō to sitometrion?

luk|12|46|	ēxei o kurios tou doulou ekeinou en ēmera ē ou prosdoka kai en ōra ē ou ginōskei, kai dichotomēsei auton, kai to meros autou meta tōn apistōn thēsei.
luk|12|47|	ekeinos de o doulos, o gnous to thelēma tou kuriou eautou kai mē etoimasas mēde poiēsas pros to thelēma autou, darēsetai pollas

luk|12|51|	dokeite oti eirēnēn paregenomēn dounai en tē gē? ouchi, legō umin, all ē diamerismon.

luk|12|53|	diameristhēsontai patēr epi uiō kai uios epi patri, mētēr epi thugatri kai thugatēr epi mētri, penthera epi tēn numphēn autēs kai numphē epi tēn pentheran autēs.
luk|12|54|	elege de kai tois ochlois otan idēte tēn nephelēn anatellousan apo dusmōn, eutheōs legete, ombros erchetai, kai ginetai outō
