luk|13|1|	parēsan de tines en autō tō kairō apaggellontes autō peri tōn galilaiōn, ōn to aima pilatos emixe meta tōn thusiōn autōn.
luk|13|2|	kai apokritheis o iēsous eipen autois dokeite oti oi galilaioi outoi amartōloi para pantas tous galilaious egenonto, oti toiauta peponthasin?
luk|13|3|	ouchi, legō umin, all ean mē metanoēte, pantes ōsautōs apoleisthe.
luk|13|4|	ē ekeinoi oi deka kai oktō, eph ous epesen o purgos en tō silōam kai apekteinen autous, dokeite oti outoi opheiletai egenonto para pantas tous anthrōpous tous katoikountas en ierousalēm?
luk|13|5|	ouchi, legō umin, all ean mē metanoēsēte, pantes omoiōs apoleisthe.
luk|13|6|	elege de tautēn tēn parabolēn sukēn eiche tis en tō ampelōni autou pephuteumenēn, kai ēlthe zētōn karpon en autē, kai ouch euren.
luk|13|7|	eipe de pros ton ampelourgon idou tria etē erchomai zētōn karpon en tē sukē tautē, kai ouch euriskō ekkopson autēn inati kai tēn gēn katargei?
luk|13|8|	o de apokritheis eipen autō kurie, aphes autēn kai touto to etos, eōs otou skapsō peri autēn kai balō kopria.
luk|13|9|	kan men poiēsē karpon ei de mēge, eis to mellon ekkopseis autēn.
luk|13|10|	ēn de didaskōn en mia tōn sunagōgōn en tois sabbasi.
luk|13|11|	kai idou gunē ēn pneuma echousa astheneias etē deka kai oktō, kai ēn sugkuptousa kai mē dunamenē anakupsai eis to panteles.
luk|13|12|	idōn de autēn o iēsous prosephōnēse kai eipen autē gunai, apolelusai tēs astheneias sou
luk|13|13|	kai epethēken autē tas cheiras kai parachrēma anōrthōthē kai edoxaze ton theon.
luk|13|14|	apokritheis de o archisunagōgos, aganaktōn oti tō sabbatō etherapeusen o iēsous, elege tō ochlō ex ēmerai eisin en ais dei ergazesthai en tautais oun erchomenoi therapeuesthe, kai mē tē ēmera tou sabbatou.
luk|13|15|	apekrithē oun autō o kurios kai eipen upokrita, ekastos umōn tō sabbatō ou luei ton boun autou ē ton onon apo tēs phatnēs kai apagagōn potizei?
luk|13|16|	tautēn de, thugatera abraam ousan, ēn edēsen o satanas idou deka kai oktō etē, ouk edei luthēnai apo tou desmou toutou tē ēmera tou sabbatou?
luk|13|17|	kai tauta legontos autou katēschunonto pantes oi antikeimenoi autō, kai pas o ochlos echairen epi pasi tois endoxois tois ginomenois up autou.
luk|13|18|	elege de tini omoia estin ē basileia tou theou, kai tini omoiōsō autēn?
luk|13|19|	omoia esti kokkō sinapeōs, on labōn anthrōpos ebalen eis kēpon eautou kai ēuxēse kai egeneto eis dendron mega, kai ta peteina tou ouranou kateskēnōsen en tois kladois autou.
luk|13|20|	palin eipe tini omoiōsō tēn basileian tou theou?
luk|13|21|	omoia esti zumē, ēn labousa gunē ekrupsen eis aleurou sata tria, eōs ou ezumōthē olon.
luk|13|22|	kai dieporeueto kata poleis kai kōmas didaskōn kai poreian poioumenos eis ierousalēm.
luk|13|23|	eipe de tis autō kurie, ei oligoi oi sōzomenoi? o de eipe pros autous
luk|13|24|	agōnizesthe eiselthein dia tēs stenēs pulēs oti polloi, legō umin, zētēsousin eiselthein kai ouk ischusousin.
luk|13|25|	aph ou an egerthē o oikodespotēs kai apokleisē tēn thuran, kai arxēsthe exō estanai kai krouein tēn thuran legontes kurie kurie, anoixon ēmin kai apokritheis erei umin, ouk oida umas pothen este.
luk|13|26|	tote arxesthe legein ephagomen enōpion sou kai epiomen, kai en tais plateiais ēmōn edidaxas
luk|13|27|	kai erei legō umin, ouk oida umas pothen este apostēte ap emou pantes oi ergatai tēs adikias.
luk|13|28|	ekei estai o klauthmos kai o brugmos tōn odontōn, otan opsēsthe abraam kai isaak kai iakōb kai pantas tous prophētas en tē basileia tou theou, umas de ekballomenous exō,
luk|13|29|	kai ēxousin apo anatolōn kai dusmōn kai apo borra kai notou, kai anaklithēsontai en tē basileia tou theou.
luk|13|30|	kai idou eisin eschatoi oi esontai prōtoi, kai eisi prōtoi oi esontai eschatoi.
luk|13|31|	en autē tē ēmera prosēlthon tines pharisaioi legontes autō exelthe kai poreuou enteuthen, oti ērōdēs thelei se apokteinai.
luk|13|32|	kai eipen autois poreuthentes eipate tē alōpeki tautē idou ekballō daimonia kai iaseis epitelō sēmeron kai aurion, kai tē tritē teleioumai
luk|13|33|	plēn dei me sēmeron kai aurion kai tē echomenē poreuesthai, oti ouk endechetai prophētēn apolesthai exō ierousalēm.
luk|13|34|	ierousalēm ierousalēm, ē apoktennousa tous prophētas kai lithobolousa tous apestalmenous pros autēn! posakis ēthelēsa episunaxai ta tekna sou on tropon ornis tēn eautēs nossian upo tas pterugas, kai ouk ēthelēsate!
luk|13|35|	idou aphietai umin o oikos umōn erēmos. legō de umin oti ou mē me idēte eōs an ēxē ote eipēte eulogēmenos o erchomenos en onomati kuriou.
luk|14|1|	kai egeneto en tō elthein auton eis oikon tinos tōn archontōn tōn pharisaiōn sabbatō phagein arton, kai autoi ēsan paratēroumenoi auton.
luk|14|2|	kai idou anthrōpos tis ēn udrōpikos emprosthen autou.
luk|14|3|	kai apokritheis o iēsous eipe pros tous nomikous kai pharisaious legōn ei exesti tō sabbatō therapeuein?
luk|14|4|	oi de ēsuchasan. kai epilabomenos iasato auton kai apeluse.
luk|14|5|	kai apokritheis pros autous eipe tinos umōn uios ē bous eis phrear empeseitai, kai ouk eutheōs anaspasei auton en tē ēmera tou sabbatou?
luk|14|6|	kai ouk ischusan antapokrithēnai autō pros tauta.
luk|14|7|	elege de pros tous keklēmenous parabolēn, epechōn pōs tas prōtoklisias exelegonto, legōn pros autous
luk|14|8|	otan klēthēs upo tinos eis gamous, mē kataklithēs eis tēn prōtoklisian, mēpote entimoteros sou ē keklēmenos up autou,
luk|14|9|	kai elthōn o se kai auton kalesas erei soi dos toutō topon kai tote arxē met aischunēs ton eschaton topon katechein.
luk|14|10|	all otan klēthēs, poreutheis anapese eis ton eschaton topon, ina otan elthē o keklēkōs se eipē soi phile, prosanabēthi anōteron tote estai soi doxa enōpion tōn sunanakeimenōn soi.
luk|14|11|	oti pas o upsōn eauton tapeinōthēsetai kai o tapeinōn eauton upsōthēsetai.
luk|14|12|	elege de kai tō keklēkoti auton otan poiēs ariston ē deipnon, mē phōnei tous philous sou mēde tous adelphous sou mēde tous suggeneis sou mēde geitonas plousious, mēpote kai autoi se antikalesōsi, kai genēsetai soi antapodoma.
luk|14|13|	all otan poiēs dochēn, kalei ptōchous, anapērous, chōlous, tuphlous,
luk|14|14|	kai makarios esē, oti ouk echousin antapodounai soi antapodothēsetai gar soi en tē anastasei tōn dikaiōn.
luk|14|15|	akousas de tis tōn sunanakeimenōn tauta eipen autō makarios os phagetai ariston en tē basileia tou theou.
luk|14|16|	o de eipen autō anthrōpos tis epoiēse deipnon mega kai ekalese pollous
luk|14|17|	kai apesteile ton doulon autou tē ōra tou deipnou eipein tois keklēmenois erchesthe, oti ēdē etoima esti panta.
luk|14|18|	kai ērxanto apo mias paraiteisthai pantes. o prōtos eipen autō agron ēgorasa, kai echō anagkēn exelthein kai idein auton erōtō se, eche me parētēmenon.
luk|14|19|	kai eteros eipe zeugē boōn ēgorasa pente, kai poreuomai dokimasai auta erōtō se, eche me parētēmenon.
luk|14|20|	kai eteros eipe gunaika egēma, kai dia touto ou dunamai elthein.
luk|14|21|	kai paragenomenos o doulos ekeinos apēggeile tō kuriō autou tauta. tote orgistheis o oikodespotēs eipe tō doulō autou exelthe tacheōs eis tas plateias kai rumas tēs poleōs, kai tous ptōchous kai anapērous kai chōlous kai tuphlous eisagage ōde.
luk|14|22|	kai eipen o doulos kurie, gegonen ōs epetaxas, kai eti topos esti.
luk|14|23|	kai eipen o kurios pros ton doulon exelthe eis tas odous kai phragmous kai anagkason eiselthein, ina gemisthē o oikos mou.
luk|14|24|	legō gar umin oti oudeis tōn andrōn ekeinōn tōn keklēmenōn geusetai mou tou deipnou.
luk|14|25|	suneporeuonto de autō ochloi polloi. kai strapheis eipe pros autous
luk|14|26|	ei tis erchetai pros me kai ou misei ton patera eautou kai tēn mētera kai tēn gunaika kai ta tekna kai tous adelphous kai tas adelphas, eti de kai tēn eautou psuchēn, ou dunatai mou mathētēs einai.
luk|14|27|	kai ostis ou bastazei ton stauron eautou kai erchetai opisō mou, ou dunatai einai mou mathētēs.
luk|14|28|	tis gar ex umōn, thelōn purgon oikodomēsai, ouchi prōton kathisas psēphizei tēn dapanēn, ei echei ta pros apartismon?
luk|14|29|	ina mēpote, thentos autou themelion kai mē ischusantos ektelesai, pantes oi theōrountes arxōntai autō empaizein,
luk|14|30|	legontes oti outos o anthrōpos ērxato oikodomein kai ouk ischusen ektelesai?
luk|14|31|	ē tis basileus, poreuomenos sumbalein eterō basilei eis polemon, ouchi prōton kathisas bouleuetai ei dunatos estin en deka chiliasin apantēsai tō meta eikosi chiliadōn erchomenō ep auton?
luk|14|32|	ei de mēge, eti porrō autou ontos presbeian aposteilas erōta ta pros eirēnēn.
luk|14|33|	outōs oun pas ex umōn, os ouk apotassetai pasi tois eautou uparchousin, ou dunatai einai mou mathētēs.
luk|14|34|	kalon to alas ean de kai to alas mōranthē, en tini artuthēsetai?
luk|14|35|	oute eis gēn oute eis koprian eutheton estin exō ballousin auto. o echōn ōta akouein akouetō.
luk|15|1|	ēsan de eggizontes autō pantes oi telōnai kai oi amartōloi akouein autou.
luk|15|2|	kai diegogguzon oi pharisaioi kai oi grammateis legontes oti outos amartōlous prosdechetai kai sunesthiei autois.
luk|15|3|	eipe de pros autous tēn parabolēn tautēn legōn
luk|15|4|	tis anthrōpos ex umōn echōn ekaton probata, kai apolesas en ex autōn, ou kataleipei ta enenēkonta ennea en tē erēmō kai poreuetai epi to apolōlos eōs ou eurē auto?
luk|15|5|	kai eurōn epitithēsin epi tous ōmous autou chairōn,
luk|15|6|	kai elthōn eis ton oikon sugkalei tous philous kai tous geitonas legōn autois sugcharēte moi oti euron to probaton mou to apolōlos.
luk|15|7|	legō umin oti outō chara estai en tō ouranō epi eni amartōlō metanoounti ē epi enenēkonta ennea dikaiois, oitines ou chreian echousi metanoias.
luk|15|8|	ē tis gunē drachmas echousa deka, ean apolesē drachmēn mian, ouchi aptei luchnon kai saroi tēn oikian kai zētei epimelōs eōs otou eurē?
luk|15|9|	kai eurousa sugkalei tas philas kai tas geitonas legousa sugcharēte moi oti euron tēn drachmēn ēn apōlesa.
luk|15|10|	outō, legō umin, chara ginetai enōpion tōn aggelōn tou theou epi eni amartōlō metanoounti.
luk|15|11|	eipe de anthrōpos tis eiche duo uious.
luk|15|12|	kai eipen o neōteros autōn tō patri pater, dos moi to epiballon meros tēs ousias. kai dieilen autois ton bion.
luk|15|13|	kai met ou pollas ēmeras sunagagōn apanta o neōteros uios apedēmēsen eis chōran makran, kai ekei dieskorpise tēn ousian autou zōn asōtōs.
luk|15|14|	dapanēsantos de autou panta egeneto limos ischuros kata tēn chōran ekeinēn, kai autos ērxato ustereisthai.
luk|15|15|	kai poreutheis ekollēthē eni tōn politōn tēs chōras ekeinēs, kai epempsen auton eis tous agrous autou boskein choirous.
luk|15|16|	kai epethumei gemisai tēn koilian autou apo tōn keratiōn ōn ēsthion oi choiroi, kai oudeis edidou autō.
luk|15|17|	eis eauton de elthōn eipe posoi misthioi tou patros mou perisseuousin artōn, egō de limō apollumai!
luk|15|18|	anastas poreusomai pros ton patera mou kai erō autō pater, ēmarton eis ton ouranon kai enōpion sou.
luk|15|19|	ouketi eimi axios klēthēnai uios sou poiēson me ōs ena tōn misthiōn sou.
luk|15|20|	kai anastas ēlthe pros ton patera autou. eti de autou makran apechontos eiden auton o patēr autou kai esplagchnisthē, kai dramōn epepesen epi ton trachēlon autou kai katephilēsen auton.
luk|15|21|	eipe de autō o uios pater, ēmarton eis ton ouranon kai enōpion sou, kai ouketi eimi axios klēthēnai uios sou.
luk|15|22|	eipe de o patēr pros tous doulous autou exenegkate tēn stolēn tēn prōtēn kai endusate auton, kai dote daktulion eis tēn cheira autou kai upodēmata eis tous podas,
luk|15|23|	kai enegkantes ton moschon ton siteuton thusate, kai phagontes euphranthōmen,
luk|15|24|	oti outos o uios mou nekros ēn kai anezēse, kai apolōlōs ēn kai eurethē. kai ērxanto euphrainesthai.
luk|15|25|	ēn de o uios autou o presbuteros en agrō kai ōs erchomenos ēggise tē oikia, ēkouse sumphōnias kai chorōn,
luk|15|26|	kai proskalesamenos ena tōn paidōn epunthaneto ti eiē tauta.
luk|15|27|	o de eipen autō oti o adelphos sou ēkei kai ethusen o patēr sou ton moschon ton siteuton, oti ugiainonta auton apelaben.
luk|15|28|	ōrgisthē de kai ouk ēthelen eiselthein. o oun patēr autou exelthōn parekalei auton.
luk|15|29|	o de apokritheis eipe tō patri idou tosauta etē douleuō soi kai oudepote entolēn sou parēlthon, kai emoi oudepote edōkas eriphon ina meta tōn philōn mou euphranthō
luk|15|30|	ote de o uios sou outos, o kataphagōn sou ton bion meta pornōn, ēlthen, ethusas autō ton moschon ton siteuton.
luk|15|31|	o de eipen autō teknon, su pantote met emou ei, kai panta ta ema sa estin
luk|15|32|	euphranthēnai de kai charēnai edei, oti o adelphos sou outos nekros ēn kai anezēse, kai apolōlōs ēn kai eurethē.
luk|16|1|	elege de kai pros tous mathētas autou anthrōpos tis ēn plousios, os eichen oikonomon, kai outos dieblēthē autō ōs diaskorpizōn ta uparchonta autou.
luk|16|2|	kai phōnēsas auton eipen autō ti touto akouō peri sou? apodos ton logon tēs oikonomias sou ou gar dunē eti oikonomein.
luk|16|3|	eipe de en eautō o oikonomos ti poiēsō, oti o kurios mou aphaireitai tēn oikonomian ap emou? skaptein ouk ischuō, epaitein aischunomai
luk|16|4|	egnōn ti poiēsō, ina, otan metastathō ek tēs oikonomias, dexōntai me eis tous oikous eautōn.
luk|16|5|	kai proskalesamenos ena ekaston tōn chreōpheiletōn tou kuriou eautou elege tō prōtō poson opheileis su tō kuriō mou?
luk|16|6|	o de eipen ekaton batous elaiou. kai eipen autō dexai sou to gramma kai kathisas tacheōs grapson pentēkonta.
luk|16|7|	epeita eterō eipe su de poson opheileis? o de eipen ekaton korous sitou. kai legei autō dexai sou to gramma kai grapson ogdoēkonta.
luk|16|8|	kai epēnesen o kurios ton oikonomon tēs adikias, oti phronimōs epoiēsen oti oi uioi tou aiōnos toutou phronimōteroi uper tous uious tou phōtos eis tēn genean tēn eautōn eisi.
luk|16|9|	kagō umin legō poiēsate eautois philous ek tou mamōna tēs adikias, ina, otan eklipēte, dexōntai umas eis tas aiōnious skēnas.
luk|16|10|	o pistos en elachistō kai en pollō pistos esti, kai o en elachistō adikos kai en pollō adikos estin.
luk|16|11|	ei oun en tō adikō mamōna pistoi ouk egenesthe, to alēthinon tis umin pisteusei?
luk|16|12|	kai ei en tō allotriō pistoi ouk egenesthe, to umeteron tis umin dōsei?
luk|16|13|	oudeis oiketēs dunatai dusi kuriois douleuein ē gar ton ena misēsei kai ton eteron agapēsei, ē enos anthexetai kai tou eterou kataphronēsei. ou dunasthe theō douleuein kai mamōna.
luk|16|14|	ēkouon de tauta panta kai oi pharisaioi philarguroi uparchontes, kai exemuktērizon auton.
luk|16|15|	kai eipen autois umeis este oi dikaiountes eautous enōpion tōn anthrōpōn, o de theos ginōskei tas kardias umōn oti to en anthrōpois upsēlon bdelugma enōpion tou theou.
luk|16|16|	o nomos kai oi prophētai eōs iōannou apo tote ē basileia tou theou euaggelizetai, kai pas eis autēn biazetai.
luk|16|17|	eukopōteron de esti ton ouranon kai tēn gēn parelthein ē tou nomou mian keraian pesein.
luk|16|18|	pas o apoluōn tēn gunaika autou kai gamōn eteran moicheuei, kai pas o apolelumenēn apo andros gamōn moicheuei.
luk|16|19|	anthrōpos de tis ēn plousios, kai enedidusketo porphuran kai busson euphrainomenos kath ēmeran lamprōs.
luk|16|20|	ptōchos de tis ēn onomati lazaros, os ebeblēto pros ton pulōna autou ēlkōmenos
luk|16|21|	kai epithumōn chortasthēnai apo tōn psichiōn tōn piptontōn apo tēs trapezēs tou plousiou alla kai oi kunes erchomenoi apeleichon ta elkē autou.
luk|16|22|	egeneto de apothanein ton ptōchon kai apenechthēnai auton upo tōn aggelōn eis ton kolpon abraam apethane de kai o plousios kai etaphē.
luk|16|23|	kai en tō adē eparas tous ophthalmous autou, uparchōn en basanois, ora ton abraam apo makrothen kai lazaron en tois kolpois autou.
luk|16|24|	kai autos phōnēsas eipe pater abraam, eleēson me kai pempson lazaron ina bapsē to akron tou daktulou autou udatos kai katapsuxē tēn glōssan mou, oti odunōmai en tē phlogi tautē.
luk|16|25|	eipe de abraam teknon, mnēsthēti oti apelabes su ta agatha sou en tē zōē sou, kai lazaros omoiōs ta kaka nun de ōde parakaleitai, su de odunasai
luk|16|26|	kai epi pasi toutois metaxu ēmōn kai umōn chasma mega estēriktai, opōs oi thelontes diabēnai enthen pros umas mē dunōntai, mēde oi ekeithen pros ēmas diaperōsin.
luk|16|27|	eipe de erōtō oun se, pater, ina pempsēs auton eis ton oikon tou patros mou
luk|16|28|	echō gar pente adelphous opōs diamarturētai autois, ina mē kai autoi elthōsin eis ton topon touton tēs basanou.
luk|16|29|	legei autō abraam echousi mōusea kai tous prophētas akousatōsan autōn.
luk|16|30|	o de eipen ouchi, pater abraam, all ean tis apo nekrōn poreuthē pros autous, metanoēsousin.
luk|16|31|	eipe de autō ei mōuseōs kai tōn prophētōn ouk akouousin, oude ean tis ek nekrōn anastē peisthēsontai.
luk|17|1|	elege de kai pros tous mathētas autou anendekton esti tou mē elthein ta skandala ouai de di ou erchetai.
luk|17|2|	lusitelei autō ei lithos mulikos perikeitai peri ton trachēlon autou kai erriptai eis tēn thalassan, ē ina skandalisē ena tōn mikrōn toutōn.
luk|17|3|	prosechete eautois. ean de amartē eis se o adelphos sou, epitimēson autō kai ean metanoēsē, aphes autō
luk|17|4|	kai ean eptakis tēs ēmeras amartē eis se kai eptakis tēs ēmeras epistrepsē pros se legōn, metanoō, aphēseis autō.
luk|17|5|	kai eipon oi apostoloi tō kuriō prosthes ēmin pistin.
luk|17|6|	eipe de o kurios ei echete pistin ōs kokkon sinapeōs, elegete an tē sukaminō tautē, ekrizōthēti kai phuteuthēti en tē thalassē, kai upēkousen an umin.
luk|17|7|	tis de ex umōn doulon echōn arotriōnta ē poimainonta, os eiselthonti ek tou agrou erei, eutheōs parelthōn anapese,
luk|17|8|	all ouchi erei autō etoimason ti deipnēsō, kai perizōsamenos diakonei moi eōs phagō kai piō, kai meta tauta phagesai kai piesai su?
luk|17|9|	mē charin echei tō doulō ekeinō oti epoiēse ta diatachthenta? ou dokō.
luk|17|10|	outō kai umeis, otan poiēsēte panta ta diatachthenta umin, legete oti douloi achreioi esmen, oti o ōpheilomen poiēsai pepoiēkamen.
luk|17|11|	kai egeneto en tō poreuesthai auton eis ierousalēm kai autos diērcheto dia mesou samareias kai galilaias.
luk|17|12|	kai eiserchomenou autou eis tina kōmēn apēntēsan autō deka leproi andres, oi estēsan porrōthen,
luk|17|13|	kai autoi ēran phōnēn legontes iēsou epistata, eleēson ēmas.
luk|17|14|	kai idōn eipen autois poreuthentes epideixate eautous tois iereusi. kai egeneto en tō upagein autous ekatharisthēsan.
luk|17|15|	eis de ex autōn, idōn oti iathē, upestrepse meta phōnēs megalēs doxazōn ton theon,
luk|17|16|	kai epesen epi prosōpon para tous podas autou eucharistōn autō kai autos ēn samareitēs.
luk|17|17|	apokritheis de o iēsous eipen ouchi oi deka ekatharisthēsan? oi de ennea pou?
luk|17|18|	ouch eurethēsan upostrepsantes dounai doxan tō theō ei mē o allogenēs outos?
luk|17|19|	kai eipen autō anastas poreuou ē pistis sou sesōke se.
luk|17|20|	eperōtētheis de upo tōn pharisaiōn pote erchetai ē basileia tou theou, apekrithē autois kai eipen ouk erchetai ē basileia tou theou meta paratērēseōs,
luk|17|21|	oude erousin idou ōde ē idou ekei idou gar ē basileia tou theou entos umōn estin.
luk|17|22|	eipe de pros tous mathētas eleusontai ēmerai ote epithumēsete mian tōn ēmerōn tou uiou tou anthrōpou idein, kai ouk opsesthe.
luk|17|23|	kai erousin umin idou ōde, idou ekei mē apelthēte mēde diōxēte.
luk|17|24|	ōsper gar ē astrapē astraptousa ek tēs up ouranon eis tēn up ouranon lampei, outōs estai kai o uios tou anthrōpou en tē ēmera autou.
luk|17|25|	prōton de dei auton polla pathein kai apodokimasthēnai apo tēs geneas tautēs.
luk|17|26|	kai kathōs egeneto en tais ēmerais nōe, outōs estai kai en tais ēmerais tou uiou tou anthrōpou
luk|17|27|	ēsthion, epinon, egamoun, exegamizonto, achri ēs ēmeras eisēlthe nōe eis tēn kibōton, kai ēlthen o kataklusmos kai apōlesen apantas.
luk|17|28|	omoiōs kai ōs egeneto en tais ēmerais lōt ēsthion, epinon, ēgorazon, epōloun, ephuteuon, ōkodomoun
luk|17|29|	ē de ēmera exēlthe lōt apo sodomōn, ebrexe pur kai theion ap ouranou kai apōlesen apantas.
luk|17|30|	kata ta auta estai ē ēmera o uios tou anthrōpou apokaluptetai.
luk|17|31|	en ekeinē tē ēmera os estai epi tou dōmatos kai ta skeuē autou en tē oikia, mē katabatō arai auta, kai o en tō agrō omoiōs mē epistrepsatō eis ta opisō.
luk|17|32|	mnēmoneuete tēs gunaikos lōt.
luk|17|33|	os ean zētēsē tēn psuchēn autou sōsai, apolesei autēn, kai os ean apolesē autēn, zōogonēsei autēn.
luk|17|34|	legō umin, tautē tē nukti duo esontai epi klinēs mias, eis paralēphthēsetai kai o eteros aphethēsetai
luk|17|35|	duo esontai alēthousai epi to auto, mia paralēphthēsetai kai ē etera aphethēsetai
luk|17|36|	duo en tō agrō, eis paralēphthēsetai kai o eteros aphethēsetai.
luk|17|37|	kai apokrithentes legousin autō pou, kurie? o de eipen autois opou to sōma, ekei episunachthēsontai kai oi aetoi.
luk|18|1|	elege de kai parabolēn autois pros to dein pantote proseuchesthai autous kai mē ekkakein,
luk|18|2|	legōn kritēs tis ēn en tini polei ton theon mē phoboumenos kai anthrōpon mē entrepomenos.
luk|18|3|	chēra de ēn en tē polei ekeinē, kai ērcheto pros auton legousa ekdikēson me apo tou antidikou mou.
luk|18|4|	kai ouk ēthelēsen epi chronon meta de tauta eipen en eautō ei kai ton theon ou phoboumai kai anthrōpon ouk entrepomai,
luk|18|5|	dia ge to parechein moi kopon tēn chēran tautēn ekdikēsō autēn, ina mē eis telos erchomenē upōpiazē me.
luk|18|6|	eipe de o kurios akousate ti o kritēs tēs adikias legei
luk|18|7|	o de theos ou mē poiēsē tēn ekdikēsin tōn eklektōn autou tōn boōntōn pros auton ēmeras kai nuktos, kai makrothumōn ep autois?
luk|18|8|	legō umin oti poiēsei tēn ekdikēsin autōn en tachei. plēn o uios tou anthrōpou elthōn ara eurēsei tēn pistin epi tēs gēs?
luk|18|9|	eipe de kai pros tinas tous pepoithotas eph eautois oti eisi dikaioi, kai exouthenountas tous loipous, tēn parabolēn tautēn
luk|18|10|	anthrōpoi duo anebēsan eis to ieron proseuxasthai, o eis pharisaios kai o eteros telōnēs.
luk|18|11|	o pharisaios statheis pros eauton tauta prosēucheto o theos, eucharistō soi oti ouk eimi ōsper oi loipoi tōn anthrōpōn, arpages, adikoi, moichoi, ē kai ōs outos o telōnēs
luk|18|12|	nēsteuō dis tou sabbatou, apodekatō panta osa ktōmai.
luk|18|13|	kai o telōnēs makrothen estōs ouk ēthelen oude tous ophthalmous eis ton ouranon eparai, all etupten eis to stēthos autou legōn o theos, ilasthēti moi tō amartōlō.
luk|18|14|	legō umin, katebē outos dedikaiōmenos eis ton oikon autou ē gar ekeinos oti pas o upsōn eauton tapeinōthēsetai, o de tapeinōn eauton upsōthēsetai.
luk|18|15|	prosepheron de autō kai ta brephē ina autōn aptētai kai idontes oi mathētai epetimēsan autois.
luk|18|16|	o de iēsous proskalesamenos auta eipen aphete ta paidia erchesthai pros me kai mē kōluete auta tōn gar toioutōn estin ē basileia tou theou.
luk|18|17|	amēn legō umin, os ean mē dexētai tēn basileian tou theou ōs paidion, ou mē eiselthē eis autēn.
luk|18|18|	kai epērōtēse tis auton archōn legōn didaskale agathe, ti poiēsas zōēn aiōnion klēronomēsō?
luk|18|19|	eipe de autō o iēsous ti me legeis agathon? oudeis agathos ei mē eis o theos.
luk|18|20|	tas entolas oidas mē moicheusēs, mē phoneusēs, mē klepsēs, mē pseudomarturēsēs, tima ton patera sou kai tēn mētera sou.
luk|18|21|	o de eipe tauta panta ephulaxamēn ek neotētos mou.
luk|18|22|	akousas de tauta o iēsous eipen autō eti en soi leipei panta osa echeis pōlēson kai diados ptōchois, kai exeis thēsauron en ouranō, kai deuro akolouthei moi.
luk|18|23|	o de akousas tauta perilupos egeneto ēn gar plousios sphodra.
luk|18|24|	idōn de auton o iēsous perilupon genomenon eipe pōs duskolōs oi ta chrēmata echontes eiseleusontai eis tēn basileian tou theou!
luk|18|25|	eukopōteron gar esti kamēlon dia trumalias raphidos eiselthein ē plousion eis tēn basileian tou theou eiselthein.
luk|18|26|	eipon de oi akousantes kai tis dunatai sōthēnai?
luk|18|27|	o de eipe ta adunata para anthrōpois dunata para tō theō estin.
luk|18|28|	eipe de o petros idou ēmeis aphēkamen panta kai ēkolouthēsamen soi.
luk|18|29|	o de eipen autois amēn legō umin oti oudeis estin os aphēken oikian ē goneis ē adelphous ē gunaika ē tekna eneken tēs basileias tou theou,
luk|18|30|	os ou mē apolabē pollaplasiona en tō kairō toutō kai en tō aiōni tō erchomenō zōēn aiōnion.
luk|18|31|	paralabōn de tous dōdeka eipe pros autous idou anabainomen eis ierosoluma kai teleiōthēsetai panta ta gegrammena dia tōn prophētōn tō uiō tou anthrōpou.
luk|18|32|	paradothēsetai gar tois ethnesi kai empaichthēsetai kai ubristhēsetai kai emptusthēsetai,
luk|18|33|	kai mastigōsantes apoktenousin auton, kai tē ēmera tē tritē anastēsetai.
luk|18|34|	kai autoi ouden toutōn sunēkan, kai ēn to rēma touto kekrummenon ap autōn, kai ouk eginōskon ta legomena.
luk|18|35|	egeneto de en tō eggizein auton eis ierichō tuphlos tis ekathēto para tēn odon prosaitōn
luk|18|36|	akousas de ochlou diaporeuomenou epunthaneto ti eiē tauta.
luk|18|37|	apēggeilan de autō oti iēsous o nazōraios parerchetai.
luk|18|38|	kai eboēse legōn iēsou uie dauid, eleēson me
luk|18|39|	kai oi proagontes epetimōn autō ina siōpēsē autos de pollō mallon ekrazen uie dauid, eleēson me.
luk|18|40|	statheis de o iēsous ekeleusen auton achthēnai pros auton. eggisantos de autou epērōtēsen auton legōn
luk|18|41|	ti soi theleis poiēsō? o de eipe kurie, ina anablepsō.
luk|18|42|	kai o iēsous eipen autō anablepson ē pistis sou sesōke se.
luk|18|43|	kai parachrēma aneblepse, kai ēkolouthei autō doxazōn ton theon kai pas o laos idōn edōken ainon tō theō.
luk|19|1|	kai eiselthōn diērcheto tēn ierichō
luk|19|2|	kai idou anēr onomati kaloumenos zakchaios, kai autos ēn architelōnēs, kai outos ēn plousios,
luk|19|3|	kai ezētei idein ton iēsoun tis esti, kai ouk ēdunato apo tou ochlou, oti tē ēlikia mikros ēn.
luk|19|4|	kai prodramōn emprosthen anebē epi sukomorean, ina idē auton, oti ekeinēs ēmelle dierchesthai.
luk|19|5|	kai ōs ēlthen epi ton topon, anablepsas o iēsous eiden auton kai eipe pros auton zakchaie, speusas katabēthi sēmeron gar en tō oikō sou dei me meinai.
luk|19|6|	kai speusas katebē, kai upedexato auton chairōn.
luk|19|7|	kai idontes pantes diegogguzon legontes oti para amartōlō andri eisēlthe katalusai.
luk|19|8|	statheis de zakchaios eipe pros ton kurion idou ta ēmisē tōn uparchontōn mou, kurie, didōmi tois ptōchois, kai ei tinos ti esukophantēsa, apodidōmi tetraploun.
luk|19|9|	eipe de pros auton o iēsous oti sēmeron sōtēria tō oikō toutō egeneto, kathoti kai autos uios abraam estin.
luk|19|10|	ēlthe gar o uios tou anthrōpou zētēsai kai sōsai to apolōlos.
luk|19|11|	akouontōn de autōn tauta prostheis eipe parabolēn, dia to eggus auton einai ierousalēm kai dokein autous oti parachrēma mellei ē basileia tou theou anaphainesthai
luk|19|12|	eipen oun anthrōpos tis eugenēs eporeuthē eis chōran makran labein eautō basileian kai upostrepsai.
luk|19|13|	kalesas de deka doulous eautou edōken autois deka mnas kai eipe pros autous pragmateusasthe en ō erchomai.
luk|19|14|	oi de politai autou emisoun auton, kai apesteilan presbeian opisō autou legontes ou thelomen touton basileusai eph ēmas.
luk|19|15|	kai egeneto en tō epanelthein auton labonta tēn basileian, kai eipe phōnēthēnai autō tous doulous toutous ois edōke to argurion, ina epignō tis ti diepragmateusato.
luk|19|16|	paregeneto de o prōtos legōn kurie, ē mna sou proseirgasato deka mnas.
luk|19|17|	kai eipen autō eu, agathe doule! oti en elachistō pistos egenou, isthi exousian echōn epanō deka poleōn.
luk|19|18|	kai ēlthen o deuteros legōn kurie, ē mna sou epoiēse pente mnas.
luk|19|19|	eipe de kai toutō kai su ginou epanō pente poleōn.
luk|19|20|	kai eteros ēlthe legōn kurie, idou ē mna sou, ēn eichon apokeimenēn en soudariō.
luk|19|21|	ephoboumēn gar se, oti anthrōpos austēros ei aireis o ouk ethēkas, kai therizeis o ouk espeiras, kai sunageis othen ou dieskorpisas.
luk|19|22|	legei autō ek tou stomatos sou krinō se, ponēre doule. ēdeis oti anthrōpos austēros eimi egō, airōn o ouk ethēka, kai therizōn o ouk espeira, kai sunagōn othen ou dieskorpisa
luk|19|23|	kai diati ouk edōkas to argurion mou epi tēn trapezan, kai egō elthōn sun tokō an epraxa auto?
luk|19|24|	kai tois parestōsin eipen arate ap autou tēn mnan kai dote tō tas deka mnas echonti.
luk|19|25|	kai eipon autō kurie, echei deka mnas.
luk|19|26|	legō gar umin oti panti tō echonti dothēsetai, apo de tou mē echontos kai o echei arthēsetai ap autou.
luk|19|27|	plēn tous echthrous mou ekeinous, tous mē thelēsantas me basileusai ep autous, agagete ōde kai katasphaxate autous emprosthen mou.
luk|19|28|	kai eipōn tauta eporeueto emprosthen anabainōn eis ierosoluma.
luk|19|29|	kai egeneto ōs ēggisen eis bēthsphagē kai bēthanian pros to oros to kaloumenon elaiōn, apesteile duo tōn mathētōn autou
luk|19|30|	eipōn upagete eis tēn katenanti kōmēn, en ē eisporeuomenoi eurēsete pōlon dedemenon, eph on oudeis pōpote anthrōpōn ekathise lusantes auton agagete.
luk|19|31|	kai ean tis umas erōta, diati luete? outōs ereite autō, oti o kurios autou chreian echei.
luk|19|32|	apelthontes de oi apestalmenoi euron kathōs eipen autois, estōta ton pōlon
luk|19|33|	luontōn de autōn ton pōlon eipon oi kurioi autou pros autous ti luete ton pōlon?
luk|19|34|	oi de eipon oti o kurios autou chreian echei.
luk|19|35|	kai ēgagon auton pros ton iēsoun, kai epirripsantes eautōn ta imatia epi ton pōlon epebibasan ton iēsoun.
luk|19|36|	poreuomenou de autou upestrōnnuon ta imatia autōn en tē odō.
luk|19|37|	eggizontos de autou ēdē pros tē katabasei tou orous tōn elaiōn ērxato apan to plēthos tōn mathētōn chairontes ainein ton theon phōnē megalē peri pasōn ōn eidon dunameōn
luk|19|38|	legontes eulogēmenos o erchomenos basileus en onomati kuriou eirēnē en ouranō kai doxa en upsistois.
luk|19|39|	kai tines tōn pharisaiōn apo tou ochlou eipon pros auton didaskale, epitimēson tois mathētais sou.
luk|19|40|	kai apokritheis eipen autois legō umin oti ean outoi siōpēsōsin, oi lithoi kekraxontai.
luk|19|41|	kai ōs ēggisen, idōn tēn polin eklausen ep autē,
luk|19|42|	legōn oti ei egnōs kai su, kai ge en tē ēmera sou tautē, ta pros eirēnēn sou! nun de ekrubē apo ophthalmōn sou
luk|19|43|	oti ēxousin ēmerai epi se kai peribalousin oi echthroi sou charaka soi kai perikuklōsousi se kai sunexousi se pantothen,
luk|19|44|	kai edaphiousi se kai ta tekna sou en soi, kai ouk aphēsousin en soi lithon epi lithō, anth ōn ouk egnōs ton kairon tēs episkopēs sou.
luk|19|45|	kai eiselthōn eis to ieron ērxato ekballein tous pōlountas en autō kai agorazontas
luk|19|46|	legōn autois gegraptai oti o oikos mou oikos proseuchēs estin umeis de auton epoiēsate spēlaion lēstōn.

luk|20|1|	kai egeneto en mia tōn ēmerōn ekeinōn didaskontos autou ton laon en tō ierō kai euaggelizomenou epestēsan oi iereis kai oi grammateis sun tois presbuterois
luk|20|2|	kai eipon pros auton legontes eipe ēmin en poia exousia tauta poieis, ē tis estin o dous soi tēn exousian tautēn?
luk|20|3|	apokritheis de eipe pros autous erōtēsō umas kagō ena logon, kai eipate moi
luk|20|4|	to baptisma iōannou ex ouranou ēn ē ex anthrōpōn?
luk|20|5|	oi de sunelogisanto pros eautous legontes oti ean eipōmen, ex ouranou, erei, diati oun ouk episteusate autō?
luk|20|6|	ean de eipōmen, ex anthrōpōn, pas o laos katalithasei ēmas pepeismenos gar estin iōannēn prophētēn einai.
luk|20|7|	kai apekrithēsan mē eidenai pothen.

luk|20|10|	kai en tō kairō apesteile pros tous geōrgous doulon ina apo tou karpou tou ampelōnos dōsousin autō oi de geōrgoi deirantes auton exapesteilan kenon.
luk|20|11|	kai prosetheto autois pempsai eteron doulon. oi de kakeinon deirantes kai atimasantes exapesteilan kenon.
luk|20|12|	kai prosetheto pempsai triton. oi de kai touton traumatisantes exebalon.
luk|20|13|	eipe de o kurios tou ampelōnos ti poiēsō? pempsō ton uion mou ton agapēton isōs touton idontes entrapēsontai.
luk|20|14|	idontes de auton oi geōrgoi dielogizonto pros eautous legontes outos estin o klēronomos deute apokteinōmen auton, ina ēmōn genētai ē klēronomia.
luk|20|15|	kai ekbalontes auton exō tou ampelōnos apekteinan. ti oun poiēsei autois o kurios tou ampelōnos?
luk|20|16|	eleusetai kai apolesei tous geōrgous toutous, kai dōsei ton ampelōna allois. akousantes de eipon mē genoito.
luk|20|17|	o de emblepsas autois eipe ti oun esti to gegrammenon touto, lithon on apedokimasan oi oikodomountes, outos egenēthē eis kephalēn gōnias?
luk|20|18|	pas o pesōn ep ekeinon ton lithon sunthlasthēsetai eph on d an pesē, likmēsei auton.
luk|20|19|	kai ezētēsan oi archiereis kai oi grammateis epibalein ep auton tas cheiras en autē tē ōra, kai ephobēthēsan ton laon egnōsan gar oti pros autous tas parabolas elege.
luk|20|20|	kai paratērēsantes apesteilan egkathetous, upokrinomenous eautous dikaious einai, ina epilabōntai autou logou eis to paradounai auton tē archē kai tē exousia tou ēgemonos.
luk|20|21|	kai epērōtēsan auton legontes didaskale, oidamen oti orthōs legeis kai didaskeis, kai ou lambaneis prosōpon, all ep alētheias tēn odon tou theou didaskeis
luk|20|22|	exestin ēmin kaisari phoron dounai ē ou?
luk|20|23|	katanoēsas de autōn tēn panourgian eipe pros autous ti me peirazete?
luk|20|24|	deixate moi dēnarion tinos echei eikona kai epigraphēn? apokrithentes de eipon kaisaros.
luk|20|25|	o de eipen autois apodote toinun ta kaisaros kaisari kai ta tou theou tō theō.

luk|20|28|	legontes didaskale, mōusēs egrapsen ēmin, ean tinos adelphos apothanē echōn gunaika, kai outos ateknos apothanē, ina labē o adelphos autou tēn gunaika kai exanastēsē sperma tō adelphō autou.
luk|20|29|	epta oun adelphoi ēsan kai o prōtos labōn gunaika apethanen ateknos
luk|20|30|	kai elaben o deuteros tēn gunaika, kai outos apethanen ateknos

luk|20|32|	usteron de pantōn kai ē gunē apethanen.
luk|20|33|	en tē anastasei oun tinos autōn ginetai gunē? oi gar epta eschon autēn gunaika.
luk|20|34|	kai apokritheis eipen autois o iēsous oi uioi tou aiōnos toutou gamousi kai ekgamizontai
luk|20|35|	oi de kataxiōthentes tou aiōnos ekeinou tuchein kai tēs anastaseōs tēs ek nekrōn oute gamousin oute gamizontai
luk|20|36|	oute gar apothanein eti dunantai isaggeloi gar eisi kai uioi eisi tou theou, tēs anastaseōs uioi ontes.
luk|20|37|	oti de egeirontai oi nekroi, kai mōusēs emēnusen epi tēs batou, ōs legei kurion ton theon abraam kai ton theon isaak kai ton theon iakōb.
luk|20|38|	theos de ouk esti nekrōn, alla zōntōn pantes gar autō zōsin.

luk|20|40|	ouketi de etolmōn eperōtan auton ouden.

luk|20|43|	eōs an thō tous echthrous sou upopodion tōn podōn sou.

luk|20|47|	oi katesthiousi tas oikias tōn chērōn kai prophasei makra proseuchontai outoi lēpsontai perissoteron krima.
luk|21|1|	anablepsas de eide tous ballontas ta dōra autōn eis to gazophulakion plousious
luk|21|2|	eide de tina chēran penichran ballousan ekei duo lepta,
luk|21|3|	kai eipen alēthōs legō umin oti ē chēra ē ptōchē autē pleion pantōn ebalen
luk|21|4|	apantes gar outoi ek tou perisseuontos autois ebalon eis ta dōra tou theou, autē de ek tou usterēmatos autēs apanta ton bion on eichen ebale.
luk|21|5|	kai tinōn legontōn peri tou ierou oti lithois kalois kai anathēmasi kekosmētai, eipe
luk|21|6|	tauta a theōreite, eleusontai ēmerai en ais ouk aphethēsetai lithos epi lithō os ou kataluthēsetai.
luk|21|7|	epērōtēsan de auton legontes didaskale, pote oun tauta estai, kai ti to sēmeion otan mellē tauta ginesthai?
luk|21|8|	o de eipe blepete mē planēthēte polloi gar eleusontai epi tō onomati mou legontes oti egō eimi kai o kairos ēggike. mē oun poreuthēte opisō autōn.
luk|21|9|	otan de akousēte polemous kai akatastasias, mē ptoēthēte dei gar tauta genesthai prōton, all ouk eutheōs to telos.
luk|21|10|	tote elegen autois egerthēsetai ethnos epi ethnos kai basileia epi basileian,
luk|21|11|	seismoi te megaloi kata topous kai limoi kai loimoi esontai, phobētra te kai sēmeia ap ouranou megala estai.
luk|21|12|	pro de toutōn pantōn epibalousin eph umas tas cheiras autōn kai diōxousi, paradidontes eis sunagōgas kai phulakas, agomenous epi basileis kai ēgemonas eneken tou onomatos mou
luk|21|13|	apobēsetai de umin eis marturion.
luk|21|14|	thesthe oun eis tas kardias umōn mē promeletan apologēthēnai
luk|21|15|	egō gar dōsō umin stoma kai sophian, ē ou dunēsontai anteipein oude antistēnai pantes oi antikeimenoi umin.
luk|21|16|	paradothēsesthe de kai upo goneōn kai suggenōn kai philōn kai adelphōn, kai thanatōsousin ex umōn,
luk|21|17|	kai esesthe misoumenoi upo pantōn dia to onoma mou
luk|21|18|	kai thrix ek tēs kephalēs umōn ou mē apolētai
luk|21|19|	en tē upomonē umōn ktēsasthe tas psuchas umōn.
luk|21|20|	otan de idēte kukloumenēn upo stratopedōn tēn ierousalēm, tote gnōte oti ēggiken ē erēmōsis autēs.
luk|21|21|	tote oi en tē ioudaia pheugetōsan eis ta orē, kai oi en mesō autēs ekchōreitōsan, kai oi en tais chōrais mē eiserchesthōsan eis autēn,
luk|21|22|	oti ēmerai ekdikēseōs autai eisi tou plērōthēnai panta ta gegrammena.
luk|21|23|	ouai de tais en gastri echousais kai tais thēlazousais en ekeinais tais ēmerais estai gar tote anagkē megalē epi tēs gēs kai orgē tō laō toutō,
luk|21|24|	kai pesountai stomati machairas, kai aichmalōtisthēsontai eis panta ta ethnē, kai ierousalēm estai patoumenē upo ethnōn achri plērōthōsi kairoi ethnōn.
luk|21|25|	kai estai sēmeia en ēliō kai selēnē kai astrois, kai epi tēs gēs sunochē ethnōn en aporia ēchousēs thalassēs kai salou,
luk|21|26|	apopsuchontōn anthrōpōn apo phobou kai prosdokias tōn eperchomenōn tē oikoumenē ai gar dunameis tōn ouranōn saleuthēsontai.
luk|21|27|	kai tote opsontai ton uion tou anthrōpou erchomenon en nephelē meta dunameōs kai doxēs pollēs.
luk|21|28|	archomenōn de toutōn ginesthai anakupsate kai eparate tas kephalas umōn, dioti eggizei ē apolutrōsis umōn.
luk|21|29|	kai eipe parabolēn autois idete tēn sukēn kai panta ta dendra.
luk|21|30|	otan probalōsin ēdē, blepontes aph eautōn ginōskete oti ēdē eggus to theros estin.
luk|21|31|	outō kai umeis, otan idēte tauta ginomena, ginōskete oti eggus estin ē basileia tou theou.
luk|21|32|	amēn legō umin oti ou mē parelthē ē genea autē eōs an panta genētai.
luk|21|33|	o ouranos kai ē gē pareleusontai, oi de logoi mou ou mē parelthōsi.
luk|21|34|	prosechete de eautois mēpote barēthōsin umōn ai kardiai en kraipalē kai methē kai merimnais biotikais, kai aiphnidios eph umas epistē ē ēmera ekeinē
luk|21|35|	ōs pagis gar epeleusetai epi pantas tous kathēmenous epi prosōpon pasēs tēs gēs.
luk|21|36|	agrupneite oun en panti kairō deomenoi ina kataxiōthēte ekphugein panta ta mellonta ginesthai kai stathēnai emprosthen tou uiou tou anthrōpou.
luk|21|37|	ēn de tas ēmeras en tō ierō didaskōn, tas de nuktas exerchomenos ēulizeto eis to oros to kaloumenon elaiōn
luk|21|38|	kai pas o laos ōrthrize pros auton en tō ierō akouein autou.
luk|22|1|	ēggize de ē eortē tōn azumōn ē legomenē pascha.
luk|22|2|	kai ezētoun oi archiereis kai oi grammateis to pōs anelōsin auton ephobounto gar ton laon.
luk|22|3|	eisēlthe de o satanas eis ioudan ton epikaloumenon iskariōtēn, onta ek tou arithmou tōn dōdeka,
luk|22|4|	kai apelthōn sunelalēse tois archiereusi kai grammateusi kai stratēgois to pōs auton paradō autois.
luk|22|5|	kai echarēsan, kai sunethento autō arguria dounai
luk|22|6|	kai exōmologēse, kai ezētei eukairian tou paradounai auton autois ater ochlou.
luk|22|7|	ēlthe de ē ēmera tōn azumōn, en ē edei thuesthai to pascha,
luk|22|8|	kai apesteile petron kai iōannēn eipōn poreuthentes etoimasate ēmin to pascha ina phagōmen.
luk|22|9|	oi de eipon autō pou theleis etoimasōmen?
luk|22|10|	o de eipen autois idou eiselthontōn umōn eis tēn polin sunantēsei umin anthrōpos keramion udatos bastazōn akolouthēsate autō eis tēn oikian ou eisporeuetai,
luk|22|11|	kai ereite tō oikodespotē tēs oikias legei soi o didaskalos, pou esti to kataluma opou to pascha meta tōn mathētōn mou phagō?
luk|22|12|	kakeinos umin deixei anōgaion mega estrōmenon ekei etoimasate.
luk|22|13|	apelthontes de euron kathōs eirēken autois, kai ētoimasan to pascha.
luk|22|14|	kai ote egeneto ē ōra, anepese, kai oi dōdeka apostoloi sun autō.
luk|22|15|	kai eipe pros autous epithumia epethumēsa touto to pascha phagein meth umōn pro tou me pathein
luk|22|16|	legō gar umin oti ouketi ou mē phagō ex autou eōs otou plērōthē en tē basileia tou theou.
luk|22|17|	kai dexamenos to potērion eucharistēsas eipe labete touto kai diamerisate eautois
luk|22|18|	legō gar umin oti ou mē piō apo tou genēmatos tēs ampelou eōs otou ē basileia tou theou elthē.
luk|22|19|	kai labōn arton eucharistēsas eklase kai edōken autois legōn touto esti to sōma mou to uper umōn didomenon touto poieite eis tēn emēn anamnēsin.
luk|22|20|	ōsautōs kai to potērion meta to deipnēsai legōn touto to potērion ē kainē diathēkē en tō aimati mou, to uper umōn ekchunomenon.
luk|22|21|	plēn idou ē cheir tou paradidontos me met emou epi tēs trapezēs.
luk|22|22|	kai o men uios tou anthrōpou poreuetai kata to ōrismenon plēn ouai tō anthrōpō ekeinō di ou paradidotai.
luk|22|23|	kai autoi ērxanto suzētein pros eautous to tis ara eiē ex autōn o touto mellōn prassein.
luk|22|24|	egeneto de kai philoneikia en autois, to tis autōn dokei einai meizōn.
luk|22|25|	o de eipen autois oi basileis tōn ethnōn kurieuousin autōn, kai oi exousiazontes autōn euergetai kalountai
luk|22|26|	umeis de ouch outōs, all o meizōn en umin ginesthō ōs o neōteros, kai o ēgoumenos ōs o diakonōn.
luk|22|27|	tis gar meizōn, o anakeimenos ē o diakonōn? ouchi o anakeimenos? egō de eimi en mesō umōn ōs o diakonōn.
luk|22|28|	umeis de este oi diamemenēkotes met emou en tois peirasmois mou
luk|22|29|	kagō diatithemai umin kathōs dietheto moi o patēr mou basileian,
luk|22|30|	ina esthiēte kai pinēte epi tēs trapezēs mou en tē basileia mou, kai kathisesthe epi thronōn krinontes tas dōdeka phulas tou israēl.
luk|22|31|	eipe de o kurios simōn simōn, idou o satanas exētēsato umas tou siniasai ōs ton siton
luk|22|32|	egō de edeēthēn peri sou ina mē eklipē ē pistis sou kai su pote epistrepsas stērixon tous adelphous sou.
luk|22|33|	o de eipen autō kurie, meta sou etoimos eimi kai eis phulakēn kai eis thanaton poreuesthai.
luk|22|34|	o de eipe legō soi, petre, ou phōnēsei sēmeron alektōr prin ē tris aparnēsē mē eidenai me.
luk|22|35|	kai eipen autois ote apesteila umas ater ballantiou kai pēras kai upodēmatōn, mē tinos usterēthēte? oi de eipon outhenos.
luk|22|36|	eipen oun autois alla nun o echōn ballantion aratō, omoiōs kai pēran, kai o mē echōn pōlēsei to imation autou kai agorasei machairan.
luk|22|37|	legō gar umin oti eti touto to gegrammenon dei telesthēnai en emoi, to kai meta anomōn elogisthē kai gar ta peri emou telos echei.
luk|22|38|	oi de eipon kurie, idou machairai ōde duo. o de eipen autois ikanon esti.
luk|22|39|	kai exelthōn eporeuthē kata to ethos eis to oros tōn elaiōn ēkolouthēsan de autō kai oi mathētai autou.
luk|22|40|	genomenos de epi tou topou eipen autois proseuchesthe mē eiselthein eis peirasmon.
luk|22|41|	kai autos apespasthē ap autōn ōsei lithou bolēn, kai theis ta gonata prosēucheto
luk|22|42|	legōn pater, ei boulei parenegkein touto to potērion ap emou plēn mē to thelēma mou, alla to son ginesthō.
luk|22|43|	ōphthē de autō aggelos ap ouranou enischuōn auton.
luk|22|44|	kai genomenos en agōnia ektenesteron prosēucheto. egeneto de o idrōs autou ōsei thromboi aimatos katabainontes epi tēn gēn.
luk|22|45|	kai anastas apo tēs proseuchēs, elthōn pros tous mathētas euren autous koimōmenous apo tēs lupēs,
luk|22|46|	kai eipen autois ti katheudete? anastantes proseuchesthe, ina mē eiselthēte eis peirasmon.
luk|22|47|	eti de autou lalountos idou ochlos, kai o legomenos ioudas, eis tōn dōdeka, proēgen autous, kai ēggise tō iēsou philēsai auton touto gar sēmeion dedōkei autois on an philēsō, autos estin.
luk|22|48|	o de iēsous eipen autō iouda, philēmati ton uion tou anthrōpou paradidōs?
luk|22|49|	idontes de oi peri auton to esomenon eipon autō kurie, ei pataxomen en machaira?
luk|22|50|	kai epataxen eis tis ex autōn ton doulon tou archiereōs kai apheilen autou to ous to dexion.
luk|22|51|	apokritheis de o iēsous eipen eate eōs toutou kai apsamenos tou ōtiou autou iasato auton.
luk|22|52|	eipe de o iēsous pros tous paragenomenous ep auton archiereis kai stratēgous tou ierou kai presbuterous ōs epi lēstēn exelēluthate meta machairōn kai xulōn.
luk|22|53|	kath ēmeran ontos mou meth umōn en tō ierō ouk exeteinate tas cheiras ep eme. all autē estin umōn ē ōra kai ē exousia tou skotous.
luk|22|54|	sullabontes de auton ēgagon kai eisēgagon auton eis ton oikon tou archiereōs. o de petros ēkolouthei makrothen.
luk|22|55|	apsantōn de puran en mesō tēs aulēs kai sugkathisantōn autōn ekathēto o petros en mesō autōn.
luk|22|56|	idousa de auton paidiskē tis kathēmenon pros to phōs kai atenisasa autō eipe kai outos sun autō ēn.
luk|22|57|	o de ērnēsato legōn gunai, ouk oida auton.
luk|22|58|	kai meta brachu eteros idōn auton ephē kai su ex autōn ei. o de petros eipen anthrōpe, ouk eimi.
luk|22|59|	kai diastasēs ōsei ōras mias allos tis diischurizeto legōn ep alētheias kai outos met autou ēn kai gar galilaios estin.
luk|22|60|	eipe de o petros anthrōpe, ouk oida o legeis. kai parachrēma, eti lalountos autou, ephōnēsen alektōr.
luk|22|61|	kai strapheis o kurios eneblepse tō petrō, kai upemnēsthē o petros tou logou tou kuriou, ōs eipen autō oti prin alektora phōnēsai aparnēsē me tris
luk|22|62|	kai exelthōn exō o petros eklause pikrōs.
luk|22|63|	kai oi andres oi sunechontes ton iēsoun enepaizon autō derontes,
luk|22|64|	kai perikalupsantes auton etupton autou to prosōpon kai epērōtōn auton legontes prophēteuson tis estin o paisas se?
luk|22|65|	kai etera polla blasphēmountes elegon eis auton.
luk|22|66|	kai ōs egeneto ēmera, sunēchthē to presbuterion tou laou, archiereis kai grammateis, kai anēgagon auton eis to sunedrion eautōn legontes
luk|22|67|	ei su ei o christos, eipe ēmin. eipe de autois ean umin eipō, ou mē pisteusēte,
luk|22|68|	ean de kai erōtēsō, ou mē apokrithēte moi ē apolusēte
luk|22|69|	apo tou nun estai o uios tou anthrōpou kathēmenos ek dexiōn tēs dunameōs tou theou.
luk|22|70|	eipon de pantes su oun ei o uios tou theou? o de pros autous ephē umeis legete oti egō eimi.
luk|22|71|	oi de eipon ti eti chreian echomen marturias? autoi gar ēkousamen apo tou stomatos autou.
luk|23|1|	kai anastan apan to plēthos autōn ēgagon auton epi ton pilaton.
luk|23|2|	ērxanto de katēgorein autou legontes touton euromen diastrephonta to ethnos kai kōluonta kaisari phorous didonai, legonta eauton christon basilea einai.
luk|23|3|	o de pilatos epērōtēsen auton legōn su ei o basileus tōn ioudaiōn? o de apokritheis autō ephē su legeis.
luk|23|4|	o de pilatos eipe pros tous archiereis kai tous ochlous oti ouden euriskō aition en tō anthrōpō toutō.
luk|23|5|	oi de epischuon legontes oti anaseiei ton laon didaskōn kath olēs tēs ioudaias, arxamenos apo tēs galilaias eōs ōde.
luk|23|6|	pilatos de akousas galilaian epērōtēsen ei o anthrōpos galilaios esti,
luk|23|7|	kai epignous oti ek tēs exousias ērōdou estin, anepempsen auton pros ērōdēn, onta kai auton en ierosolumois en tautais tais ēmerais.
luk|23|8|	o de ērōdēs idōn ton iēsoun echarē lian ēn gar ex ikanou thelōn idein auton dia to akouein auton polla peri autou, kai ēlpize ti sēmeion idein up autou ginomenon.
luk|23|9|	epērōta de auton en logois ikanois autos de ouden apekrinato autō.
luk|23|10|	eistēkeisan de oi grammateis kai oi archiereis eutonōs katēgorountes autou.
luk|23|11|	exouthenēsas de auton o ērōdēs sun tois strateumasin autou kai empaixas, peribalōn auton esthēta lampran anepempsen auton tō pilatō.
luk|23|12|	egenonto de philoi o te ērōdēs kai o pilatos en autē tē ēmera met allēlōn proupērchon gar en echthra ontes pros eautous.
luk|23|13|	pilatos de sugkalesamenos tous archiereis kai tous archontas kai ton laon
luk|23|14|	eipe pros autous prosēnegkate moi ton anthrōpon touton ōs apostrephonta ton laon, kai idou egō enōpion umōn anakrinas ouden euron en tō anthrōpō toutō aition ōn katēgoreite kat autou.
luk|23|15|	all oude ērōdēs anepempsa gar umas pros auton kai idou ouden axion thanatou esti pepragmenon autō.
luk|23|16|	paideusas oun auton apolusō.
luk|23|17|	anagkēn de eichen apoluein autois kata eortēn ena.
luk|23|18|	anekraxan de pamplēthei legontes aire touton, apoluson de ēmin barabban
luk|23|19|	ostis ēn dia stasin tina genomenēn en tē polei kai phonon beblēmenos eis tēn phulakēn.
luk|23|20|	palin oun o pilatos prosephōnēse, thelōn apolusai ton iēsoun.
luk|23|21|	oi de epephōnoun legontes staurōson staurōson auton.
luk|23|22|	o de triton eipe pros autous ti gar kakon epoiēsen outos? ouden axion thanatou euron en autō paideusas oun auton apolusō.
luk|23|23|	oi de epekeinto phōnais megalais aitoumenoi auton staurōthēnai, kai katischuon ai phōnai autōn kai tōn archiereōn.
luk|23|24|	o de pilatos epekrine genesthai to aitēma autōn,
luk|23|25|	apeluse de autois ton barabban ton dia stasin kai phonon beblēmenon eis tēn phulakēn, on ētounto, ton de iēsoun paredōke tō thelēmati autōn.
luk|23|26|	kai ōs apēgagon auton, epilabomenoi simōnos tinos kurēnaiou, erchomenou ap agrou, epethēkan autō ton stauron pherein opisō tou iēsou.
luk|23|27|	ēkolouthei de autō polu plēthos tou laou kai gunaikōn, ai kai ekoptonto kai ethrēnoun auton.
luk|23|28|	strapheis de pros autas o iēsous eipe thugateres ierousalēm, mē klaiete ep eme, plēn eph eautas klaiete kai epi ta tekna umōn.
luk|23|29|	oti idou erchontai ēmerai en ais erousi makariai ai steirai kai koiliai ai ouk egennēsan, kai mastoi oi ouk ethēlasan.
luk|23|30|	tote arxontai legein tois oresi, pesete eph ēmas, kai tois bounois, kalupsate ēmas
luk|23|31|	oti ei en tō ugrō xulō tauta poiousin, en tō xērō ti genētai?
luk|23|32|	ēgonto de kai eteroi duo kakourgoi sun autō anairethēnai.
luk|23|33|	kai ote apēlthon epi ton topon ton kaloumenon kranion, ekei estaurōsan auton kai tous kakourgous, on men ek dexiōn on de ex aristerōn.
luk|23|34|	o de iēsous elege pater, aphes autois ou gar oidasi ti poiousi. diamerizomenoi de ta imatia autou eballon klēron.
luk|23|35|	kai eistēkei o laos theōrōn. exemuktērizon de kai oi archontes sun autois legontes allous esōse, sōsatō eauton, ei outos estin o christos o tou theou eklektos.
luk|23|36|	enepaizon de autō kai oi stratiōtai proserchomenoi kai oxos prospherontes autō
luk|23|37|	kai legontes ei su ei o basileus tōn ioudaiōn, sōson seauton.
luk|23|38|	ēn de kai epigraphē gegrammenē ep autō grammasin ellēnikois kai rōmaikois kai ebraikois outos estin o basileus tōn ioudaiōn.
luk|23|39|	eis de tōn kremasthentōn kakourgōn eblasphēmei auton legōn ei su ei o christos, sōson seauton kai ēmas.
luk|23|40|	apokritheis de o eteros epetima autō legōn oude phobē su ton theon, oti en tō autō krimati ei?
luk|23|41|	kai ēmeis men dikaiōs axia gar ōn epraxamen apolambanomen outos de ouden atopon epraxe.
luk|23|42|	kai elege tō iēsou mnēsthēti mou, kurie, otan elthēs en tē basileia sou.
luk|23|43|	kai eipen autō o iēsous amēn legō soi, sēmeron met emou esē en tō paradeisō.
luk|23|44|	ēn de ōsei ōra ektē kai skotos egeneto eph olēn tēn gēn eōs ōras enatēs, tou ēliou ekleipontos,
luk|23|45|	kai eschisthē to katapetasma tou naou meson
luk|23|46|	kai phōnēsas phōnē megalē o iēsous eipe pater, eis cheiras sou paratithemai to pneuma mou kai tauta eipōn exepneusen.
luk|23|47|	idōn de o ekatontarchos to genomenon edoxase ton theon legōn ontōs o anthrōpos outos dikaios ēn.
luk|23|48|	kai pantes oi sumparagenomenoi ochloi epi tēn theōrian tautēn, theōrountes ta genomena, tuptontes eautōn ta stēthē upestrephon.
luk|23|49|	eistēkeisan de pantes oi gnōstoi autou apo makrothen, kai gunaikes ai sunakolouthēsasai autō apo tēs galilaias, orōsai tauta.

luk|23|51|	outos ouk ēn sugkatatetheimenos tē boulē kai tē praxei autōn—apo arimathaias poleōs tōn ioudaiōn, os prosedecheto kai autos tēn basileian tou theou,

luk|24|1|	tē de mia tōn sabbatōn orthrou batheos ēlthon epi to mnēma pherousai a ētoimasan arōmata, kai tines sun autais.

luk|24|5|	emphobōn de genomenōn autōn kai klinousōn to prosōpon eis tēn gēn eipon pros autas ti zēteite ton zōnta meta tōn nekrōn?

luk|24|8|	kai emnēsthēsan tōn rēmatōn autou,

luk|24|12|	o de petros anastas edramen epi to mnēmeion, kai parakupsas blepei ta othonia keimena mona, kai apēlthe pros eauton, thaumazōn to gegonos.
luk|24|13|	kai idou duo ex autōn ēsan poreuomenoi en autē tē ēmera eis kōmēn apechousan stadious exēkonta apo ierousalēm, ē onoma emmaous.
luk|24|14|	kai autoi ōmiloun pros allēlous peri pantōn tōn sumbebēkotōn toutōn.
luk|24|15|	kai egeneto en tō omilein autous kai suzētein kai autos o iēsous eggisas suneporeueto autois
luk|24|16|	oi de ophthalmoi autōn ekratounto tou mē epignōnai auton.
luk|24|17|	eipe de pros autous tines oi logoi outoi ous antiballete pros allēlous peripatountes kai este skuthrōpoi?
luk|24|18|	apokritheis de o eis, ō onoma kleopas, eipe pros auton su monos paroikeis en ierousalēm kai ouk egnōs ta genomena en autē en tais ēmerais tautais?
luk|24|19|	kai eipen autois poia? oi de eipon autō ta peri iēsou tou nazōraiou, os egeneto anēr prophētēs dunatos en ergō kai logō enantion tou theou kai pantos tou laou,
luk|24|20|	opōs te paredōkan auton oi archiereis kai oi archontes ēmōn eis krima thanatou kai estaurōsan auton.
luk|24|21|	ēmeis de ēlpizomen oti autos estin o mellōn lutrousthai ton israēl alla ge sun pasi toutois tritēn tautēn ēmeran agei sēmeron aph ou tauta egeneto.
luk|24|22|	alla kai gunaikes tines ex ēmōn exestēsan ēmas genomenai orthriai epi to mnēmeion,

luk|24|25|	kai autos eipe pros autous ō anoētoi kai bradeis tē kardia tou pisteuein epi pasin ois elalēsan oi prophētai!
luk|24|26|	ouchi tauta edei pathein ton christon kai eiselthein eis tēn doxan autou?
luk|24|27|	kai arxamenos apo mōuseōs kai apo pantōn tōn prophētōn diērmēneuen autois en pasais tais graphais ta peri eautou.

luk|24|29|	kai parebiasanto auton legontes meinon meth ēmōn, oti pros esperan esti kai kekliken ē ēmera. kai eisēlthe tou meinai sun autois.

luk|24|39|	idete tas cheiras mou kai tous podas mou, oti autos egō eimi psēlaphēsate me kai idete, oti pneuma sarka kai ostea ouk echei kathōs eme theōreite echonta.
luk|24|40|	kai touto eipōn epedeixen autois tas cheiras kai tous podas.

joh|1|1|	en archē ēn o logos, kai o logos ēn pros ton theon, kai theos ēn o logos.
joh|1|2|	outos ēn en archē pros ton theon.
joh|1|3|	panta di autou egeneto, kai chōris autou egeneto oude en o gegonen.
joh|1|4|	en autō zōē ēn, kai ē zōē ēn to phōs tōn anthrōpōn.
joh|1|5|	kai to phōs en tē skotia phainei, kai ē skotia auto ou katelaben.
joh|1|6|	egeneto anthrōpos apestalmenos para theou, onoma autō iōannēs
joh|1|7|	outos ēlthen eis marturian, ina marturēsē peri tou phōtos, ina pantes pisteusōsi di autou.
joh|1|8|	ouk ēn ekeinos to phōs, all ina marturēsē peri tou phōtos.
joh|1|9|	ēn to phōs to alēthinon, o phōtizei panta anthrōpon erchomenon eis ton kosmon.
joh|1|10|	en tō kosmō ēn, kai o kosmos di autou egeneto, kai o kosmos auton ouk egnō.
joh|1|11|	eis ta idia ēlthe, kai oi idioi auton ou parelabon.
joh|1|12|	osoi de elabon auton, edōken autois exousian tekna theou genesthai, tois pisteuousin eis to onoma autou,
joh|1|13|	oi ouk ex aimatōn, oude ek thelēmatos sarkos, oude ek thelēmatos andros, all ek theou egennēthēsan.
joh|1|14|	kai o logos sarx egeneto kai eskēnōsen en ēmin, kai etheasametha tēn doxan autou, doxan ōs monogenous para patros, plērēs charitos kai alētheias.
joh|1|15|	iōannēs marturei peri autou kai kekrage legōn outos ēn on eipon, o opisō mou erchomenos emprosthen mou gegonen, oti prōtos mou ēn.
joh|1|16|	kai ek tou plērōmatos autou ēmeis pantes elabomen, kai charin anti charitos
joh|1|17|	oti o nomos dia mōuseōs edothē, ē charis kai ē alētheia dia iēsou christou egeneto.
joh|1|18|	theon oudeis eōrake pōpote o monogenēs uios o ōn eis ton kolpon tou patros, ekeinos exēgēsato.
joh|1|19|	kai autē estin ē marturia tou iōannou, ote apesteilan oi ioudaioi ex ierosolumōn iereis kai leuitas ina erōtēsōsin auton su tis ei?
joh|1|20|	kai ōmologēse, kai ouk ērnēsato kai ōmologēsen oti ouk eimi egō o christos.
joh|1|21|	kai ērōtēsan auton ti oun? ēlias ei su? kai legei ouk eimi. o prophētēs ei su? kai apekrithē, ou.
joh|1|22|	eipon oun autō tis ei? ina apokrisin dōmen tois pempsasin ēmas ti legeis peri seautou?
joh|1|23|	ephē egō phōnē boōntos en tē erēmō, euthunate tēn odon kuriou, kathōs eipen ēsaias o prophētēs.
joh|1|24|	kai oi apestalmenoi ēsan ek tōn pharisaiōn
joh|1|25|	kai ērōtēsan auton kai eipon autō ti oun baptizeis, ei su ouk ei o christos oute ēlias oute o prophētēs?
joh|1|26|	apekrithē autois o iōannēs legōn egō baptizō en udati mesos de umōn estēken on umeis ouk oidate.
joh|1|27|	autos estin o opisō mou erchomenos, os emprosthen mou gegonen, ou egō ouk eimi axios ina lusō autou ton imanta tou upodēmatos.
joh|1|28|	tauta en bēthania egeneto peran tou iordanou, opou ēn iōannēs baptizōn.
joh|1|29|	tē epaurion blepei o iōannēs ton iēsoun erchomenon pros auton kai legei ide o amnos tou theou o airōn tēn amartian tou kosmou.

joh|1|41|	ēn andreas o adelphos simōnos petrou eis ek tōn duo tōn akousantōn para iōannou kai akolouthēsantōn autō.

joh|1|47|	kai eipen autō nathanaēl ek nazaret dunatai ti agathon einai? legei autō philippos erchou kai ide.

joh|1|51|	apekrithē iēsous kai eipen autō oti eipon soi, eidon se upokatō tēs sukēs, pisteueis? meizō toutōn opsei.

joh|3|1|	ēn de anthrōpos ek tōn pharisaiōn, nikodēmos onoma autō, archōn tōn ioudaiōn.
joh|3|2|	outos ēlthe pros auton nuktos kai eipen autō rabbi, oidamen oti apo theou elēluthas didaskalos oudeis gar tauta ta sēmeia dunatai poiein a su poieis, ean mē ē o theos met autou.
joh|3|3|	apekrithē iēsous kai eipen autō amēn amēn legō soi, ean mē tis gennēthē anōthen, ou dunatai idein tēn basileian tou theou.
joh|3|4|	legei pros auton o nikodēmos pōs dunatai anthrōpos gennēthēnai gerōn ōn? mē dunatai eis tēn koilian tēs mētros autou deuteron eiselthein kai gennēthēnai?
joh|3|5|	apekrithē iēsous amēn amēn legō soi, ean mē tis gennēthē ex udatos kai pneumatos, ou dunatai eiselthein eis tēn basileian tou theou.
joh|3|6|	to gegennēmenon ek tēs sarkos sarx esti, kai to gegennēmenon ek tou pneumatos pneuma esti.
joh|3|7|	mē thaumasēs oti eipon soi, dei umas gennēthēnai anōthen.
joh|3|8|	to pneuma opou thelei pnei, kai tēn phōnēn autou akoueis, all ouk oidas pothen erchetai kai pou upagei outōs esti pas o gegennēmenos ek tou pneumatos.
joh|3|9|	apekrithē nikodēmos kai eipen autō pōs dunatai tauta genesthai?
joh|3|10|	apekrithē iēsous kai eipen autō su ei o didaskalos tou israēl kai tauta ou ginōskeis?
joh|3|11|	amēn amēn legō soi oti o oidamen laloumen kai o eōrakamen marturoumen, kai tēn marturian ēmōn ou lambanete.

joh|6|59|	tauta eipen en sunagōgē didaskōn en kapernaoum.

joh|8|40|	nun de zēteite me apokteinai, anthrōpon os tēn alētheian umin lelalēka, ēn ēkousa para tou theou touto abraam ouk epoiēsen.
joh|8|41|	umeis poieite ta erga tou patros umōn. eipon oun autō ēmeis ek porneias ou gegennēmetha ena patera echomen, ton theon.
joh|8|42|	eipen oun autois o iēsous ei o theos patēr umōn ēn, ēgapate an eme egō gar ek tou theou exēlthon kai ēkō oude gar ap emautou elēlutha, all ekeinos me apesteile.
joh|8|43|	diati tēn lalian tēn emēn ou ginōskete? oti ou dunasthe akouein ton logon ton emon.

joh|19|25|	oi men oun stratiōtai tauta epoiēsan. eistēkeisan de para tō staurō tou iēsou ē mētēr autou kai ē adelphē tēs mētros autou, maria ē tou klōpa kai maria ē magdalēnē.

joh|19|34|	all eis tōn stratiōtōn logchē autou tēn pleuran enuxe, kai eutheōs exēlthen aima kai udōr.
joh|19|35|	kai o eōrakōs memarturēke, kai alēthinē autou estin ē marturia, kakeinos oiden oti alēthē legei, ina kai umeis pisteusēte.
joh|19|36|	egeneto gar tauta, ina ē graphē plērōthē, ostoun ou suntribēsetai autou.
joh|19|37|	kai palin etera graphē legei opsontai eis on exekentēsan.
joh|19|38|	meta de tauta ērōtēse ton pilaton iōsēph o apo arimathaias, ōn mathētēs tou iēsou, kekrummenos de dia ton phobon tōn ioudaiōn, ina arē to sōma tou iēsou kai epetrepsen o pilatos. ēlthen oun kai ēre to sōma tou iēsou.
joh|19|39|	ēlthe de kai nikodēmos o elthōn pros ton iēsoun nuktos to prōton, pherōn migma smurnēs kai aloēs ōs litras ekaton.
joh|19|40|	elabon oun to sōma tou iēsou kai edēsan auto en othoniois meta tōn arōmatōn, kathōs ethos esti tois ioudaiois entaphiazein.

joh|19|42|	ekei oun dia tēn paraskeuēn tōn ioudaiōn, oti eggus ēn to mnēmeion, ethēkan ton iēsoun.
joh|20|1|	tē de mia tōn sabbatōn maria ē magdalēnē erchetai prōi skotias eti ousēs eis to mnēmeion, kai blepei ton lithon ērmenon ek tou mnēmeiou.

act|2|28|	egnōrisas moi odous zōēs, plērōseis me euphrosunēs meta tou prosōpou sou.
act|2|29|	andres adelphoi, exon eipein meta parrēsias pros umas peri tou patriarchou dauid oti kai eteleutēse kai etaphē kai to mnēma autou estin en ēmin achri tēs ēmeras tautēs.
act|2|30|	prophētēs oun uparchōn, kai eidōs oti orkō ōmosen autō o theos ek karpou tēs osphuos autou to kata sarka anastēsein ton christon kathisai epi tou thronou autou,
act|2|31|	proidōn elalēse peri tēs anastaseōs tou christou oti ou kateleiphthē ē psuchē autou eis adou oude ē sarx autou eide diaphthoran.
act|2|32|	touton ton iēsoun anestēsen o theos, ou pantes ēmeis esmen martures.
act|2|33|	tē dexia oun tou theou upsōtheis, tēn te epaggelian tou agiou pneumatos labōn para tou patros, exechee touto o nun umeis blepete kai akouete.
act|2|34|	ou gar dauid anebē eis tous ouranous, legei de autos eipen o kurios tō kuriō mou, kathou ek dexiōn mou
act|2|35|	eōs an thō tous echthrous sou upopodion tōn podōn sou.
act|2|36|	asphalōs oun ginōsketō pas oikos israēl oti kai kurion kai christon auton o theos epoiēse, touton ton iēsoun on umeis estaurōsate.
act|2|37|	akousantes de katenugēsan tē kardia, eipon te pros ton petron kai tous loipous apostolous ti poiēsomen, andres adelphoi?
act|2|38|	petros de ephē pros autous metanoēsate, kai baptisthētō ekastos umōn epi tō onomati iēsou christou eis aphesin amartiōn, kai lēpsesthe tēn dōrean tou agiou pneumatos.
act|2|39|	umin gar estin ē epaggelia kai tois teknois umōn kai pasi tois eis makran, osous an proskalesētai kurios o theos ēmōn.

act|2|43|	egeneto de pasē psuchē phobos, polla te terata kai sēmeia dia tōn apostolōn egineto.
act|2|44|	pantes de oi pisteuontes ēsan epi to auto kai eichon apanta koina,

act|3|1|	epi to auto de petros kai iōannēs anebainon eis to ieron epi tēn ōran tēs proseuchēs tēn enatēn.
act|3|2|	kai tis anēr chōlos ek koilias mētros autou uparchōn ebastazeto, on etithoun kath ēmeran pros tēn thuran tou ierou tēn legomenēn ōraian tou aitein eleēmosunēn para tōn eisporeuomenōn eis to ieron
act|3|3|	os idōn petron kai iōannēn mellontas eisienai eis to ieron ērōta eleēmosunēn.
act|3|4|	atenisas de petros eis auton sun tō iōannē eipe blepson eis ēmas.
act|3|5|	o de epeichen autois prosdokōn ti par autōn labein.
act|3|6|	eipe de petros argurion kai chrusion ouch uparchei moi o de echō touto soi didōmi en tō onomati iēsou christou tou nazōraiou egeire kai peripatei.

act|3|11|	kratountos de tou iathentos chōlou ton petron kai iōannēn sunedrame pros autous pas o laos epi tē stoa tē kaloumenē solomōntos ekthamboi.

act|3|13|	o theos abraam kai isaak kai iakōb, o theos tōn paterōn ēmōn, edoxase ton paida autou iēsoun on umeis men paredōkate kai ērnēsasthe auton kata prosōpon pilatou, krinantos ekeinou apoluein
act|3|14|	umeis de ton agion kai dikaion ērnēsasthe, kai ētēsasthe andra phonea charisthēnai umin,
act|3|15|	ton de archēgon tēs zōēs apekteinate, on o theos ēgeiren ek nekrōn, ou ēmeis martures esmen.
act|3|16|	kai epi tē pistei tou onomatos autou touton, on theōreite kai oidate, estereōse to onoma autou, kai ē pistis ē di autou edōken autō tēn oloklērian tautēn apenanti pantōn umōn.
act|3|17|	kai nun, adelphoi, oida oti kata agnoian epraxate, ōsper kai oi archontes umōn
act|3|18|	o de theos a prokatēggeile dia stomatos pantōn tōn prophētōn autou pathein ton christon, eplērōsen outō.
act|3|19|	metanoēsate oun kai epistrepsate eis to exaleiphthēnai umōn tas amartias,

act|3|22|	mōusēs men gar pros tous pateras eipen oti prophētēn umin anastēsei kurios o theos umōn ek tōn adelphōn umōn ōs eme autou akousesthe kata panta osa an lalēsē pros umas.
act|3|23|	estai de pasa psuchē, ētis ean mē akousē tou prophētou ekeinou, exolothreuthēsetai ek tou laou.

act|4|1|	lalountōn de autōn pros ton laon epestēsan autois oi iereis kai o stratēgos tou ierou kai oi saddoukaioi,

act|5|1|	anēr de tis ananias onomati sun sappheirē tē gunaiki autou epōlēse ktēma

act|5|3|	eipe de petros anania, diati eplērōsen o satanas tēn kardian sou, pseusasthai se to pneuma to agion kai nosphisasthai apo tēs timēs tou chōriou?
act|5|4|	ouchi menon soi emene kai prathen en tē sē exousia upērche? ti oti ethou en tē kardia sou to pragma touto? ouk epseusō anthrōpois, alla tō theō.

act|6|1|	en de tais ēmerais tautais plēthunontōn tōn mathētōn egeneto goggusmos tōn ellēnistōn pros tous ebraious, oti paretheōrounto en tē diakonia tē kathēmerinē ai chērai autōn.
act|6|2|	proskalesamenoi de oi dōdeka to plēthos tōn mathētōn eipon ouk areston estin ēmas kataleipsantas ton logon tou theou diakonein trapezais.
act|6|3|	episkepsasthe oun, adelphoi, andras ex umōn marturoumenous epta, plēreis pneumatos agiou kai sophias, ous katastēsomen epi tēs chreias tautēs
act|6|4|	ēmeis de tē proseuchē kai tē diakonia tou logou proskarterēsomen.
act|6|5|	kai ēresen o logos enōpion pantos tou plēthous kai exelexanto stephanon, andra plērē pisteōs kai pneumatos agiou, kai philippon kai prochoron kai nikanora kai timōna kai parmenan kai nikolaon prosēluton antiochea,
act|6|6|	ous estēsan enōpion tōn apostolōn, kai proseuxamenoi epethēkan autois tas cheiras.
act|6|7|	kai o logos tou theou ēuxane, kai eplēthuneto o arithmos tōn mathētōn en ierousalēm sphodra, polus te ochlos tōn ioudaiōn upēkouon tē pistei.
act|6|8|	stephanos de plērēs pisteōs kai dunameōs epoiei terata kai sēmeia megala en tō laō.
act|6|9|	anestēsan de tines tōn ek tēs sunagōgēs tēs legomenēs libertinōn kai kurēnaiōn kai alexandreōn kai tōn apo kilikias kai asias suzētountes tō stephanō,
act|6|10|	kai ouk ischuon antistēnai tē sophia kai tō pneumati ō elalei.
act|6|11|	tote upebalon andras legontas oti akēkoamen autou lalountos rēmata blasphēma eis mōusēn kai ton theon
act|6|12|	sunekinēsan te ton laon kai tous presbuterous kai tous grammateis, kai epistantes sunērpasan auton kai ēgagon eis to sunedrion,
act|6|13|	estēsan te marturas pseudeis legontas o anthrōpos outos ou pauetai rēmata blasphēma lalōn kata tou topou tou agiou kai tou nomou

act|7|1|	eipe de o archiereus ei ara tauta outōs echei?
act|7|2|	o de ephē andres adelphoi kai pateres, akousate. o theos tēs doxēs ōphthē tō patri ēmōn abraam onti en tē mesopotamia, prin ē katoikēsai auton en charran,
act|7|3|	kai eipe pros auton exelthe ek tēs gēs sou kai ek tēs suggeneias sou, kai deuro eis gēn ēn an soi deixō.
act|7|4|	tote exelthōn ek gēs chaldaiōn katōkēsen en charran. kakeithen meta to apothanein ton patera autou metōkisen auton eis tēn gēn tautēn eis ēn umeis nun katoikeite
act|7|5|	kai ouk edōken autō klēronomian en autē oude bēma podos, kai epēggeilato dounai autō eis kataschesin autēn kai tō spermati autou met auton, ouk ontos autō teknou.
act|7|6|	elalēse de outōs o theos, oti estai to sperma autou paroikon en gē allotria, kai doulōsousin auto kai kakōsousin etē tetrakosia
act|7|7|	kai to ethnos ō ean douleusōsi krinō egō, eipen o theos kai meta tauta exeleusontai kai latreusousi moi en tō topō toutō.
act|7|8|	kai edōken autō diathēkēn peritomēs kai outōs egennēse ton isaak kai perietemen auton tē ēmera tē ogdoē, kai o isaak ton iakōb, kai o iakōb tous dōdeka patriarchas.
act|7|9|	kai oi patriarchai zēlōsantes ton iōsēph apedonto eis aigupton.
act|7|10|	kai ēn o theos met autou, kai exeileto auton ek pasōn tōn thlipseōn autou, kai edōken autō charin kai sophian enantion pharaō basileōs aiguptou, kai katestēsen auton ēgoumenon ep aigupton kai olon ton oikon autou.
act|7|11|	ēlthe de limos eph olēn tēn gēn aiguptou kai chanaan kai thlipsis megalē, kai ouch euriskon chortasmata oi pateres ēmōn.
act|7|12|	akousas de iakōb onta sita en aiguptō exapesteile tous pateras ēmōn prōton
act|7|13|	kai en tō deuterō anegnōristhē iōsēph tois adelphois autou, kai phaneron egeneto tō pharaō to genos tou iōsēph.
act|7|14|	aposteilas de iōsēph metekalesato ton patera autou iakōb kai pasan tēn suggeneian autou en psuchais ebdomēkonta pente.
act|7|15|	katebē de iakōb eis aigupton kai eteleutēsen autos kai oi pateres ēmōn,
act|7|16|	kai metetethēsan eis suchem kai etethēsan en tō mnēmati ō ōnēsato abraam timēs arguriou para tōn uiōn emmor tou suchem.
act|7|17|	kathōs de ēggizen o chronos tēs epaggelias ēn ōmosen o theos tō abraam, ēuxēsen o laos kai eplēthunthē en aiguptō,
act|7|18|	achris ou anestē basileus eteros, os ouk ēdei ton iōsēph.
act|7|19|	outos katasophisamenos to genos ēmōn ekakōse tous pateras ēmōn tou poiein ektheta ta brephē autōn, eis to mē zōogoneisthai
act|7|20|	en ō kairō egennēthē mōusēs, kai ēn asteios tō theō os anetraphē mēnas treis en tō oikō tou patros autou.
act|7|21|	ektethenta de auton aneileto auton ē thugatēr pharaō kai anethrepsato auton eautē eis uion.
act|7|22|	kai epaideuthē mōusēs pasē sophia aiguptiōn, ēn de dunatos en logois kai en ergois.
act|7|23|	ōs de eplērouto autō tessarakontaetēs chronos, anebē eis tēn kardian autou episkepsasthai tous adelphous autou tous uious israēl.
act|7|24|	kai idōn tina adikoumenon ēmunato, kai epoiēsato ekdikēsin tō kataponoumenō pataxas ton aiguption.
act|7|25|	enomize de sunienai tous adelphous autou oti o theos dia cheiros autou didōsin autois sōtērian oi de ou sunēkan.
act|7|26|	tē te epiousē ēmera ōphthē autois machomenois, kai sunēlasen autous eis eirēnēn eipōn andres, adelphoi este umeis ina ti adikeite allēlous?
act|7|27|	o de adikōn ton plēsion apōsato auton eipōn tis se katestēsen archonta kai dikastēn eph ēmōn?
act|7|28|	mē anelein me su theleis on tropon aneiles chthes ton aiguption?
act|7|29|	ephuge de mōusēs en tō logō toutō kai egeneto paroikos en gē madiam, ou egennēsen uious duo.
act|7|30|	kai plērōthentōn etōn tessarakonta ōphthē autō en tē erēmō tou orous sina aggelos kuriou en phlogi puros batou.
act|7|31|	o de mōusēs idōn ethaumaze to orama proserchomenou de autou katanoēsai egeneto phōnē kuriou pros auton
act|7|32|	egō o theos tōn paterōn sou, o theos abraam kai o theos isaak kai o theos iakōb. entromos de genomenos mōusēs ouk etolma katanoēsai.
act|7|33|	eipe de autō o kurios luson to upodēma tōn podōn sou. o gar topos en ō estēkas gē agia estin.
act|7|34|	idōn eidon tēn kakōsin tou laou mou tou en aiguptō kai tou stenagmou autōn ēkousa, kai katebēn exelesthai autous kai nun deuro apostelō se eis aigupton.
act|7|35|	touton ton mōusēn on ērnēsanto eipontes tis se katestēsen archonta kai dikastēn? touton o theos archonta kai lutrōtēn apesteilen en cheiri aggelou tou ophthentos autō en tē batō.
act|7|36|	outos exēgagen autous poiēsas terata kai sēmeia en gē aiguptō kai en eruthra thalassē kai en tē erēmō etē tessarakonta.
act|7|37|	outos estin o mōusēs o eipōn tois uiois israēl prophētēn umin anastēsei kurios o theos umōn ek tōn adelphōn umōn ōs eme autou akousesthe.
act|7|38|	outos estin o genomenos en tē ekklēsia en tē erēmō meta tou aggelou tou lalountos autō en tō orei sina kai tōn paterōn ēmōn, os edexato logia zōnta dounai ēmin.

act|7|41|	kai emoschopoiēsan en tais ēmerais ekeinais kai anēgagon thusian tō eidōlō, kai euphrainonto en tois ergois tōn cheirōn autōn.

act|8|1|	egeneto de en ekeinē tē ēmera diōgmos megas epi tēn ekklēsian tēn en ierosolumois pantes de diesparēsan kata tas chōras tēs ioudaias kai samareias, plēn tōn apostolōn.
act|8|2|	sunekomisan de ton stephanon andres eulabeis kai epoiēsan kopeton megan ep autō.

act|8|4|	oi men oun diasparentes diēlthon euaggelizomenoi ton logon.

act|8|15|	oitines katabantes prosēuxanto peri autōn opōs labōsi pneuma agion
act|8|16|	oupō gar ēn ep oudeni autōn epipeptōkos, monon de bebaptismenoi upērchon eis to onoma tou kuriou iēsou.

act|8|19|	legōn dote kamoi tēn exousian tautēn, ina ō ean epithō tas cheiras lambanē pneuma agion.
act|8|20|	petros de eipe pros auton to argurion sou sun soi eiē eis apōleian, oti tēn dōrean tou theou enomisas dia chrēmatōn ktasthai.
act|8|21|	ouk esti soi meris oude klēros en tō logō toutō ē gar kardia sou ouk estin eutheia enōpion tou theou.
act|8|22|	metanoēson oun apo tēs kakias sou tautēs, kai deēthēti tou theou ei ara aphethēsetai soi ē epinoia tēs kardias sou
act|8|23|	eis gar cholēn pikrias kai sundesmon adikias orō se onta.
act|8|24|	apokritheis de o simōn eipe deēthēte umeis uper emou pros ton theon opōs mēden epelthē ep eme ōn eirēkate.
act|8|25|	oi men oun diamarturamenoi kai lalēsantes ton logon tou kuriou upestrepsan eis ierousalēm, pollas te kōmas tōn samareitōn euēggelisanto.
act|8|26|	aggelos de kuriou elalēse pros philippon legōn anastēthi kai poreuou kata mesēmbrian epi tēn odon tēn katabainousan apo ierousalēm eis gazan autē estin erēmos.
act|8|27|	kai anastas eporeuthē. kai idou anēr aithiops eunouchos dunastēs kandakēs tēs basilissēs aithiopōn, os ēn epi pasēs tēs gazēs autēs, os elēluthei proskunēsōn eis ierousalēm,
act|8|28|	ēn te upostrephōn kai kathēmenos epi tou armatos autou, kai aneginōske ton prophētēn ēsaian.

act|8|31|	o de eipe pōs gar an dunaimēn, ean mē tis odēgēsē me? parekalese te ton philippon anabanta kathisai sun autō.
act|8|32|	ē de periochē tēs graphēs ēn aneginōsken ēn autē ōs probaton epi sphagēn ēchthē kai ōs amnos enantion tou keirontos auton aphōnos, outōs ouk anoigei to stoma autou.
act|8|33|	en tē tapeinōsei autou ē krisis autou ērthē tēn de genean autou tis diēgēsetai? oti airetai apo tēs gēs ē zōē autou.

act|8|37|	eipe de o philippos ei pisteueis ex olēs tēs kardias, exestin. apokritheis de eipe pisteuō ton uion tou theou einai ton iēsoun christon.

act|9|1|	o de saulos eti empneōn apeilēs kai phonou eis tous mathētas tou kuriou, proselthōn tō archierei
act|9|2|	ētēsato par autou epistolas eis damaskon pros tas sunagōgas, opōs ean tinas eurē tēs odou ontas, andras te kai gunaikas, dedemenous agagē eis ierousalēm.
act|9|3|	en de tō poreuesthai egeneto auton eggizein tē damaskō, kai exaiphnēs periēstrapsen auton phōs apo tou ouranou,
act|9|4|	kai pesōn epi tēn gēn ēkouse phōnēn legousan autō saoul saoul, ti me diōkeis?
act|9|5|	eipe de tis ei, kurie? o de kurios eipen egō eimi iēsous on su diōkeis
act|9|6|	alla anastēthi kai eiselthe eis tēn polin, kai lalēthēsetai soi ti se dei poiein.
act|9|7|	oi de andres oi sunodeuontes autō eistēkeisan eneoi, akouontes men tēs phōnēs, mēdena de theōrountes.
act|9|8|	ēgerthē de o saulos apo tēs gēs, aneōgmenōn te tōn ophthalmōn autou oudena eblepe cheiragōgountes de auton eisēgagon eis damaskon.
act|9|9|	kai ēn ēmeras treis mē blepōn, kai ouk ephagen oude epien.
act|9|10|	ēn de tis mathētēs en damaskō onomati ananias, kai eipe pros auton o kurios en oramati anania. o de eipen idou egō, kurie.
act|9|11|	o de kurios pros auton anastas poreuthēti epi tēn rumēn tēn kaloumenēn eutheian kai zētēson en oikia iouda saulon onomati tarsea idou gar proseuchetai,
act|9|12|	kai eiden en oramati andra onomati ananian eiselthonta kai epithenta autō cheira, opōs anablepsē.
act|9|13|	apekrithē de ananias kurie, akēkoa apo pollōn peri tou andros toutou, osa kaka epoiēse tois agiois sou en ierousalēm
act|9|14|	kai ōde echei exousian para tōn archiereōn dēsai pantas tous epikaloumenous to onoma sou.
act|9|15|	eipe de pros auton o kurios poreuou, oti skeuos eklogēs moi estin outos tou bastasai to onoma mou enōpion ethnōn kai basileōn uiōn te israēl
act|9|16|	egō gar upodeixō autō osa dei auton uper tou onomatos mou pathein.
act|9|17|	apēlthe de ananias kai eisēlthen eis tēn oikian, kai epitheis ep auton tas cheiras eipe saoul adelphe, o kurios apestalke me, iēsous o ophtheis soi en tē odō ē ērchou, opōs anablepsēs kai plēsthēs pneumatos agiou.
act|9|18|	kai eutheōs apepeson apo tōn ophthalmōn autou ōsei lepides, aneblepse te, kai anastas ebaptisthē, kai labōn trophēn enischusen.
act|9|19|	egeneto de o saulos meta tōn ontōn en damaskō mathētōn ēmeras tinas,
act|9|20|	kai eutheōs en tais sunagōgais ekērusse ton iēsoun oti outos estin o uios tou theou.
act|9|21|	existanto de pantes oi akouontes kai elegon ouch outos estin o porthēsas en ierousalēm tous epikaloumenous to onoma touto, kai ōde eis touto elēluthen, ina dedemenous autous agagē epi tous archiereis?
act|9|22|	saulos de mallon enedunamouto kai sunechune tous ioudaious tous katoikountas en damaskō, sumbibazōn oti outos estin o christos.
act|9|23|	ōs de eplērounto ēmerai ikanai, sunebouleusanto oi ioudaioi anelein auton
act|9|24|	egnōsthē de tō saulō ē epiboulē autōn. paretēroun te tas pulas ēmeras te kai nuktos opōs auton anelōsi
act|9|25|	labontes de auton oi mathētai nuktos kathēkan dia tou teichous chalasantes en spuridi.
act|9|26|	paragenomenos de o saulos eis ierousalēm epeirato kollasthai tois mathētais kai pantes ephobounto auton, mē pisteuontes oti esti mathētēs.
act|9|27|	barnabas de epilabomenos auton ēgage pros tous apostolous, kai diēgēsato autois pōs en tē odō eide ton kurion kai oti elalēsen autō, kai pōs en damaskō eparrēsiasato en tō onomati tou iēsou.
act|9|28|	kai ēn met autōn eisporeuomenos kai ekporeuomenos en ierousalēm kai parrēsiazomenos en tō onomati tou kuriou iēsou,
act|9|29|	elalei te kai sunezētei pros tous ellēnistas oi de epecheiroun auton anelein.

act|9|31|	ai men oun ekklēsiai kath olēs tēs ioudaias kai galilaias kai samareias eichon eirēnēn oikodomoumenai kai poreuomenai tō phobō tou kuriou, kai tē paraklēsei tou agiou pneumatos eplēthunonto.
