act|13|21|	kakeithen ētēsanto basilea, kai edōken autois o theos ton saoul uion kis, andra ek phulēs beniamin, etē tessarakonta
act|13|22|	kai metastēsas auton ēgeiren autois ton dauid eis basilea, ō kai eipe marturēsas euron dauid ton tou iessai, andra kata tēn kardian mou, os poiēsei panta ta thelēmata mou.
act|13|23|	toutou o theos apo tou spermatos kat epaggelian ēgage tō israēl sōtērian,
act|13|24|	prokēruxantos iōannou pro prosōpou tēs eisodou autou baptisma metanoias panti tō laō israēl.
act|13|25|	ōs de eplērou o iōannēs ton dromon, elege tina me uponoeite einai? ouk eimi egō, all idou erchetai met eme ou ouk eimi axios to upodēma tōn podōn lusai.
act|13|26|	andres adelphoi, uioi genous abraam kai oi en umin phoboumenoi ton theon, umin o logos tēs sōtērias tautēs apestalē.
act|13|27|	oi gar katoikountes en ierousalēm kai oi archontes autōn touton agnoēsantes, kai tas phōnas tōn prophētōn tas kata pan sabbaton anaginōskomenas krinantes eplērōsan,
act|13|28|	kai mēdemian aitian thanatou eurontes ētēsanto pilaton anairethēnai auton.
act|13|29|	ōs de etelesan panta ta peri autou gegrammena, kathelontes apo tou xulou ethēkan eis mnēmeion.
act|13|30|	o de theos ēgeiren auton ek nekrōn
act|13|31|	os ōphthē epi ēmeras pleious tois sunanabasin autō apo tēs galilaias eis ierousalēm, oitines eisi martures autou pros ton laon.
act|13|32|	kai ēmeis umas euaggelizometha tēn pros tous pateras epaggelian genomenēn, oti tautēn o theos ekpeplērōke tois teknois autōn, ēmin, anastēsas iēsoun,
act|13|33|	ōs kai en tō psalmō tō deuterō gegraptai uios mou ei su, egō sēmeron gegennēka se.
act|13|34|	oti de anestēsen auton ek nekrōn mēketi mellonta upostrephein eis diaphthoran, outōs eirēken, oti dōsō umin ta osia dauid ta pista.
act|13|35|	dio kai en eterō legei ou dōseis ton osion sou idein diaphthoran.
act|13|36|	dauid men gar idia genea upēretēsas tē tou theou boulē ekoimēthē kai prosetethē pros tous pateras autou kai eide diaphthoran
act|13|37|	on de o theos ēgeiren, ouk eide diaphthoran.
act|13|38|	gnōston oun estō umin, andres adelphoi, oti dia toutou umin aphesis amartiōn kataggelletai,
act|13|39|	kai apo pantōn ōn ouk ēdunēthēte en tō nomō mōuseōs dikaiōthēnai, en toutō pas o pisteuōn dikaioutai.
act|13|40|	blepete oun mē epelthē eph umas to eirēmenon en tois prophētais
act|13|41|	idete, oi kataphronētai, kai thaumasate kai aphanisthēte, oti ergon egō ergazomai en tais ēmerais umōn, ergon ō ou mē pisteusēte ean tis ekdiēgētai umin.
act|13|42|	exiontōn de autōn ek tēs sunagōgēs tōn ioudaiōn parekaloun ta ethnē eis to metaxu sabbaton lalēthēnai autois ta rēmata tauta.
act|13|43|	lutheisēs de tēs sunagōgēs ēkolouthēsan polloi tōn ioudaiōn kai tōn sebomenōn prosēlutōn tō paulō kai tō barnaba, oitines proslalountes autois epeithon autous prosmenein tē chariti tou theou.
act|13|44|	tō te erchomenō sabbatō schedon pasa ē polis sunēchthē akousai ton logon tou theou.
act|13|45|	idontes de oi ioudaioi tous ochlous eplēsthēsan zēlou kai antelegon tois upo tou paulou legomenois antilegontes kai blasphēmountes.

act|13|47|	outō gar entetaltai ēmin o kurios tetheika se eis phōs ethnōn tou einai se eis sōtērian eōs eschatou tēs gēs.

act|13|49|	diephereto de o logos tou kuriou di olēs tēs chōras.
act|13|50|	oi de ioudaioi parōtrunan tas sebomenas gunaikas kai tas euschēmonas kai tous prōtous tēs poleōs kai epēgeiran diōgmon epi ton paulon kai ton barnaban, kai exebalon autous apo tōn oriōn autōn.

act|13|52|	oi de mathētai eplērounto charas kai pneumatos agiou.
act|14|1|	egeneto de en ikoniō kata to auto eiselthein autous eis tēn sunagōgēn tōn ioudaiōn kai lalēsai outōs ōste pisteusai ioudaiōn te kai ellēnōn polu plēthos.
act|14|2|	oi de apeithountes ioudaioi epēgeiran kai ekakōsan tas psuchas tōn ethnōn kata tōn adelphōn.
act|14|3|	ikanon men oun chronon dietripsan parrēsiazomenoi epi tō kuriō tō marturounti tō logō tēs charitos autou, didonti sēmeia kai terata ginesthai dia tōn cheirōn autōn.
act|14|4|	eschisthē de to plēthos tēs poleōs, kai oi men ēsan sun tois ioudaiois, oi de sun tois apostolois.
act|14|5|	ōs de egeneto ormē tōn ethnōn te kai ioudaiōn sun tois archousin autōn ubrisai kai lithobolēsai autous,
act|14|6|	sunidontes katephugon eis tas poleis tēs lukaonias lustran kai derbēn kai tēn perichōron,
act|14|7|	kakei ēsan euaggelizomenoi.
act|14|8|	kai tis anēr en lustrois adunatos tois posin ekathēto, chōlos ek koilias mētros autou uparchōn, os oudepote peripepatēkei.
act|14|9|	outos ēkouse tou paulou lalountos os atenisas autō kai idōn oti pistin echei tou sōthēnai,
act|14|10|	eipe megalē tē phōnē anastēthi epi tous podas sou orthos. kai ēlato kai periepatei.
act|14|11|	oi de ochloi idontes o epoiēsen o paulos epēran tēn phōnēn autōn lukaonisti legontes oi theoi omoiōthentes anthrōpois katebēsan pros ēmas
act|14|12|	ekaloun te ton men barnaban dia, ton de paulon ermēn, epeidē autos ēn o ēgoumenos tou logou.
act|14|13|	o de iereus tou dios tou ontos pro tēs poleōs autōn, taurous kai stemmata epi tous pulōnas enegkas, sun tois ochlois ēthele thuein.
act|14|14|	akousantes de oi apostoloi barnabas kai paulos, diarrēxantes ta imatia autōn eisepēdēsan eis ton ochlon krazontes
act|14|15|	kai legontes andres, ti tauta poieite? kai ēmeis omoiopatheis esmen umin anthrōpoi, euaggelizomenoi umas apo toutōn tōn mataiōn epistrephein epi ton theon ton zōnta, os epoiēse ton ouranon kai tēn gēn kai tēn thalassan kai panta ta en autois
act|14|16|	os en tais parōchēmenais geneais eiase panta ta ethnē poreuesthai tais odois autōn

act|14|18|	kai tauta legontes molis katepausan tous ochlous tou mē thuein autois.
act|14|19|	epēlthon de apo antiocheias kai ikoniou ioudaioi, kai peisantes tous ochlous kai lithasantes ton paulon esuran exō tēs poleōs, nomisantes auton tethnanai.
act|14|20|	kuklōsantōn de auton tōn mathētōn anastas eisēlthen eis tēn polin, kai tē epaurion exēlthe sun tō barnaba eis derbēn.

act|14|22|	epistērizontes tas psuchas tōn mathētōn, parakalountes emmenein tē pistei, kai oti dia pollōn thlipseōn dei ēmas eiselthein eis tēn basileian tou theou.
act|14|23|	cheirotonēsantes de autois presbuterous kat ekklēsian kai proseuxamenoi meta nēsteiōn parethento autous tō kuriō, eis on pepisteukasi.
act|14|24|	kai dielthontes tēn pisidian ēlthon eis pamphulian,

act|15|1|	kai tines katelthontes apo tēs ioudaias edidaskon tous adelphous oti ean mē peritemnēsthe tō ethei mōuseōs, ou dunasthe sōthēnai.
act|15|2|	genomenēs oun staseōs kai zētēseōs ouk oligēs tō paulō kai tō barnaba pros autous, etaxan anabainein paulon kai barnaban kai tinas allous ex autōn pros tous apostolous kai presbuterous eis ierousalēm peri tou zētēmatos toutou.
act|15|3|	oi men oun propemphthentes upo tēs ekklēsias diērchonto tēn phoinikēn kai samareian ekdiēgoumenoi tēn epistrophēn tōn ethnōn, kai epoioun charan megalēn pasi tois adelphois.
act|15|4|	paragenomenoi de eis ierousalēm apedechthēsan upo tēs ekklēsias kai tōn apostolōn kai tōn presbuterōn, anēggeilan te osa o theos epoiēse met autōn, kai oti ēnoixe tois ethnesi thuran pisteōs.
act|15|5|	exanestēsan de tines tōn apo tēs aireseōs tōn pharisaiōn pepisteukotes, legontes oti dei peritemnein autous paraggellein te tērein ton nomon mōuseōs.

act|15|31|	anagnontes de echarēsan epi tē paraklēsei.

act|16|1|	katēntēse de eis derbēn kai lustran. kai idou mathētēs tis ēn ekei onomati timotheos, uios gunaikos tinos ioudaias pistēs, patros de ellēnos,
act|16|2|	os emartureito upo tōn en lustrois kai ikoniō adelphōn.
act|16|3|	touton ēthelēsen o paulos sun autō exelthein, kai labōn perietemen auton dia tous ioudaious tous ontas en tois topois ekeinois ēdeisan gar apantes ton patera autou oti ellēn upērchen.
act|16|4|	ōs de dieporeuonto tas poleis, paredidoun autois phulassein ta dogmata ta kekrimena upo tōn apostolōn kai tōn presbuterōn tōn en ierousalēm.
act|16|5|	ai men oun ekklēsiai estereounto tē pistei kai eperisseuon tō arithmō kath ēmeran.

act|16|9|	kai orama dia tēs nuktos ōphthē tō paulō anēr tis ēn makedōn estōs, parakalōn auton kai legōn diabas eis makedonian boēthēson ēmin.
act|16|10|	ōs de to orama eiden, eutheōs ezētēsamen exelthein eis tēn makedonian, sumbibazontes oti proskeklētai ēmas o kurios euaggelisasthai autous.
act|16|11|	anachthentes oun apo tēs trōados euthudromēsamen eis samothrakēn, tē de epiousē eis neapolin,

act|16|13|	tē te ēmera tōn sabbatōn exēlthomen exō tēs poleōs para potamon ou enomizeto proseuchē einai, kai kathisantes elaloumen tais sunelthousais gunaixi.
act|16|14|	kai tis gunē onomati ludia, porphuropōlis poleōs thuateirōn, sebomenē ton theon, ēkouen, ēs o kurios diēnoixe tēn kardian prosechein tois laloumenois upo tou paulou.
act|16|15|	ōs de ebaptisthē kai o oikos autēs, parekalese legousa ei kekrikate me pistēn tō kuriō einai, eiselthontes eis ton oikon mou meinate kai parebiasato ēmas.
act|16|16|	egeneto de poreuomenōn ēmōn eis proseuchēn paidiskēn tina echousan pneuma puthōnos apantēsai ēmin, ētis ergasian pollēn pareiche tois kuriois autēs manteuomenē.
act|16|17|	autē katakolouthēsasa tō paulō kai tō sila ekraze legousa outoi oi anthrōpoi douloi tou theou tou upsistou eisin, oitines kataggellousin ēmin odon sōtērias.
act|16|18|	touto de epoiei epi pollas ēmeras. diaponētheis de o paulos kai epistrepsas tō pneumati eipe paraggellō soi en tō onomati iēsou christou exelthein ap autēs. kai exēlthen autē tē ōra.
act|16|19|	idontes de oi kurioi autēs oti exēlthen ē elpis tēs ergasias autōn, epilabomenoi ton paulon kai ton silan eilkusan eis tēn agoran epi tous archontas,
act|16|20|	kai prosagagontes autous tois stratēgois eipon outoi oi anthrōpoi ektarassousin ēmōn tēn polin ioudaioi uparchontes,
act|16|21|	kai kataggellousin ethē a ouk exestin ēmin paradechesthai oude poiein rōmaiois ousi.
act|16|22|	kai sunepestē o ochlos kat autōn. kai oi stratēgoi perirrēxantes autōn ta imatia ekeleuon rabdizein,
act|16|23|	pollas te epithentes autois plēgas ebalon eis phulakēn, paraggeilantes tō desmophulaki asphalōs tērein autous
act|16|24|	os paraggelian toiautēn eilēphōs ebalen autous eis tēn esōteran phulakēn kai tous podas autōn ēsphalisato eis to xulon.
act|16|25|	kata de to mesonuktion paulos kai silas proseuchomenoi umnoun ton theon epēkroōnto de autōn oi desmioi.
act|16|26|	aphnō de seismos egeneto megas, ōste saleuthēnai ta themelia tou desmōtēriou, aneōchthēsan te parachrēma ai thurai pasai kai pantōn ta desma anethē.
act|16|27|	exupnos de genomenos o desmophulax kai idōn aneōgmenas tas thuras tēs phulakēs, spasamenos machairan emellen eauton anairein, nomizōn ekpepheugenai tous desmious.
act|16|28|	ephōnēse de phōnē megalē o paulos legōn mēden praxēs seautō kakon apantes gar esmen enthade.
act|16|29|	aitēsas de phōta eisepēdēse, kai entromos genomenos prosepese tō paulō kai tō sila,
act|16|30|	kai proagagōn autous exō ephē kurioi, ti me dei poiein ina sōthō?
act|16|31|	oi de eipon pisteuson epi ton kurion iēsoun christon, kai sōthēsē su kai o oikos sou.
act|16|32|	kai elalēsan autō ton logon tou kuriou kai pasi tois en tē oikia autou.
act|16|33|	kai paralabōn autous en ekeinē tē ōra tēs nuktos elousen apo tōn plēgōn, kai ebaptisthē autos kai oi autou pantes parachrēma,
act|16|34|	anagagōn te autous eis ton oikon autou parethēke trapezan, kai ēgalliato panoiki pepisteukōs tō theō.

act|16|36|	apēggeile de o desmophulax tous logous toutous pros ton paulon, oti apestalkasin oi stratēgoi ina apoluthēte. nun oun exelthontes poreuesthe en eirēnē.

act|17|1|	diodeusantes de tēn amphipolin kai apollōnian ēlthon eis thessalonikēn, opou ēn ē sunagōgē tōn ioudaiōn.

act|17|4|	kai tines ex autōn epeisthēsan kai proseklērōthēsan tō paulō kai tō sila, tōn te sebomenōn ellēnōn polu plēthos gunaikōn te tōn prōtōn ouk oligai.

act|17|10|	oi de adelphoi eutheōs dia tēs nuktos exepempsan ton te paulon kai ton silan eis beroian, oitines paragenomenoi eis tēn sunagōgēn apēesan tōn ioudaiōn.
act|17|11|	outoi de ēsan eugenesteroi tōn en thessalonikē, oitines edexanto ton logon meta pasēs prothumias, to kath ēmeran anakrinontes tas graphas ei echoi tauta outōs.
act|17|12|	polloi men oun ex autōn episteusan, kai tōn ellēnidōn gunaikōn tōn euschēmonōn kai andrōn ouk oligoi.

act|17|14|	eutheōs de tote ton paulon exapesteilan oi adelphoi poreuesthai ōs epi tēn thalassan upemenon de o te silas kai o timotheos ekei.

act|17|18|	tines de tōn epikoureiōn kai tōn stoikōn philosophōn suneballon autō, kai tines elegon ti an theloi o spermologos outos legein? oi de xenōn daimoniōn dokei kataggeleus einai oti ton iēsoun kai tēn anastasin euēggelizeto autois.

act|17|23|	dierchomenos gar kai anatheōrōn ta sebasmata umōn euron kai bōmon en ō epegegrapto, agnōstō theō. on oun agnoountes eusebeite, touton egō kataggellō umin.

act|18|1|	meta de tauta chōristheis o paulos ek tōn athēnōn ēlthen eis korinthon
act|18|2|	kai eurōn tina ioudaion onomati akulan, pontikon tō genei, prosphatōs elēluthota apo tēs italias, kai priskillan gunaika autou, dia to diatetachenai klaudion chōrizesthai pantas tous ioudaious apo tēs rōmēs, prosēlthen autois,

act|18|15|	ei de zētēma esti peri logou kai onomatōn kai nomou tou kath umas, opsesthe autoi kritēs gar egō toutōn ou boulomai einai.

act|20|19|	douleuōn tō kuriō meta pasēs tapeinophrosunēs kai pollōn dakruōn kai peirasmōn tōn sumbantōn moi en tais epiboulais tōn ioudaiōn,
act|20|20|	ōs ouden upesteilamēn tōn sumpherontōn tou mē anaggeilai umin kai didaxai umas dēmosia kai kat oikous,
act|20|21|	diamarturomenos ioudaiois te kai ellēsi tēn eis ton theon metanoian kai pistin tēn eis ton kurion ēmōn iēsoun christon.
act|20|22|	kai nun idou egō dedemenos tō pneumati poreuomai eis ierousalēm, ta en autē sunantēsonta moi mē eidōs,
act|20|23|	plēn oti to pneuma to agion kata polin diamarturetai legon oti desma me kai thlipseis menousin.
act|20|24|	all oudenos logon poioumai oude echō tēn psuchēn mou timian emautō, ōs teleiōsai ton dromon mou meta charas kai tēn diakonian ēn elabon para tou kuriou iēsou, diamarturasthai to euaggelion tēs charitos tou theou.
act|20|25|	kai nun idou egō oida oti ouketi opsesthe to prosōpon mou umeis pantes, en ois diēlthon kērussōn tēn basileian tou theou.
act|20|26|	dio marturomai umin en tē sēmeron ēmera oti katharos egō apo tou aimatos pantōn

act|20|28|	prosechete oun eautois kai panti tō poimniō en ō umas to pneuma to agion etheto episkopous, poimainein tēn ekklēsian tou kuriou kai theou, ēn periepoiēsato dia tou idiou aimatos.

act|20|30|	kai ex umōn autōn anastēsontai andres lalountes diestrammena tou apospan tous mathētas opisō autōn.

act|20|32|	kai ta nun paratithemai umas, adelphoi, tō theō kai tō logō tēs charitos autou tō dunamenō epoikodomēsai kai dounai umin klēronomian en tois ēgiasmenois pasin.
act|20|33|	arguriou ē chrusiou ē imatismou oudenos epethumēsa

act|20|36|	kai tauta eipōn, theis ta gonata autou sun pasin autois prosēuxato.

act|21|1|	ōs de egeneto anachthēnai ēmas apospasthentas ap autōn, euthudromēsantes ēlthomen eis tēn kō, tē de exēs eis tēn rodon, kakeithen eis patara.
act|21|2|	kai eurontes ploion diaperōn eis phoinikēn epibantes anēchthēmen.
act|21|3|	anaphanentes de tēn kupron kai katalipontes autēn euōnumon epleomen eis surian, kai katēchthēmen eis turon ekeise gar ēn to ploion apophortizomenon ton gomon.
act|21|4|	kai aneurontes tous mathētas epemeinamen autou ēmeras epta oitines tō paulō elegon dia tou pneumatos mē anabainein eis ierosoluma.
act|21|5|	ote de egeneto ēmas exartisai tas ēmeras, exelthontes eporeuometha propempontōn ēmas pantōn sun gunaixi kai teknois eōs exō tēs poleōs, kai thentes ta gonata epi ton aigialon prosēuxametha,
act|21|6|	kai aspasamenoi allēlous epebēmen eis to ploion, ekeinoi de upestrepsan eis ta idia.
act|21|7|	ēmeis de ton ploun dianusantes apo turou katēntēsamen eis ptolemaida, kai aspasamenoi tous adelphous emeinamen ēmeran mian par autois.
act|21|8|	tē de epaurion exelthontes ēlthomen eis kaisareian, kai eiselthontes eis ton oikon philippou tou euaggelistou, ontos ek tōn epta, emeinamen par autō.
act|21|9|	toutō de ēsan thugateres parthenoi tessares prophēteuousai.

act|21|11|	kai elthōn pros ēmas kai aras tēn zōnēn tou paulou, dēsas te autou tous podas kai tas cheiras eipe tade legei to pneuma to agion ton andra ou estin ē zōnē autē, outō dēsousin eis ierousalēm oi ioudaioi kai paradōsousin eis cheiras ethnōn.
act|21|12|	ōs de ēkousamen tauta, parekaloumen ēmeis te kai oi entopioi tou mē anabainein auton eis ierousalēm.
act|21|13|	apekrithē te o paulos ti poieite klaiontes kai sunthruptontes mou tēn kardian? egō gar ou monon dethēnai, alla kai apothanein eis ierousalēm etoimōs echō uper tou onomatos tou kuriou iēsou.
act|21|14|	mē peithomenou de autou ēsuchasamen eipontes to thelēma tou kuriou ginesthō.

act|21|18|	tē de epiousē eisēei o paulos sun ēmin pros iakōbon, pantes te paregenonto oi presbuteroi.
act|21|19|	kai aspasamenos autous exēgeito kath en ekaston ōn epoiēsen o theos en tois ethnesi dia tēs diakonias autou.
act|21|20|	oi de akousantes edoxazon ton kurion, eipon te autō theōreis, adelphe, posai muriades eisin ioudaiōn tōn pepisteukotōn, kai pantes zēlōtai tou nomou uparchousi.
act|21|21|	katēchēthēsan de peri sou oti apostasian didaskeis apo mōuseōs tous kata ta ethnē pantas ioudaious, legōn mē peritemnein autous ta tekna mēde tois ethesi peripatein.
act|21|22|	ti oun esti? pantōs dei plēthos sunelthein akousontai gar oti elēluthas.

act|21|24|	toutous paralabōn agnisthēti sun autois kai dapanēson ep autois ina xurēsōntai tēn kephalēn, kai gnōsi pantes oti ōn katēchēntai peri sou ouden estin, alla stoicheis kai autos ton nomon phulassōn.

act|23|1|	atenisas de o paulos tō sunedriō eipen andres adelphoi, egō pasē suneidēsei agathē pepoliteumai tō theō achri tautēs tēs ēmeras.

act|24|1|	meta de pente ēmeras katebē o archiereus ananias meta tōn presbuterōn kai rētoros tertullou tinos, oitines enephanisan tō ēgemoni kata tou paulou.

act|25|1|	phēstos oun epibas tē eparchia meta treis ēmeras anebē eis ierosoluma apo kaisareias

act|28|15|	kakeithen oi adelphoi akousantes ta peri ēmōn exēlthon eis apantēsin ēmin achris appiou phorou kai triōn tabernōn, ous idōn o paulos eucharistēsas tō theō elabe tharsos.
act|28|16|	ote de ēlthomen eis rōmēn, o ekatontarchēs paredōke tous desmious tō stratopedarchē tō de paulō epetrapē menein kath eauton sun tō phulassonti auton stratiōtē.
act|28|17|	egeneto de meta ēmeras treis sugkalesasthai ton paulon tous ontas tōn ioudaiōn prōtous sunelthontōn de autōn elege pros autous andres adelphoi, egō ouden enantion poiēsas tō laō ē tois ethesi tois patrōois desmios ex ierosolumōn paredothēn eis tas cheiras tōn rōmaiōn
act|28|18|	oitines anakrinantes me eboulonto apolusai dia to mēdemian aitian thanatou uparchein en emoi.

act|28|20|	dia tautēn oun tēn aitian parekalesa umas idein kai proslalēsai eneken gar tēs elpidos tou israēl tēn alusin tautēn perikeimai.
act|28|21|	oi de pros auton eipon ēmeis oute grammata peri sou edexametha apo tēs ioudaias, oute paragenomenos tis tōn adelphōn apēggeilen ē elalēse ti peri sou ponēron.
act|28|22|	axioumen de para sou akousai a phroneis peri men gar tēs aireseōs tautēs gnōston estin ēmin oti pantachou antilegetai.
act|28|23|	taxamenoi de autō ēmeran ēkon pros auton eis tēn xenian pleiones, ois exetitheto diamarturomenos tēn basileian tou theou peithōn te autous ta peri tou iēsou apo te tou nomou mōuseōs kai tōn prophētōn apo prōi eōs esperas.
act|28|24|	kai oi men epeithonto tois legomenois, oi de ēpistoun.

rom|5|2|	di ou kai tēn prosagōgēn eschēkamen tē pistei eis tēn charin tautēn en ē estēkamen, kai kauchōmetha ep elpidi tēs doxēs tou theou.
rom|5|3|	ou monon de, alla kai kauchōmetha en tais thlipsesin, eidotes oti ē thlipsis upomonēn katergazetai,
rom|5|4|	ē de upomonē dokimēn, ē de dokimē elpida,
rom|5|5|	ē de elpis ou kataischunei, oti ē agapē tou theou ekkechutai en tais kardiais ēmōn dia pneumatos agiou tou dothentos ēmin.
rom|5|6|	eti gar christos ontōn ēmōn asthenōn kata kairon uper asebōn apethane.
rom|5|7|	molis gar uper dikaiou tis apothaneitai uper gar tou agathou tacha tis kai tolma apothanein.
rom|5|8|	sunistēsi de tēn eautou agapēn eis ēmas o theos, oti eti amartōlōn ontōn ēmōn christos uper ēmōn apethane.
rom|5|9|	pollō oun mallon dikaiōthentes nun en tō aimati autou sōthēsometha di autou apo tēs orgēs.
rom|5|10|	ei gar echthroi ontes katēllagēmen tō theō dia tou thanatou tou uiou autou, pollō mallon katallagentes sōthēsometha en tē zōē autou
rom|5|11|	ou monon de, alla kai kauchōmenoi en tō theō dia tou kuriou ēmōn iēsou christou, di ou nun tēn katallagēn elabomen.
rom|5|12|	dia touto ōsper di enos anthrōpou ē amartia eis ton kosmon eisēlthe kai dia tēs amartias o thanatos, kai outōs eis pantas anthrōpous o thanatos diēlthen, eph ō pantes ēmarton—
rom|5|13|	achri gar nomou amartia ēn en kosmō, amartia de ouk ellogeitai mē ontos nomou
rom|5|14|	all ebasileusen o thanatos apo adam mechri mōuseōs kai epi tous mē amartēsantas epi tō omoiōmati tēs parabaseōs adam, os esti tupos tou mellontos.
rom|5|15|	all ouch ōs to paraptōma, outō kai to charisma. ei gar tō tou enos paraptōmati oi polloi apethanon, pollō mallon ē charis tou theou kai ē dōrea en chariti tē tou enos anthrōpou iēsou christou eis tous pollous eperisseuse.
rom|5|16|	kai ouch ōs di enos amartēsantos to dōrēma to men gar krima ex enos eis katakrima, to de charisma ek pollōn paraptōmatōn eis dikaiōma.
rom|5|17|	ei gar tō tou enos paraptōmati o thanatos ebasileuse dia tou enos, pollō mallon oi tēn perisseian tēs charitos kai tēs dōreas tēs dikaiosunēs lambanontes en zōē basileusousi dia tou enos iēsou christou.
rom|5|18|	ara oun ōs di enos paraptōmatos eis pantas anthrōpous eis katakrima, outō kai di enos dikaiōmatos eis pantas anthrōpous eis dikaiōsin zōēs.
rom|5|19|	ōsper gar dia tēs parakoēs tou enos anthrōpou amartōloi katestathēsan oi polloi, outō kai dia tēs upakoēs tou enos dikaioi katastathēsontai oi polloi.
rom|5|20|	nomos de pareisēlthen ina pleonasē to paraptōma. ou de epleonasen ē amartia, upereperisseusen ē charis,
rom|5|21|	ina ōsper ebasileusen ē amartia en tō thanatō, outō kai ē charis basileusē dia dikaiosunēs eis zōēn aiōnion dia iēsou christou tou kuriou ēmōn.
rom|6|1|	ti oun eroumen? epimenoumen tē amartia ina ē charis pleonasē?
rom|6|2|	mē genoito. oitines apethanomen tē amartia, pōs eti zēsomen en autē?
rom|6|3|	ē agnoeite oti osoi ebaptisthēmen eis christon iēsoun, eis ton thanaton autou ebaptisthēmen?
rom|6|4|	sunetaphēmen oun autō dia tou baptismatos eis ton thanaton, ina ōsper ēgerthē christos ek nekrōn dia tēs doxēs tou patros, outō kai ēmeis en kainotēti zōēs peripatēsōmen.
rom|6|5|	ei gar sumphutoi gegonamen tō omoiōmati tou thanatou autou, alla kai tēs anastaseōs esometha,
rom|6|6|	touto ginōskontes, oti o palaios ēmōn anthrōpos sunestaurōthē ina katargēthē to sōma tēs amartias, tou mēketi douleuein ēmas tē amartia
rom|6|7|	o gar apothanōn dedikaiōtai apo tēs amartias.

rom|6|12|	mē oun basileuetō ē amartia en tō thnētō umōn sōmati eis to upakouein autē en tais epithumiais autou,
rom|6|13|	mēde paristanete ta melē umōn opla adikias tē amartia, alla parastēsate eautous tō theō ōs ek nekrōn zōntas kai ta melē umōn opla dikaiosunēs tō theō.
rom|6|14|	amartia gar umōn ou kurieusei ou gar este upo nomon, all upo charin.
rom|6|15|	ti oun? amartēsomen oti ouk esmen upo nomon, all upo charin? mē genoito.
rom|6|16|	ouk oidate oti ō paristanete eautous doulous eis upakoēn, douloi este ō upakouete, ētoi amartias eis thanaton ē upakoēs eis dikaiosunēn?
rom|6|17|	charis de tō theō oti ēte douloi tēs amartias, upēkousate de ek kardias eis on paredothēte tupon didachēs,
rom|6|18|	eleutherōthentes de apo tēs amartias edoulōthēte tē dikaiosunē.
rom|6|19|	anthrōpinon legō dia tēn astheneian tēs sarkos umōn. ōsper gar parestēsate ta melē umōn doula tē akatharsia kai tē anomia eis tēn anomian, outō nun parastēsate ta melē umōn doula tē dikaiosunē eis agiasmon.
rom|6|20|	ote gar douloi ēte tēs amartias, eleutheroi ēte tē dikaiosunē.
rom|6|21|	tina oun karpon eichete tote eph ois nun epaischunesthe? to gar telos ekeinōn thanatos.
rom|6|22|	nuni de eleutherōthentes apo tēs amartias doulōthentes de tō theō echete ton karpon umōn eis agiasmon, to de telos zōēn aiōnion.
rom|6|23|	ta gar opsōnia tēs amartias thanatos, to de charisma tou theou zōē aiōnios en christō iēsou tō kuriō ēmōn.
rom|7|1|	ē agnoeite, adelphoi ginōskousi gar nomon lalō oti o nomos kurieuei tou anthrōpou eph oson chronon zē?
rom|7|2|	ē gar upandros gunē tō zōnti andri dedetai nomō ean de apothanē o anēr, katērgētai apo tou nomou tou andros.
rom|7|3|	ara oun zōntos tou andros moichalis chrēmatisei ean genētai andri eterō ean de apothanē o anēr, eleuthera estin apo tou nomou, tou mē einai autēn moichalida genomenēn andri eterō.
rom|7|4|	ōste, adelphoi mou, kai umeis ethanatōthēte tō nomō dia tou sōmatos tou christou eis to genesthai umas eterō, tō ek nekrōn egerthenti, ina karpophorēsōmen tō theō.
rom|7|5|	ote gar ēmen en tē sarki, ta pathēmata tōn amartiōn ta dia tou nomou enērgeito en tois melesin ēmōn eis to karpophorēsai tō thanatō

rom|7|13|	to oun agathon emoi gegone thanatos? mē genoito alla ē amartia, ina phanē amartia, dia tou agathou moi katergazomenē thanaton, ina genētai kath uperbolēn amartōlos ē amartia dia tēs entolēs.
rom|7|14|	oidamen gar oti o nomos pneumatikos estin egō de sarkikos eimi, pepramenos upo tēn amartian.

rom|7|16|	ei de o ou thelō touto poiō, sumphēmi tō nomō oti kalos.
rom|7|17|	nuni de ouketi egō katergazomai auto, all ē oikousa en emoi amartia.

rom|7|19|	ou gar o thelō poiō agathon, all o ou thelō kakon touto prassō.

rom|10|1|	adelphoi, ē men eudokia tēs emēs kardias kai ē deēsis ē pros ton theon uper tou israēl estin eis sōtērian
rom|10|2|	marturō gar autois oti zēlon theou echousin, all ou kat epignōsin.
rom|10|3|	agnoountes gar tēn tou theou dikaiosunēn, kai tēn idian dikaiosunēn zētountes stēsai, tē dikaiosunē tou theou ouch upetagēsan.
rom|10|4|	telos gar nomou christos eis dikaiosunēn panti tō pisteuonti.
rom|10|5|	mōusēs gar graphei tēn dikaiosunēn tēn ek tou nomou, oti o poiēsas auta anthrōpos zēsetai en autois
rom|10|6|	ē de ek pisteōs dikaiosunē outō legei mē eipēs en tē kardia sou, tis anabēsetai eis ton ouranon? tout esti christon katagagein

rom|10|16|	all ou pantes upēkousan tō euaggeliō ēsaias gar legei kurie, tis episteuse tē akoē ēmōn?

rom|10|19|	alla legō, mē ouk egnō israēl? prōtos mōusēs legei egō parazēlōsō umas ep ouk ethnei, epi ethnei asunetō parorgiō umas.

rom|16|20|	o de theos tēs eirēnēs suntripsei ton satanan upo tous podas umōn en tachei. ē charis tou kuriou ēmōn iēsou christou meth umōn.
rom|16|21|	aspazontai umas timotheos o sunergos mou, kai loukios kai iasōn kai sōsipatros oi suggeneis mou.
rom|16|22|	aspazomai umas egō tertios o grapsas tēn epistolēn en kuriō.
rom|16|23|	aspazetai umas gaios o xenos mou kai tēs ekklēsias olēs. aspazetai umas erastos o oikonomos tēs poleōs kai kouartos o adelphos.
rom|16|24|	ē charis tou kuriou ēmōn iēsou christou meta pantōn umōn amēn.
1co|1|1|	paulos, klētos apostolos iēsou christou dia thelēmatos theou, kai sōsthenēs o adelphos,
1co|1|2|	tē ekklēsia tou theou tē ousē en korinthō, ēgiasmenois en christō iēsou, klētois agiois, sun pasi tois epikaloumenois to onoma tou kuriou ēmōn iēsou christou en panti topō autōn te kai ēmōn
1co|1|3|	charis umin kai eirēnē apo theou patros ēmōn kai kuriou iēsou christou.
1co|1|4|	eucharistō tō theō mou pantote peri umōn epi tē chariti tou theou tē dotheisē umin en christō iēsou,
1co|1|5|	oti en panti eploutisthēte en autō, en panti logō kai pasē gnōsei,
1co|1|6|	kathōs to marturion tou christou ebebaiōthē en umin,
1co|1|7|	ōste umas mē ustereisthai en mēdeni charismati, apekdechomenous tēn apokalupsin tou kuriou ēmōn iēsou christou
1co|1|8|	os kai bebaiōsei umas eōs telous anegklētous en tē ēmera tou kuriou ēmōn iēsou christou.
1co|1|9|	pistos o theos di ou eklēthēte eis koinōnian tou uiou autou iēsou christou tou kuriou ēmōn.
1co|1|10|	parakalō de umas, adelphoi, dia tou onomatos tou kuriou ēmōn iēsou christou, ina to auto legēte pantes, kai mē ē en umin schismata, ēte de katērtismenoi en tō autō noi kai en tē autē gnōmē.
1co|1|11|	edēlōthē gar moi peri umōn, adelphoi mou, upo tōn chloēs oti erides en umin eisi.
1co|1|12|	legō de touto, oti ekastos umōn legei egō men eimi paulou, egō de apollō, egō de kēpha, egō de christou.
1co|1|13|	memeristai o christos? mē paulos estaurōthē uper umōn? ē eis to onoma paulou ebaptisthēte?
1co|1|14|	eucharistō tō theō oti oudena umōn ebaptisa ei mē krispon kai gaion,
1co|1|15|	ina mē tis eipē oti eis to emon onoma ebaptisa.
1co|1|16|	ebaptisa de kai ton stephana oikon loipon ouk oida ei tina allon ebaptisa.
1co|1|17|	ou gar apesteile me christos baptizein, all euaggelizesthai, ouk en sophia logou, ina mē kenōthē o stauros tou christou.
1co|1|18|	o logos gar o tou staurou tois men apollumenois mōria esti, tois de sōzomenois ēmin dunamis theou esti.
1co|1|19|	gegraptai gar apolō tēn sophian tōn sophōn, kai tēn sunesin tōn sunetōn athetēsō.
1co|1|20|	pou sophos? pou grammateus? pou suzētētēs tou aiōnos toutou? ouchi emōranen o theos tēn sophian tou kosmou toutou?
1co|1|21|	epeidē gar en tē sophia tou theou ouk egnō o kosmos dia tēs sophias ton theon, eudokēsen o theos dia tēs mōrias tou kērugmatos sōsai tous pisteuontas.
1co|1|22|	epeidē kai ioudaioi sēmeion aitousi kai ellēnes sophian zētousin,
1co|1|23|	ēmeis de kērussomen christon estaurōmenon, ioudaiois men skandalon, ellēsi de mōrian,
1co|1|24|	autois de tois klētois, ioudaiois te kai ellēsi, christon theou dunamin kai theou sophian
1co|1|25|	oti to mōron tou theou sophōteron tōn anthrōpōn esti, kai to asthenes tou theou ischuroteron tōn anthrōpōn esti.
1co|1|26|	blepete gar tēn klēsin umōn, adelphoi, oti ou polloi sophoi kata sarka, ou polloi dunatoi, ou polloi eugeneis,
1co|1|27|	alla ta mōra tou kosmou exelexato o theos ina tous sophous kataischunē, kai ta asthenē tou kosmou exelexato o theos ina kataischunē ta ischura,
1co|1|28|	kai ta agenē tou kosmou kai ta exouthenēmena exelexato o theos, kai ta mē onta, ina ta onta katargēsē,
1co|1|29|	opōs mē kauchēsētai pasa sarx enōpion tou theou.
1co|1|30|	ex autou de umeis este en christō iēsou, os egenēthē ēmin sophia apo theou, dikaiosunē te kai agiasmos kai apolutrōsis,
1co|1|31|	ina, kathōs gegraptai, o kauchōmenos en kuriō kauchasthō.
1co|2|1|	kagō elthōn pros umas, adelphoi, ēlthon ou kath uperochēn logou ē sophias kataggellōn umin to marturion tou theou.
1co|2|2|	ou gar ekrina tou eidenai ti en umin ei mē iēsoun christon, kai touton estaurōmenon.
1co|2|3|	kai egō en astheneia kai en phobō kai en tromō pollō egenomēn pros umas,
1co|2|4|	kai o logos mou kai to kērugma mou ouk en peithois anthrōpinēs sophias logois, all en apodeixei pneumatos kai dunameōs,
1co|2|5|	ina ē pistis umōn mē ē en sophia anthrōpōn, all en dunamei theou.
1co|2|6|	sophian de laloumen en tois teleiois, sophian de ou tou aiōnos toutou, oude tōn archontōn tou aiōnos toutou tōn katargoumenōn
1co|2|7|	alla laloumen sophian theou en mustēriō, tēn apokekrummenēn, ēn proōrisen o theos pro tōn aiōnōn eis doxan ēmōn,
1co|2|8|	ēn oudeis tōn archontōn tou aiōnos toutou egnōken ei gar egnōsan, ouk an ton kurion tēs doxēs estaurōsan
1co|2|9|	alla kathōs gegraptai, a ophthalmos ouk eide kai ous ouk ēkouse kai epi kardian anthrōpou ouk anebē, a ētoimasen o theos tois agapōsin auton.
1co|2|10|	ēmin de o theos apekalupse dia tou pneumatos autou to gar pneuma panta ereuna, kai ta bathē tou theou.
1co|2|11|	tis gar oiden anthrōpōn ta tou anthrōpou ei mē to pneuma tou anthrōpou to en autō? outō kai ta tou theou oudeis oiden ei mē to pneuma tou theou.
1co|2|12|	ēmeis de ou to pneuma tou kosmou elabomen, alla to pneuma to ek tou theou, ina eidōmen ta upo tou theou charisthenta ēmin.
1co|2|13|	a kai laloumen ouk en didaktois anthrōpinēs sophias logois, all en didaktois pneumatos agiou, pneumatikois pneumatika sugkrinontes.
1co|2|14|	psuchikos de anthrōpos ou dechetai ta tou pneumatos tou theou mōria gar autō esti, kai ou dunatai gnōnai, oti pneumatikōs anakrinetai.
1co|2|15|	o de pneumatikos anakrinei men panta, autos de up oudenos anakrinetai.
1co|2|16|	tis gar egnō noun kuriou, os sumbibasei auton? ēmeis de noun christou echomen.
1co|3|1|	kai egō, adelphoi, ouk ēdunēthēn umin lalēsai ōs pneumatikois, all ōs sarkikois, ōs nēpiois en christō.
1co|3|2|	gala umas epotisa kai ou brōma oupō gar ēdunasthe. all oute eti nun dunasthe eti gar sarkikoi este.
1co|3|3|	opou gar en umin zēlos kai eris kai dichostasiai, ouchi sarkikoi este kai kata anthrōpon peripateite?
1co|3|4|	otan gar legē tis, egō men eimi paulou, eteros de egō apollō, ouchi sarkikoi este?
1co|3|5|	tis oun esti paulos, tis de apollōs all ē diakonoi di ōn episteusate, kai ekastō ōs o kurios edōken?
1co|3|6|	egō ephuteusa, apollōs epotisen, all o theos ēuxanen
1co|3|7|	ōste oute o phuteuōn esti ti oute o potizōn, all o auxanōn theos.
1co|3|8|	o phuteuōn de kai o potizōn en eisin ekastos de ton idion misthon lēpsetai kata ton idion kopon.
1co|3|9|	theou gar esmen sunergoi theou geōrgion, theou oikodomē este.
1co|3|10|	kata tēn charin tou theou tēn dotheisan moi ōs sophos architektōn themelion tetheika, allos de epoikodomei ekastos de blepetō pōs epoikodomei
1co|3|11|	themelion gar allon oudeis dunatai theinai para ton keimenon, os estin iēsous christos.
1co|3|12|	ei de tis epoikodomei epi ton themelion touton chruson, arguron, lithous timious, xula, chorton, kalamēn,
1co|3|13|	ekastou to ergon phaneron genēsetai ē gar ēmera dēlōsei oti en puri apokaluptetai kai ekastou to ergon opoion esti to pur dokimasei.
1co|3|14|	ei tinos to ergon menei o epōkodomēse, misthon lēpsetai
1co|3|15|	ei tinos to ergon katakaēsetai, zēmiōthēsetai, autos de sōthēsetai, outōs de ōs dia puros.
1co|3|16|	ouk oidate oti naos theou este kai to pneuma tou theou oikei en umin?
1co|3|17|	ei tis ton naon tou theou phtheirei, phtherei touton o theos o gar naos tou theou agios estin, oitines este umeis.
1co|3|18|	mēdeis eauton exapatatō ei tis dokei sophos einai en umin en tō aiōni toutō, mōros genesthō, ina genētai sophos.
1co|3|19|	ē gar sophia tou kosmou toutou mōria para tō theō esti. gegraptai gar o drassomenos tous sophous en tē panourgia autōn
1co|3|20|	kai palin kurios ginōskei tous dialogismous tōn sophōn, oti eisi mataioi.
1co|3|21|	ōste mēdeis kauchasthō en anthrōpois panta gar umōn estin,
1co|3|22|	eite paulos eite apollōs eite kēphas eite kosmos eite zōē eite thanatos eite enestōta eite mellonta, panta umōn estin,
1co|3|23|	umeis de christou, christos de theou.
1co|4|1|	outōs ēmas logizesthō anthrōpos, ōs upēretas christou kai oikonomous mustēriōn theou.
1co|4|2|	o de loipon zēteitai en tois oikonomois, ina pistos tis eurethē.
1co|4|3|	emoi de eis elachiston estin ina uph umōn anakrithō ē upo anthrōpinēs ēmeras all oude emauton anakrinō
1co|4|4|	ouden gar emautō sunoida all ouk en toutō dedikaiōmai o de anakrinōn me kurios estin.
1co|4|5|	ōste mē pro kairou ti krinete, eōs an elthē o kurios, os kai phōtisei ta krupta tou skotous kai phanerōsei tas boulas tōn kardiōn, kai tote o epainos genēsetai ekastō apo tou theou.
1co|4|6|	tauta de, adelphoi, meteschēmatisa eis emauton kai apollō di umas, ina en ēmin mathēte to mē uper o gegraptai phronein, ina mē eis uper tou enos phusiousthe kata tou eterou.
1co|4|7|	tis gar se diakrinei? ti de echeis o ouk elabes? ei de kai elabes, ti kauchasai ōs mē labōn?
1co|4|8|	ēdē kekoresmenoi este, ēdē eploutēsate, chōris ēmōn ebasileusate kai ophelon ge ebasileusate, ina kai ēmeis umin sumbasileusōmen.
1co|4|9|	dokō gar oti o theos ēmas tous apostolous eschatous apedeixen, ōs epithanatious, oti theatron egenēthēmen tō kosmō, kai aggelois kai anthrōpois.
1co|4|10|	ēmeis mōroi dia christon, umeis de phronimoi en christō ēmeis astheneis, umeis de ischuroi umeis endoxoi, ēmeis de atimoi.

1co|4|13|	blasphēmoumenoi parakaloumen ōs perikatharmata tou kosmou egenēthēmen, pantōn peripsēma eōs arti.
1co|4|14|	ouk entrepōn umas graphō tauta, all ōs tekna mou agapēta nouthetō.
1co|4|15|	ean gar murious paidagōgous echēte en christō, all ou pollous pateras en gar christō iēsou dia tou euaggeliou egō umas egennēsa.
1co|4|16|	parakalō oun umas, mimētai mou ginesthe.
1co|4|17|	dia touto epempsa umin timotheon, os esti teknon mou agapēton kai piston en kuriō, os umas anamnēsei tas odous mou tas en christō, kathōs pantachou en pasē ekklēsia didaskō.
1co|4|18|	ōs mē erchomenou de mou pros umas ephusiōthēsan tines

1co|4|20|	ou gar en logō ē basileia tou theou, all en dunamei.

1co|5|1|	olōs akouetai en umin porneia, kai toiautē porneia, ētis oude en tois ethnesin onomazetai, ōste gunaika tina tou patros echein.
1co|5|2|	kai umeis pephusiōmenoi este, kai ouchi mallon epenthēsate, ina exarthē ek mesou umōn o to ergon touto poiēsas!
1co|5|3|	egō men gar ōs apōn tō sōmati, parōn de tō pneumati, ēdē kekrika ōs parōn ton outō touto katergasamenon,
1co|5|4|	en tō onomati tou kuriou ēmōn iēsou christou sunachthentōn umōn kai tou emou pneumatos sun tē dunamei tou kuriou ēmōn iēsou christou

1co|6|3|	ouk oidate oti aggelous krinoumen? mēti ge biōtika?

1co|6|12|	panta moi exestin, all ou panta sumpherei panta moi exestin, all ouk egō exousiasthēsomai upo tinos.

1co|7|1|	peri de ōn egrapsate moi, kalon anthrōpō gunaikos mē aptesthai
1co|7|2|	dia de tas porneias ekastos tēn eautou gunaika echetō, kai ekastē ton idion andra echetō.
1co|7|3|	tē gunaiki o anēr tēn opheilomenēn eunoian apodidotō, omoiōs de kai ē gunē tō andri.
1co|7|4|	ē gunē tou idiou sōmatos ouk exousiazei, all o anēr omoiōs de kai o anēr tou idiou sōmatos ouk exousiazei, all ē gunē.
1co|7|5|	mē apostereite allēlous, ei mē ti an ek sumphōnou pros kairon, ina scholazēte tē nēsteia kai tē proseuchē kai palin epi to auto sunerchēsthe, ina mē peirazē umas o satanas dia tēn akrasian umōn.
1co|7|6|	touto de legō kata suggnōmēn, ou kat epitagēn.
1co|7|7|	thelō gar pantas anthrōpous einai ōs kai emauton all ekastos idion charisma echei ek theou, os men outōs, os de outōs.
1co|7|8|	legō de tois agamois kai tais chērais, kalon autois estin ean meinōsin ōs kagō.
1co|7|9|	ei de ouk egkrateuontai, gamēsatōsan kreisson gar esti gamēsai ē purousthai.
1co|7|10|	tois de gegamēkosi paraggellō, ouk egō, all o kurios, gunaika apo andros mē chōristhēnai
1co|7|11|	ean de kai chōristhē, menetō agamos ē tō andri katallagētō kai andra gunaika mē aphienai.
1co|7|12|	tois de loipois egō legō, ouch o kurios ei tis adelphos gunaika echei apiston, kai autē suneudokei oikein met autou, mē aphietō autēn
1co|7|13|	kai gunē ei tis echei andra apiston, kai autos suneudokei oikein met autēs, mē aphietō auton.
1co|7|14|	ēgiastai gar o anēr o apistos en tē gunaiki, kai ēgiastai ē gunē ē apistos en tō andri epei ara ta tekna umōn akatharta esti, nun de agia estin.
1co|7|15|	ei de o apistos chōrizetai, chōrizesthō. ou dedoulōtai o adelphos ē ē adelphē en tois toioutois. en de eirēnē keklēken ēmas o theos.
1co|7|16|	ti gar oidas, gunai, ei ton andra sōseis? ē ti oidas, aner, ei tēn gunaika sōseis?
1co|7|17|	ei mē ekastō ōs emerisen o theos, ekaston ōs keklēken o kurios, outō peripateitō. kai outōs en tais ekklēsiais pasais diatassomai.
1co|7|18|	peritetmēmenos tis eklēthē? mē epispasthō. en akrobustia tis eklēthē? mē peritemnesthō.
1co|7|19|	ē peritomē ouden esti, kai ē akrobustia ouden estin, alla tērēsis entolōn theou.
1co|7|20|	ekastos en tē klēsei ē eklēthē, en tautē menetō.
1co|7|21|	doulos eklēthēs? mē soi meletō all ei kai dunasai eleutheros genesthai, mallon chrēsai.
1co|7|22|	o gar en kuriō klētheis doulos apeleutheros kuriou estin omoiōs kai o eleutheros klētheis doulos esti christou.

1co|12|1|	peri de tōn pneumatikōn, adelphoi, ou thelō umas agnoein.
1co|12|2|	oidate oti, ote ethnē ēte, pros ta eidōla ta aphōna ōs an ēgesthe apagomenoi.
1co|12|3|	dio gnōrizō umin oti oudeis en pneumati theou lalōn legei anathema iēsoun, kai oudeis dunatai eipein kurion iēsoun ei mē en pneumati agiō.
1co|12|4|	diaireseis de charismatōn eisi, to de auto pneuma
1co|12|5|	kai diaireseis diakoniōn eisi, kai o autos kurios
1co|12|6|	kai diaireseis energēmatōn eisin, o de autos esti theos, o energōn ta panta en pasin.
1co|12|7|	ekastō de didotai ē phanerōsis tou pneumatos pros to sumpheron.

1co|12|9|	eterō de pistis en tō autō pneumati, allō de charismata iamatōn en tō autō pneumati,
1co|12|10|	allō de energēmata dunameōn, allō de prophēteia, allō de diakriseis pneumatōn, eterō de genē glōssōn, allō de ermēneia glōssōn
1co|12|11|	panta de tauta energei to en kai to auto pneuma, diairoun idia ekastō kathōs bouletai.
1co|12|12|	kathaper gar to sōma en esti kai melē echei polla, panta de ta melē tou sōmatos tou enos, polla onta, en esti sōma, outō kai o christos
1co|12|13|	kai gar en eni pneumati ēmeis pantes eis en sōma ebaptisthēmen, eite ioudaioi eite ellēnes, eite douloi eite eleutheroi, kai pantes eis en pneuma epotisthēmen.
1co|12|14|	kai gar to sōma ouk estin en melos, alla polla.
1co|12|15|	ean eipē o pous, oti ouk eimi cheir, ouk eimi ek tou sōmatos,—ou para touto ouk estin ek tou sōmatos?
1co|12|16|	kai ean eipē to ous, oti ouk eimi ophthalmos, ouk eimi ek tou sōmatos,—ou para touto ouk estin ek tou sōmatos?
1co|12|17|	ei olon to sōma ophthalmos, pou ē akoē? ei olon akoē, pou ē osphrēsis?
1co|12|18|	nuni de o theos etheto ta melē en ekaston autōn en tō sōmati kathōs ēthelēsen.
1co|12|19|	ei de ēn ta panta en melos, pou to sōma?
1co|12|20|	nun de polla men melē, en de sōma.
1co|12|21|	ou dunatai de ophthalmos eipein tē cheiri chreian sou ouk echō ē palin ē kephalē tois posi chreian umōn ouk echō
1co|12|22|	alla pollō mallon ta dokounta melē tou sōmatos asthenestera uparchein anagkaia esti,
1co|12|23|	kai a dokoumen atimotera einai tou sōmatos, toutois timēn perissoteran peritithemen, kai ta aschēmona ēmōn euschēmosunēn perissoteran echei,
1co|12|24|	ta de euschēmona ēmōn ou chreian echei. all o theos sunekerase to sōma, tō usterounti perissoteran dous timēn,
1co|12|25|	ina mē ē schisma en tō sōmati, alla to auto uper allēlōn merimnōsi ta melē
1co|12|26|	kai eite paschei en melos, sumpaschei panta ta melē, eite doxazetai en melos, sugchairei panta ta melē.
1co|12|27|	umeis de este sōma christou kai melē ek merous.

gal|3|1|	ō anoētoi galatai, tis umas ebaskane tē alētheia mē peithesthai, ois kat ophthalmous iēsous christos proegraphē en umin estaurōmenos?
gal|3|2|	touto monon thelō mathein aph umōn ex ergōn nomou to pneuma elabete ē ex akoēs pisteōs?
gal|3|3|	outōs anoētoi este? enarxamenoi pneumati nun sarki epiteleisthe?
gal|3|4|	tosauta epathete eikē? ei ge kai eikē.
gal|3|5|	o oun epichorēgōn umin to pneuma kai energōn dunameis en umin, ex ergōn nomou ē ex akoēs pisteōs?
gal|3|6|	kathōs abraam episteuse tō theō, kai elogisthē autō eis dikaiosunēn.
gal|3|7|	ginōskete ara oti oi ek pisteōs, outoi eisin uioi abraam.
gal|3|8|	proidousa de ē graphē oti ek pisteōs dikaioi ta ethnē o theos, proeuēggelisato tō abraam oti eneulogēthēsontai en soi panta ta ethnē.
gal|3|9|	ōste oi ek pisteōs eulogountai sun tō pistō abraam.
gal|3|10|	osoi gar ex ergōn nomou eisin, upo kataran eisi gegraptai gar epikataratos pas os ouk emmenei en pasi tois gegrammenois en tō bibliō tou nomou tou poiēsai auta
gal|3|11|	oti de en nomō oudeis dikaioutai para tō theō, dēlon oti o dikaios ek pisteōs zēsetai.
gal|3|12|	o de nomos ouk estin ek pisteōs, all o poiēsas auta anthrōpos zēsetai en autois.

gal|3|14|	ina eis ta ethnē ē eulogia tou abraam genētai en christō iēsou, ina tēn epaggelian tou pneumatos labōmen dia tēs pisteōs.
gal|3|15|	adelphoi, kata anthrōpon legō omōs anthrōpou kekurōmenēn diathēkēn oudeis athetei ē epidiatassetai.
gal|3|16|	tō de abraam errethēsan ai epaggeliai kai tō spermati autou ou legei, kai tois spermasin, ōs epi pollōn, all ōs eph enos, kai tō spermati sou, os esti christos.
gal|3|17|	touto de legō diathēkēn prokekurōmenēn upo tou theou eis christon o meta etē tetrakosia kai triakonta gegonōs nomos ouk akuroi, eis to katargēsai tēn epaggelian.
gal|3|18|	ei gar ek nomou ē klēronomia, ouketi ex epaggelias tō de abraam di epaggelias kecharistai o theos.

gal|3|20|	o de mesitēs enos ouk estin, o de theos eis estin.
gal|3|21|	o oun nomos kata tōn epaggeliōn tou theou? mē genoito. ei gar edothē nomos o dunamenos zōopoiēsai, ontōs an ek nomou ēn ē dikaiosunē
gal|3|22|	alla sunekleisen ē graphē ta panta upo amartian, ina ē epaggelia ek pisteōs iēsou christou dothē tois pisteuousi.

gal|3|25|	elthousēs de tēs pisteōs ouketi upo paidagōgon esmen.

gal|4|1|	legō de, eph oson chronon o klēronomos nēpios estin, ouden diapherei doulou, kurios pantōn ōn,
gal|4|2|	alla upo epitropous esti kai oikonomous achri tēs prothesmias tou patros.

gal|4|16|	ōste echthros umōn gegona alētheuōn umin?

gal|5|1|	tē eleutheria oun, ē christos ēmas ēleutherōse, stēkete, kai mē palin zugō douleias enechesthe.

gal|6|2|	allēlōn ta barē bastazete, kai outōs anaplērōsate ton nomon tou christou.

eph|3|1|	toutou charin egō paulos o desmios tou christou iēsou uper umōn tōn ethnōn,

phi|1|5|	epi tē koinōnia umōn eis to euaggelion apo prōtēs ēmeras achri tou nun,

phi|1|7|	kathōs esti dikaion emoi touto phronein uper pantōn umōn dia to echein me en tē kardia umas, en te tois desmois mou kai en tē apologia kai bebaiōsei tou euaggeliou sugkoinōnous mou tēs charitos pantas umas ontas.
phi|1|8|	martus gar mou estin o theos, ōs epipothō pantas umas en splagchnois iēsou christou.

phi|1|14|	kai tous pleionas tōn adelphōn en kuriō pepoithotas tois desmois mou perissoterōs tolman aphobōs ton logon lalein.

phi|1|21|	emoi gar to zēn christos kai to apothanein kerdos.

phi|2|13|	o theos gar estin o energōn en umin kai to thelein kai to energein uper tēs eudokias.

phi|2|16|	logon zōēs epechontes, eis kauchēma emoi eis ēmeran christou, oti ouk eis kenon edramon oude eis kenon ekopiasa.

phi|2|18|	to d auto kai umeis chairete kai sugchairete moi.

phi|2|20|	oudena gar echō isopsuchon, ostis gnēsiōs ta peri umōn merimnēsei
phi|2|21|	oi pantes gar ta eautōn zētousin, ou ta christou iēsou.
phi|2|22|	tēn de dokimēn autou ginōskete, oti ōs patri teknon sun emoi edouleusen eis to euaggelion.
phi|2|23|	touton men oun elpizō pempsai ōs an apidō ta peri eme exautēs
phi|2|24|	pepoitha de en kuriō oti kai autos tacheōs eleusomai.
phi|2|25|	anagkaion de ēgēsamēn epaphroditon ton adelphon kai sunergon kai sustratiōtēn mou, umōn de apostolon kai leitourgon tēs chreias mou, pempsai pros umas,
phi|2|26|	epeidē epipothōn ēn pantas umas, kai adēmonōn dioti ēkousate oti ēsthenēse.
phi|2|27|	kai gar ēsthenēse paraplēsion thanatou all o theos auton ēleēsen, ouk auton de monon, alla kai eme, ina mē lupēn epi lupēn schō.
phi|2|28|	spoudaioterōs oun epempsa auton, ina idontes auton palin charēte, kagō alupoteros ō.
phi|2|29|	prosdechesthe oun auton en kuriō meta pasēs charas, kai tous toioutous entimous echete,
phi|2|30|	oti dia to ergon tou christou mechri thanatou ēggise, parabouleusamenos tē psuchē ina anaplērōsē to umōn usterēma tēs pros me leitourgias.
phi|3|1|	to loipon, adelphoi mou, chairete en kuriō. ta auta graphein umin emoi men ouk oknēron, umin de asphales.
phi|3|2|	blepete tous kunas, blepete tous kakous ergatas, blepete tēn katatomēn
phi|3|3|	ēmeis gar esmen ē peritomē, oi pneumati theou latreuontes kai kauchōmenoi en christō iēsou kai ouk en sarki pepoithotes,
phi|3|4|	kaiper egō echōn pepoithēsin kai en sarki. ei tis dokei allos pepoithenai en sarki, egō mallon
phi|3|5|	peritomē oktaēmeros, ek genous israēl, phulēs beniamin, ebraios ex ebraiōn, kata nomon pharisaios,
phi|3|6|	kata zēlon diōkōn tēn ekklēsian, kata dikaiosunēn tēn en nomō genomenos amemptos.
phi|3|7|	all atina ēn moi kerdē, tauta ēgēmai dia ton christon zēmian.
phi|3|8|	alla menounge kai ēgoumai panta zēmian einai dia to uperechon tēs gnōseōs christou iēsou tou kuriou mou, di on ta panta ezēmiōthēn, kai ēgoumai skubala einai ina christon kerdēsō
phi|3|9|	kai eurethō en autō mē echōn emēn dikaiosunēn tēn ek nomou, alla tēn dia pisteōs christou, tēn ek theou dikaiosunēn epi tē pistei,
phi|3|10|	tou gnōnai auton kai tēn dunamin tēs anastaseōs autou kai tēn koinōnian tōn pathēmatōn autou, summorphoumenos tō thanatō autou,
phi|3|11|	ei pōs katantēsō eis tēn exanastasin tōn nekrōn.
phi|3|12|	ouch oti ēdē elabon ē ēdē teteleiōmai, diōkō de ei kai katalabō, eph ō kai katelēphthēn upo tou christou iēsou.
phi|3|13|	adelphoi, egō emauton oupō logizomai kateilēphenai
phi|3|14|	en de, ta men opisō epilanthanomenos tois de emprosthen epekteinomenos kata skopon diōkō epi to brabeion tēs anō klēseōs tou theou en christō iēsou.
phi|3|15|	osoi oun teleioi, touto phronōmen kai ei ti eterōs phroneite, kai touto o theos umin apokalupsei.
phi|3|16|	plēn eis o ephthasamen, tō autō stoichein kanoni, to auto phronein.
phi|3|17|	summimētai mou ginesthe, adelphoi, kai skopeite tous outō peripatountas, kathōs echete tupon ēmas.
phi|3|18|	polloi gar peripatousin,—ous pollakis elegon umin, nun de kai klaiōn legō, tous echthrous tou staurou tou christou,
phi|3|19|	ōn to telos apōleia, ōn o theos ē koilia kai ē doxa en tē aischunē autōn, oi ta epigeia phronountes!
phi|3|20|	ēmōn gar to politeuma en ouranois uparchei, ex ou kai sōtēra apekdechometha kurion iēsoun christon,
phi|3|21|	os metaschēmatisei to sōma tēs tapeinōseōs ēmōn eis to genesthai auto summorphon tō sōmati tēs doxēs autou kata tēn energeian tou dunasthai auton kai upotaxai autō ta panta.
phi|4|1|	ōste, adelphoi mou agapētoi kai epipothētoi, chara kai stephanos mou, outō stēkete en kuriō, agapētoi.
phi|4|2|	euodian parakalō kai suntuchēn parakalō to auto phronein en kuriō
phi|4|3|	nai erōtō kai se, suzuge gnēsie, sullambanou autais, aitines en tō euaggeliō sunēthlēsan moi meta kai klēmentos kai tōn loipōn sunergōn mou, ōn ta onomata en biblō zōēs.
phi|4|4|	chairete en kuriō pantote palin erō, chairete.
phi|4|5|	to epieikes umōn gnōsthētō pasin anthrōpois. o kurios eggus.
phi|4|6|	mēden merimnate, all en panti tē proseuchē kai tē deēsei meta eucharistias ta aitēmata umōn gnōrizesthō pros ton theon.
phi|4|7|	kai ē eirēnē tou theou ē uperechousa panta noun phrourēsei tas kardias umōn kai ta noēmata umōn en christō iēsou.
phi|4|8|	to loipon, adelphoi, osa estin alēthē, osa semna, osa dikaia, osa agna, osa prosphilē, osa euphēma, ei tis aretē kai ei tis epainos, tauta logizesthe
phi|4|9|	a kai emathete kai parelabete kai ēkousate kai eidete en emoi, tauta prassete kai o theos tēs eirēnēs estai meth umōn.
phi|4|10|	echarēn de en kuriō megalōs oti ēdē pote anethalete to uper emou phronein eph ō kai ephroneite, ēkaireisthe de.
phi|4|11|	ouch oti kath usterēsin legō egō gar emathon en ois eimi autarkēs einai.
phi|4|12|	oida kai tapeinousthai, oida kai perisseuein en panti kai en pasi memuēmai kai chortazesthai kai peinan, kai perisseuein kai ustereisthai
phi|4|13|	panta ischuō en tō endunamounti me christō.
phi|4|14|	plēn kalōs epoiēsate sugkoinōnēsantes mou tē thlipsei.
phi|4|15|	oidate de kai umeis, philippēsioi, oti en archē tou euaggeliou, ote exēlthon apo makedonias, oudemia moi ekklēsia ekoinōnēsen eis logon doseōs kai lēpseōs ei mē umeis monoi,
phi|4|16|	oti kai en thessalonikē kai apax kai dis eis tēn chreian moi epempsate.
phi|4|17|	ouch oti epizētō to doma, all epizētō ton karpon ton pleonazonta eis logon umōn.
phi|4|18|	apechō de panta kai perisseuō peplērōmai dexamenos para epaphroditou ta par umōn, osmēn euōdias, thusian dektēn, euareston tō theō.
phi|4|19|	o de theos mou plērōsei pasan chreian umōn kata ton plouton autou en doxē en christō iēsou.
phi|4|20|	tō de theō kai patri ēmōn ē doxa eis tous aiōnas tōn aiōnōn amēn.

col|1|1|	paulos, apostolos iēsou christou dia thelēmatos theou, kai timotheos o adelphos,
col|1|2|	tois en kolossais agiois kai pistois adelphois en christō charis umin kai eirēnē apo theou patros ēmōn kai kuriou iēsou christou.
col|1|3|	eucharistoumen tō theō kai patri tou kuriou ēmōn iēsou christou pantote peri umōn proseuchomenoi,
col|1|4|	akousantes tēn pistin umōn en christō iēsou kai tēn agapēn tēn eis pantas tous agious,
col|1|5|	dia tēn elpida tēn apokeimenēn umin en tois ouranois, ēn proēkousate en tō logō tēs alētheias tou euaggeliou
col|1|6|	tou parontos eis umas, kathōs kai en panti tō kosmō, kai esti karpophoroumenon kai auxanomenon kathōs kai en umin, aph ēs ēmeras ēkousate kai epegnōte tēn charin tou theou en alētheia,
col|1|7|	kathōs kai emathete apo epaphra tou agapētou sundoulou ēmōn, os esti pistos uper umōn diakonos tou christou,
col|1|8|	o kai dēlōsas ēmin tēn umōn agapēn en pneumati.
col|1|9|	dia touto kai ēmeis, aph ēs ēmeras ēkousamen, ou pauometha uper umōn proseuchomenoi kai aitoumenoi ina plērōthēte tēn epignōsin tou thelēmatos autou en pasē sophia kai sunesei pneumatikē,
col|1|10|	peripatēsai umas axiōs tou kuriou eis pasan areskeian, en panti ergō agathō karpophorountes kai auxanomenoi eis tēn epignōsin tou theou,
col|1|11|	en pasē dunamei dunamoumenoi kata to kratos tēs doxēs autou eis pasan upomonēn kai makrothumian,
col|1|12|	meta charas eucharistountes tō theō kai patri tō ikanōsanti ēmas eis tēn merida tou klērou tōn agiōn en tō phōti,
col|1|13|	os errusato ēmas ek tēs exousias tou skotous kai metestēsen eis tēn basileian tou uiou tēs agapēs autou,
col|1|14|	en ō echomen tēn apolutrōsin, tēn aphesin tōn amartiōn
col|1|15|	os estin eikōn tou theou tou aoratou, prōtotokos pasēs ktiseōs,
col|1|16|	oti en autō ektisthē ta panta, ta en tois ouranois kai ta epi tēs gēs, ta orata kai ta aorata, eite thronoi eite kuriotētes eite archai eite exousiai ta panta di autou kai eis auton ektistai
col|1|17|	kai autos esti pro pantōn, kai ta panta en autō sunestēke,
col|1|18|	kai autos estin ē kephalē tou sōmatos, tēs ekklēsias os estin archē, prōtotokos ek tōn nekrōn, ina genētai en pasin autos prōteuōn,
col|1|19|	oti en autō eudokēse pan to plērōma katoikēsai
col|1|20|	kai di autou apokatallaxai ta panta eis auton, eirēnopoiēsas dia tou aimatos tou staurou autou, di autou eite ta epi tēs gēs eite ta en tois ouranois.
col|1|21|	kai umas pote ontas apēllotriōmenous kai echthrous tē dianoia en tois ergois tois ponērois,
col|1|22|	nuni de apokatēllaxen en tō sōmati tēs sarkos autou dia tou thanatou, parastēsai umas agious kai amōmous kai anegklētous katenōpion autou,
col|1|23|	ei ge epimenete tē pistei tethemeliōmenoi kai edraioi kai mē metakinoumenoi apo tēs elpidos tou euaggeliou ou ēkousate, tou kēruchthentos en pasē tē ktisei tē upo ton ouranon, ou egenomēn egō paulos diakonos.
col|1|24|	nun chairō en tois pathēmasi mou uper umōn kai antanaplērō ta usterēmata tōn thlipseōn tou christou en tē sarki mou uper tou sōmatos autou, o estin ē ekklēsia,
col|1|25|	ēs egenomēn egō diakonos kata tēn oikonomian tou theou tēn dotheisan moi eis umas, plērōsai ton logon tou theou,

col|1|28|	on ēmeis kataggellomen nouthetountes panta anthrōpon kai didaskontes panta anthrōpon en pasē sophia, ina parastēsōmen panta anthrōpon teleion en christō iēsou
col|1|29|	eis o kai kopiō agōnizomenos kata tēn energeian autou tēn energoumenēn en emoi en dunamei.
col|2|1|	thelō gar umas eidenai ēlikon agōna echō peri umōn kai tōn en laodikeia kai osoi ouch eōrakasi to prosōpon mou en sarki,
col|2|2|	ina paraklēthōsin ai kardiai autōn, sumbibasthentōn en agapē kai eis panta plouton tēs plērophorias tēs suneseōs, eis epignōsin tou mustēriou tou theou kai patros kai tou christou,
col|2|3|	en ō eisi pantes oi thēsauroi tēs sophias kai tēs gnōseōs apokruphoi.
col|2|4|	touto de legō ina mē tis umas paralogizētai en pithanologia
col|2|5|	ei gar kai tē sarki apeimi, alla tō pneumati sun umin eimi, chairōn kai blepōn umōn tēn taxin kai to stereōma tēs eis christon pisteōs umōn.
col|2|6|	ōs oun parelabete ton christon iēsoun ton kurion, en autō peripateite,

col|2|9|	oti en autō katoikei pan to plērōma tēs theotētos sōmatikōs,

col|2|11|	en ō kai perietmēthēte peritomē acheiropoiētō en tē apekdusei tou sōmatos tōn amartiōn tēs sarkos, en tē peritomē tou christou,
col|2|12|	suntaphentes autō en tō baptismati, en ō kai sunēgerthēte dia tēs pisteōs tēs energeias tou theou tou egeirantos auton ek tōn nekrōn.
col|2|13|	kai umas, nekrous ontas en tois paraptōmasi kai tē akrobustia tēs sarkos umōn, sunezōopoiēsen umas sun autō, charisamenos ēmin panta ta paraptōmata,
col|2|14|	exaleipsas to kath ēmōn cheirographon tois dogmasin o ēn upenantion ēmin, kai auto ēren ek tou mesou prosēlōsas auto tō staurō
col|2|15|	apekdusamenos tas archas kai tas exousias edeigmatisen en parrēsia, thriambeusas autous en autō.
col|2|16|	mē oun tis umas krinetō en brōsei ē en posei ē en merei eortēs ē noumēnias ē sabbatōn,
col|2|17|	a esti skia tōn mellontōn, to de sōma christou.
col|2|18|	mēdeis umas katabrabeuetō thelōn en tapeinophrosunē kai thrēskeia tōn aggelōn, a mē eōraken embateuōn, eikē phusioumenos upo tou noos tēs sarkos autou,
col|2|19|	kai ou kratōn tēn kephalēn, ex ou pan to sōma dia tōn aphōn kai sundesmōn epichorēgoumenon kai sumbibazomenon auxei tēn auxēsin tou theou.

col|3|1|	ei oun sunēgerthēte tō christō, ta anō zēteite, ou o christos estin en dexia tou theou kathēmenos,
col|3|2|	ta anō phroneite, mē ta epi tēs gēs.

col|3|4|	otan o christos phanerōthē, ē zōē ēmōn, tote kai umeis sun autō phanerōthēsesthe en doxē.
col|3|5|	nekrōsate oun ta melē umōn ta epi tēs gēs, porneian, akatharsian, pathos, epithumian kakēn, kai tēn pleonexian, ētis estin eidōlolatria,
col|3|6|	di a erchetai ē orgē tou theou epi tous uious tēs apeitheias,

col|3|16|	o logos tou christou enoikeitō en umin plousiōs, en pasē sophia didaskontes kai nouthetountes eautous psalmois kai umnois kai ōdais pneumatikais, en chariti adontes en tē kardia umōn tō kuriō.

col|4|1|	oi kurioi to dikaion kai tēn isotēta tois doulois parechesthe, eidotes oti kai umeis echete kurion en ouranois.
col|4|2|	tē proseuchē proskartereite, grēgorountes en autē en eucharistia,
col|4|3|	proseuchomenoi ama kai peri ēmōn, ina o theos anoixē ēmin thuran tou logou, lalēsai to mustērion tou christou, di o kai dedemai,
col|4|4|	ina phanerōsō auto ōs dei me lalēsai.
col|4|5|	en sophia peripateite pros tous exō, ton kairon exagorazomenoi.
col|4|6|	o logos umōn pantote en chariti, alati ērtumenos, eidenai pōs dei umas eni ekastō apokrinesthai.
col|4|7|	ta kat eme panta gnōrisei umin tuchikos o agapētos adelphos kai pistos diakonos kai sundoulos en kuriō,
col|4|8|	on epempsa pros umas eis auto touto, ina gnō ta peri umōn kai parakalesē tas kardias umōn,
col|4|9|	sun onēsimō tō pistō kai agapētō adelphō, os estin ex umōn panta umin gnōriousi ta ōde.
col|4|10|	aspazetai umas aristarchos o sunaichmalōtos mou, kai markos o anepsios barnaba,—peri ou elabete entolas ean elthē pros umas, dexasthe auton
col|4|11|	kai iēsous o legomenos ioustos, oi ontes ek peritomēs, outoi monoi sunergoi eis tēn basileian tou theou, oitines egenēthēsan moi parēgoria.
col|4|12|	aspazetai umas epaphras o ex umōn, doulos christou, pantote agōnizomenos uper umōn en tais proseuchais, ina stēte teleioi kai peplērōmenoi en panti thelēmati tou theou
col|4|13|	marturō gar autō oti echei zēlon polun uper umōn kai tōn en laodikeia kai tōn en ierapolei.
col|4|14|	aspazetai umas loukas o iatros o agapētos kai dēmas.
col|4|15|	aspasasthe tous en laodikeia adelphous kai numphan kai tēn kat oikon autou ekklēsian
col|4|16|	kai otan anagnōsthē par umin ē epistolē, poiēsate ina kai en tē laodikeōn ekklēsia anagnōsthē, kai tēn ek laodikeias ina kai umeis anagnōte.
col|4|17|	kai eipate archippō blepe tēn diakonian ēn parelabes en kuriō, ina autēn plērois.
col|4|18|	o aspasmos tē emē cheiri paulou. mnēmoneuete mou tōn desmōn. ē charis meth umōn amēn.
1th|1|1|	paulos kai silouanos kai timotheos tē ekklēsia thessalonikeōn en theō patri kai kuriō iēsou christō charis umin kai eirēnē apo theou patros ēmōn kai kuriou iēsou christou.
1th|1|2|	eucharistoumen tō theō pantote peri pantōn umōn mneian umōn poioumenoi epi tōn proseuchōn ēmōn,
1th|1|3|	adialeiptōs mnēmoneuontes umōn tou ergou tēs pisteōs kai tou kopou tēs agapēs kai tēs upomonēs tēs elpidos tou kuriou ēmōn iēsou christou emprosthen tou theou kai patros ēmōn,
1th|1|4|	eidotes, adelphoi ēgapēmenoi upo theou, tēn eklogēn umōn,
1th|1|5|	oti to euaggelion ēmōn ouk egenēthē eis umas en logō monon, alla kai en dunamei kai en pneumati agiō kai en plērophoria pollē, kathōs oidate oioi egenēthēmen en umin di umas
1th|1|6|	kai umeis mimētai ēmōn egenēthēte kai tou kuriou dexamenoi ton logon en thlipsei pollē meta charas pneumatos agiou,
1th|1|7|	ōste genesthai umas tupous pasi tois pisteuousin en tē makedonia kai en tē achaia.
1th|1|8|	aph umōn gar exēchētai o logos tou kuriou ou monon en tē makedonia kai en tē achaia, alla kai en panti topō ē pistis umōn ē pros ton theon exelēluthen, ōste mē chreian ēmas echein lalein ti
1th|1|9|	autoi gar peri ēmōn apaggellousin opoian eisodon eschomen pros umas, kai pōs epestrepsate pros ton theon apo tōn eidōlōn douleuein theō zōnti kai alēthinō,
1th|1|10|	kai anamenein ton uion autou ek tōn ouranōn, on ēgeiren ek tōn nekrōn, iēsoun ton ruomenon ēmas apo tēs orgēs tēs erchomenēs.
1th|2|1|	autoi gar oidate, adelphoi, tēn eisodon ēmōn tēn pros umas oti ou kenē gegonen,
1th|2|2|	alla propathontes kai ubristhentes, kathōs oidate, en philippois, eparrēsiasametha en tō theō ēmōn lalēsai pros umas to euaggelion tou theou en pollō agōni.
1th|2|3|	ē gar paraklēsis ēmōn ouk ek planēs oude ex akatharsias, oute en dolō,
1th|2|4|	alla kathōs dedokimasmetha upo tou theou pisteuthēnai to euaggelion, outō laloumen, ouch ōs anthrōpois areskontes, alla tō theō tō dokimazonti tas kardias ēmōn.
1th|2|5|	oute gar pote en logō kolakeias egenēthēmen, kathōs oidate, oute en prophasei pleonexias, theos martus,
1th|2|6|	oute zētountes ex anthrōpōn doxan, oute aph umōn oute apo allōn, dunamenoi en barei einai ōs christou apostoloi,
1th|2|7|	all egenēthēmen ēpioi en mesō umōn, ōs an trophos thalpē ta eautēs tekna
1th|2|8|	outōs omeiromenoi umōn eudokoumen metadounai umin ou monon to euaggelion tou theou, alla kai tas eautōn psuchas, dioti agapētoi ēmin gegenēsthe.
1th|2|9|	mnēmoneuete gar, adelphoi, ton kopon ēmōn kai ton mochthon nuktos gar kai ēmeras ergazomenoi pros to mē epibarēsai tina umōn ekēruxamen eis umas to euaggelion tou theou.
1th|2|10|	umeis martures kai o theos ōs osiōs kai dikaiōs kai amemptōs umin tois pisteuousin egenēthēmen,
1th|2|11|	kathaper oidate ōs ena ekaston umōn ōs patēr tekna eautou
1th|2|12|	parakalountes umas kai paramuthoumenoi kai marturomenoi eis to peripatēsai umas axiōs tou theou tou kalountos umas eis tēn eautou basileian kai doxan.
1th|2|13|	dia touto kai ēmeis eucharistoumen tō theō adialeiptōs, oti paralabontes logon akoēs par ēmōn tou theou edexasthe ou logon anthrōpōn, alla kathōs estin alēthōs, logon theou, os kai energeitai en umin tois pisteuousin.
1th|2|14|	umeis gar mimētai egenēthēte, adelphoi, tōn ekklēsiōn tou theou tōn ousōn en tē ioudaia en christō iēsou, oti ta auta epathete kai umeis upo tōn idiōn sumphuletōn kathōs kai autoi upo tōn ioudaiōn,
1th|2|15|	tōn kai ton kurion apokteinantōn iēsoun kai tous idious prophētas, kai ēmas ekdiōxantōn, kai theō mē areskontōn, kai pasin anthrōpois enantiōn,
1th|2|16|	kōluontōn ēmas tois ethnesi lalēsai ina sōthōsin, eis to anaplērōsai autōn tas amartias pantote. ephthase de ep autous ē orgē eis telos.
1th|2|17|	ēmeis de, adelphoi, aporphanisthentes aph umōn pros kairon ōras, prosōpō ou kardia, perissoterōs espoudasamen to prosōpon umōn idein en pollē epithumia.
1th|2|18|	dio ēthelēsamen elthein pros umas, egō men paulos kai apax kai dis, kai enekopsen ēmas o satanas.
1th|2|19|	tis gar ēmōn elpis ē chara ē stephanos kauchēseōs ē ouchi kai umeis emprosthen tou kuriou ēmōn iēsou christou en tē autou parousia?
1th|2|20|	umeis gar este ē doxa ēmōn kai ē chara.
1th|3|1|	dio mēketi stegontes eudokēsamen kataleiphthēnai en athēnais monoi,
1th|3|2|	kai epempsamen timotheon, ton adelphon ēmōn kai diakonon tou theou kai sunergon ēmōn en tō euaggeliō tou christou, eis to stērixai umas kai parakalesai umas peri tēs pisteōs umōn,
1th|3|3|	to mēdena sainesthai en tais thlipsesi tautais. autoi gar oidate oti eis touto keimetha
1th|3|4|	kai gar ote pros umas ēmen, proelegomen umin oti mellomen thlibesthai, kathōs kai egeneto kai oidate.
1th|3|5|	dia touto kagō mēketi stegōn epempsa eis to gnōnai tēn pistin umōn, mē pōs epeirasen umas o peirazōn kai eis kenon genētai o kopos ēmōn.
1th|3|6|	arti de elthontos timotheou pros ēmas aph umōn kai euaggelisamenou ēmin tēn pistin kai tēn agapēn umōn, kai oti echete mneian ēmōn agathēn, pantote epipothountes ēmas idein kathaper kai ēmeis umas,
1th|3|7|	dia touto pareklēthēmen, adelphoi, eph umin epi pasē tē thlipsei kai anagkē ēmōn dia tēs umōn pisteōs
1th|3|8|	oti nun zōmen, ean umeis stēkēte en kuriō.
1th|3|9|	tina gar eucharistian dunametha tō theō antapodounai peri umōn epi pasē tē chara ē chairomen di umas emprosthen tou theou ēmōn,
1th|3|10|	nuktos kai ēmeras uperekperissou deomenoi eis to idein umōn to prosōpon kai katartisai ta usterēmata tēs pisteōs umōn?
1th|3|11|	autos de o theos kai patēr ēmōn kai o kurios ēmōn iēsous christos kateuthunai tēn odon ēmōn pros umas
1th|3|12|	umas de o kurios pleonasai kai perisseusai tē agapē eis allēlous kai eis pantas, kathaper kai ēmeis eis umas,
1th|3|13|	eis to stērixai umōn tas kardias amemptous en agiōsunē emprosthen tou theou kai patros ēmōn en tē parousia tou kuriou ēmōn iēsou christou meta pantōn tōn agiōn autou.
1th|4|1|	to loipon oun, adelphoi, erōtōmen umas kai parakaloumen en kuriō iēsou, kathōs parelabete par ēmōn to pōs dei umas peripatein kai areskein theō, ina perisseuēte mallon
1th|4|2|	oidate gar tinas paraggelias edōkamen umin dia tou kuriou iēsou.
1th|4|3|	touto gar esti thelēma tou theou, o agiasmos umōn, apechesthai umas apo tēs porneias,
1th|4|4|	eidenai ekaston umōn to eautou skeuos ktasthai en agiasmō kai timē,
1th|4|5|	mē en pathei epithumias kathaper kai ta ethnē ta mē eidota ton theon,
1th|4|6|	to mē uperbainein kai pleonektein en tō pragmati ton adelphon autou, dioti ekdikos o kurios peri pantōn toutōn, kathōs kai proeipomen umin kai diemarturametha.
1th|4|7|	ou gar ekalesen ēmas o theos epi akatharsia, all en agiasmō.
1th|4|8|	toigaroun o athetōn ouk anthrōpon athetei, alla ton theon ton kai donta to pneuma autou to agion eis umas.
1th|4|9|	peri de tēs philadelphias ou chreian echete graphein umin autoi gar umeis theodidaktoi este eis to agapan allēlous
1th|4|10|	kai gar poieite auto eis pantas tous adelphous tous en olē tē makedonia. parakaloumen de umas, adelphoi, perisseuein mallon
1th|4|11|	kai philotimeisthai ēsuchazein kai prassein ta idia kai ergazesthai tais idiais chersin umōn, kathōs umin parēggeilamen,
1th|4|12|	ina peripatēte euschēmonōs pros tous exō kai mēdenos chreian echēte.
1th|4|13|	ou thelomen de umas agnoein, adelphoi, peri tōn kekoimēmenōn, ina mē lupēsthe kathōs kai oi loipoi oi mē echontes elpida.
1th|4|14|	ei gar pisteuomen oti iēsous apethane kai anestē, outō kai o theos tous koimēthentas dia tou iēsou axei sun autō.
1th|4|15|	touto gar umin legomen en logō kuriou, oti ēmeis oi zōntes oi perileipomenoi eis tēn parousian tou kuriou ou mē phthasōmen tous koimēthentas
1th|4|16|	oti autos o kurios en keleusmati, en phōnē archaggelou kai en salpiggi theou katabēsetai ap ouranou, kai oi nekroi en christō anastēsontai prōton,
1th|4|17|	epeita ēmeis oi zōntes oi perileipomenoi ama sun autois arpagēsometha en nephelais eis apantēsin tou kuriou eis aera, kai outō pantote sun kuriō esometha.
1th|4|18|	ōste parakaleite allēlous en tois logois toutois.
1th|5|1|	peri de tōn chronōn kai tōn kairōn, adelphoi, ou chreian echete umin graphesthai
1th|5|2|	autoi gar akribōs oidate oti ē ēmera kuriou ōs kleptēs en nukti outōs erchetai.
1th|5|3|	otan gar legōsin, eirēnē kai asphaleia, tote aiphnidios autois ephistatai olethros, ōsper ē ōdin tē en gastri echousē, kai ou mē ekphugōsin.
1th|5|4|	umeis de, adelphoi, ouk este en skotei, ina ē ēmera umas ōs kleptēs katalabē
1th|5|5|	pantes umeis uioi phōtos este kai uioi ēmeras. ouk esmen nuktos oude skotous.
1th|5|6|	ara oun mē katheudōmen ōs kai oi loipoi, alla grēgorōmen kai nēphōmen.
1th|5|7|	oi gar katheudontes nuktos katheudousi, kai oi methuskomenoi nuktos methuousin
1th|5|8|	ēmeis de ēmeras ontes nēphōmen, endusamenoi thōraka pisteōs kai agapēs kai perikephalaian elpida sōtērias
1th|5|9|	oti ouk etheto ēmas o theos eis orgēn, all eis peripoiēsin sōtērias dia tou kuriou ēmōn iēsou christou,
1th|5|10|	tou apothanontos uper ēmōn, ina eite grēgorōmen eite katheudōmen ama sun autō zēsōmen.
1th|5|11|	dio parakaleite allēlous kai oikodomeite eis ton ena, kathōs kai poieite.
1th|5|12|	erōtōmen de umas, adelphoi, eidenai tous kopiōntas en umin kai proistamenous umōn en kuriō kai nouthetountas umas,
1th|5|13|	kai ēgeisthai autous uperekperissou en agapē dia to ergon autōn. eirēneuete en eautois.
1th|5|14|	parakaloumen de umas, adelphoi, noutheteite tous ataktous, paramutheisthe tous oligopsuchous, antechesthe tōn asthenōn, makrothumeite pros pantas.
1th|5|15|	orate mē tis kakon anti kakou tini apodō, alla pantote to agathon diōkete kai eis allēlous kai eis pantas.
1th|5|16|	pantote chairete,
1th|5|17|	adialeiptōs proseuchesthe,
1th|5|18|	en panti eucharisteite touto gar thelēma theou en christō iēsou eis umas.
1th|5|19|	to pneuma mē sbennute,
1th|5|20|	prophēteias mē exoutheneite.
1th|5|21|	panta de dokimazete, to kalon katechete
1th|5|22|	apo pantos eidous ponērou apechesthe.
1th|5|23|	autos de o theos tēs eirēnēs agiasai umas oloteleis, kai oloklēron umōn to pneuma kai ē psuchē kai to sōma amemptōs en tē parousia tou kuriou ēmōn iēsou christou tērētheiē.
1th|5|24|	pistos o kalōn umas, os kai poiēsei.
1th|5|25|	adelphoi, proseuchesthe peri ēmōn.
1th|5|26|	aspasasthe tous adelphous pantas en philēmati agiō.
1th|5|27|	orkizō umas ton kurion anagnōsthēnai tēn epistolēn pasi tois agiois adelphois.
1th|5|28|	ē charis tou kuriou ēmōn iēsou christou meth umōn amēn.
2th|1|1|	paulos kai silouanos kai timotheos tē ekklēsia thessalonikeōn en theō patri ēmōn kai kuriō iēsou christō
2th|1|2|	charis umin kai eirēnē apo theou patros ēmōn kai kuriou iēsou christou.
2th|1|3|	eucharistein opheilomen tō theō pantote peri umōn, adelphoi, kathōs axion estin, oti uperauxanei ē pistis umōn kai pleonazei ē agapē enos ekastou pantōn umōn eis allēlous,
2th|1|4|	ōste ēmas autous en umin kauchasthai en tais ekklēsiais tou theou uper tēs upomonēs umōn kai pisteōs en pasi tois diōgmois umōn kai tais thlipsesin ais anechesthe,
2th|1|5|	endeigma tēs dikaias kriseōs tou theou, eis to kataxiōthēnai umas tēs basileias tou theou, uper ēs kai paschete,
2th|1|6|	eiper dikaion para theō antapodounai tois thlibousin umas thlipsin
2th|1|7|	kai umin tois thlibomenois anesin meth ēmōn en tē apokalupsei tou kuriou iēsou ap ouranou met aggelōn dunameōs autou
2th|1|8|	en puri phlogos, didontos ekdikēsin tois mē eidosi theon kai tois mē upakouousi tō euaggeliō tou kuriou ēmōn iēsou christou,
2th|1|9|	oitines dikēn tisousin olethron aiōnion apo prosōpou tou kuriou kai apo tēs doxēs tēs ischuos autou,
2th|1|10|	otan elthē endoxasthēnai en tois agiois autou kai thaumasthēnai en pasi tois pisteusasin, oti episteuthē to marturion ēmōn eph umas, en tē ēmera ekeinē.
2th|1|11|	eis o kai proseuchometha pantote peri umōn, ina umas axiōsē tēs klēseōs o theos ēmōn kai plērōsē pasan eudokian agathōsunēs kai ergon pisteōs en dunamei,
2th|1|12|	opōs endoxasthē to onoma tou kuriou ēmōn iēsou christou en umin, kai umeis en autō, kata tēn charin tou theou ēmōn kai kuriou iēsou christou.
2th|2|1|	erōtōmen de umas, adelphoi, uper tēs parousias tou kuriou ēmōn iēsou christou kai ēmōn episunagōgēs ep auton,
2th|2|2|	eis to mē tacheōs saleuthēnai umas apo tou noos mēte throeisthai mēte dia pneumatos mēte dia logou mēte di epistolēs ōs di ēmōn, ōs oti enestēken ē ēmera tou christou.
2th|2|3|	mē tis umas exapatēsē kata mēdena tropon oti ean mē elthē ē apostasia prōton kai apokaluphthē o anthrōpos tēs amartias, o uios tēs apōleias,
2th|2|4|	o antikeimenos kai uperairomenos epi panta legomenon theon ē sebasma, ōste auton eis ton naon tou theou ōs theon kathisai, apodeiknunta eauton oti esti theos.
2th|2|5|	ou mnēmoneuete oti eti ōn pros umas tauta elegon umin?
2th|2|6|	kai nun to katechon oidate, eis to apokaluphthēnai auton en tō eautou kairō
2th|2|7|	to gar mustērion ēdē energeitai tēs anomias, monon o katechōn arti eōs ek mesou genētai
2th|2|8|	kai tote apokaluphthēsetai o anomos, on o kurios analōsei tō pneumati tou stomatos autou kai katargēsei tē epiphaneia tēs parousias autou
2th|2|9|	ou estin ē parousia kat energeian tou satana en pasē dunamei kai sēmeiois kai terasi pseudous
2th|2|10|	kai en pasē apatē tēs adikias en tois apollumenois, anth ōn tēn agapēn tēs alētheias ouk edexanto eis to sōthēnai autous
2th|2|11|	kai dia touto pempsei autois o theos energeian planēs eis to pisteusai autous tō pseudei,
2th|2|12|	ina krithōsi pantes oi mē pisteusantes tē alētheia, all eudokēsantes en tē adikia.
2th|2|13|	ēmeis de opheilomen eucharistein tō theō pantote peri umōn, adelphoi ēgapēmenoi upo kuriou, oti eileto umas o theos ap archēs eis sōtērian en agiasmō pneumatos kai pistei alētheias,
2th|2|14|	eis o ekalesen umas dia tou euaggeliou ēmōn eis peripoiēsin doxēs tou kuriou ēmōn iēsou christou.
2th|2|15|	ara oun, adelphoi, stēkete, kai krateite tas paradoseis as edidachthēte eite dia logou eite di epistolēs ēmōn.
2th|2|16|	autos de o kurios ēmōn iēsous christos kai o theos kai patēr ēmōn, o agapēsas ēmas kai dous paraklēsin aiōnian kai elpida agathēn en chariti,
2th|2|17|	parakalesai umōn tas kardias kai stērixai umas en panti logō kai ergō agathō.
2th|3|1|	to loipon, proseuchesthe, adelphoi, peri ēmōn, ina o logos tou kuriou trechē kai doxazētai, kathōs kai pros umas,
2th|3|2|	kai ina rusthōmen apo tōn atopōn kai ponērōn anthrōpōn ou gar pantōn ē pistis.
2th|3|3|	pistos de estin o kurios, os stērixei umas kai phulaxei apo tou ponērou.
2th|3|4|	pepoithamen de en kuriō eph umas oti a paraggellomen umin kai poieite kai poiēsete.
2th|3|5|	o de kurios kateuthunai umōn tas kardias eis tēn agapēn tou theou kai eis tēn upomonēn tou christou.
2th|3|6|	paraggellomen de umin, adelphoi, en onomati tou kuriou ēmōn iēsou christou, stellesthai umas apo pantos adelphou ataktōs peripatountos kai mē kata tēn paradosin ēn parelabon par ēmōn.
2th|3|7|	autoi gar oidate pōs dei mimeisthai ēmas, oti ouk ētaktēsamen en umin,
2th|3|8|	oude dōrean arton ephagomen para tinos, all en kopō kai mochthō, nukta kai ēmeran ergazomenoi, pros to mē epibarēsai tina umōn
2th|3|9|	ouch oti ouk echomen exousian, all ina eautous tupon dōmen umin eis to mimeisthai ēmas.
2th|3|10|	kai gar ote ēmen pros umas, touto parēggellomen umin, oti ei tis ou thelei ergazesthai, mēde esthietō.
2th|3|11|	akouomen gar tinas peripatountas en umin ataktōs, mēden ergazomenous, alla periergazomenous
2th|3|12|	tois de toioutois paraggellomen kai parakaloumen dia tou kuriou ēmōn iēsou christou, ina meta ēsuchias ergazomenoi ton eautōn arton esthiōsin.
2th|3|13|	umeis de, adelphoi, mē ekkakēsēte kalopoiountes.
2th|3|14|	ei de tis ouch upakouei tō logō ēmōn dia tēs epistolēs, touton sēmeiousthe, kai mē sunanamignusthe autō, ina entrapē
2th|3|15|	kai mē ōs echthron ēgeisthe, alla noutheteite ōs adelphon.
2th|3|16|	autos de o kurios tēs eirēnēs dōē umin tēn eirēnēn dia pantos en panti tropō. o kurios meta pantōn umōn.
2th|3|17|	o aspasmos tē emē cheiri paulou, o esti sēmeion en pasē epistolē outō graphō.
2th|3|18|	ē charis tou kuriou ēmōn iēsou christou meta pantōn umōn amēn.
1ti|1|1|	paulos, apostolos iēsou christou kat epitagēn theou sōtēros ēmōn kai kuriou iēsou christou tēs elpidos ēmōn,
1ti|1|2|	timotheō gnēsiō teknō en pistei charis, eleos, eirēnē apo theou patros ēmōn kai christou iēsou tou kuriou ēmōn.
1ti|1|3|	kathōs parekalesa se prosmeinai en ephesō, poreuomenos eis makedonian, ina paraggeilēs tisi mē eterodidaskalein
1ti|1|4|	mēde prosechein muthois kai genealogiais aperantois, aitines zētēseis parechousi mallon ē oikonomian theou tēn en pistei
1ti|1|5|	to de telos tēs paraggelias estin agapē ek katharas kardias kai suneidēseōs agathēs kai pisteōs anupokritou,
1ti|1|6|	ōn tines astochēsantes exetrapēsan eis mataiologian,
1ti|1|7|	thelontes einai nomodidaskaloi, mē noountes mēte a legousi mēte peri tinōn diabebaiountai.
1ti|1|8|	oidamen de oti kalos o nomos, ean tis autō nomimōs chrētai,
1ti|1|9|	eidōs touto, oti dikaiō nomos ou keitai, anomois de kai anupotaktois, asebesi kai amartōlois, anosiois kai bebēlois, patrolōais kai mētrolōais, androphonois,
1ti|1|10|	pornois, arsenokoitais, andrapodistais, pseustais, epiorkois, kai ei ti eteron tē ugiainousē didaskalia antikeitai,
1ti|1|11|	kata to euaggelion tēs doxēs tou makariou theou, o episteuthēn egō.
1ti|1|12|	kai charin echō tō endunamōsanti me christō iēsou tō kuriō ēmōn, oti piston me ēgēsato, themenos eis diakonian
1ti|1|13|	ton proteron onta blasphēmon kai diōktēn kai ubristēn all ēleēthēn, oti agnoōn epoiēsa en apistia,
1ti|1|14|	uperepleonase de ē charis tou kuriou ēmōn meta pisteōs kai agapēs tēs en christō iēsou.
1ti|1|15|	pistos o logos kai pasēs apodochēs axios, oti christos iēsous ēlthen eis ton kosmon amartōlous sōsai, ōn prōtos eimi egō
1ti|1|16|	alla dia touto ēleēthēn, ina en emoi prōtō endeixētai iēsous christos tēn pasan makrothumian, pros upotupōsin tōn mellontōn pisteuein ep autō eis zōēn aiōnion.
1ti|1|17|	tō de basilei tōn aiōnōn, aphthartō, aoratō, monō sophō theō, timē kai doxa eis tous aiōnas tōn aiōnōn amēn.
1ti|1|18|	tautēn tēn paraggelian paratithemai soi, teknon timothee, kata tas proagousas epi se prophēteias, ina strateuē en autais tēn kalēn strateian,
1ti|1|19|	echōn pistin kai agathēn suneidēsin, ēn tines apōsamenoi peri tēn pistin enauagēsan
1ti|1|20|	ōn estin umenaios kai alexandros, ous paredōka tō satana, ina paideuthōsi mē blasphēmein.

1ti|2|2|	uper basileōn kai pantōn tōn en uperochē ontōn, ina ēremon kai ēsuchion bion diagōmen en pasē eusebeia kai semnotēti.
1ti|2|3|	touto gar kalon kai apodekton enōpion tou sōtēros ēmōn theou,
1ti|2|4|	os pantas anthrōpous thelei sōthēnai kai eis epignōsin alētheias elthein.

1ti|3|1|	pistos o logos ei tis episkopēs oregetai, kalou ergou epithumei.

1ti|3|6|	mē neophuton, ina mē tuphōtheis eis krima empesē tou diabolou.

1ti|4|1|	to de pneuma rētōs legei oti en usterois kairois apostēsontai tines tēs pisteōs, prosechontes pneumasi planois kai didaskaliais daimoniōn,

2ti|2|1|	su oun, teknon mou, endunamou en tē chariti tē en christō iēsou,

2ti|2|3|	su oun kakopathēson ōs kalos stratiōtēs iēsou christou.

2ti|2|19|	o mentoi stereos themelios tou theou estēken, echōn tēn sphragida tautēn egnō kurios tous ontas autou kai apostētō apo adikias pas o onomazōn to onoma kuriou.
2ti|2|20|	en megalē de oikia ouk esti monon skeuē chrusa kai argura, alla kai xulina kai ostrakina, kai a men eis timēn, a de eis atimian.
2ti|2|21|	ean oun tis ekkatharē eauton apo toutōn, estai skeuos eis timēn, ēgiasmenon kai euchrēston tō despotē, eis pan ergon agathon ētoimasmenon.
2ti|2|22|	tas de neōterikas epithumias pheuge, diōke de dikaiosunēn, pistin, agapēn, eirēnēn meta tōn epikaloumenōn ton kurion ek katharas kardias.

heb|4|1|	phobēthōmen oun mē pote, kataleipomenēs epaggelias eiselthein eis tēn katapausin autou, dokē tis ex umōn usterēkenai.

jam|1|4|	ē de upomonē ergon teleion echetō, ina ēte teleioi kai oloklēroi, en mēdeni leipomenoi.
jam|1|5|	ei de tis umōn leipetai sophias, aiteitō para tou didontos theou pasin aplōs kai ouk oneidizontos, kai dothēsetai autō

jam|1|7|	mē gar oiesthō o anthrōpos ekeinos oti lēpsetai ti para tou kuriou.
jam|1|8|	anēr dipsuchos akatastatos en pasais tais odois autou.
jam|1|9|	kauchasthō de o adelphos o tapeinos en tō upsei autou,
jam|1|10|	o de plousios en tē tapeinōsei autou, oti ōs anthos chortou pareleusetai.
jam|1|11|	aneteile gar o ēlios sun tō kausōni kai exērane ton chorton, kai to anthos autou exepese, kai ē euprepeia tou prosōpou autou apōleto. outō kai o plousios en tais poreiais autou maranthēsetai.
jam|1|12|	makarios anēr os upomenei peirasmon oti dokimos genomenos lēpsetai ton stephanon tēs zōēs, on epēggeilato o kurios tois agapōsin auton.
jam|1|13|	mēdeis peirazomenos legetō oti apo theou peirazomai o gar theos apeirastos esti kakōn, peirazei de autos oudena.

jam|1|16|	mē planasthe, adelphoi mou agapētoi
