jam|1|18|	boulētheis apekuēsen ēmas logō alētheias eis to einai ēmas aparchēn tina tōn autou ktismatōn.

jam|1|20|	orgē gar andros dikaiosunēn theou ou katergazetai.

1pe|1|8|	on ouk eidotes agapate, eis on arti mē orōntes, pisteuontes de agalliasthe chara aneklalētō kai dedoxasmenē,

apo|12|14|	kai edothēsan tē gunaiki duo pteruges tou aetou tou megalou, ina petētai eis tēn erēmon eis ton topon autēs, opōs trephētai ekei kairon kai kairous kai ēmisu kairou apo prosōpou tou opheōs.

apo|13|1|	kai estathēn epi tēn ammon tēs thalassēs kai eidon ek tēs thalassēs thērion anabainon, echon kerata deka kai kephalas epta, kai epi tōn keratōn autou deka diadēmata, kai epi tas kephalas autou onomata blasphēmias.
apo|13|2|	kai to thērion o eidon ēn omoion pardalei, kai oi podes autou ōs arkou, kai to stoma autou ōs stoma leontos. kai edōken autō o drakōn tēn dunamin autou kai ton thronon autou kai exousian megalēn—
apo|13|3|	kai mian ek tōn kephalōn autou ōs esphagmenēn eis thanaton. kai ē plēgē tou thanatou autou etherapeuthē, kai ethaumasen olē ē gē opisō tou thēriou,
apo|13|4|	kai prosekunēsan tō drakonti tō dedōkoti tēn exousian tō thēriō, kai prosekunēsan tō thēriō legontes tis omoios tō thēriō? tis dunatai polemēsai met autou?

apo|13|8|	kai proskunēsousin auton pantes oi katoikountes epi tēs gēs, ōn ou gegraptai to onoma en tō bibliō tēs zōēs tou arniou tou esphagmenou apo katabolēs kosmou.
apo|13|9|	ei tis echei ous, akousatō.
apo|13|10|	ei tis eis aichmalōsian apagei, eis aichmalōsian upagei ei tis en machaira apoktennei, dei auton en machaira apoktanthēnai. ōde estin ē upomonē kai ē pistis tōn agiōn.
apo|13|11|	kai eidon allo thērion anabainon ek tēs gēs, kai eiche kerata duo omoia arniō, kai elalei ōs drakōn.

apo|13|16|	kai poiei pantas, tous mikrous kai tous megalous, kai tous plousious kai tous ptōchous, kai tous eleutherous kai tous doulous, ina dōsōsin autois charagma epi tēs cheiros autōn tēs dexias ē epi tōn metōpōn autōn,

apo|14|1|	kai eidon, kai idou to arnion estēkos epi to oros siōn, kai met autou ekaton tessarakonta tessares chiliades, echousai to onoma autou kai to onoma tou patros autou gegrammenon epi tōn metōpōn autōn.

apo|18|13|	kai kinamōmon kai amōmon kai thumiamata, kai muron kai libanon kai oinon kai elaion kai semidalin kai siton kai ktēnē kai probata, kai ippōn kai redōn kai sōmatōn, kai psuchas anthrōpōn.

apo|18|15|	oi emporoi toutōn, oi ploutēsantes ap autēs, apo makrothen stēsontai dia ton phobon tou basanismou autēs klaiontes kai penthountes,
apo|18|16|	legontes ouai ouai, ē polis ē megalē, ē peribeblēmenē bussinon kai porphuroun kai kokkinon kai kechrusōmenē en chrusiō kai lithō timiō kai margaritais, oti mia ōra ērēmōthē o tosoutos ploutos.
apo|18|17|	kai pas kubernētēs kai pas o epi topon pleōn, kai nautai kai osoi tēn thalassan ergazontai, apo makrothen estēsan,
apo|18|18|	kai ekrazon blepontes ton kapnon tēs purōseōs autēs, legontes tis omoia tē polei tē megalē?
apo|18|19|	kai ebalon choun epi tas kephalas autōn kai ekrazon klaiontes kai penthountes, legontes ouai ouai, ē polis ē megalē, en ē eploutēsan pantes oi echontes ta ploia en tē thalassē ek tēs timiotētos autēs oti mia ōra ērēmōthē.
apo|18|20|	euphrainou ep autē, ourane, kai oi agioi kai oi apostoloi kai oi prophētai, oti ekrinen o theos to krima umōn ex autēs.
apo|18|21|	kai ēren eis aggelos ischuros lithon ōs mulon megan kai ebalen eis tēn thalassan legōn outōs ormēmati blēthēsetai babulōn ē megalē polis, kai ou mē eurethē eti.
apo|18|22|	kai phōnē kitharōdōn kai mousikōn kai aulētōn kai salpistōn ou mē akousthē en soi eti, kai pas technitēs pasēs technēs ou mē eurethē en soi eti, kai phōnē mulou ou mē akousthē en soi eti,
apo|18|23|	kai phōs luchnou ou mē phanē en soi eti, kai phōnē numphiou kai numphēs ou mē akousthē en soi eti oti oi emporoi sou ēsan oi megistanes tēs gēs, oti en tē pharmakeia sou eplanēthēsan panta ta ethnē,
apo|18|24|	kai en autē aimata prophētōn kai agiōn eurethē kai pantōn tōn esphagmenōn epi tēs gēs.
apo|19|1|	meta tauta ēkousa ōs phōnēn megalēn ochlou pollou en tō ouranō legontōn allēlouia ē sōtēria kai ē doxa kai ē dunamis tou theou ēmōn,
apo|19|2|	oti alēthinai kai dikaiai ai kriseis autou oti ekrine tēn pornēn tēn megalēn, ētis diephtheire tēn gēn en tē porneia autēs, kai exedikēse to aima tōn doulōn autou ek cheiros autēs.
apo|19|3|	kai deuteron eirēkan allēlouia kai o kapnos autēs anabainei eis tous aiōnas tōn aiōnōn.
apo|19|4|	kai epesan oi eikosi kai tessares presbuteroi kai ta tessara zōa kai prosekunēsan tō theō tō kathēmenō epi tō thronō legontes amēn, allēlouia.
apo|19|5|	kai phōnē apo tou thronou exēlthe legousa aineite ton theon ēmōn pantes oi douloi autou kai oi phoboumenoi auton, oi mikroi kai oi megaloi.
apo|19|6|	kai ēkousa ōs phōnēn ochlou pollou kai ōs phōnēn udatōn pollōn kai ōs phōnēn brontōn ischurōn, legontōn allēlouia oti ebasileuse kurios o theos o pantokratōr.
apo|19|7|	chairōmen kai agalliōmetha kai dōmen tēn doxan autō, oti ēlthen o gamos tou arniou kai ē gunē autou ētoimasen eautēn.
apo|19|8|	kai edothē autē ina peribalētai bussinon lampron katharon to gar bussinon ta dikaiōmata tōn agiōn esti.
apo|19|9|	kai legei moi grapson, makarioi oi eis to deipnon tou gamou tou arniou keklēmenoi. kai legei moi outoi oi logoi alēthinoi tou theou eisi.
apo|19|10|	kai epesa emprosthen tōn podōn autou proskunēsai autō. kai legei moi ora mē sundoulos sou eimi kai tōn adelphōn sou tōn echontōn tēn marturian iēsou tō theō proskunēson ē gar marturia tou iēsou esti to pneuma tēs prophēteias.
apo|19|11|	kai eidon ton ouranon aneōgmenon, kai idou ippos leukos, kai o kathēmenos ep auton, kaloumenos pistos kai alēthinos, kai en dikaiosunē krinei kai polemei
apo|19|12|	oi de ophthalmoi autou ōs phlox puros, kai epi tēn kephalēn autou diadēmata polla, echōn onomata gegrammena, kai onoma gegrammenon o oudeis oiden ei mē autos,
apo|19|13|	kai peribeblēmenos imation bebammenon en aimati, kai keklētai to onoma autou, o logos tou theou.
apo|19|14|	kai ta strateumata ta en tō ouranō ēkolouthei autō epi ippois leukois, endedumenoi bussinon leukon katharon.
apo|19|15|	kai ek tou stomatos autou ekporeuetai romphaia oxeia distomos, ina en autē patassē ta ethnē kai autos poimanei autous en rabdō sidēra kai autos patei tēn lēnon tou oinou tou thumou tēs orgēs tou theou tou pantokratoros.
apo|19|16|	kai echei epi to imation kai epi ton mēron autou onoma gegrammenon, basileus basileōn kai kurios kuriōn.
apo|19|17|	kai eidon ena aggelon estōta en tō ēliō, kai ekraxen en phōnē megalē legōn pasi tois orneois tois petomenois en mesouranēmati deute sunachthēte eis to deipnon to mega tou theou,
apo|19|18|	ina phagēte sarkas basileōn kai sarkas chiliarchōn kai sarkas ischurōn kai sarkas ippōn kai tōn kathēmenōn ep autōn, kai sarkas pantōn eleutherōn te kai doulōn, kai mikrōn te kai megalōn.
apo|19|19|	kai eidon to thērion kai tous basileis tēs gēs kai ta strateumata autōn sunēgmena poiēsai ton polemon meta tou kathēmenou epi tou ippou kai meta tou strateumatos autou.
apo|19|20|	kai epiasthē to thērion kai o met autou pseudoprophētēs o poiēsas ta sēmeia enōpion autou, en ois eplanēse tous labontas to charagma tou thēriou kai tous proskunountas tē eikoni autou zōntes eblēthēsan oi duo eis tēn limnēn tou puros tēn kaiomenēn en theiō.
apo|19|21|	kai oi loipoi apektanthēsan en tē romphaia tou kathēmenou epi tou ippou, tē exelthousē ek tou stomatos autou kai panta ta ornea echortasthēsan ek tōn sarkōn autōn.
apo|20|1|	kai eidon aggelon katabainonta ek tou ouranou, echonta tēn klein tēs abussou kai alusin megalēn epi tēn cheira autou.
apo|20|2|	kai ekratēse ton drakonta, ton ophin ton archaion, os esti diabolos kai o satanas o planōn tēn oikoumenēn, kai edēsen auton chilia etē,
apo|20|3|	kai ebalen auton eis tēn abusson, kai ekleise kai esphragisen epanō autou, ina mē plana eti ta ethnē, achri telesthē ta chilia etē meta tauta dei auton luthēnai mikron chronon.
apo|20|4|	kai eidon thronous, kai ekathisan ep autous, kai krima edothē autois, kai tas psuchas tōn pepelekismenōn dia tēn marturian iēsou kai dia ton logon tou theou, kai oitines ou prosekunēsan to thērion oute tēn eikona autou, kai ouk elabon to charagma epi to metōpon autōn kai epi tēn cheira autōn kai ezēsan kai ebasileusan meta tou christou chilia etē
apo|20|5|	kai oi loipoi tōn nekrōn ouk ezēsan eōs telesthē ta chilia etē. autē ē anastasis ē prōtē.
apo|20|6|	makarios kai agios o echōn meros en tē anastasei tē prōtē epi toutōn o deuteros thanatos ouk echei exousian, all esontai iereis tou theou kai tou christou, kai basileusousi met autou chilia etē.
apo|20|7|	kai otan telesthē ta chilia etē, luthēsetai o satanas ek tēs phulakēs autou,
apo|20|8|	kai exeleusetai planēsai ta ethnē ta en tais tessarsi gōniais tēs gēs, ton gōg kai ton magōg, sunagagein autous eis ton polemon, ōn o arithmos autōn ōs ē ammos tēs thalassēs.
apo|20|9|	kai anebēsan epi to platos tēs gēs, kai ekukleusan tēn parembolēn tōn agiōn kai tēn polin tēn ēgapēmenēn kai katebē pur ek tou ouranou apo tou theou kai katephagen autous
apo|20|10|	kai o diabolos o planōn autous eblēthē eis tēn limnēn tou puros kai tou theiou, opou kai to thērion kai o pseudoprophētēs, kai basanisthēsontai ēmeras kai nuktos eis tous aiōnas tōn aiōnōn.
apo|20|11|	kai eidon thronon megan leukon kai ton kathēmenon ep autō, ou apo prosōpou ephugen ē gē kai o ouranos, kai topos ouch eurethē autois.
apo|20|12|	kai eidon tous nekrous, tous megalous kai tous mikrous, estōtas enōpion tou thronou, kai biblia ēnoichthēsan kai allo biblion ēnoichthē, o esti tēs zōēs kai ekrithēsan oi nekroi ek tōn gegrammenōn en tois bibliois kata ta erga autōn.
apo|20|13|	kai edōken ē thalassa tous nekrous tous en autē, kai o thanatos kai o adēs edōkan tous nekrous tous en autois, kai ekrithēsan ekastos kata ta erga autōn.
apo|20|14|	kai o thanatos kai o adēs eblēthēsan eis tēn limnēn tou puros outos o thanatos o deuteros estin.
apo|20|15|	kai ei tis ouch eurethē en tē biblō tēs zōēs gegrammenos, eblēthē eis tēn limnēn tou puros.
apo|21|1|	kai eidon ouranon kainon kai gēn kainēn o gar prōtos ouranos kai ē prōtē gē apēlthon, kai ē thalassa ouk estin eti.
apo|21|2|	kai tēn polin tēn agian ierousalēm kainēn eidon katabainousan ek tou ouranou apo tou theou, ētoimasmenēn ōs numphēn kekosmēmenēn tō andri autēs.
apo|21|3|	kai ēkousa phōnēs megalēs ek tou ouranou legousēs idou ē skēnē tou theou meta tōn anthrōpōn, kai skēnōsei met autōn, kai autoi laos autou esontai, kai autos o theos met autōn estai,
apo|21|4|	kai exaleipsei ap autōn o theos pan dakruon apo tōn ophthalmōn autōn, kai o thanatos ouk estai eti, oute penthos oute kraugē oute ponos ouk estai eti oti ta prōta apēlthon.
apo|21|5|	kai eipen o kathēmenos epi tō thronō idou kaina poiō panta. kai legei moi grapson, oti outoi oi logoi pistoi kai alēthinoi eisi.
apo|21|6|	kai eipe moi gegonen. egō to a kai to ō, ē archē kai to telos. egō tō dipsōnti dōsō ek tēs pēgēs tou udatos tēs zōēs dōrean.
apo|21|7|	o nikōn, estai autō tauta, kai esomai autō theos kai autos estai moi uios.
apo|21|8|	tois de deilois kai apistois kai ebdelugmenois kai phoneusi kai pornois kai pharmakois kai eidōlolatrais kai pasi tois pseudesi to meros autōn en tē limnē tē kaiomenē en puri kai theiō, o estin o thanatos o deuteros.
apo|21|9|	kai ēlthen eis tōn epta aggelōn tōn echontōn tas epta phialas tas gemousas tōn epta plēgōn tōn eschatōn, kai elalēse met emou legōn deuro deixō soi tēn numphēn tēn gunaika tou arniou.
apo|21|10|	kai apēnegke me en pneumati ep oros mega kai upsēlon, kai edeixe moi tēn polin tēn agian ierousalēm katabainousan ek tou ouranou apo tou theou,
apo|21|11|	echousan tēn doxan tou theou o phōstēr autēs omoios lithō timiōtatō, ōs lithō iaspidi krustallizonti
apo|21|12|	echousa teichos mega kai upsēlon, echousa pulōnas dōdeka, kai epi tois pulōsin aggelous dōdeka, kai onomata epigegrammena, a estin onomata tōn dōdeka phulōn tōn uiōn israēl.
apo|21|13|	ap anatolōn pulōnes treis, kai apo borra pulōnes treis, kai apo notou pulōnes treis, kai apo dusmōn pulōnes treis.
apo|21|14|	kai to teichos tēs poleōs echon themelious dōdeka, kai ep autōn dōdeka onomata tōn dōdeka apostolōn tou arniou.
apo|21|15|	kai o lalōn met emou eiche metron kalamon chrusoun, ina metrēsē tēn polin kai tous pulōnas autēs kai to teichos autēs.
apo|21|16|	kai ē polis tetragōnos keitai, kai to mēkos autēs oson kai to platos. kai emetrēse tēn polin en tō kalamō epi stadious dōdeka chiliadōn to mēkos kai to platos kai to upsos autēs isa esti.
apo|21|17|	kai emetrēse to teichos autēs ekaton tessarakonta tessarōn pēchōn, metron anthrōpou, o estin aggelou.

apo|21|19|	oi themelioi tou teichous tēs poleōs panti lithō timiō kekosmēmenoi o themelios o prōtos iaspis, o deuteros sappheiros, o tritos chalkēdōn, o tetartos smaragdos,
apo|21|20|	o pemptos sardonux, o ektos sardion, o ebdomos chrusolithos, o ogdoos bērullos, o enatos topazion, o dekatos chrusoprasos, o endekatos uakinthos, o dōdekatos amethustos.
apo|21|21|	kai oi dōdeka pulōnes dōdeka margaritai ana eis ekastos tōn pulōnōn ēn ex enos margaritou. kai ē plateia tēs poleōs chrusion katharon ōs ualos diaugēs.
apo|21|22|	kai naon ouk eidon en autē o gar kurios o theos o pantokratōr naos autēs esti, kai to arnion.
apo|21|23|	kai ē polis ou chreian echei tou ēliou oude tēs selēnēs ina phainōsin autē ē gar doxa tou theou ephōtisen autēn, kai o luchnos autēs to arnion.
apo|21|24|	kai peripatēsousi ta ethnē dia tou phōtos autēs, kai oi basileis tēs gēs pherousi tēn doxan kai tēn timēn autōn eis autēn,
apo|21|25|	kai oi pulōnes autēs ou mē kleisthōsin ēmeras nux gar ouk estai ekei
apo|21|26|	kai oisousi tēn doxan kai tēn timēn tōn ethnōn eis autēn.
apo|21|27|	kai ou mē eiselthē eis autēn pan koinon kai o poiōn bdelugma kai pseudos, ei mē oi gegrammenoi en tō bibliō tēs zōēs tou arniou.
apo|22|1|	kai edeixe moi potamon udatos zōēs lampron ōs krustallon, ekporeuomenon ek tou thronou tou theou kai tou arniou.
apo|22|2|	en mesō tēs plateias autēs kai tou potamou enteuthen kai ekeithen xulon zōēs, poioun karpous dōdeka, kata mēna ekaston apodidoun ton karpon autou, kai ta phulla tou xulou eis therapeian tōn ethnōn.
apo|22|3|	kai pan katathema ouk estai eti kai o thronos tou theou kai tou arniou en autē estai, kai oi douloi autou latreusousin autō
apo|22|4|	kai opsontai to prosōpon autou, kai to onoma autou epi tōn metōpōn autōn.
apo|22|5|	kai nux ouk estai eti, kai ou chreia luchnou kai phōtos ēliou, oti kurios o theos phōtiei autous, kai basileusousin eis tous aiōnas tōn aiōnōn.
apo|22|6|	kai legei moi outoi oi logoi pistoi kai alēthinoi, kai kurios o theos tōn pneumatōn tōn prophētōn apesteile ton aggelon autou deixai tois doulois autou a dei genesthai en tachei.
apo|22|7|	kai idou erchomai tachu. makarios o tērōn tous logous tēs prophēteias tou bibliou toutou.
apo|22|8|	kagō iōannēs o akouōn kai blepōn tauta. kai ote ēkousa kai eblepsa, epesa proskunēsai emprosthen tōn podōn tou aggelou tou deiknuontos moi tauta.
apo|22|9|	kai legei moi ora mē sundoulos sou eimi kai tōn adelphōn sou tōn prophētōn kai tōn tērountōn tous logous tou bibliou toutou tō theō proskunēson.
apo|22|10|	kai legei moi mē sphragisēs tous logous tēs prophēteias tou bibliou toutou o kairos gar eggus estin.
apo|22|11|	o adikōn adikēsatō eti, kai o ruparos rupareuthētō eti, kai o dikaios dikaiosunēn poiēsatō eti, kai o agios agiasthētō eti.
apo|22|12|	idou erchomai tachu, kai o misthos mou met emou, apodounai ekastō ōs to ergon estai autou.
apo|22|13|	egō to a kai to ō, o prōtos kai o eschatos, archē kai telos.
apo|22|14|	makarioi oi poiountes tas entolas autou, ina estai ē exousia autōn epi to xulon tēs zōēs, kai tois pulōsin eiselthōsin eis tēn polin.
apo|22|15|	exō oi kunes kai oi pharmakoi kai oi pornoi kai oi phoneis kai oi eidōlolatrai kai pas o philōn kai poiōn pseudos.
apo|22|16|	egō iēsous epempsa ton aggelon mou marturēsai umin tauta epi tais ekklēsiais. egō eimi ē riza kai to genos dauid, o astēr o lampros o prōinos.
apo|22|17|	kai to pneuma kai ē numphē legousin erchou. kai o akouōn eipatō erchou. kai o dipsōn erchesthō, kai o thelōn labetō udōr zōēs dōrean.
apo|22|18|	marturō egō panti tō akouonti tous logous tēs prophēteias tou bibliou toutou. ean tis epithē epi tauta, epithēsei o theos ep auton tas plēgas tas gegrammenas en tō bibliō toutō
apo|22|19|	kai ean tis aphelē apo tōn logōn tou bibliou tēs prophēteias tautēs, aphelei o theos to meros autou apo tou xulou tēs zōēs kai ek tēs poleōs tēs agias, tōn gegrammenōn en tō bibliō toutō.
apo|22|20|	legei o marturōn tauta nai erchomai tachu. amēn, nai erchou, kurie iēsou.
apo|22|21|	ē charis tou kuriou iēsou christou meta pantōn tōn agiōn amēn.
